Dharmasamuccaya

bhikṣuṇā avalokitasiṃhena samudbhāvitaḥ

dharmasamuccayaḥ

prathamam udānam

(jitadharmakāyavargāḥ parivarto hyanityatā ।
apramādaḥ kāmatṛṣṇe strī ca madyena te daśa ।।

jitavargaḥ

maṅgalācaraṇam

।। om namo buddhāya ।।

prahīṇasarvāsrava nirmalaśrīryaḥ kleśajambālanimagnalokam ।
kṛpāguṇenodaharatsamena praṇamyate asmai tribhavottamāya ।।

granthakārapratijñā

saddharma smṛtyupasthānasūtravaipulyasāgarāt ।
gāthāḥ samuddhariṣyāmi lokalocanatatparāḥ ।।

mokṣasyāyatanāni ṣaṭ

apramādastathā śraddhā vīryārambhastathā dhṛtiḥ ।
jñānābhyāsaḥ saṃtāśleṣo mokṣasyāyatanāni ṣaṭ ।।

nava śāntisamprāptihetavaḥ

dānaṃ śīlaṃ damaḥ kṣāntirmaitrībhūteṣvahiṃsatā ।
karuṇāmuditopekṣā śāntisamprāptihetavaḥ ।।

narakasyāgrahetavaḥ

cāpalyaṃ pāpasaṃśleṣaḥ krūratā vitathaṃ vacaḥ ।
mithyādṛṣṭiḥ pramādaśca narakasyāgrahetavaḥ ।।

preteṣu ṣaṭ udbhavakāraṇāni

mātsaryamīrṣyā kaṭuvākyatā hi pramādasevā viratiḥ śubhācca ।
tattveṣvabhidroharataṃ manaśca preteṣu panthāna ihodbhavanti ।।

tiryagyonau udbhavasādhanāni

ajñānasevā jaḍa ca buddheḥ saddharmanāśaḥ priyamaithunatvam ।
āhāraśaktiḥ prabalā ca nidrā tiryaggatau ca pravadanti hetum ।।

karmaphalam

aśubhaṃ trividhaṃ kṛtvā kāyavāṅmanasāṃ mahat ।
uttarottarasambaddhaṃ karmaṇā sampradṛśyate ।।

bālānāmapi sambaddhamuttarottarameva tat ।
śubhañca trividhaṃ kṛtvā sādhavo yānti nirvṛtim ।।

tasmāt karmaphalaṃ matvā pramādasya ca varjanam ।
śreyase kriyate buddheretat sukhamanuttamam ।।

dānaśīlavato nityaṃ sarvasattvānukampinaḥ ।
siddhayanti sarvaśastulyāstasmācchīlaparo bhavet ।।

kasya kāryasiddhiḥ bhavati?

maitrīkaruṇāyuktasya gatākāṃkṣasya dehinaḥ ।
parānugrahayuktasya kāryasiddhirdhruvaṃ sthitā ।।

santuṣṭasyāpramattasya sarvasattvahitaiṣiṇaḥ ।
rāgadveṣavimuktasya kāryasiddhirdhruvaṃ sthitā ।।

mitrāmitraprahīṇasya samacittasya dehinaḥ ।
apāyagatibhinnasya kāryasiddhirdhruvaṃ sthitā ।।

evaṃ ca tasya dhīrasya dharmadānaratasya ca ।
mātsaryerṣyāpramuktasya kāryasiddhirdhruvaṃ sthitā ।।

saṃvarasthasya śāntasya gurupūjāratasya ca ।
kāryākāryavidhijñasya kāryasiddhirdhruvaṃ sthitā ।।

aśaṭhasyātidakṣasya priyavākyasya nityaśaḥ ।
dhyānādhyayanaśaktasya kāryasiddhirdhruvaṃ sthitā ।।

deśakālavidhijñasya sādhyāsādhyaṃ vijānataḥ ।
śakyopāyavidhijñasya kāryasiddhirdhruvaṃ sthitā ।।

krodhādivijayasādhanamukhena dharmatāsvarūpanirūpaṇam

akrodhena hataḥ krodhaḥ kṣamayā krūratā jitā ।
dharmeṇa nirjito adharmaḥ prabhayā vijitaṃ tamaḥ ।।

satyādeḥ praśaṃsā

mṛṣāvākyaṃ satyahataṃ paiśunyaṃ ca samādhinā ।
pārūṣyaṃ mārdava jitaṃ abaddhaṃ bandhanā jitam ।।

prāṇātipāto maitryā ca steyaṃ dānaiḥ sadā jitam ।
ayoniśomanaskāro yonijena sadā jitaḥ ।।

avidyā vidyayā jitā divasena tathā kṣapā ।
śuklapakṣeṇa ca kṛṣṇapakṣo sarvaśo jitaḥ ।।

mithyākāmeṣvavijito buddhayā tattvavicārayā ।
āryāṣṭāṅgena mārgeṇa yonijena sadā jitaḥ ।।

vaiśāradyaiścaturbhiśca kadarya jitameva tat ।
vismṛtiśca hatā smṛtyā kṣaṇenātmānameva ca ।।

araṇyavāsaniyatairjitā rāgavaśā narāḥ ।
meruṇā parvatā jitā vanamālikā ।।

samudreṇa jitā sarve tīrthā jalasambhavāḥ ।
ādityatejovijitā sarve ca grahatārakāḥ ।।

nityā jitā anityena dāridrayaṃ dānasampadā ।
śāṭhyaṃ na mārdava jitaṃ satyenānṛtiko hataḥ ।।

bhūtena nirjito abhūto vahninā tarusampadaḥ ।
pipāsā vijitā toyairjighitsā bhojanaistathā ।।

vīryapraśaṃsā

siṃhena vijitāḥ sarve mṛgāḥ sattvādhikāśca ye ।
santāpena mahecchā ca jitā nityaṃ prakīrtyate ।।

dayā praśasyate nityamadayā naiva śasyate ।
vīryeṇa nirjitaṃ sarva kausīdyaṃ mohavardhanam ।।

tattvadarśipuruṣapraśaṃsā jñānādhikaiḥ sadā dāntaiḥ puruṣaistattvada bhiḥ ।
vijitāḥ krūrakarmāṇo mithyāvādādhikā narāḥ ।।

buddhena nirjitāḥ sarve tīrthyāḥ kuṭilavādinaḥ ।
asurā vijitā devairdharmateyaṃ vyavasthitā ।।

।। iti jitavargaḥ prathamaḥ ।।

dharmopadeśavargaḥ

guruḥ kīdṛgbhavet?

yo hi deśayate dharma kṣemaṃ nirvāṇagāminam ।
sa sarvabandhanacchettā gururbhavati dehinām ।।

chittvā mohamayaṃ pāśaṃ yo hi deśayate śivam ।
sanmārgadeśakaḥ prokto durmārgavinivārakaḥ ।।

dharmasya pravaratvam yena dharmeṇa manujāstaranti bhavasāgaram ।
saddharmaprabaraḥ prokto na dharmo laukiko hi saḥ ।।

kṣetrāṇīmāni catvāri vidyante yasya dehinaḥ ।
tasyedaṃ saphalaṃ janma kathitaṃ mārgadeśakaiḥ ।।

sakalendriyatāṃ prāpya labdhvā buddhasya śāsanam ।
yo na dharmarato martyaḥ sa paścādanutapyate ।।

yamasāyujyam vyāsaktamanasāṃ nityaṃ nityaṃ kāmagaveṣiṇām ।
putradāraprasaktānāmantako abhyeti dehinām ।।

cittasya vaśīkaraṇam saṅkalpadoṣamanasaṃ taistairdoṣaiḥ samākulam ।
cittaṃ nayatyupāyena cittabaddhā hi dehinaḥ ।।

durdamasyāticaṇḍasya siddhiprepsorviśeṣataḥ ।
na cittasya vaśaṃ gacchet śatrubhūtaṃ hi tannṛṇām ।।

saśrutena sudiṣṭena bhāvitenāpyanekaśaḥ ।
dharmeṇa śāmyate cittaṃ jālineva yathā hayaḥ ।।

saddharmaśravaṇaphalam saddharmaśravaṇaṃ kṛtvā pāpād viramate pumān ।
śreyase pratipattiṃ ca nityamevopapadyate ।।

saddharmaśravaṇaṃ kṛtvā manaḥ prahalādamṛcchati ।
kuśalaṃ cāsya sumahat sandhāne sampratīkṣate ।।

śrutvā bhavati dharmātmā śrutvā pāpaṃ na kurvate ।
śrutvā karmaphalaṃ jñātvā nirvāṇamadhigacchati ।।

śrutvā vedayate dharma śrutvā buddhaḥ prasīdati ।
śrutvā dharmaṃ vimokṣāya yatate paṇḍito naraḥ ।।

dharmalakṣaṇatattvajñaḥ śrutvā bhavati mānavaḥ ।
tasmācchrutvā prayatnena buddhiḥ kāryā prayatnataḥ ।।

śrutvā saṃsāravimukhāṃ kathāṃ sugatadeśitām ।
prahāya tṛṣṇāṃ vividhāṃ prayāti padamavyayam ।।

caturvidhāṃ pratyayitāṃ dharmāṇāṃ codamavyayau ।
śrutvā tāṃ jñāyate sarvā pumān śraddhāvibhāvitaḥ ।।

skandhāyatanadhātūnāṃ yadetallakṣaṇadvayam ।
śrutvā tajjñāyate sarva tasmāt dharmaparo bhavet ।।

prabalā ye trayo doṣāḥ sarvasaṃsārabandhanāḥ ।
te praṇaśyantyaśeṣeṇa saddharmaśravaṇena vai ।।

pravṛtterlakṣaṇaṃ kṛtsnaṃ nivṛtteścāpyaśeṣataḥ ।
śrutimāṃstat prajānāti tasmācchrutamanuttamam ।।

mṛtyukālopapannasya vedanārtasya dehinaḥ ।
na vyathā śrutamālambya svalpāpi hṛdi jāyate ।।

samyagjñānena ye dagdhāḥ kleśavṛkṣāḥ samantataḥ ।
na teṣāmudbhavo bhūyaḥ kadācidupalabhyate ।।

apramādavidagdhaṃ hi śrutaṃ sarva sukhodayam ।
śreyasaśva śrutaṃ mūlaṃ tasmācchrutaparo bhavet ।।

saddharmaśravaṇaṃ śrutvā vṛddhāṃścopāsya paṇḍitaḥ ।
prayātyanuttamaṃ sthānaṃ jarāmaraṇavarjitam ।।

dharmeṇa vartate śrutvā duḥkhānmucyeta vai yathā ।
śrutvā bhavati maitryātmā tasmācchreyaḥ paraṃ śrutam ।।

kāyavāṅmanasāṃ buddhiḥ śrutvā bhavati dehinām ।
tasmāt sadbuddhikāmo yastena śrotavyamādarāt ।।

śrutvā bhāvaṃ samāśritya dṛḍhavīryaparākramam ।
taranti puruṣāstūrṇa tribhava vipulaṃ mahat ।।

śrutvā yaḥ puruṣaḥ sarvairdhanavānabhijāyate ।
aśrutārthadhanairyuktaṃ daridraṃ prāhustaṃ budhāḥ ।।

saddharmanāśaphalam

saddharmadhananaṣṭasya guruṇā varjitasya ca ।
viphalaṃ jīvitaṃ ceṣṭaṃ pāpairupahatasya ca ।।

pramādādīnāmaniṣṭaphalasādhanatvam

pramādinaḥ kusīdastha pāpamitrasya dehinaḥ ।
jīvitaṃ niṣphalaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ bījamuptaṃ yathosare ।।

śāstraprāmāṇyam

śrutadṛṣṭivinirmuktamarthamāhurvicakṣaṇāḥ ।
na cakṣurbhyāṃ vinirmuktamarthamityabhidhīyate ।।

dharmasevanāgrahaḥ yo hi dharma parityajya adharmamanutiṣṭhati ।
sa bhaiṣajyaṃ parityajya vyādhimevopasevate ।।

sevatāṃ sevatāṃ puṃsāṃ dharmo bhavatyanekaśaḥ ।
varṣāṇāṃ samavāyena yathodyānaṃ pravardhate ।।

iha vajrāsane bhūmirna saṃsāre anyathā bhavet ।
bodhicittasamutthānaṃ bodhiprāptistathottamā ।।

dharmacārī praśāntātmā kāyotthāyī samāhitaḥ ।
avaśyaṃ śubhabhāgīsyāt sa pramādena vañcitaḥ ।।

jñānasevanāgrahaḥ tasmājjñānaguṇānmatvā jñānaṃ seveta paṇḍitaḥ ।
nahyajñānena saṃyuktaṃ pumān kaścit pratibhavet ।।

dharmānusāriṇī śraddhā dharmānusāriṇī śraddhā yathā yāti sukhāvahā ।
sātidurgatisanyaktā vyasaneṣu mahad balam ।।

pradīpakalpā tamasi vyādhitānāmivauṣadham ।
arthānāṃ netra bhūtā sā daridrāṇāṃ mahadbalam ।।

bhavādyairhriyamāṇānāṃ pūrvabhūtā sukhāvahā ।
pramādamadamattānāṃ sā pramādavighātikā ।।

śāntapadaprāpteḥ phalam sa hi yattatpadaṃ śāntaṃ nirvāṇamunibhirvṛtam ।
tat prāpayatyakhedena samyagjñānapuraḥsaram ।।

।। iti dharmopadeśavargaḥ dvitīyaḥ ।।

kāyajugutsāvargaḥ

kāyasya svarūpanirūpaṇam

satkārairvṛhaṇairmāsairapi śayyāsanādibhiḥ ।
na svīkartumayaṃ kāyaḥ kadācit kenacit kṛtaḥ ।।

kāyasya riputvam

kṛtaghnasyāvidakṣasya nityaṃ randhraprahāriṇaḥ ।
kaḥ kāyasya riporartha pāpaṃ kuryād vicakṣaṇaḥ ।।

rogānī tamanarthānāṃ bahūnā bhājanaṃ tathā ।
aśucyaṅgasya nikaraṃ kāyamityabhidhīyate ।।

avijñeyaṃ maraṇaṃ jīvitañca kṣaṇikam

upasthitamavijñeyaṃ maraṇaṃ tattvacintakaiḥ ।
jīvitaṃ ca kṣaṇādūrdhvaṃ na gacchati nirūpyate ।।

kāyasya heyatvam

āyuṣkarmārthanirmāṇametaṃ kāyaṃ tyajyayam ।
api viddhastathā śete kāṣṭhaloṣṭhasamo bhuvi ।।

kṣaṇe kṣaṇe api kāyo ayaṃ jīryate na nivartate ।
tathā yauvanamadairbālā muhayante ।।

dhanadhānyamadairmattāḥ kurvantyahitamātmanaḥ ।
tannāśamupayātyevaṃ sa ca pāpena dahayate ।।

adhārmikanindā

na manuṣyā manuṣyāste yebhyo dharmo na rocate ।
na mārge ca sthitāstattve nirvāṇapuragāmike ।।

manuṣyayoneḥ bhavasāgarataraṇopāyaḥ

kathaṃ prāpya hi mānuṣyaṃ śreyasāmālayaṃ mahat ।
na jñānaplavamārūhaya taranti bhavasāgarāt ।।

jīvanasya kṣaṇikatā

vidyudālātasadṛśaṃ gandharvanagaropamam ।
sadā tad yāti rabhasaṃ jīvitaṃ sarvadehinām ।।

śarīre na madaṃ kuryāt kṣaṇike bhaṅgure sadā ।
itvare capale asāre jarāmaraṇabhīruke ।।

dhyāyinānnagataṃ hyetat śokānāmālayo mahān ।
śubhāśubhānāṃ kṣetraṃ ca śarīramavadhīyate ।।

saphalajīvanarahasyam

jñānaśīladayādānairyasya gātraṃ vibhūṣitam ।
tasya sattvaikasārasya śarīraṃ saphalaṃ matam ।।

dhātujñānāt mokṣaḥ

dhātūnāṃ mārakāt sarvamidaṃ muktaṃ kalevaram ।
śarīradhātu vicayāt sākṣād bhavati netarāt ।।

śarīradhātuṃ yo muktvā dhātuṣvanyeṣu rajyate ।
sa dhātukatvaśikṣāto duḥkhenaiva pramucyate ।।

hiraṇyadhāturna tathā duḥkhaśāntyai hi vartate ।
śarīradhātutattvajño yathā duḥkhāt pramucyate ।।

duḥkhād duḥkhodayastena duḥkhī na parirakṣyate ।
pravīṇo rājacaurādibhayaiḥ sarvairūpadrutam ।।

tasmādanarthakaṃ nityaṃ dūratastaṃ vivarjayet ।
varjanāt sukhito duṣṭasaṅgrahād duḥkhitaḥ pumān ।।

śarīradhātutattvajño dhātulakṣaṇatattvavit ।
dhyānādhyayanasaṃsakto dahati kleśaparvatān ।।

tasmāccharīrajān dhātūn paṇḍitaḥ pratyavekṣate ।
teṣāṃ svalakṣaṇaṃ jñātvā mokṣo bhavati dehinām ।।

।। iti kāyajugupsāvargastṛtīyaḥ ।।

parivartavargaḥ

kasya kālaḥ parivartate

kāmairevāvitṛṣṇasya tṛṣṇayā tṛṣitasya ca ।
cañcalendriyacittasya kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।।

anityadhyeyatā yasya sukhasaktasya dehinaḥ ।
strīdarśanena mattasya kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।।

jātimaraṇavaśyasya mohitasya ca tṛṣṇayā ।
bālasya tu janasyāsya kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।।

gaticārakabaddhasya udvegavaśagasya ca ।
pramādaviṣamūḍhasya kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।।

auddhatyādiprasaktasya gātraśobhāratasya ca ।
lābhairatṛptamanasaḥ kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।।

pañcabandhanabaddhasya ṣaḍbhirvyāmohitasya ca ।
trailokyavidhimūḍhasya kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।।

vinipātānabhijñasya vitarkopahatasya ca ।
janasya saktamanasaḥ kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।।

tatkālaramaṇīyeṣu pariṇāmahiteṣu ca ।
kāmeṣu saktamanasaḥ kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।।

pūrvaduḥkhānabhijñasya divyasaukhyaratasya ca ।
viprayogānabhijñasya kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।।

karmajālena baddhasya manasyeva viceṣṭinaḥ ।
satpathāt paribhraṣṭasya kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।।

bhavadoṣānabhijñasya tṛṣṇayā mūḍhacetasaḥ ।
mohāndhakāramagnasya kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।।

kāmaikapāśabaddhasya niḥsahāyasya dehinaḥ ।
devīgaṇavimūḍhasyaṃ kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।।

indriyād vyapakṛṣṭasya satpathabhrāmitasya ca ।
traidhātukarasajñasya kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।।

saṃvarāsaṃvarajñasya vyāpādabahulasya ca ।
naṣṭasambuddhamārgasya kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।।

hitāhitavahirgasya kāryākāryajaḍasya ca ।
krīḍābāla sadṛśasya kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।।

nadīprastravaṇocceṣu vanopavanabhūmiṣu ।
krīḍātatparasyāsya kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।।

vimānagiripṛṣṭheṣu dharmākaravaneṣu ca ।
ramataḥ kāmabhogeṣu kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।।

karmadharma vipākeṣu nirāsaktasya dehinaḥ ।
kevalāhārasaktasya kālo ayaṃ parivartate ।।

śarīrasthitasyāpi śarīrānabhijñatā

karmaṇāyuḥ pariśrāntaṃ traidhātukamidaṃ sadā ।
bhramanti cakravannityaṃ na ca vindanti bāliśāḥ ।।

jagataḥ doṣānabhijñatā

vinipātocchru yamayaṃ yo nāmārohate jagat ।
na ca doṣāvadheyatvaṃ prakurvanti vimohitāḥ ।।

dhīrasya kāmaparivarjanaṃ saukhyahetuḥ

etat paramaṃ saukhyaṃ yat kāmaparivarjanam ।
vītakāṃkṣasya dhīrasya gataśokasya tāpinaḥ ।।

munīnāṃ caramapadaprāptiphalam

tadādimadhyanidhane kalyāṇaṃ kṣemamuttamam ।
yad prāpyamunayaḥ śrāntāścaranti vigatajvarāḥ ।।

duḥkhahetavaḥ kāmāḥ

satkāmajaṃ bhavet saukhyaṃ vinipātagataṃ tu tat ।
na hi kāmaviśeṣaṃ ca kiñcid duḥkhavipākajam ।।

tasmāt kāmeṣu matimān na lubhyet kathañcana ।
te hi saṃsāraduḥkhānāṃ hetubhūtāḥ sudāruṇāḥ ।।

vanopavanaśaileṣu padmākaravaneṣu ca ।
vibhrāntāstṛṣṇayā bālāḥ patanti saha daivataiḥ ।।

śubhakarmāsakteḥ upadeśaḥ

kāñcaneṣu śaileṣu vaidūryaśikhareṣu ca ।
kṣīyate hi śubhaṃ karma yatasva saha daivataiḥ ।।

kalpavṛkṣeṣu ramyeṣu nadīprastravaṇeṣu ca ।
caratastaiḥ śubhaṃ kṣīṇaṃ yatasva saha daivataiḥ ।।

bhūmibhāgeṣu ramyeṣu ratnākaravaneṣu ca ।
na śubhaṃ te sadā cīrṇa yatasva saha daivataiḥ ।।

pañcātmakena vīryeṇa manaḥprahalādakāriṇā ।
hatasya gatakālasya yatasva saha daivataiḥ ।।

devānāṃ hitānabhijñatā

kāmaṃ saṃsakta manasairnityaṃ viṣayatatparaiḥ ।
na jñāyate hitaṃ devairyadamantrāhitaṃ bhavet ।।

devanindā

alpaśiṣṭamidaṃ puṇyaṃ cyavanaṃ samupasthitam ।
gantavyamanyatra suraiḥ sukarmaphalabhojibhiḥ ।।

ye nityaṃ śubhasaṃsaktāḥ kurvanti vā śubhaṃ sadā ।
teṣāṃ visadṛśo heturmūrkhāṇāṃ hi vivartate ।।

ke mṛtyuṃ pratīkṣante

bhuktvā mṛtyuṃ pratīkṣante te janāḥ kāmamohitāḥ ।
śubhaśīlatamo ajñānāḥ sarvadā na parāyaṇāḥ ।।

bhuktvā mṛtyuṃ pratīkṣante te janāḥ kāmamohitāḥ ।
ye na karmavipākasya jñānaṃ roṣavadhe ratāḥ ।।

bhuktvā mṛtyuṃ pratīkṣante te janāḥ kāmamohitāḥ ।
prajñāpayanti na samā stṛṣṇāgniparivāritāḥ ।।

bhuktvā mṛtyuṃ pratīkṣante te janāḥ kāmamohitāḥ ।
viprayogakṛtaṃ duḥkhaṃ ye na paśyanti dāruṇam ।।

bhuktvā mṛtyuṃ pratīkṣante te janāḥ kāmamohitāḥ ।
strījanāsaktahṛdayā na vindanti punarbhavam ।।

bhuktvā mṛtyuṃ pratīkṣante te janāḥ kāmamohitāḥ ।
vipattivyādhiśokebhyo nodvijanti kathañcana ।।

bhuktvā mṛtyuṃ pratīkṣante te janāḥ kāmamohitāḥ ।
ye pāpamitrasaṃsarga prakurvanti mahārūṣam ।।

bhuktvā mṛtyuṃ pratīkṣante te janāḥ kāmamohitāḥ ।
bhāvitaṃ cetasā yairna na ca tattvapraveśitā ।।

bhuktvā mṛtyuṃ pratīkṣante te janāḥ kāmamohitāḥ ।
yena sarvāsvavasthāsu saṃsārabhayabhīravaḥ ।।

bhuktvā mṛtyuṃ pratīkṣante te janāḥ kāmamohitāḥ ।
kāryākāryeṣu ye nityaṃ na subhāṣitacetasaḥ ।।

bhuktvā mṛtyuṃ pratīkṣante te janāḥ kāmamohitāḥ ।
ye na tattvadhiyo nityaṃ sarvabhūtahite ratāḥ ।।

bhuktvā mṛtyuṃ pratīkṣante te janāḥ kāmamohitāḥ ।
ye śarīra sukhārthena dharma hiṃsanti mohitāḥ ।।

paṇḍitalakṣaṇam

ekāntamanasā nityaṃ śubhaṃ kāryaṃ prayatnataḥ ।
aśubhaṃ ca sadā varjyametat paṇḍitalakṣaṇam ।।

vinipātasādhanāni

kṣayaṃ yātaṃ ca yat śīlaṃ spṛṣṭvā yaḥ samupāgataḥ ।
pramādāvañcito avaśyaṃ vinipāto bhaviṣyati ।।

viṣayiṇaḥ parivartanaśīlatā na tu viṣayāṇām

gatā gacchanti yāsyanti deveśāścaiva sarvataḥ ।
tiṣṭhanti śikhare ramye nānāratnavibhūṣite ।।

vaidūryaśikharā ramyāstathānye vanamālinaḥ ।
viṣayāstādṛśā eva janastu parivartate ।।

vanopavanaramyāṇi bhūmibhāgāni sarvaśaḥ ।
tiṣṭhantyavikalānyeva janastu parivartate ।।

vaidūryamayanālāni kāñcanāni viśeṣataḥ ।
padmākarāṇi tānyeva janastu parivartate ।।

sarāṃsi sarito ramyāḥ pakṣisaṅghairnirantaram ।
tathaivāvikalā hyete janastu parivartate ।।

vimānāni rathāścaiva harmyāṇi ca tathaiva ca ।
tiṣṭhantyavikalā hyete janastu parivartate ।।

parivartanaṃ lokasya viṣayairvañcitasya ca ।
tathāpi nāmalokasya nodvego hṛdi jāyate ।।

abhyāsena kharī bhūtaṃ cittaṃ saṃsāracāriṇam ।
yena manye mahad duḥkhaṃ hṛdaye naiva vartate ।।

śūlikena yathā baddhāḥ paśavo gṛhapañjare ।
ekaikaśo vinaśyanti śeṣāṇāṃ nāsti sambhramaḥ ।।

sukhāya kāmināmeva iyaṃ bhūmiravasthitā ।
cyutāścaivopapannāśca tathāmī bāliśāḥ surāḥ ।।

viṣayonmukhānāṃ maraṇānabhijñatvam

pramādāya hatāḥ sattvā mṛtyuḥ kṣaṇikaduḥkhadaḥ ।
nāvabuddhayanti maraṇaṃ paśuvad vītasambhramāḥ ।।

te paścād dīrghamanasaḥ kālasya vaśamāgatāḥ ।
paścāttāpamayo vahnirdhakṣyate niṣpratikṣayaḥ ।।

dāruṇaṃ niṣpratīkāramavaśyaṃ rūpadehinām ।
maraṇaṃ kālavaśagaṃ tad viditvāgamaṃ caret ।।

viprayogāntāḥ sarve saṃyogāḥ

samāgamāḥ priyāloke viyogāścāpriyāḥ sadā ।
saṃyogo viprayogānto dharmateyaṃ sanātanā ।।

kṣaṇe lave muhūrte ca divārātrau tathādhvani ।
maraṇaṃ cintayed dhīrastasya nāsti pratikriyā ।।

gatakalmaṣā eva śāntimadhigacchanti

smṛtimagnyāṃ praśaṃsanti yeṣāṃ maraṇasaṃbhavā ।
śreyasaikaparāṃ śānti prayāntiṃ gatakalmaṣāḥ ।।

mṛtyorarthamanusmṛtya doṣo ayaṃ kasya sammataḥ ।
nirdoṣaṃ hi manaḥ sarvaṃ śāntaṃ bhavati nityaśaḥ ।।

tathāgataiḥ apramādaparaṃ śreṣṭhamuktam

apramādaparaṃ śreṣṭhamidamuktaṃ tathāgataiḥ ।
yanmṛtyoḥ smaraṇaṃ nityamaśubhānāṃ ca varjanam ।।

।। iti parivartavargaścaturthaḥ ।।

anityatāvargaḥ

sukhaṃ kṣayāntam

kṣayāntaṃ hi sukhaṃ sarva na sukhaṃ vidyate dhruvam ।
saṃsṛjenna sukhaṃ tasmāt yadīcchet sukhamātmanaḥ ।।

mṛtyuḥ sarvānapi ākarṣati

gacchatāṃ tiṣṭhatāṃ caiva hasatāṃ krīḍatāmapi ।
avisahyo mahāvego mṛtyurnaśyati dāruṇaḥ ।।

na tatstha mihāmutra yatrāsau pratipadyate ।
tathāpi nāma saṃmūḍhā janayitvā vaśaṃgataḥ ।।

na sthavirameva vā ।
gṛhasthamagṛhasthaṃ vā yadāsau nāpakarṣati ।।

sukhitaṃ duḥkhitaṃ vāpi guṇavantaṃ tathaiva ca ।
vratasthamavratasthaṃ vā yadāsau nāpakarṣati ।।

duḥśīlaṃ śīlavantaṃ ca ।
rājānaṃ cottamaṃ cāpi yadāsau nāpakarṣati ।।

daivaṃ vā nārakaṃ vāpi tiryañca pratajaṃ tathā ।
pramattamapramattaṃ vā yadāsau nāpakarṣati ।।

kāmadhātūpapannaṃ vā rūpadhātau sthitañca yaḥ ।
ārupyadhātūpapannaṃ vā yadāsau nāpakarṣati ।।

karmapāśo jarādaṇḍo vyādhidaṇḍo mahāvanam ।
raktopamo mṛtyurayaṃ sattvānādāya gacchati ।।

evaṃvidhe pratibhaye mṛtyau paramadāruṇe ।
surāḥ kāmavimohitāḥ ।।

patanāntaṃ sarvasukhaṃ santyajet

yad duḥkhaṃ cyavamānasya devalokāt surasya ca ।
narake yadbhavaṃ duḥkhaṃ viprayogapuraḥsaram ।।

viṣamākṣikasaṃyuktaṃ yathānnaṃ cāpi ।
devagataṃ saukhyaṃ patanāntaṃ visarjayet ।।

kṣīṇapuṇyasya dīnasya svadārairvarjitasya ca ।
yad duḥkhaṃ cyavamānasya tasyaupamyaṃ na vidyate ।।

sukṛtakṣīṇamandasya dvipasyeva gatattviṣaḥ ।
śāmyati devasya yadduḥkhaṃ mahadduḥkhaṃ prajāyate ।।

devasyāpi cyavanam

tṛṣṇāviṣayavṛddhasya śokopahatacetasaḥ ।
mandavāgdehaceṣṭasya devasya cyavanād bhayam ।।

duḥkhasya viṣayataratvam

yathā yathā sukhāsvādāḥ kāmā paramavañcakāḥ ।
tathā bhavatyeva teṣāṃ duḥkhaṃ mahattaram ।।

yatamānasya yad duḥkhaṃ devalokān prajāyate ।
tasyāntareṇa narakaṃ kalāṃ nārhati ṣoḍaśīm ।।

cyavanāntaṃ devalokaṃ maraṇāntaṃ tadā bhuvi ।
dṛṣṭvā duḥkhaṃ ।।

saukhyaṃ patanāntam

patanāntaṃ sadā saukhyaṃ nāsti lokasya nityajāḥ ।
tad buddhvā kāraṇaṃ sarva śreyase kriyatāṃ manaḥ ।।

sarva duḥkhāntam

sarve kṣayāntā nicayā patanāntā samucchrayāḥ ।
saṃyogā viprayogāntā maraṇāntaṃ hi jīvitam ।।

jātasya maraṇaṃ nityaṃ na tasyāstīti nityatā ।
na bhūtārāvitānena triṣu dhātuṣu dṛśyate ।।

garbhameke vinaśyanti tathaike sūtikāgṛhe ।
parisarpaṇakāścaike tathaiva ।।

maraṇaṃ dhruvam

udayāstaṃ ca gamanaṃ bhāskarasya pradṛśyate ।
tathā jātasya sarvasya sthitaṃ maraṇamagrataḥ ।।

sarva sukhaṃ kṣayāntam

kṣayāntaṃ hi sukhaṃ sarva yo na vindati mohadhīḥ ।
sa paścānmaraṇe prāpte ।।

kuśalaṃ kārya priyaḥ sadā ।
sukhaṃ hi dharmācaraṇaṃ kathayanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।।

anityamadhruvaṃ sarva pariṇāme kaṭuḥ sadā ।
saṃsāraḥ kathito buddherhetustattvavicāraṇe ।।

devāḥ sukhapramattā ye teṣāṃ sukhamaśāśvatam ।
cyavamānasya ca yadduḥkhaṃ devalokāt surasya hi ।।

tasyopamānaṃ naivāsti narakānnarakaṃ hi tat ।
kimete nāvabudhyante patanāntaṃ sadā sukham ।।

ajarāmaravallokaṃ paśyanti sukhamohitāḥ ।

cyutyupapattimallokaḥ saṃkhyā tasya na vidyate ।
na codvijanti puruṣāstṛṣṇayā parivañcitāḥ ।।

abhiyāti sadā janma tvaritaṃ yāti yauvanam ।

saṃyogo viprayogaśca sahajaḥ paridṛśyate ।
vimūḍhā nānupaśyanti viṣayaiḥ parivañcitāḥ ।।

tṛṣṇāvivaśā devāḥ cyavanti

cyavanti devāḥ vivaśāstṛṣṇayā parimohitāḥ ।
sā bhūmistāni padmāni vanāni vividhāni ca ।।

sarvapadārthānāmāpātaramaṇīyatvam

śikharāgrāṇi ramyāṇi ratnavanti mahānti ca ।
sarāṃsi nadyo vividhā ratnapāṣāṇabhūṣitāḥ ।।

vṛkṣā vicitrakusumāḥ paṅktibhirvividhaiḥ sthitāḥ ।
harmyāgrāṇi ca ramyāṇi ratnavanti mahānti ca ।।

kalpavṛkṣā hemamayā kecidvaidūrya nirmalāḥ ।
rājatāstapanīyāśca vimiśrā vararohiṇaḥ ।।

bhramarairūpagītāśca vibhānti kamalākarāḥ ।
vibhūṣaṇāni ramyāṇi devārhāṇi ca sarvataḥ ।।

sarva kṣaṇikam

sarvametat tathaivāsti janastu parivartate ।
māyābudbudaphenābhaṃ gandharvanagaropamam ।।

sukhaṃ sarvasya devasya tṛṣṇayā vañcitasya hi ।
sa vināśya janaṃ sarva bhrāmayitvā bhavārṇave ।।

tṛṣṇaiva duḥkhamūlam

tṛṣṇā viṣāgnisadṛśā lokānāmatra tiṣṭhati ।
avitṛptā kāmabhogairapi taptā sukhodbhavā ।।

kālānalena nirdagdhā kva te devagaṇāḥ gatāḥ ।
sarvathādhigatā yeyaṃ tṛṣṇā lokavitanvinī ।।

yayā vimohitā devāḥ kālasya vaśamāgatāḥ ।
devāsurā narā yakṣā narake yānti jaṅgamāḥ ।।

kālapāśayojitaṃ traidhātukamidam

gacchanti vivaśāḥ sarve kālapāśaṃ durāsadam ।
traidhātukamidaṃ sarva kālapāśena yojitam ।।

tṛṣṇāvimohitāḥ maraṇaṃ na paśyanti

na ca paśyanti vivaśāstṛṣṇāmohena mohitāḥ ।
anena hi yathā devāḥ śataśo atha sahastraśaḥ ।।

gatāḥ kālāgninirdagdhā viṣayairdhanasaṃbhavaiḥ ।
parasya dṛśyate maraṇamātmano naiva dṛśyate ।।

paścātte vyasane prāpte vindante duḥkhamātmanaḥ ।
pramādakaluṣaṃ ceto viṣayābhirataṃ sadā ।।

na vindanti dhruvaṃ mṛtyuṃ dehināṃ sahajasthitam ।
sukhottaramanāśasya pramādābhiratasya ca ।।

mṛtyusainyamupaitīdaṃ pramāthi viṣasannibham ।
na mantrauṣadhakarmāṇi na devā nāsurāstathā ।।

kālapāśabaddhasya na ko api trātā

kālapāśena baddhasya trātāro na bhavanti te ।
rajasā guṇṭhitaṃ vaktraṃ ātmano naiva vindati ।।

tṛṣṇāyā heyatve hetuḥ

prāpteścyavanabhūto ayaṃ mṛtyuḥ paścād bhaviṣyati ।
lolupasya sadā yatnairavitṛptasya tṛṣṇayā ।।

sahasābhyeti maraṇaṃ yannadṛṣṭaṃ sukhārthinām ।
ayaṃ tavāgraho duḥkhaṃ mṛtyunā preṣito mahān ।।

asmādanantaraṃ mṛtyurbhaviṣyati sudāruṇaḥ ।
mahāgirivarādasmāt vanopavanabhūṣitāt ।।

baddhānarā viṣayagā svakarmaphalabhoginaḥ ।

krīḍāvihāriṇastāvat kvacit tṛṣṇāsukhaṃ na hi ।
tarṣyayā tṛṣṇayā mūḍhāḥ patanti vivaśā bhuvi ।।

dhūmasyānantaraṃ vahniryathā bhavati nityaśaḥ ।
tathā cyavanaliṅgasya pṛṣṭhataścyavanaṃ sthitam ।।

jātyā jātyā dhruvaṃ mṛtyuścārogye sati ruk sthitā ।
sampattau vyasanaprāptiyauvane sahajā jarā ।
sarvaiḥ priyairviyogaśca na saṃyogo dhruvaṃ sthitaḥ ।।

dharmatāyāḥ mahattvam

dharmateyaṃ sadāloke samyagbuddhena deśitā ।
ubhayasya kṣayo nāśo janasyo parivartate ।।

jātau satyāṃ yathā mṛtyuravaśyaṃ sthita eva hi ।
kṣīyate sukṛtaṃ karma āyūṃṣi kṣaṇikāni hi ।।

saṃvarādikaṃ bhajadhvam

saṃvara dharmavinaye bhajadhvaṃ puruṣottamāḥ ।
abhyeti yauvanaṃ sarvaṃ jīvitaṃ cānugacchati ।।

sarvasya nāśaśālitvam

naśyanti sarvadā sarvā mā pramāde manaḥkṛthā ।
na nityaṃ labhyate svargo na nityaṃ kṣaṇasampadā ।।

yasya yāvannābhipatanaṃ tāvat kṣipraṃ yujyatām ।
।।

ayaṃ sa hi drumavano nānāratnavibhūṣitaḥ ।
latāgahvarasaṃcchannaḥ padmākaravibhūṣitaḥ ।।

jāmbūnadamayaiśśuddhaiḥ prāsādaiḥ ratnacitritaiḥ ।
nānāvidhaiḥ prastravaṇairlatābhirupaśobhitaḥ ।।

karmasākṣījanasyāsya bhitvā gaganamucchritaḥ ।
kalpāgnivirato meruḥ sarvathā na bhaviṣyati ।।

kiṃ punarye surāstatra phenabudbudasannibhāḥ ।
utpadyante vinaśyanti pramādamadamohitāḥ ।।

sukhaduḥkhamanantaṃ ca svecchākāmaphalodbhavam ।
devalokād yathā devāḥ patanti narake punaḥ ।।

tad duḥkhaṃ paramaṃ kaṭu

śarīramānasaiduḥkhairvidyamāneṣu sarvataḥ ।
na tacchakyaṃ pramatte syāt tadduḥkhaṃ paramaṃ kaṭu ।।

viyogaduḥkhaṃ duḥkhanāmagrataḥ paripaṭhyate ।
taccadevagatau nityamagrataḥ sampravartate ।।

sarvapriyairmanāpaiśca viprayogo bhaviṣyati ।
na ca devāḥ prapaśyadhvaṃ maraṇāntaṃ hi jīvitam ।।

cyutikāle tu samprāpte vihvalendriyacetasā ।
jānīdhvaṃ tatparaṃ duḥkhaṃ yadavaśyaṃ bhaviṣyati ।।

sarvaṃ kṣaṇikam

akālacakrapratimaṃ gandharvanagaropamam ।
tribhave saṃbhavaṃ sarva phenabudbudasannibham ।।

yaḥ phenarāśau saṃmūḍhaḥ kuryācchādanasaṃstaram ।
sa mūḍhaḥ saṃskṛte kuryādabhisvādaṃ bhramātmakam ।।

mṛtyumahimā

na devā na narā yakṣā nāsurā garuḍāstathā ।
trāyante mṛtyusamaye karmaṇā paritapyatām ।।

yāvannāyāti samaye mṛtyurājaḥ sudāruṇaḥ ।
tāvattu sukṛtaṃ kārya mā paścāt paritapyatha ।।

yadbhūtakāmajaṃ saukhyaṃ prākṛtaṃ viṣayodbhavam ।
mṛtyukāle samutpanne tiṣṭhanti na budharṣamā ।।

kiṃ kariṣyanti saukhyāni kiṃ striyaḥ kiñcabāndhavāḥ ।
mṛtyunā hriyamāṇasya devalokāt samantataḥ ।।

sthirāstā bhūmayaḥ sarvā vanopavanabhūṣitāḥ ।
mṛtyurajjvā vibaddhaśca tvantu kālena nīyase ।।

ākāśe jaladā yadvada vāyunā samudīritāḥ ।
saṃśliṣṭāśca viyujyante saṃsāre prāṇinastathā ।।

ṛtau ṛtau yathā puṣpamāgatairdṛśyate naraiḥ ।
vyatīte tu ṛtau sarve pratiyānti yathāgatāḥ ।।

yathā kāle samutpanne modante sukṛtaiḥ surāḥ ।
vyatīte tu śubhe kāle pratiyānti yathāgatāḥ ।।

ṛtau ṛtau yathā vṛkṣe parṇajāyate anekaśaḥ ।
vyatīte tu śubhe kāle śīryate tat samantataḥ ।।

yathā parṇopamādetanna saukhyamabhayaṃ bhave ।
śīryate satataṃ saukhyaṃ nāsaukhyaṃ vidyate dhruvam ।।

prābṛṭkāle yathā varṣamākāśe na nivartate ।
tathā saukhyamidaṃ sarva gacchati na nivartate ।।

barhiṇāṃ ca yathā nādo vāyunā samudīritaḥ ।
śrūyate tatpraṇāśāya tathā saukhyamidaṃ smṛtam ।।

yathā hi jvalane kṣiptaṃ dhruvaṃ kālaṃ pradahayate ।
tathā vahanyupamaḥ kālaḥ kāṣṭhavaccaratāṃ smṛtaḥ ।।

āgatāśca gatāścaike śataśo atha sahastraśaḥ ।
saṃvego na bhavatyeṣā tṛṣṇayā mohitāstathā ।।

yathā yathā mahāsaukhyaṃ svayaṃ bhogo yathā yathā ।
tathā tathā mahad duḥkhaṃ patanāntodbhavaṃ dhruvam ।।

jātyādi duḥkhaparamparā

jātirduḥkhā jarā duḥkhā maraṇaṃ duḥkhameva ca ।
priyaiśca saha viśleṣo duḥkhasyaiṣā paramparā ।।

mṛtyunā na bibhet

ekasya patanaṃ dṛṣṭvā kathaṃ nodvijate janaḥ ।
mamāpi patanaṃ hyetat sarvapāpairbhaviṣyati ।।

yaḥ paśyati bhayaṃ dūrāt pratipattau ca vartate ।
mprāpte mṛtyusamaye na vibheti gatavyathaḥ ।।

vibhujyamāno daunaiśca mṛtyuḥ svajanabāndhavaiḥ ।
yadduḥkhaṃ mṛtyusamaye tanna śakyaṃ prabhāṣitum ।।

patanāntaṃ hi maraṇaṃ patamāno yathā giriḥ ।
niṣpratyanīkaṃ balavat puruṣānapakarṣati ।
saṃśliṣyate mahāvegaḥ samprahārī ca sarvadā ।।

taṃ jñātvā mā pramādeṣu stubadhvaṃ devasattamāḥ ।
saṃśleṣayati viśleṣaṃ yauvane ca sadā jarā ।।

jīvite ca sadā mṛtyuḥ padametat sadā sthitam ।
anityenāgnināvaśyaṃ dagdhabyo yatra gocaraḥ ।।

kalpānte kiṃ punardevā ye phenakadalīsamāḥ ।
na tadasti bhavet kiñcid yad jñānaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ calam ।।

yannityaṃ sukhaṃ vā syādetatsthānaṃ na vidyate ।
upasthitamiva jñeyaṃ maraṇaṃ sarvajantubhiḥ ।।

yasmāt tasya pratīkāraḥ sarvopāyairna śakyate ।
rūpaṃ kṣaṇikameteṣāṃ vayo api kṣaṇikaṃ tathā ।।

kṣīyate ca tathā saukhyaṃ na ca buddhayantyamedhasaḥ ।
yadā tat sarvameteṣāmanekaṃ śubhalakṣaṇam ।।

janmataḥ kālacakreṇa paripāṭayā vināśitam ।
tathaivaitat purā naṣṭamanekaśatalakṣaṇam ।।

tathaitadapi janmaiṣāṃ mṛtyurājo hariṣyati ।
pramādamanasāṃ hyeṣāṃ nityaṃ sukhavihāriṇām ।।

nidhanāya kālapāśo ayamabhyeti sukhanāśakaḥ ।
sukhārogyabalaprāṇapriyaviśleṣakārakaḥ ।।

balavanmṛtyurājo asau samīpamupasarpati ।
yaḥ samīpagato hyeṣāṃ pramattānāmanekaśaḥ ।।

sukhanāśaḥ suniścitaḥ

jīvitaṃ saha saukhyena tvaritaṃ nāśayiṣyati ।
dīrghakālamidaṃ dhvastaṃ pramādāpahatāḥ surāḥ ।।

nāvabuddhayanti mohāndhāḥ saukhyena pratibodhitāḥ ।
yadā hīnaprabhāhyete vihvalendriyacetasaḥ ।।

yamalokaṃ patiṣyanti tadā jñānasya tatphalam ।
jīyate bata kālo ayaṃ kṣaṇikaṃ ca yathā sukham ।।

tathāpi raktamanaso nāvabuddhayantyacakṣuṣaḥ ।
ramyād ramyataraṃ yānti nityaṃ sukhavihāriṇaḥ ।।

prayāsyanti yathā hayete mṛtyurājo hariṣyati ।
jarā jātivipattīnāṃ yo na mūḍho viṣīdati ।।

sa paścāt mṛtyusamaye tapyate ।
sukhaṃ deveṣu samprāpya guṇasammatam ।।

kṛtahutaṃ vināśāntaṃ kṣaṇikaṃ jīvitaṃ calam ।
yathā hi yad vināśāntaṃ tathaiṣāmapi jīvitam ।।

acireṇāpi kālena bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ ।
yāvannāyāti maraṇaṃ yāvad buddhiranāvilā ।।

manasā dharmaratiḥ kāryā

tāvaddharmarataṃ dhārya manobalena dhīmatā ।
sarvajīvitanāśāya sarvasaukhyakṣayāya ca ।।

priyaviyogaḥ niścitaḥ

sarvapriyaviyogāya mṛtyurāśrayameti ca ।
tasminnāpte mahādhyāne mṛtyuḥ paramadāruṇaḥ ।।

nānyat trāṇamṛte dharmāt tasmād dharmarato bhavet ।
upapannasya devasya yā prītirupapadyate ।।

nāsau cyavanaduḥkhasya kalāmarhati ṣoḍaśīm ।
mṛtyukāle samutpanne na kaścit kasyacit tathā ।।

sarvasya nāśatvam

na ca gacchantimapyekaṃ padamekaṃ hi gacchati ।
yadā jātaṃ tadāramya naro mṛtyuparāyaṇaḥ ।।

nānāmohaparītastu bhayametanna vidyate ।
yadā te cyavanaṃ prāpte bhavabhogakaraṃ param ।।

tadā vindati mūḍhātmā yad bhayaṃ mṛtyujaṃ mahat ।
viṣayoragasandaṣṭā tṛṣṇā viṣavimohitā ।।

na vindanti sadā devāścyavanānte mahad bhayam ।
cyavanti ca tathā duḥkhamutpādayanti dehinām ।।

yathopapattiścyavanaṃ devānāṃ samprajāyate ।
karmavāyusamudbhrāntaṃ prayogeṇa ca duḥkhitam ।।

puruṣaṃ nayate mṛtyuravaśaṃ ।
na mātaro na pitaro na mitrāṇi na bāndhavāḥ ।।

sahāyatāṃ vrajantīyaṃ puruṣaṃ kālacoditam ।
asahāyo janaścāyaṃ janaḥ prakṛtivañcitaḥ ।।

mana eva pāśabandhanam

kevalaṃ tu manaḥpāśairbandhanairbadhyate janaḥ ।
na janaḥ svajanaśceha trātā bhavati kasyacita ।।

gṛhīta iva keśeṣu mṛtyunā dharmamācaret
mṛtyukāle samutpanne svajano api yathā janaḥ ।
yastvaṃ paśyasi devānāṃ sukhametanmahodayam ।।

tat prasahyamahādevo mṛtyurājo hariṣyati ।
tvaritaṃ yāti janmedaṃ na ca vindati bāliśaḥ ।।

paścāttu vyasane prāpte prativindanti duḥkhinaḥ ।
yadi duḥkhādbhayaṃ tvaritaṃ yadi mṛtyubhayaśca yaḥ ।।

dharme hi kriyatāṃ buddhirevaṃ sukhamavāpsyatha ।
vināśāntaṃ sadā saukhyamanityaṃ sarvataścalam ।।

devatvaṃ patanāntam

sarvadevakṛtaṃ saukhyaṃ na ca vindanti mohitāḥ ।
abhūtvā ca cyavantyete bhūtvāvaśyaṃ hi cañcalāḥ ।।

devāḥ patanabhāvāya dharmateyaṃ vyavasthitā ।
pramattāḥ kāmabhogeṣu ye devāścalamānasāḥ ।।

na paśyanti surāstīvraṃ vyasanāntaṃ hi jīvitam ।
yadaiva jāyate devastadaiva maraṇāya saḥ ।।

śreyase matiḥ karttavyā

divasānte yathā rātriravaśyaṃ pratipadyate ।
divasaṃ jīvitaṃ proktaṃ rātriḥ sthānmaraṇopamā ।।

tasmāt tadubhayaṃ jñātvā śreyase kriyatāṃ manaḥ ।
tadetadartha nṛṇāṃ hi strīrāgavaśavartinām ।।

tadiṣṭaṃ mṛtyusainyena prasahayamavamarditam ।
bhāvābhāvādibhirmūḍhān vañcayitvā striyo narān ।।

prayānti mṛtyusamaye svakarmaphalabhoginaḥ ।
padmopavanaśaileṣu nadīnāṃ nirjhareṣu ca ।।

bahuśaḥ krīḍanaṃ kṛtvā kūpāyābhigatāḥ priyāḥ ।
avaśyambhāvi maraṇamavaśyaṃ ca viyogitā ।।

tathāpi nāma puruṣā nityaṃ rāgavaśānugāḥ ।
sukhitaṃ duḥkhitaṃ vā jīrṇamanyatra yauvanam ।।

mṛtyurājo avamardati

duṣkulīnaṃ kulīnaṃ vā mṛtyurājo avamardati ।
surūpaṃ vā virūpaṃ vā balavantaṃ tathābalam ।।

sanāthaṃ naṣṭanāthaṃ vā mṛtyurājo avamardati ।
rājānaṃ vā tathā mṛtyuḥ gṛhiṇaṃ vā tathā yatim ।।

krūraṃ vā mṛdukaṃ vāpi mṛtyurājo avamardati ।
nirdhanaṃ vā daridraṃ vā saguṇaṃ nirguṇaṃ tathā ।।

striyaṃ vā puruṣaṃ vāpi mṛtyurājo avamardati ।
pravāsinaṃ gṛhasthaṃ vā jale vāpi sthalesthitam ।।

sthitaṃ vā giriśṛṅgeṣu mṛtyurājo avamardati ।
jāgarantaṃ tathā suptaṃ bhuñjānaṃ vā tathā sthitam ।।

pramāthī sarvalokasya mṛtyurājo avamardati ।
bhūmisthaṃ vimānasthaṃ videśasthaṃ tathā gṛhe ।।

krakacaḥ kālacakro ayaṃ mṛtyurājo avamardati ।
bhāgyavantaṃ tathā dhanya nistriśaṃ dharmikam ।।

rogiṇaṃ svasthadehaṃ vā mṛtyurājo avamardati ।
caṇḍaṃ suśīlinaṃ cāpi kadarya dhaninaṃ tathā ।।

pramattamapramattaṃ vā mṛtyurājo avamardati ।
nārakeyaṃ tathā pretaṃ tiryañco manujaṃ tathā ।।

anivṛttabalotsāho mṛtyurājo avamardati ।
kāmadhātau ca ye devā rūpadhātau ca ye sthitāḥ ।।

tān sarvān hi pratibalān mṛtyurājo avamardati ।
ārūpyeṣu ca ye devāḥ samāpattiniveśakāḥ ।
tān sarvānapi vai devān mṛtyurājo avamardati ।।

sarva vināśāntam

yad jātaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ kiñcid tad vināśāntameva hi ।
tannāsti saṃskṛtaṃ kiñcid yasya nāśo ca vidyate ।
mṛtyorbalamidaṃ jñātvā kāmadoṣaṃ ca sarvataḥ ।।

tṛṣṇayā vañcanaṃ cāpi viramadhvaṃ bhavārṇavāt ।
tadaitad vyasanaṃ matvā mṛtyorapi calācalam ।।

sudāntaṃ kriyatāṃ cittam

sudāntaṃ kriyatāṃ cittaṃ yenedaṃ bhrāmyate jagat ।
vanopavanaśailebhyo vimānebhyaśca sarvataḥ ।।

sarvadevāḥ paciṣyanti kālāgnivinipātitāḥ ।
pramādamanaso mūḍhā bhūyo viṣayajihimatāḥ ।।

tṛṣṇāpāśena sambaddhā devāḥ yāsyanti durgatim ।
rabhasaṃ jīvitaṃ saukhyaṃ prayāti khalu dehinām ।।

na ca vindanti vibudhā jātyandhā iva satpatham ।
jalabudbudasaṃkāśaṃ jīvitaṃ sarvadehinām ।।

nadītaraṅgacapalaṃ yauvanaṃ vyativartate ।
anityā kaṭākṣekṣāpraduḥkhāstuṣitāḥ surāḥ ।।

rāgasya heyatvam

nirvāyatyavaśo dīno dīpaḥ snehakṣayādiva ।
karmakṣayaparikṣipto dvādaśāro mahābalaḥ ।।

dharmacakro bhavatyeṣa nipātī syānna cañcalaḥ ।
vicitraviṣayāramyā anekasukhamaṇḍitāḥ ।।

kālagrāsāḥ sarve bhavanti

tuṣitāḥ patanti vivaśāḥ kālasya vaśamāgatāḥ ।
kālasya vaśamāpannā yathā rohanti pādapāḥ ।।

te punaḥ kālamāsādya bhavanti vigatatviṣaḥ ।
yathā kālaṃ samāpadya bhavanti sukhitāḥ surāḥ ।।

punastamaiva saṃsṛtya patanti vivaśā hi te ।
karmakālaṃ samāsādya loko ayaṃ parivartate ।।

sukhaṃ vrajati duḥkhaṃ hi kālasya vaśamāgataḥ ।
yadvṛttaṃ prākśubhaṃ karma tacca duṣṭamahodayam ।।

tadidaṃ bhuñjate svargaṃ kṣīyate ca tataḥ punaḥ ।
sahetukasya sarvasya kṣaṇikasya viśeṣataḥ ।।

anityatāparāmarśo nāsau bhavati sarvataḥ ।
ye bhāvāḥ saṃskṛtā nityāḥ sarve te vipralobhinaḥ ।।

vipralobhya janaṃ yāti dharmateyaṃ vyavasthitā ।
śīghrasrotā yathā nadyastathā saukhyaṃ śarīriṇām ।।

kṣaṇikaṃ jīvitaṃ sarva na ca vindanti bāliśāḥ ।
jarā vyādhiśca mṛtyuśca vipattiḥ karmasaṃkṣaye ।।

bhavantyetāni devānāṃ nityānāṃ kāmacāriṇām ।
nāyurdhruvaṃ bhavatyeva na saukhyaṃ triṣu dhātuṣu ।।

na vindanti vivaśā devāḥ kāmena mohitāḥ ।
varṣadhārā yathākāśe duḥsthā bhavati sarvataḥ ।।

tathā saukhyamidaṃ sarva varṣadhāropamaṃ sadā ।
vāyunā pāṃsavo yānti anyonya parighaṭṭitāḥ ।।

bhrāmyate gagane avaśyastathā śleṣaḥ śarīriṇām ।
suciramapi saṃramyaṃ nityatā nāsti dehinām ।।

acintyārthe saukhyamidaṃ na ca vindanti bāliśāḥ ।
vāteritaṃ tu yat saukhyaṃ vināśāntaṃ bhaviṣyati ।।

sukhasya duḥkhamiśritatvam

vināśaṃ naiva budhyanti kāminaścittavañcitāḥ ।
duḥkhamiśraṃ sukhamidaṃ pracchannamiva vidyate ।।

padmamālāparicchinno viṣapūrṇo yathā ghaṭaḥ ।
odanaṃ viṣasammiśraṃ maraṇāntaṃ tat tathā ।।

tathā saukhyamidaṃ sarva tasmāt tat parivarjayet ।
ādau madhye tathā cānte narakāya bhaviṣyati ।।

utpādasthitibhaṅgāni sarvāṇi vastūni

utpādasthitabhṅgāntaṃ sarva saṃskṛtamucyate ।
sarva ca saṃskṛtaṃ saukhyaṃ nanu bhaṭṭārameva tat ।।

bhaṭṭārañca vilāsaśca vyayakṣaṇikaṃ tathā ।
sukhaṃ ca jīvitaṃ sarva tasmāt tat parivarjayet ।।

ādau madhye tathā cānte śreyasyeva manaḥ sadā ।
sudāntaḥ śuddhacitasya mṛtyukāle na sīdati ।।

maraṇasyāvaśyambhāvitvam

avaśyambhāvi maraṇaṃ priyasya ca viyogatā ।
na ca cintayataḥ kāle viṣaye vipralobhinaḥ ।।

jarāmaraṇacakraṃ tamaviṣahyaṃ sudāruṇam ।
pādapān devagān sattvān na ca buddhayantyacakṣuṣaḥ ।।

sarvasya jātasya cyavanaṃ bhavati

cyavamānasya devasya vikalendriyacetasaḥ ।
yad duḥkhaṃ sukaraṃ tasya naupamyamiha vidyate ।।

yathā yathā mahat saukhyaṃ tṛṣṇopahatacetasaḥ ।
tathā tathā mahad duḥkhaṃ cyavamānasya duḥsaham ।।

kṛtvā hi saṃskṛtaṃ karma na jñātvā karmaṇaḥ sthitiḥ ।
mṛtyukāle samutpanne paścāttāpena dahayate ।।

mṛtyoḥ pūrvameva svahitamādheyam

yāvannāpyeti maraṇaṃ yāvacca kṣaṇasampadaḥ ।
tāvat svahitamādheyameṣa mārgaḥ sukhāvahaḥ ।।

cyavanaṃ devalokeṣu maraṇaṃ narabhūmiṣu ।
viditvā kaḥ pumān āsthāṃ kuryātsopadrave bhave ।।

sarva vināśi

tailavartipraṇāśena dīpanāśo yathā dhruvam ।
karmakriyā tathā kasya vinipātaḥ surālayāt ।
bhittināśo yathāvaśyaṃ cittanāśo dhruvaṃsthitaḥ ।।

karmanāśāttathā saukhyamavaśyaṃ vinipadyate ।
kṣīṇapuṇyāḥ nipatyante devāḥ sarve surālayāt ।।

anityataiṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ sattvānāṃ vinipātikā ।
mṛtyuḥ pivati bhūtāni jarā pivati yauvanam ।।

vyādhiḥ pivati cārogyaṃ na ca loko avabudhyate ।
upapannāḥ subahuśaḥ pratītāścāpyanekaśaḥ ।।

jāyate jīryate cāyaṃ cyavane copapadyate ।
na kṣaṇo asti muhūrto vā parivartastathāpi vā ।।

yatra mṛtyurvilambena na ca loko avabudhyate ।
upapannāstu bahuśaḥ pratītāścāpyanekaśaḥ ।।

yanna mṛtyuvilambaḥ syānna ca loko avabudhyate ।
anityaṃ jīvitaṃ sarva na vilambi ca yauvanam ।।

sarvabhūtānyanityāni na ca loko avabudhyate ।
ante krameṇa naśyanti bhāvāḥ kṣaṇavilamvinaḥ ।।

sambaddhāḥ karmasūtreṇa na ca loko avabudhyate ।
devakoṭisahastrāṇi vanopavanasevinām ।।

nimīlitāni kālena na ca loko avabudhyate ।
paṅkābhāvacarā devāḥ pramattā bhogatṛṣṇayā ।।

yāsyanti vilayaṃ sarve na ca loko avabudhyate ।
phenabudbudasaṅkāśaṃ svapnadravyopamaṃ sukham ।।

kṣayaṃ prayāti śīghraṃ ca na ca loko avabudhyate ।
sarvasya sarvathā sarvo vināśo niyato bhave ।।

na ca bālasya saṃsārānnirvedamupapadyate ।
na sarvaḥ sarvathā sarva sarvopāyaiḥ prayatnaśaḥ ।
saṃtrātā bhavane prāpte mṛtyukāle sudāruṇe ।।

mṛtyurityabhidhīyate

vyucchettā sarvasaukhyānāṃ duḥkhanāmākaro mahān ।
viśleṣaḥ sarvabandhānāṃ mṛtyurityabhidhīyate ।।

bhayopanetā bhūtānāṃ duḥkhānāmudadhiḥ samaḥ ।
vyāmohakarttā buddhīnāṃ mṛtyurityabhidhīyate ।।

sañchettā jīvitānāmindriyāṇāṃ ca nāśakaḥ ।
amṛśyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ mṛtyurityabhidhīyate ।।

adhṛṣyaḥ sarvabhūtānāmajeyaḥ sarvakarmaṇām ।
vināśaḥ sarvasattvānāṃ mṛtyurityabhidhīyate ।।

avaśyambhāvi tattvānāmantakaṃ sarvadehinām ।
nikāyabhāganāśo ayaṃ mṛtyurityabhidhīyate ।।

sadeva yakṣagandharvapiśācoragarakṣasām ।
kālacakravināśī mṛtyurityabhidhīyate ।।

asaṃyamī pramāthī ca bahnivat sarvadehinām ।
krūraścāvinivarttyaśca mṛtyurityabhidhīyate ।।

skandhāyatananāśaśca ārupyasyātha cetasaḥ ।
kāladharmo mahāveśo mṛtyurityabhidhīyate ।।

śreyase matiḥ karaṇīyā na tu pramāde
sa eva dhā ve śīghraṃ vinipātāya dehinām ।
śreyase kriyatāṃ yatno mā pramādeḥ manaḥ kṛthāḥ ।।

gataṃ jīvanaṃ nāyāti

yathā gamanaṃ pakṣiṇāṃ pavanasya vā ।
tathā śīghrataraṃ yāti jīvitaṃ sarvadehinām ।।

gato nivartate vāyurnivartante ca pakṣiṇaḥ ।
jīvitaṃ yanniruddhaṃ tu tasya nāgamanaṃ punaḥ ।।

drutaṃ kṣīyanti karmāṇi drutamabhyeti cāntakaḥ ।
avaśyambhāvi viśleṣaṃ na ca vindanti devatāḥ ।।

anirvāyo mahāvegaścatuḥsatyanivarhaṇaḥ ।
avaśyambhāvi balavāneṣa mṛtyurupaiti ca ।।

śruti pramādino devāḥ sukhena parivañcitāḥ ।
na vindanti mahad duḥkhaṃ yadavaśyaṃ bhaviṣyati ।।

saṃskṛtasya hi sarvasya samayasya viśeṣataḥ ।
vināśo bhavati sau dharmateyaṃ bhave bhave ।।

jarāyauvananāśāya prāṇanāśāya cāntakaḥ ।
vipattibhūtanāśāya sthitā nāśahetavaḥ ।।

evaṃvidhe mahāghore vyasane mahad bhaye ।
pramādino hi yad devāḥ nūnamete ca cetanāḥ ।।

anāgatabhayaṃ yo hi paśyati jñānacakṣuṣā ।
sa paṇḍita iti jñeyo viparītastu bāliśaḥ ।।

karmakṣaye sukhasya nāśaḥ

vimūḍhamanasaḥ sarve vañcitāḥ svena cetasā ।
karmakṣaye tu naśyanti dīpā snehavaśādiva ।।

anekaviṣayāṇāṃ ca idaṃ saukhyamanuttamam ।
bhuktvā karmakṣayo bhūta vinipāto bhaviṣyati ।।

anityatvānavagamādadharmaratiḥ
jalataraṅgacapalaṃ jīvitaṃ yāti dehinām ।
na ca budbudaniḥsāramavagacchanti bāliśāḥ ।।

phenarāśiściraṃ tiṣṭhed upāyaiḥ katibhirnanu ।
na tu devāściraṃ tiṣṭhantyanityo bhāvanamiti ।।

lobhavaśādeva mṛtyorupekṣā

kṛṣyate bhūriyaṃ sarvā manujaiḥ phalakāṃkṣibhiḥ ।
na ca saṃdṛśyate mṛtyurlābhasaktairapaṇḍitaiḥ ।।

kṣaṇe kṣaṇe vivardhante lobhāśā mohite jane ।
na ca vindanti saṃsārāḥ kṣīyamāṇāḥ kṣaṇe kṣaṇe ।।

daṇḍatrayamupasaṃharati

jarādaṇḍo ayamabhyeti yauvanāntakaro nṛṇām ।
ārogyaśaktināśāya vyādhidaṇḍo ayamāgataḥ ।
daṇḍatrayamidaṃ ghoraṃ sasurāsuranāśakam ।।

abhyeti na ca mūḍho ayaṃ lokaṃ paśyati bāliśaḥ ।
parasparaṃ pralobhācca svajanaṃ snehacañcalam ।।

mohabaddhāḥ mṛtyuṃ viyogaṃ ca nāvagacchanti
gacchatyanyonyasaṃśliṣṭo mohabaddhe jane janaḥ ।
putrapautraprapautrāṇāṃ vaśagāścāpi ye narāḥ ।।

karmaskandhasya duḥkhāvahatvam

sarve tena bhaviṣyanti tvaṃ tu saṅgena bādhyase ।
jīvitāntakaraḥ śatrurna viśaṅko mahābalaḥ ।।

so avilambī mahāvego mṛtyureṣo abhyupaiti ca ।
calācalavidhirjñeyaḥ karmaskandhairnidarśitaḥ ।।

devādīnāṃ kṣayo bhavati

devanāgāḥ gandharvā piśācoragarākṣasāḥ ।
na śaktāścyavane kṣāntaṃ balaṃ tasya tathāgatam ।।

tattvadarśako durgatiṃ nādhigacchati

calācalavidhirjñeyaḥ karmaṇā tattvadarśakaḥ ।
aliptaḥ pāpakairdharmairna sa gacchati durgatim ।।

iti anityatāvargaḥ pañcamaḥ

apramādavargaḥ

pramādaratasya na mokṣaḥ

yaḥ pramādarato janturnāsau mokṣāya kalpate ।
pramādaviṣamūḍhasya nirvāṇaṃ dūrameva tat ।।

na pramāde manaḥ kāryam

na pramādeṣu badhyet pramādaḥ śatruruttamaḥ ।
pramādaparamā devāḥ patanti narake punaḥ ।।

svabhāvatāmimāṃ jñātvā dharmāṇāmudayavyayam ।
na pramāde manaḥ kārya pramādaviṣamuttamam ।।

pramādāpramādayoḥ parasparavirodhitvam
apramādo amṛtapadaṃ pramādo mṛtyunaḥ padam ।
apramattā na bhriyante pramattāstu sadātmṛtāḥ ।।

yathā viṣaṃ tathā vahniḥ pramādaḥ prāṇināṃ tathā ।
pramādonmāditāḥ satvāḥ duḥkhād duḥkhaṃ prayānti te ।।

apramattāḥ sadāmartyāḥ sarva prakramasaṃskṛtāḥ ।
prayānti paramāṃ śānti pramādo yatra nāsti hi ।।

yaḥ pramāde rato janturna śubhānyanuceṣṭate ।
tasya dharmavimūḍhasya kutaḥ svargo bhaviṣyati? ।।

pramādaṃ varjayed yasmāt pramādaṃ viṣamuttamam ।
apramattā na bhriyante pramattāstu sadātmṛtāḥ ।।

saubhāgyaṃ prāpya yo martyaḥ pramādeṣu ca vartate ।
na paṇḍita itikhyāto viparītastu nānyathā ।।

na pramādasya kālo hi harṣasya na kathañcana ।
vyāmohajananācceto mṛtyukāle mahābale ।।

pramādamukhena pramādavarṇanam

harṣo dhūmaḥ pramādo agnirdevān dahati naikaśaḥ ।
viṣayairmohitā mūḍhā na ca vindantyacakṣuṣaḥ ।।

avyucchinnāni paśyanti saṃskārāṇi ca dehinām ।
yathā hi viṣayairmūḍhā nāvagacchanti yaddviṣaḥ ।।

tasmāt pramādaṃ viṣavat kathayanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।
sukhaṃ na dṛśyate pūrva pramādomandabuddhibhiḥ ।।

pramādopakṛtāḥ prayānti narakaṃ punaḥ ।
phale prāpte pramādo ayaṃ paścāt santapyate vyathā ।।

pramādo anarthakaraḥ

sarvānarthakaro dṛṣṭaḥ pramādaḥ paṇḍitaiḥ naraiḥ ।
tathā ca kuśalaṃ prāyo yaḥ pramādaṃ na sevate ।।

duḥkhaṃ yasya bhavediṣṭaṃ sa pramādaṃ niṣevatām ।
na pramādaparaḥ kaścit kadācit sukhamāpnuyāt ।।

pramādaśūnyānāmacyutapadaprāptiḥ

pramādaviratāḥ santo gacchanti padamacyutam ।
nā pramādaparaḥ kaścinnarake duḥkhitānnayet ।।

yadi devāḥ sahantīmaṃ ramante mandamedhasaḥ ।
tiraścāṃ hi surāṇāṃ ca viśeṣo naiva vidyate ।।

pramādavaśāt devalokād patanti

pratyekaṃ karmavaicitryaṃ pramādaparamāḥ surāḥ ।
nāvagacchanti patanaṃ devalokād bhaviṣyati ।।

sannikṛṣṭaṃ sadā duḥkhaṃ patanaṃ vā bhaviṣyati ।
devalokottarā devā yathā syāt sukhamātmanaḥ ।।

devalokaṃ samāsādya yaḥ pramādeṣu rakṣate ।
sa kṣīṇaśubhakarmāntaṃ cyavanānte vibudhyate ।।

mā pramādaparobhūyāḥ pramādo nocitaḥ suraiḥ ।
pramādairdoṣavihatāścyavanti tridaśālayāt ।।

pramādavaśagaḥ puruṣaḥ nāśameti

dahyate puruṣaḥ sarvaḥ pramādena vimohitaḥ ।
sa paścād vigate tasmin pratyādeśena rakṣyate ।।

doṣodbhavāmimāṃ bhūmiṃ pramādāvṛttaśādvalam ।
vicaranti sadā mūḍhāḥ surāḥ satkṛtamohitāḥ ।।

cañcalā viṣamāstīvrā pramādāḥ kāmahetavaḥ ।
na teṣāṃ viśvased vīro yasmāt svapnopamā hi te ।।

kāmaḥ nārakasya heturiti

na svapno narake hetuḥ kāmāḥ svapnasya hetukāḥ ।
tasmāt kāmamimaṃ muktvā nityaṃ sucaritaṃ caret ।।

apramādātsarva prāptuṃ śaknoti

yatrāvāptaṃ padaṃ kṛtsnaṃ suraiḥ kāmavimohitaiḥ ।
tat prāpyate padaṃ vīrairapramādaparairnaraiḥ ।।

pramādamūlasaṃsāraḥ

pramādamūlasaṃsāro devānāmālayastathā ।
ye pramādaviṣairmattāste magnā bhavasaṅkaṭe ।।

tamaḥ pramādamūlañca avidyā hayapakārikā ।
andhakāreṇa ye mūḍhāsteṣāṃ cakṣurna vidyate ।।

pramādaḥ mohātmakaḥ

tejasā hi tathā mūlairagninā na ca kathyate ।
mohānāṃ pravarastadvat pramādaḥ parikīrtyate ।।
pramādānalataptena manasā tad viceṣṭate ।
muhayante yena te bālāḥ prayānti narakaṃ punaḥ ।।

pramādonmāditaḥ sukhamevānubhavati

pramādonmāditā devāstrividhā ye calātmakāḥ ।
viyogaduḥkhaṃ vismṛtya saṃyoge sukhakāṃkṣiṇaḥ ।।

patanāntameva jīvanam

upasthite mahāduḥkhe patanānte hi jīvite ।
paścād vahanti virasaṃ patanāntaṃ sukhaṃ calam ।।

saṃyogo viprayogāntaḥ patanāntaḥ sukhaṃ sadā ।
jarāntaṃ yauvanaṃ sarva karmāntaḥ sarvadehinām ।।

saṃsāraḥ karmanāṭakasambaddhaḥ

śubhāśubhena baddhā hi karmaṇā sarvadehinaḥ ।
naṭavannaṭayantyete gatyāṃ gatyāṃ pṛthak pṛthak ।।

karmanāṭakasambaddhaḥ saṃsāro bhramate sadā ।
na tatra viśvaseddhīmānanityā karmaṇāṃ gatiḥ ।।

pramādaḥ paramodoṣaḥ

sarvapāpāni viṣavat pramādaḥ paribarjyatām ।
pramādena tu ye muktā tīrṇāsti bhavārṇavāt ।।

prapātapatito doṣī kadācidapi jīvati ।
na pramādaprapatitaḥ kadāpi sukhavān bhavet ।।

pramādaḥ paramo doṣaḥ kadācit sarvakarmasu ।
na rātrau na divā tasya śubhaṃ bhavati karhicit ।।

yat sukhaṃ laukikaṃ kiñcid yacca lokottaraṃ matam ।
naśyate tat pramādena tasmāt tat parivarjayet ।।

apramādo amṛtapadam

apramādo amṛtapadaṃ pramādo mṛtyunaḥ padam ।
apramādena te devāḥ devānāṃ śreṣṭhatāṃ gatāḥ ।।

pramādamūlaḥ saṃsāraḥ apramādaśca gatiḥ ।
tasmād pramādavirataḥ sukhī bhavati sarvadā ।।

duḥkhād vibheti cet pramādaṃ parityajet

icchate yatsukhaṃ nityaṃ yaśca duḥkhād vibheti ।
sa pramādād viramet pramādo viṣavannṛṇām ।।

pramādanidrāvihatā pramādaviṣamohitāḥ ।
prapātaṃ hi prapadyante janāḥ śukla kṛtātmakāḥ ।।

apramādaḥ paraṃ śreyaḥ

apramādaḥ paraṃ śreyo na pramādaḥ kathañcanaḥ ।
apramādena sukhinaḥ pramādena duḥkhitāḥ ।।

pramādamūḍhāḥ narakaṃ vrajanti

pramādamūḍhā hi narā bhūyo madyena mohitā ।
dhik pramādavimūḍhāste caranti narakaṃ punaḥ ।।

pramādavāgurābaddhā viṣayārṇavasaṃsthitāḥ ।
tṛṣṇāviṣayasambaddho devaḥ krīḍatyanekaśaḥ ।।

jātamātrasya devasya tat kṣaṇaṃ kṣīyate sukham ।
na vindanti vivaśāḥ pramādāvṛttacetasaḥ ।।

pramādavaśaḥ kāmavaśago atṛpta eva tiṣṭhati
pramādod bhrāntamanaso nityaṃ viṣayatatparāḥ ।
atṛptāḥ kāmabhogeṣu sukhena sukhitā hi ca ।।

kāmānalena sandagdhāḥ vipramādena mohitāḥ ।
na vindanti balaṃ sarva vināśāntaṃ hi jīvitam ।।

anekāni sahastrāṇi surāṇāṃ niyutāni ca ।
kāmānalena sandagdhāḥ pramādena vimohitāḥ ।।

pramādayutāḥ patanti

hriyate puruṣaḥ sarvaḥ pramādena vimohitaḥ ।
sa paścād vyasane prāpte budhyate tasya tatphalam ।।

viṣavat prāṇahṛd dṛṣṭaḥ pramādastattvadarśibhiḥ ।
agnivad dahyate nityaṃ śastravacca nikṛntatiḥ ।।

mitravad dṛśyate pūrva paścād bhavati śatruvat ।
vahiśaḥ sarvadevānāṃ pramādaḥ sampravartate ।।

devāsuramanuṣyāṇāṃ nāgānāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।
pramādaḥ kāraṇaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ sarvānnarthān karoti saḥ ।।

yaḥ pramādahato nityaṃ nāsau kalyāṇamarhati ।
kalyāṇavarjitaḥ puruṣo narakānupakarṣati ।।

vividhā kṛtayastiryag pramādaparivañcitāḥ ।
maithune bhojane caiva yeṣāṃ buddhiḥ sadāratāḥ ।।

yadā sucaritaṃ karma cāntībhūtaṃ divaukasām ।
bhaviṣyati tadābhūyaḥ kva yāsyanti pramādinaḥ ।।

pramādavāriṇāṃ duḥṣṭāḥ karmavāyubhirāhatāḥ ।
patanti vṛkṣavad devā gatyāṃ gatyāṃ pṛthak pṛthak ।।

surāṇāmapi saṃvegajanitaḥ śoko jāyate

śataśo na hutaścaiva divi jātā divaukasaḥ ।
na ca saṃvegajanito hṛdi śokaḥ prajāyate ।।

pramādakaluṣaṃ pītvā mohātpānaṃ divaukasaḥ ।
patanti narakaṃ tīvraṃ vahninā parivāritam ।।

sudurlabhasya mānuṣasya janmanaḥ sāphalyavaiphalye

sulabdhaṃ mānuṣaṃ janma ye labdhvā apramādinaḥ ।
kurvanti sukṛtaṃ karma devalokopagāminaḥ ।।

durlabhaṃ mānuṣaṃ karma labdhvāpi ye pramādinaḥ ।
te pramādāt paribhrāntāḥ patanti narake narāḥ ।।

mṛtyusamaye pramādī tapatyeva

pramādaratasattvo yaḥ kṛpayā parivartate ।
sa paścānmṛtyusamaye tapyate svenacetasā ।।

pramādasya dāhakatvam

na tathā dahyate vahnirna ca śastraṃ vikṛntati ।
pañcendriyasamudbhūtaṃ pramādo dahyate tathā ।।

sukharūpaṃ tathā duḥkhaṃ mitrarūpaṃ tathā ripuḥ ।
pramādināṃ hi tannityaṃ tasmāttaṃ parivarjayet ।।

pramādatṛṣṇayā miśro rāgastadanuvardhakaḥ ।
trayaste ripavaḥ kruṣṭāḥ nāśayanti sukhaṃ nṛṇām ।।

ye pramādaratā nityaṃ na ca dharmaratā budhāḥ ।
te mṛtyusamaye prāpte yamadūtaiḥ parākṛtāḥ ।।

viṣavatpramādaṃ matvā tatparityāginaḥdhanyā

pramādaṃ viṣavad ye tu parirakṣanti paṇḍitāḥ ।
te mṛtyusamaye prāpte bhavanti sukhabhāginaḥ ।।

pramādaḥ paramo mṛtyurapramādaḥ paraṃ sukham ।
tasmāt sukhārthināḥ nityaṃ mā pramāde matiṃ kṛthāḥ ।।

dhātvāyatana sammohaḥ śreyasāṃ vidhna

dhātvāyatanasammohaḥ śreyasāṃ vighnakārakaḥ ।
sanyāsaḥ sarvakarmāṇāṃ pramādaḥ sampravartate ।।

doṣayantravilagnāya māyādvārasya dūtakaḥ ।
sammohasyāgraṇī pāpaḥ pramādaḥ sampravartate ।।

pramādaratāḥ mṛtyumukhaṃ prati gacchanti

ye pramādaratā bālāste mṛtyorhastamāsthitāḥ ।
pramādasevakā ye tu te sarve nidhanaṃgatā ।।

pramādino devā api kṣīṇapuṇyāḥ bhavanti

puṇyakṣayāya devānāṃ pramādena vihiṃsitāḥ ।
patanti sukhasaṃmūḍhāstrāṇaṃ teṣāṃ tadā kutaḥ ।।

saddharmācaraṇaṃ bhūtadayaiva

eko dharmastathāśreyaḥ kṛpayā saṃyataḥ pṛthuḥ ।
kṣāntiścāpi sadā yuktā dayā bhūteṣu sarvadā ।।

balabhūtā bhavantyete mṛtyukāle mahābhaye ।
tasmāt pramādarahitaiḥ sevanīyāḥ prayatnataḥ ।।

vidyāvidhijñasyaiva prāṇinaḥ śāntirjāyate

avidyāvartanaṃ śreyo vidyāyā rakṣaṇaṃ sadā ।
vidyāvidhijño yaḥ pramādastasya śāmyati ।
puruṣārtho niyato yat pramādasya varjanam ।।

apramādaratasyaiva puruṣārthasiddhirbhavati
apramādaratasyaiva puruṣārthaḥ satāṃ mataḥ ।
pramādo bandhanaṃ prāyo muktistasyāpramādataḥ ।।

pramādasevanād bandhanam

mokṣabandhanayoretallakṣaṇaṃ syāt satāṃ matam
evaṃ matvā sadā devo yaḥ pramādena rakṣati ।
sa paścānmṛtyusamaye jñāsyate tasya tatphalam ।।

santoṣa eva nirvāṇasādhanam

yathā yathā hi santoṣaḥ sevyate yatibhiḥ sadā ।
tathā tathā hi nirvāṇamanike tasya vartate ।।

virāgaḥ sarvakāmeṣu nirvāṇe ca pravartatām ।
nāsau mārasya viṣayaḥ kadācit sampravartate ।।

jñānenaiva duḥkhaprahāṇam

narāṇāṃ paśya manaso nityaṃ vyāpārameva ca ।
udyogaśca sadājñānaṃ sa kathaṃ duḥkhameṣyati ।।

kaḥ bandhanamukto bhavati?

atītabhayasampannaḥ pratyutpanne ca buddhimān ।
anāgatavidhijño yaḥ sa muktaḥ kleśabandhanāt ।।

apramādarato nityamaviśvāse ca kātaraḥ ।
saṃjñānasevī vimalo nirvāṇasyāntike sthitaḥ ।।

mahatsukhaṃ pramādena naśyati

pramādenāpi naśyanti devāḥ prāpyamahatsukham ।
kiṃ punaryena vā mūḍhāḥ pramādavaśasevinaḥ ।।

mṛtaḥ sa naro bhavati yaḥ pramādavihāravān ।
jīvite ca pramatto ayaṃ satataṃ jñānadhāraṇe ।।

pramādāpramādayorantaram

apramādapramādābhyāmidamantaramiṣyate ।
mṛtyuṃ ca varjayed doṣaṃ pramādaṃ duḥkhamūlakam ।।

nityaṃ pramuditā devāḥ nityaṃ pramuditā vayam ।
pakṣiṇāṃ ca surāṇāṃ ca viśeṣo nopalabhyate ।।

na dharmācaraṇaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ mokṣacaryā na yātyasau ।
tathaiva yadi devānāṃ te gatāḥ pakṣibhiḥ samā ।।

ye pramādavinirmuktā ye ca dharmaratāḥ sadā ।
te devāḥ satpathā loke na pramādavihāriṇaḥ ।।

yadi krīḍāratā devāḥ pramādacaritāḥ sadā ।
devānāṃ ca khagānāṃ ca viśeṣo nopalabhyate ।।

dharmapatitaḥ jātyā na śobhate

karmaṇāṃ tu viśeṣeṇa jātirdharmairviśiṣyate ।
na dharmapatitaḥ kaścid jātyā bhavati śobhanaḥ ।।

yena nindanti saṃsāramimaṃ sarvakṣayātmakam ।
te surāpisamā nityaṃ pakṣibhirmūḍhabuddhibhiḥ ।।

yeṣāmevasthitā buddhiramatā dharmagocare ।
te devāḥ sammattā loke na pramādavicāriṇaḥ ।।

ye janmahetuprabhavaṃ duḥkhaṃ budhyanti śobhanam ।
te devā na tu ye saktāḥ kāmeṣu hitakāriṣu ।।

viyujyamānā bahuśo bhṛtyasvajanabāndhavaiḥ ।
ye nodvijanti saṃsāre te devāḥ pakṣibhiḥ samāḥ ।।

madyapānādhikaḥ pramādaḥ

madyapānādhiko dṛṣṭaḥ pramādastattvadarśibhiḥ ।
jīryate madyapānaṃ hi pramādo naiva jīryate ।।

pramādamatto gatipañcake bhramate

pramādopahatoloko bhramate gatipañcake ।
tasmāt pramādamatto hi sarvopāyairviśiṣyate ।।

pramādaḥ madyādapi hīnataraḥ

ekāhaṃ paramaṃ madyaṃ pramādayati dehinaḥ ।
pramādaḥ kalpakoṭibhirbhramato api na jīryate ।।

ye pramādairvirahitāste gatāḥ padamavyayam ।
ye tu pramādavaśagāste bhavanti khagā narāḥ ।।

hitārthinā manuṣyeṇa pramādovarjya eva hi ।
yasmāt pramādavaśagāḥ kleśā buddhena deśitāḥ ।।

devānāṃ kṛte api pramādo heya eva

khagā yadi pramādena kurvanti laghucetasaḥ ।
kasmāddevāḥ pramādaṃ na jahaṃti viśeṣataḥ ।।

yastu dūrāt pramādena bhayaṃ nāvaiti durmatiḥ ।
so avaśyaṃ vyasane prāpte paścāttāpena dahyate ।।

patanaṃ devalokāt te dānai rakṣanti dāruṇam ।
tad vicintya pramādaste na saṃsevyaḥ kathañcana ।।

ye pramādaratā nityaṃ na te saukhyasya bhāginaḥ ।
pramādo duḥkhamūlaśca mūlamekaṃ sudāruṇam ।।

padmakoṭisahastrāṇi niyutānyarbudāni ca ।
asaṃkhyāni ca devānāṃ pramādena vitanvitāḥ ।।

apramādaḥ paraṃ mitraṃ pramādaśca śatruḥ

apramādaḥ paraṃ nityaṃ hitakaraṃ nṛṇām ।
pramādastu paraṃ śatrustasyanmitraparo bhavet ।।

śubhasyāntakaro hayeṣa viṣavad dāruṇaṃ param ।
durgatīnāṃ paraṃ mārgaḥ pramāda iti kathyate ।।

pramādena pramattā ye viṣayaiścāpi rañjitāḥ ।
narāste mūḍhamanaso nityaṃ duḥkhasya bhoginaḥ ।।

jñānaśūnyāḥ bhayaduḥkhamavigaṇya paśubhiḥ samāḥ bhavanti

yeṣāṃ bhayaṃ na duḥkhaṃ na ca jñānāvalokanam ।
paśubhiste samāviṣṭā na purā sukhakāṃkṣiṇaḥ ।।

āhāramaithunaratiḥ paśūnāṃ hṛdi vartate ।
sā ratiryadi devānāṃ te gatāḥ paśubhiḥ samāḥ ।।

pramādaḥ mṛtyoḥ paryāya eva

krīḍantyatiśayaṃ hyete mṛtyorgamye puraḥsthitā ।
samprāpte mṛtyusamaye phalaṃ dāsyanti ।।

viṣavat pariheyo sarvairapi ।
mṛtyoḥ paryāyanāmaiṣa pramādo hṛdi dehinām ।।

pramādena hatān pūrvaṃ paścānmṛtyuḥ pramardati ।
dharmajīvitasaukhyānāṃ tamekāṃśaṃ prakathyate ।।

apramāda eva svargamārgaḥ

apramāda iti khyātaḥ svargamārga pradeśakaḥ ।
arthānathau samāvetau paścānmokṣastathaiva ।।

apramādaḥ guṇaḥ pramāda eva doṣaḥ

apramādaḥ pramādaśca guṇadoṣasamāvibhau ।
tatraiva mūḍhamanaso vijānanti ca dehinaḥ ।।

śatruṇā saha rakṣanti jñāne pariharanti ca ।
pramādaviṣavṛkṣasya śākhāstistraḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ ।।

jarā vyādhiśca mṛtyuñca nityaṃ tasyoparisthitāḥ ।
jarādayo na bādhyante puruṣaṃ satkriyānvitam ।।

apramādī sadā bhayanirmuktaḥ san sukhītiṣṭhati

saṃsāre tiṣṭhate dhīmānapramādarataḥ sadā ।
nikṛntanti sadā doṣā na pramādaṃ pariṣvajet ।।

sadā bhayavinirmuktaḥ sukhaṃ prāpnotyanuttamam ।
pramādācca yat saukhyaṃ śāśvataṃ sa bhayaṃ hi tat ।।

yattu tasmād vinirmuktaṃ tat saukhyaṃ dhruvamacyutam ।
śataśo manujā pramādena vimohitāḥ ।।

tathāpi nāma vaśagāste pramāde pratiṣṭhitāḥ ।
catvāro hi viparyāsāḥ pramādasyoparisthitāḥ ।।

pramādavirahāttepi naśyanti lokaśatravaḥ ।
yadanekavikalpo ayamanekabhayasaṅkaṭaḥ ।।

pramādarahitāḥ devāḥ santo acyutaṃ sukhamaśnute
saṃsāro bhramate duḥkhe tat pramādasya ceṣṭitam ।
ekaḥ pramādavirahāt prāpyate sukhamacyutam ।।

pramādena vinaśyanti sarvadharmā hatāstravāḥ ।
devānāṃ ca pramādo ayamuparyupari vartate ।।

kathaṃ pramādasammūḍhāḥ devā yāsyanti nirvṛtim ।
tade t saumyamanasā cintayitvā vikalpayet ।।

tathā me hita māstheyaṃ yathā yat syāt ।
ye devā yacca tatsaukhyaṃ paśyan yadapikiñcana ।।

saṃskṛtasyaiva dhruvapadaprāptirbhavati

tat sarva dhruvaṃ gatvā saṃskṛtasyaiṣa sambhavaḥ ।
avaśyaṃ te vinaśyanti ye bhāvāḥ saṃskṛtāścalāḥ ।।

pramādavaśād devā api duḥkhabhāginaḥ bhavanti

pramādaniratā nityaṃ duḥkhasya bhāginaḥ ।
pramādāpahatajano yasteṣāṃ kurute matiḥ ।।

saṃviyoge samutpanne duḥkhena paritapyate ।
viṣayeṣu sakāmeṣu tṛṣṇāvanagateṣu ca ।।

tena te vañcitā devāḥ pramādavaśavartinaḥ ।
mūlametadanarthānāṃ yatpramādānusevanam ।।

pramādavarjanaṃ kṣemakaram

tasyaitad varjanaṃ dhanyaṃ sarvakṣemakaraṃ mahat ।
satvā naivāpannasukhā duḥkhaiścāpi samanvitāḥ ।।

tathā buddhiranuṣṭheyā yathā matsyā jalānugāḥ ।
svarge pramādavaśagā strīvidheyāśca te surāḥ ।।

pramādino duḥkhabhāgino bhavanti

te strīvahnivinirdagdhā nityaṃ duḥkhasya bhāginaḥ ।
tasmāt prayatnaśo devairaṅganā parivarjanam ।।

karttavyaṃ kāmalolasya manasā dhṛtivardhanam ।
kāryākāryevimūḍhasya dharmādharme tathaiva ca ।।

puruṣasyātmabhaṅgasya nirvāṇaṃ dūrameva tat ।
gurutābhāvatattvajño nipuṇo dharmagocaraḥ ।।

dharmiṇa eva sukhamāpnuvanti

dharmākāṃkṣī phalākāṃkṣī tādṛśaṃ labhate sukham ।
nidhautamaghakalmāṣāḥ nityaṃ dharmānuvartinaḥ ।।

pramādavimohitā eva duḥkhamāpnuvanti

sukhinaste sadā dṛṣṭā na pramādavihāriṇaḥ ।
pramādāpahataḥ pūrva pramādena vimohitaḥ ।।

madyena devo api pramādameti

devo vā puruṣaścāpi na sukhasyāntike hi saḥ ।
mṛtaḥ sa puruṣo nityaṃ yo madyena pramādyati ।।

madyadoṣādhṛtāḥ sarve bhavanti narake narāḥ ।
asaṃsargacaro doṣo madyamityabhidhīyate ।।

madyena mohitā nityaṃ devāḥ narakagāminaḥ ।
asambhūteṣu rakṣante na sambhūte kathañcanaḥ ।।

madātsvākāramalinā devāḥ kāmairvimohitāḥ ।
kāmena mohitā devā madyenāpi tathaiva ca ।।

pramādī tattvaṃ na paśyati

na tattvamatra paśyanti jātyandhā iva satpatham ।
pramādākulitaṃ cittaṃ na tattvamanupaśyati ।।

pramādaścāgnivattasmāt parivarjyaḥ samantataḥ ।
pramādena vinaśyanti kuśalā dharmayonayaḥ ।।

pramādaviṣasevanaṃ nāśāyaiva jāyate

mārga ca viṣasaṃspṛṣṭaṃ sarvathā naiva paśyati ।
daśadharmā vinaśyanti pramādaviṣasevinām ।।

dhyānāni caiva catvāri praṇaśyanti pramādinaḥ ।
apramādaṃ praśaṃsanti buddhāḥ kāmavivarjitāḥ ।।

apramattā jarāmuktā bhavanti

pramādañca jugupsanti jarāmaraṇapañjaram ।
apramattā jarāmuktā pramattā duḥkhabhoginaḥ ।।

pramāda eva bandhanam ।

pramādo bandhanaṃ hayetad duḥkhitaṃ mandabuddhinām ।
apramādena kuśalā devānāṃ samitiṅgatāḥ ।।

tasmāt te patitā bhūyo ye pramādānusevinaḥ ।
pramattapuruṣaḥ sarva saṃsārānnaiva mucyate ।।

pramādapāśapāśena yena baddhā hi dehinaḥ ।
akārya kāryasadṛśaṃ kārya kurvanti sarvadā ।।

apramādinaḥ kalyāṇaparamparāmāpnuvanti

apramādānnaraḥ sarva viparītaṃ paśyati ।
na laukikeṣu kāryeṣu kuto na śraiyaseṣu ca ।।

pramādaṃ na praśaṃsanti paṇḍitā buddhipāragāḥ ।
yathā śubhaṃ parikṣīṇaṃ bhaviṣyati divaukasām ।।

pramādaphalaṃ hānikaram

tadā pramādasya phalaṃ jñāsyanti kaṭukaṃ hi tat ।
kāmasaṃsaktamanasāṃ tasyānte sukhasevinām ।।

bhaviṣyati sukhaṃ tasmād vinipātodayo mahān ।
viṣayābhimukhepsūnāṃ nityamāśāgatātmanām ।।

strīdarśanasumattānāṃ vinipāto bhaviṣyati ।
niṣevante pramādarāgasevinaḥ ।।

tāḥ sarvā mṛtyusamaye parityakṣyanti yoṣitaḥ ।
cyavamānaṃ suraṃ sarve na kaścidanugacchati ।।

mokṣābhilāṣiṇaḥ duṣkṛtaṃ tyajanti

karmaṇā pṛṣṭhataḥ sarva gacchantamanuyāti ca ।
yuktaṃ ca sadā sevyaṃ varjanīyaṃ ca duṣkṛtam ।।

pramādaṃ ca madaṃ jahayāt pramāda rato bhavet ।
pramādo bhavamūlo ayaṃ pramādastu na śāntaye ।।

pramādāpramādau vicintya dhīraḥ sukhamedhate

apramādapramādābhyāmidamuktaṃ svalakṣaṇam ।
tad vicintya sadā dhīraḥ sukhaṃ sucaritaṃ caret ।।

dharmacārī kadāpi duḥkhaṃ nāpnoti

na dharmacārī puruṣaḥ kadācid duḥkhamṛcchaiti ।
saṃsarantyatha saṃsāre prāṇinaḥ svena karmaṇā ।।

pramādo vinipātāya

kimarthamihaloko ayaṃ pramādena vihanyate ।
pramādaḥ śreyasāṃ nāśaḥ pramādo bandhanaṃ param ।।

pramādo vinipātāya pramādo narakāya ca ।
duḥkhasya heturevaikaḥ pramādaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।।

apramādarato nirvāṇamadhigacchati

tasmāt sukhārthī puruṣaḥ pramādaṃ parivarjayet ।
yaiḥ pramādaḥ parityaktaḥ prāptaṃ taiḥ padamacyutam ।।

apramādarato yo hi nirvāṇasyaiva so antike ।
apramādapadaṃ hayetannirvāṇasyāgrataḥ padam ।।

pramattaḥ sadaiva duḥkhito bhavati

pramādo vinipātāya hetureṣaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।
pramattaḥ puruṣaḥ sarvaḥ sonmāda iva lakṣyate ।।

laghutvaṃ yāti loke asmin pratyavāyeṣu pacyate ।
pramattaḥ puruṣaḥ śakto viparīteṣu vartate ।।

hetau karmavipāke ca mṛtyūtpattau tathaiva ca ।
pramādāgniśca yaṃ tīkṣṇo narakānupakarṣati ।
tasmānnarakamokṣārtha pramādaṃ vinivarjayet ।।

ye pramādaṃ vinirjitya nityaṃ jñānaratā narāḥ ।
te kleśabandhanaṃ chitvā padaṃ yātāḥ sukhodayam ।।

karmasūtrairnibaddhāśca cittadolāṃ samāśritāḥ ।
bhramanti vibhave sattvā mā pramādeṣu rakṣathaḥ ।।

sukhī bhavati duḥkhī vai duḥkhitaścāpi sukhitaḥ ।
bhartāpi tṛpto bhavati mā pramādeṣu rakṣathaḥ ।।

mātā pitā vā bhavati bhāryā mātṛtvameva ca ।
parivarto mahāneṣu mā pramādeṣu rakṣathaḥ ।।

pramādājjāyate rāgo rāgād dveṣaḥ prapadyate ।
sa doṣapathamāpanno narakānupadhāvati ।।

prajñāruḍhaḥ pramādaśūnyaḥ san śivaṃ panthānamāpnoti

prajñāprāsādamāroha yogakṣemamanuttamam ।
eṣa panthāḥ śivaḥ śreṣṭho yaḥ pramādavivarjitaḥ ।
tena mārgeṇa satataṃ nirvāṇaṃ yānti paṇḍitāḥ ।।

virodho mārgasampattau cittasantānadūṣakaḥ ।
āchettā dharmasetūnāṃ pramādaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।।

pramādopahatāḥ nāśaṃ yānti

smṛti sandūṣakaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ mokṣāya vṛttināśakaḥ ।
durgatīnāṃ paraṃ netā pramādaḥ sampravartate ।।

aneka puruṣaḥ kṣipto nātmano vindate hitam ।
nāvācyaṃ na ca kāryāṇāṃ vindate amṛtakopamaḥ ।।

ta ete paśubhistulyā devavigrahadhāriṇaḥ ।
pramādopahatā mūḍhā nṛtyanti ca hasanti ca ।।

utpannāvicyutāḥ mārgāt kṣāntiṃ ye nāśayanti ca ।
nṛbhavārṇavabhūtā ye te pramādānudhāvinaḥ ।।

janakaḥ sarvadoṣāṇāṃ bandhanaṃ pāpakarmaṇām ।
pramoṣaḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ pramādāriḥ pravartate ।।

sarveṣāṃ śubhakarmāṇāṃ pramādaḥ śatrureva

nādhyātmikāni karmāṇi na bāhayāni kathañcana ।
pramādopahato janturjānīte naṣṭamāsanaḥ ।।

krīḍāyāṃ vyagramanaso nṛtyagāndharvalālasāḥ ।
atṛṣṇārviṣayairdivyairnakṣyanti vibudhālayāḥ ।।

bhayasthāne hasantyete pramādena vimohitāḥ ।
mārgāmārga na vindanti jātyandhena surāḥ samāḥ ।।

kāmadhātāveva pramattāḥ bhramanti

kāmadhātau bhramanyete cakravadgati pañcake ।
dhyānebhyo yaddhi patanaṃ tat pramādasya ceṣṭitam ।।

pramādaceṣṭitaṃ karmapatanāya jāyate

ārūpyebhyaśca yatsthānaṃ caturthaṃ prāpyalaukikāt ।
bhramanti bhramadolāyāṃ tat pramādasya ceṣṭitam ।।

pramādabandhanairbaddhaṃ tṛṣṇāpāśaiśca yantritam ।
traidhātukamidaṃ kṛtsnaṃ na ca buddhayantya cetasaḥ ।।

yat prayānti dharmasthānaṃ tṛṣṇābhayadarśitāḥ ।
na bhūyaḥ khedamāyāti tat pramādasya ceṣṭitam ।।

pramādavaśāt duḥkhamevāpnoti janaḥ

priyaviśleṣajaṃ nṛṇāṃ yadduḥkhaṃ hṛdi jāyate ।
sevanād yat pramādasya kathayanti tathāgatā ।।

anarthā hi trayo loke yairidaṃ naśyate jagat ।
vyādhirjarā ca mṛtyuśca pramādālasya sambhavāḥ ।।

prarohanti yathā bhūmau savauṣadhitṛṇādayaḥ ।
tathā pramādināṃ kleṣāḥ pravartante pṛthagvidhāḥ ।।

pramādasya viṣāṅkuraḥ

strīśleṣo madyapānaṃ ca krīḍā ca viṣayaiḥ saha ।
cāpalyamayakausīdyaṃ pramādasya viṣāṅkuraḥ ।।

pramādāpramādayorlakṣaṇam

pramādaḥ paramaṃ duḥkhapramādaḥ paraṃ sukham ।
samāsāllakṣaṇaṃ proktamapramādapramādayoḥ ।।

ataḥ pramādo na sevyaḥ

tasmāt pramādo na nareṇa sevyaḥ, sa durgatīnāṃ prathamāgrameva ।
vihāya taṃ duḥkhasahastrayoniṃ, prayānti buddhā bhavapāragrayam ।।

।। iti apramādavargaḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ ।।

kāmajugupsāvargaḥ

kāmasya narakahetutvam

na kāmeṣu ratiṃ kuryāt kāmāḥ paramavañcakāḥ ।
saṃsārabandhanā ghorāḥ sarve narakahetavaḥ ।।

yaḥ saṃrakṣati kāmeṣu tasya duḥkhamanantakam ।
na kāmoragadaṣṭasya sukhamasti kathañcana ।।

rāgādivaśagānāṃ ceṣṭitam

varaṃ niśitadhāreṇa kṣureṇa svayamātmanaḥ ।
saṃkṣoditā bhavejjihvā na coktaṃ kāmagaṃva ।।

rāgeṇa vañcitāḥ sattvā dveṣeṇa paripīḍitāḥ ।
mohasya vaśamāpannā bhāṣante amadhuraṃ vacaḥ ।।

rāgavaśagaḥ sadā duḥkhatamamanubhavati

alparāgānniruddho yaḥ kurute duṣkṛtaṃ bahu ।
sa rāgavaśago mūḍho duḥkhād duḥkhamavāpnuyāt ।।

kāmapariṇatimāha

atṛptirasmāt kāmāste na sukhā nāpi śāśvatāḥ ।
pariṇāme mahātīvrāstasmāt tān parivarjayet ।।

rāgābhibhūtāḥ puruṣā narakālayavartinaḥ ।
na rāgavaśagā ye tu na teṣāṃ narakād bhayam ।।

kāmaviṣaṃ parityājyam

caṇḍācaṇḍisamutthāśca caṇḍāśca pariṇāmataḥ ।
kāmā viṣāgnipratimāḥ parivarjyāḥ prayatnataḥ ।।
parivarjitakāmasya nityaṃ mokṣaratasya ca ।
naśyantyakuśalā dharmāstamaḥ sūryodaye tathā ।।

kāmānalaḥ narake pātayati

indriyāṇīndriyārthajño mohayitvā pṛthagvidhāḥ ।
narake pātayantyete kāmāḥ bālamanoharāḥ ।।

rāgāgneḥ mahimā

pañcendriyaprasaktasya viṣayaiḥ pañcabhistathā ।
muhūrtamapi rāgāgnirviṣayairnaiva tṛpyati ।।

saṃśleṣājjāyate vahnirviśleṣānnaiva jāyate ।
saṃśleṣādapi viśleṣo gnirjīryate nṛṇām ।।

dūrānna dāhako vahnirviṣayastasya nāsti saḥ ।
dūrāntikasamo ghoro rāgāgniratidāhakaḥ ।।

saṅkalpakāṣṭhaprabhavaḥ spṛhākuṭilavegavān ।
tṛṣṇā ghṛtaprasakto ayaṃ rāgāgnirapi dāhakaḥ ।।

dagdhvā śarīrametaddhi jvalanaḥ sampraśāmyate ।
nāmarūpavinirmukto rāgāgnirnaiva śāmyate ।।

udvejayati bhūtāni vahniḥ paramadāhakaḥ ।
rāgāgniratitīkṣṇo api nodvegaṃ kurute nṛṇām ।।

pañcendriyasamuttho ayaṃ viṣayaiḥ pañcabhirvṛtaḥ ।
tṛṣṇāsamīraṇabalād rāgāgni prajāḥ ।।

vitarkāraṇisambhūto viṣayaiḥ parivardhitaḥ ।
kāṣṭhavad dahyate tena na ca dṛśyo janasya saḥ ।।

yathā yathā hi prabalo rāgāgnistapyate mahān ।
tathā tathā rāgāndhaiḥ svasukhaṃ parisevyate ।।

agniḥ prakāśako bhavati rāgāgnistamasāvṛtaḥ ।
tasmācchiśiravad dhīmān rāgāgniṃ parivarjayet ।।

viṣayapariṇāmamāha

viṣayābhirato janturna sukhī syāt kathañcana ।
viṣayāḥ viṣayairdaṣṭāḥ pariṇāme ca dāruṇāḥ ।।

nādye nānte na madhye ca nāsmiṃlloke na cāpare ।
sukhadā viṣayā kāmaṃ bhavantīha kathañcana ।।

bāliśasya hi sarvasya tṛṣṇākrīḍanasaṃbhavaiḥ ।
na tṛpto viṣayairagnirjvalanasya yathendhanaiḥ ।।

atṛptoḥ viṣayaiḥ sarvo jano ayaṃ parivañcitaḥ ।
mṛtyunābhyāsanirata etairdoṣairvidahyate ।।

kāmamohāndhānāṃ sthitimāha

sukhānāṃ kāmacārāṇāṃ mohasya khalu ceṣṭitam ।
tadeva yadi devānāṃ khagaiḥ syuste samāḥ surāḥ ।।

kalpānteṣvabhisantaptaḥ śasyate saritāṃ patiḥ ।
na dṛṣṭistṛpyate rūpaiḥ kalpakoṭiśatairapi ।।

syāt samudrasya caryāptiḥ salilairvaśagādibhiḥ ।
na tu dṛṣṭiḥ samudrasya rūpārthaistṛptirasti hi ।।

avitṛptasya kāmebhyaḥ kiṃ sukhaṃ parikalpyate ।
tṛptiryāsti vitṛṣṇasya gataśokasya dehinaḥ ।।

mādyante bahumohāndhā na ca buddhayanti bāliśāḥ ।
mandena kṣaṇikā yadvat malayendhanapādapāḥ ।।

kāmā asārāḥ vañcakāśca bhavanti

svapnapramoṣadharmāṇo gandharvanagaropamāḥ ।
riktāstucchā asārāśca kāmāḥ paramavañcakāḥ ।।

mā mohena samāḥ kiṃ pākasadṛśopamāḥ ।
kāmā lokahitakarā vahnivat parikīrtitāḥ ।।

kāmasyādīnavaṃ jñātvā yena tatphalamohitāḥ ।
tena taddarśakāḥ prītā gatakāṃkṣasya ।।

nyathā cintyamānānāṃ yathā prāptā punastathā ।
sarvataḥ pāpakartāraḥ kāmā loke viṣopamāḥ ।।

kāmairatṛptamanasaste te devāścyutāḥ punaḥ ।
patanti narake mūḍhāḥ kāmena parivañcitāḥ ।।

nārīṃ nindayati

nadītaraṅgacapalā vidyullekhasamāśca te ।
mīnāvartabalā nāryaḥ kāmalokaviṣāspadāḥ ।।

vicintitā vivardhante varddhitā vahnisannibhāḥ ।
ādau cānte tathā kāmāstasmāt kāmān vivarjayet ।।

kāmasevanaphalam

yathā yathā hi sevyante vivardhante tathā tathā ।
vahnijvālāsamāsṛṣṭāḥ kāmāḥ kaṭuvipākinaḥ ।।

kāmavarjanaphalam āha

evaṃ doṣaṃ sadā jñātvā dhīraḥ kāmān vivarjayet ।
parivartitakāmasya sukhaṃ bhavati naiṣṭhikam ।।

kāmāgniḥ devānnapi pātayati

asaṅkhyāni sahasrāṇi devānāṃ niyutāni ca ।
patanti kāmadahanaṃ narakaṃ vahnibhairavam ।।

yathāgniviṣaśastrāṇi varjayanti sukhārthinaḥ ।
tathā kāmāḥ sadā varjyā hetavo narakasya te ।।

na dṛṣṭo na śrutaḥ kaścid yaḥ kāmavaśagaḥ pumān ।
na kāmairvipralabdhaḥ syānna ca duḥkhena pīḍitaḥ ।।

tasmādalamalaṃ kāmairmā caiteṣu manaḥ kṛthāḥ ।
sarve sarvāsvavasthāsu kāmā vahniviṣopamāḥ ।।

anādirmati saṃsāre śatravaścittasambhavāḥ ।
ahantvāttu bhavet prītirna sā kāmaiḥ kathañcana ।।

sakalmaṣā kaṭuphalā duḥkhāt kāmodbhavā ratiḥ ।
yā tu kāmavinirmuktā sā ratiḥ pari ।।

yoginaḥ paramā gatiḥ

tāṃ samāśritya gacchanti yoginaḥ paramāṃ gatim ।
na tu kāmakṛtā prītirnayate padamacyutam ।।

kāmajaratiṃ nindati

āpātamadhurā ramyā vipāke jvalanopamā ।
ratirbhavati kāmāgnijanyā narakagāminī ।।

āpātaramyā madhurā madhye ramyā ca sarvadā ।
śāntamante ca vimalaṃ nayate padamacyutam ।।

ādyantamadhyakalyāṇī nityaṃ māteva śobhanā ।
tāṃ vyudasya kathaṃ bālā rakṣante ।।

kāmakṛtā ratiḥ nirataṃ tapati

madhyādinidhane duḥkhā nityaṃ doṣādibhirvṛtā ।
kathaṃ sā sevyate bālairyā na dṛṣṭā sukhāvahā ।।

viṣamañjarivad ramyā sparśe jvalanasambhavā ।
tathā kāmakṛtā prītiḥ pariṇāme viṣopamā ।।

hūyamāno yathā vahnirjvalanena praśāmyati ।
dāhena ca prarohaḥ syāt tadvat kāmakṛtā ratiḥ ।।

pataṅgaḥ paśyati hyagni dāhadoṣaṃ na paśyati ।
tathā kāmakṛtāṃ prītiṃ paśyantyakṛtabuddhayaḥ ।।

yastu rāgakṛto dāhaḥ pacyate kāmināṃ sadā ।
pataṅgasadṛśaṃ dāhaṃ sarvathā nai paśyati ।।

kāmapramādāt patanaṃ dhruvameva

tasmāt kāma tyaktvā nityaṃ jīvatha he surāḥ ।
bhavantu mā vṛthā janmapramādena prapātanam ।।

saṃkṣīṇaśubhakarmāṇo nityaṃ kāmairvimohitāḥ ।
taṃ hitvā narakaṃ yānti kāmamohena vañcitāḥ ।।

kāmamohitaḥ viṣavṛkṣamayaṃ puṣpaṃ pibati

viṣavṛkṣamayaṃ puṣpaṃ pīyate bhramarairyathā ।
tathā viṣātmakamidaṃ sukhaṃ bhuṅkte hi mohitaḥ ।।

jīveyuḥ pāmarāḥ kecit viṣaṃ pītvāpi durbhagāḥ ।
na kāmaviṣapītasya jīvitaṃ durlabhaṃ bhavet ।।

yathā hi narake vahnirjvalayatya vicāriṇam ।
tathā kāmamayo vahnirdahatīha divaukasaḥ ।।

kāmāgniḥ hiṃsaka eva

śrutipāśamayo vahniḥ pretāneṣa dahatyati ।
dahane hiṃsako vahnirnṛṇāṃ paryeṣaṇātmakaḥ ।।

evamagnisamaṃ tāvat parihārya samantataḥ ।
sarvalokamaśeṣeṇa dahyate kāmamohitaḥ ।।

viṣayāsaktaṃ manaḥ vyasane pātayati

viṣayeṣu sadācittaṃ dhāvantaṃ cañcalaṃ mahat ।
na tyājyaṃ vyasane mūḍha yad paśyasi bhaviṣyati ।।

kāmeṣu rakṣa te cittaṃ vyasanenāvabudhyate ।
vyasanaughe samutpanne tat paścāt paritapyate ।।

kāmamohitāḥ mahadbhayamapi na paśyanti

vṛthā kāmamadairmattā devāḥ prakṛtidurbalāḥ ।
bhramanti bhramitāḥ kāmairna paśyanti mahad bhayam ।।

viśvasanti hi ye devāḥ kāmeṣvahitakāriṣu ।
vyatirekeṣu te paścāt pratibudhyantyamedhasaḥ ।।

kāmāḥ paramavañcakā bhavanti

na ca paśyanti budhāścittena parivañcitāḥ ।
kṣaṇikā madhurā jātāḥ kāmāḥ paramavañcakāḥ ।।

kāma prati na viśvaset

śataśaśca sahastraiśca koṭiśaḥ padmaśastathā ।
labdhā naṣṭā punaḥ kāmā na teṣāṃ viścaset pumān ।।

kāmairmohitaḥ pataṅgasamo narakāgninā dahyate

viṣayād bandhanaṃ tīvraṃ sarve narakahetavaḥ ।
tasmādatyantatastyaktvā śreyase kriyatāṃ manaḥ ।।

rāgeṇa rañjitāḥ pūrvaṃ dveṣeṇa ca tiraskṛtāḥ ।
mohena mohitāścaiva te aśrutākṛtakāriṇaḥ ।।

kāmārthaireṣyate bālaḥ punaḥ kāmairvimohitaḥ ।
sa pataṅgasamo mūḍhaḥ dahyate narakāgninā ।।

kāmavaśagāḥ suralokādapi patanti

avaśyambhāvi patanaṃ suralokāt samantataḥ ।
na jñātvā kāmavaśago syādiha kathañcana ।।

kāmena vañcitāḥ sattvāḥ kāmena ca vimohitāḥ ।
kāmapāśāpakṛṣṭāste patanti narake sadā ।।

kāmaṃ tyaktva svahite manaḥ karttavyam

tadetad vyasanaṃ sattvāḥ svahite kriyatāṃ manaḥ ।
manasāpi svadāntena nānutapyanti dehinaḥ ।।

manoviṣeṇa ye daṣṭāḥ kāmavegena sarvadā ।
te mūḍhā mṛtyuvaśagāḥ kāmānalahatā narāḥ ।।

na tṛptirasti kāmānāṃ tṛṣṇayā hitakāriṇām ।
tṛṣṇāpi tṛptijanikā mano naiva hi tṛpyati ।।

jñānadīpenaijendriyāṇāṃ viṣayebhyastṛptirjāyate

na jātu viṣayaistṛptirindriyāṇāṃ bhaviṣyati ।
yadi na jñānadīpena kṣapayiṣyanti ।।

nārīsevanena nāśaḥ suniścitaḥ

yoṣitaḥ sevyamānā hi vitarkaśatamālikāḥ ।
pravardhati yathā vahnirvāyunā samudīritaḥ ।।

kāmāgnidīptāḥ kadāpi śāntiṃ nāpnuvanti

taṃ matvā vegarabhasā nityaṃ kāmo agnidīpitaḥ ।
kāmān hāpayati jñānī buddhatattvavicintakaḥ ।।

ye nityaṃ bhrāntamanaso nityaṃ viṣayatatparāḥ ।
ramante vibudhāḥ sarve tat sarvaṃ mohaceṣṭitam ।।

sevyamāno hi vibudhairviṣayāgnirvivardhate ।
pāśenānena saṃyukto vahnirvāyusamīritaḥ ।।

rāgavivaśā amarā api patanti

amarāḥ rāgavivaśā nityaṃ viṣayatatparāḥ ।
devalokāt patantyete moharāgeṇa vañcitāḥ ।।

ramante viṣayairete tatra tallīnamānasāḥ ।
na ca vindanti yad duḥkhaṃ viprayogo bhaviṣyati ।।

viyogajaṃ duḥkhaṃ kaṣṭapradameva

yadetat sukhamevādau divyaṃ pañcaguṇānvitam ।
viyogajasya duḥkhasya kalāṃ nārhatiṣoḍaśīm ।।

kāmānāṃ tadvighāto hi janenaivopayujyate ।
satṛṣṇasya tathā tṛptiḥ kāmebhyo naiva jāyate ।।

kāmānusevinaḥ duḥkhaṃ kadāpi śāntiṃ nādhigacchati

anapekṣitacittasya nityaṃ kāmānusevinaḥ ।
dīrgharātrānuśayikaṃ duḥkhaṃ naiva praśāmyate ।।

tvaritaṃ rakṣyate mūḍho vyasanenaiva budhyate ।
paścāttu vyasane prāpte jānīte yasya tat phalam ।।

āsvādabhadrakā hyete kāmāḥ paramadāruṇāḥ ।
dūtakān narakasyaitān carantyahitakāriṇaḥ ।।

viṣayāgnidagdhāḥ narakaṃ yānti

yasteṣāṃ viśvaset martyo jñānacakṣurvigarhitaḥ ।
viṣayāgnirabhratulyaḥ sa yāti narakaṃ naraḥ ।।

alpāsvādālpahṛdayā nityaṃ puruṣavañcakāḥ ।
gandharvanagaraprakhyāḥ kāmā āsvādabhadrakāḥ ।।

viṣayamohitāḥ devā api durgati yānti

dīpaprabhā sañchanneva punaḥ punaḥ ।
na ca bindatyamanaso devā viṣayamohitāḥ ।।

viṣayeṇātirabhasā nityaṃ kāmavaśānugāḥ ।
na vidanti mahad duḥkhaṃ yadavaśyaṃ bhaviṣyati ।।

ramaṇīyāni kāmāni yasyaivaṃ jāyate matiḥ ।
sa paścād vyasane prāpte mūḍho asau vipralapyate ।।

na kāmena madāndhasya viṣayairmohitasya ca ।
naityikaṃ bhavati śarmma yatsukhānāmanuttamam ।।

ādhyātmikasukhāpekṣayā kāmasukhaṃ hīnatamam

yacca kāmasukhaṃ loke yacca tṛṣṇodbhavaṃ sukham ।
ekasyādhyātmikasyedaṃ kalāṃ nārhatiṣoḍaśīm ।।

kāmī kadāpi sukhaṃ nāśnute

na sukhī vartate tāvadya yasya kāmo hṛdi sthitaḥ ।
sa sarvaduḥkhabhāgārho narakānupadhāvati ।।

na tṛptirvidyate kāmairapi śataṃ nṛṇām ।
yatra saukhyaṃ na tatrāsti tṛptirviṣayasevinām ।।

sevyamānāḥ sadā kāmā vardhante ca muhurmuhuḥ ।
te vardhitā viṣasamā bhavanti vinipātinaḥ ।।

vipattikuśalā ghorā nityaṃ patanahetavaḥ ।
na ca teṣāṃ parityāgaṃ kurvanti viṣayotsavāḥ ।।

yasya dṛṣṭisamudrasya rūpaistṛptirna vidyate ।
tathā śarmamanojñaiśca rasatṛptirna vidyate ।।

gandhairapi sadā ghrāṇaṃ na tṛptimadhigacchati ।
sparśāḥ sammukhasaṃsparśāḥ sevyante naiva tṛpyate ।।

śabdaiḥ kāntaiḥ sumadhuraiḥ śrotrameti na tarpaṇam ।
mano api tṛptiviśvastaṃ vardhamānaṃ na tṛpyati ।।

indriyāṇi kāmabhūmiṣu pātayanti

ṣaḍendriyāṇi capalānyādhṛtāni ratau punaḥ ।
bhramanti muṣitā nityaṃ kāmabhūmiṣvanekaśaḥ ।।

na tṛptirasti devānāṃ gajānāṃ vai tṛṇairyathā ।
analasya svabhāvo ayaṃ tasya tṛptirna vidyate ।।

ṣaḍete vahnayastīvrā vitarkānilamūrchitāḥ ।
bhramanti muṣitā nityaṃ kāmabhūmiṣvanekaśaḥ ।।

indriyadagdhā narakaṃ yānti

tairayaṃ dahyate loko na ca vindatyabuddhimān ।
āsvādabhadrakā hayete narakasya ca hetavaḥ ।।

kāmamohitaḥ sukhavañcito bhavati

kāmā viṣayalobhāste lelihānā yathoragāḥ ।
vilocanavaro hayeṣa na ca kāmairvimohitaḥ ।।

kāmavaśīnaraḥ netrahīnā mūḍhataraḥ

sukhānusāriṇaḥ kāmo narakānupadhāvati ।
na netrahīno narake pātyate satkriyānvitaḥ ।।

tasmād varaṃ vicakṣuḥ syānna tu kāmavaśo naraḥ ।
aśakyavañcitā mūḍhāḥ kāmairahitakāribhiḥ ।।

kāmacāriṇāṃ jñānādikaṃ durlabham

anirvidyanti kāmebhyo mohitāḥ svena cetasā ।
na jñānaṃ nāpi vijñānaṃ vidyate kāmacāriṇām ।।

kāmaḥ mṛtyubhavanaṃ nayati

yad duḥkhakāmajaṃ hatvā punaḥ kāmavaśānugāḥ ।
mitrarūpā ca ye kāmāḥ kimpākaphalasannibhāḥ ।
nayanti mṛtyubhavanaṃ durgatīśca punaḥ punaḥ ।।

anivarttya yathā toyamāpagānāmanekaśaḥ ।
tathā saukhyagataṃ nṛṇāṃ sarvathā na vivartate ।।

vanopavanabhogeṣu sukhaprāpteṣvanekaśaḥ ।
yo na tṛpyati kāmeṣu sa naro adhamagāmikaḥ ।।

pramādo pahato jantuḥ kāmāsvādeṣu tatparaḥ ।
rūpeṣu rakṣyate nityaṃ pariṇāme ca vidyate ।।

ghanacchāyāsvarūpāṇi karmamiśrāṇi yāni vai ।
tāni caiva kathaṃ devāḥ śakṣyante kāmagocare ।।

kāmāḥ kadāpi na sevyāḥ
yadi nityā bhaveyurna kāmāste syurviṣopamāḥ ।।
kāmatṛṣṇāduḥkhakarī

tathāpi kāmatṛṣṇā yā na sā jāti vilakṣaṇā ।
prāgeva nityaṃ duḥkhāya śūnyamātmānameva ca ।।

teṣu duḥkhavipākeṣu kathaṃ rakṣantyabuddhayaḥ ।
kāmāsvādeṣu rakṣyante bāliśāḥ mandabuddhayaḥ ।
ādīnavaṃ na buddhayante kimpākaphalasannibham ।।

rūpaśabdādibaddho ayaṃ tṛṣṇāviprakṛto janaḥ ।
dīpyate vivaśo nityaṃ, kukarmaphalamohitam ।।

āsvādayitvā puruṣāḥ kāmān viṣaphalopamān ।
tṛṣṇayā tṛptamanasaḥ patanti narake punaḥ ।।

yathābhivarṣate toyaṃ vardhante sarito yathā ।
tathā kāmābhivarṣeṇa devānāṃ vardhate analaḥ ।।

kāmasukhasya nānto vidyate

jalasambhavamīno api dṛśyate tṛṣṇayāturaḥ ।
evaṃ sukhābhivṛddhā ca na vitṛpyati devatā ।।

ākāśasya yathā nānto vidyate nāpi saṃśayaḥ ।
evaṃ kāmeṣu nāstyantaḥ kāmināṃ nāsti saṃkṣayaḥ ।।

salilādibhiratṛptasya sāgarasyormimālinaḥ ।
na tu kāmairatṛptasya tṛptirasti kathañcana ।।

aprāptairviṣayairdevā na vitṛpyanti bāliśāḥ ।
viṣayairnaiva tṛpyanti sukhalālasatatparāḥ ।।

kāmastāpāya, na tu śāntyai

saṃprāpte vyasane tīvre cyavamānepyanekaśaḥ ।
tapyate viṣaye tasmāt paraṃ kāmo na śakyate ।।

vilokya puruṣānete kāmaviśvāsaghātinaḥ ।
tyajanti vyasane prāptā vipadyante hi te narāḥ ।।

atṛptasya sukhaṃ nāsti viṣayaiścāpi tṛpyate ।
ye vā tṛiptikarā dṛṣṭāstān buddhvā vivarjayet ।।

viṣayānparityajya śāntiḥ sevyā

sukhamūlā sadā śāntirasukhā viṣayā matāḥ ।
tasmācchāntisukhā devā varjayitvā viṣayoragān ।।

badhabandhanarogādi viṣayebhyo mahadbhayam ।
sambhrāntiriha saṃsāre viṣayaireva jāyate ।।

saṃyogā viprayogāntāḥ śataśo atha sahastraśaḥ ।
jātau jātau sadā dṛṣṭāḥ saugataistattvadarśibhiḥ ।।

aneka sukhasaṃsāraḥ viṣayātmaka eva

anekasukhasaṃsāro viṣayeṣu hi vidyate ।
viṣayaiśca bhavet sarva jātau jātau prajāyate ।।

kaṣṭairyairanakāmairna śakyate amūḍhacetasā ।
punastāneva mohāndhāḥ sevante akṛtabuddhayaḥ ।।

viṣayaśatrusevinaḥ bāliśāḥ bhavanti

varjate hi sadā śatruvañcanāśaṅkayā naraḥ ।
viṣayāḥ śatrubhūtā hi na vaśyante kathañcana ।।

kāmabaddhāḥ sadā mohabāliśā vā bhavanti te ।
na tyajanti kathaṃ mūḍhā mohitāḥ svena karmaṇā ।।

yathā bahnibhayāt kaścid vahnimevopasevate ।
tathā viṣayasaṃmūḍho viṣayānupasevate ।।

snāyusaṅgrathitaḥ pāśo dṛṣṭiramyo yathā bhavet ।
tathā viṣayaramyo ayaṃ pāśaḥ paramadāruṇaḥ ।।

kāmasukhaṃ nāśāya bhavati

kiṃpākasya yathāsvādo madhurāgro mahodayaḥ ।
paścād bhavati nāśāya sukhaṃ tadvadidaṃ nṛṇām ।।

pradīpasya śikhāṃ yāvat pataṅgo mohamūrchitaḥ ।
patate dahyate caiva tathedaṃ sukhamiṣyate ।।

ajñātvā hi tathā bālā ramyadehasukhecchayā ।
spṛśanti jvalanaṃ tadvat sukhametad bhaviṣyati ।।

tṛṣṇāvighāta eva sukhāya jāyate

yathā ramyo vanamṛgastṛṣṇārta upadhāvati ।
na ca tṛṣṇāvighāto asya tadidaṃ sukhamiṣyate ।।

na tṛptā na ca tṛpyanti na ca tṛptirbhaviṣyati ।
viṣayaiḥ sarvadevānāṃ tasmāt kāmo na śāntaye ।।

viṣayaiḥ pramattāḥ duḥkhamanubhavanti

pratyutpannasukhāḥ kāmā nāntakalyāṇakārakāḥ ।
rañjitā viṣayairdevā vikṣiptamanasaḥ sadā ।।

nānāsaukhyapramattasya viṣayairvañcitasya ca ।
samprāpte mṛtyukāle ca na śamāyāsya vidyate ।।

anukrameṇa maraṇamabhyeti tacca vidyate ।
viṣayāpahatairdevaiḥ kāmavyāsaktabuddhibhiḥ ।।

kāmā ahitakāriṇo bhavanti

jānīyādadya me devā yad duḥkhaṃ viprayogajam ।
muhūrtamapi kāmeṣu na kuryāt tatra saṃsthitim ।।

rāgāgninā dagdho vimohito jāyate

anityātmabhayāḥ kāmā nityaṃ cāhitakāriṇaḥ ।
tathā vimohitān kālaḥ punastānanusevate ।।

rāgāgninā pradahayante nityaṃ devāḥ pramohitāḥ ।
dahyamānāḥ punastattvaṃ praśaṃsanti punaḥ punaḥ ।।

rathacakravatsadā bhrāntā viṣayavimohitāḥ bhavanti

viṣayeṣu na rakṣyante teṣāṃ duḥkhamiva sthitam ।
traidhātukamidaṃ sarva bhrāmyate rathacakravat ।।

gandharvanagarasadṛśāḥ kāmāḥ bhavanti

sattvā avidyayā mugdhā nityaṃ duḥkhasya bhoginaḥ ।
vidyudālātacakreṇa samāḥ kāmāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।
svapne gandharvanagarasadṛśā vipralambhinaḥ ।।

pañcaskandhamatirduḥkhitastiṣṭhati

anityaduḥkhaśūnyeṣu na kuryānmatimātmavān ।
pañcaskandhāsuraiḥ proktaḥ śubhai riktaḥ svabhāvataḥ ।।

anyathā viṣavad vijñaḥ kāmeṣu ca prasahyate ।
sa budhaḥ pāragaḥ śāntaḥ sattvānāmanukampakaḥ ।।

nirvāṇonmukha eva doṣācchāntimadhigacchati hitvā kleśamayaṃ pāśaṃ nirvāṇasyāntike sthitaḥ ।।

kāmavibhrāntasya śāntikathā vṛthā

prabhavenna ca doṣeṣu kāmacaryāratasya ca ।
vibhrāntamanasastasya kutaḥ śāntirbhaviṣyati? ।।

vibhrāntaṃ paśyatu mano viṣayeṣu pradhāvati ।
saddharmapathavibhrānto narakeṣūpapadyate ।।

aśaktaprāptavibhraṣṭe kiṃ kāmairvidyutopamaiḥ ।
kiṃpākaviṣaśastrāgnisannibhairduḥkhahetubhiḥ? ।।

kāmāgniḥ viṣayasevanena vardhate

yathā yathā hi sevyante vardhante te tathā tathā ।
avitṛptikarā hyete vahnidāhasya hetavaḥ ।।

kāmān varjayitvaiva sukhamaśnuvate janāḥ
dāhadoṣeṇa sambhrāntāḥ ye surāḥ sukhakāṅkṣiṇaḥ ।
varjayitvāśivān kāmāstataḥ saukhyaṃ bhaviṣyati ।।

kāmāḥ vidyud guṇopamāḥ cañcalāḥ

vañcayitvā janaṃ mūḍhaṃ śāṭī kṛtyeva bandhanam ।
pratyayo netracapalaḥ kāmā vidyud guṇopamāḥ ।।

uparyupari kāmā yaiḥ sevyante kāmatṛṣṇayā ।
te rāgavahninā dagdhā dāhād dāhamavāpnuyāt ।।

atimūḍhatamā hyete ye surāḥ kāmamohitāḥ ।
athavā ye na gacchanti yatsukhāt sukhamuttamam ।।

nirvāṇagāmino nāsti vinā muktyā kutaḥ sukham? ।
tasmāt kāmānna seveta kaṣṭaḥ kāmasamāgamaḥ ।।

indriyāṇi na tṛpyante viṣayai rāgasevinaḥ ।
atṛptau ca kutaḥ śarma sarvathā sampraveśate ।।

tasyāgramubhayād vetti saṃsārād duḥkhasāgarāt ।
kāmān tṛṣṇāviṣayagān parityajati pāpakān ।।

kāmodayavyayau samyagavadheyau

etāni girikūṭāni ramyāṇi vividhairdrumaiḥ ।
dhyāyante tāni saṃśritya kāmānāmudayavyayau ।।

śīlena śraddhayā ca iṣṭasādhanaṃ karttavyam

na kāmabandhanestṛptāḥ kāmajaṃ nidhanaṃ hi tat ।
na śīlaśraddhe yeneṣṭe labhyate aśivakāraṇam ।
kāmajaṃ nidhanaṃ hyetat saṃsārāṭavideśakam ।।

pāpāni parityajya sukhāvahaḥ śāntimārgaḥ sevanīyaḥ

yatra kāmavisaṃyuktaṃ bandhanaṃ vanamucyate ।
yatra bhāsayate pāpād yatra śāntiḥ sukhāvahā ।
tat kevalaṃ mahājñānaṃ kathyate nidhanaṃ dhanam ।।

kāmatṛṣṇābhyāṃ vimuktaḥ śivamāpnoti

ye prasaktā na kāmeṣu tṛṣṇayā na pralobhitāḥ ।
te śivaṃ sthānamāpannā na kāmāgnipraveśakāḥ ।।

avitṛptāḥ narāḥ naśyantyeva

tṛptirnāsti sadā kāmairna kāmāḥ śāntaye smṛtāḥ ।
tṛṣṇāsahāyasaṃyuktā jvalanti jvalanopamāḥ ।।

avitṛptā vinaśyanti narā devāstathoragāḥ ।
te kevalaṃ praṇaṣṭā hi narakāgni pradarśakāḥ ।।

tṛṣṇāmohitasya mṛtyuradhipatiḥ

vitarkāpahatasyāsya viṣayairvañcitasya ca ।
tṛṣṇayā mohitasyaiṣa mṛtyū rājā bhaviṣyati ।।

kāmāsaktāḥ pathyāpathyaṃ na vijānanti

saṃsaktakāmabhogeṣu pathyāpathyaṃ na vidyate ।
janā vimohitāḥ sarvaiviṣayaiḥ kāmasaṃjñakaiḥ ।।

kāmavaśānugāḥ viṣayaireva badhyante

viṣayaireva kṛṣyante ye surā mūḍhacetasaḥ ।
ye buddhaguṇairyuktā na te kāmavaśānugāḥ ।।

adhīra' paribhāṣā

pratyutpanneṣu kāmeṣu sadoṣeṣu viśeṣataḥ ।
yo na muhyati saukhyeṣu sa adhīra' iti kathyate ।।

kāmapatitānāṃ surāṇāṃ sthitimāha

svapnakāyavicitreṣu jvālāmālopameṣu ca ।
gandharvapuratulyeṣu kāmeṣu patitāḥ surāḥ ।।

tṛṣṇājanakabhūteṣu vināśāntakareṣu ca ।
kāntāreṣu viśāleṣu kāmeṣu patitāḥ surāḥ ।।

ittvareṣu trichidreṣu nadīvegopameṣu ca ।
cañcaleṣvatidurgeṣu patitāḥ surāḥ ।।

pavanoddhṛtavegormijalacandre caleṣu ca ।
atātacakralokeṣu kāmeṣu patitāḥ surāḥ ।।

samaṃ vidyullatācakramṛgatṛṣṇopameṣu ca ।
phenavaccāpyasāreṣu kāmeṣu patitāḥ surāḥ ।।

kadalīgarbhatulyeṣu gajakarṇopameṣu ca ।
nadītaraṅgavegeṣu kāmeṣu patitāḥ surāḥ ।।

kiṃpākaphalatulyeṣu vahnisannibhajātiṣu ।
māyāraśminibheṣveṣu kāmeṣu patitāḥ surāḥ ।।

jñānāṅkuśena kāmo varjanīyaḥ

jñānāṅkuśena vāryante viṣayāstattvadarśibhiḥ ।
ye amuktāścapalāstīvrāḥ sarvānarthakarā matāḥ ।।

viṣayā eva narakapātahetavaḥ

viṣayāśā ca mūḍhānāṃ saṅkalpahṛtacetasām ।
mṛtyupāśo ayamabhyeti jīvitāśā bandhakaḥ ।।

pacanti niraye kāmāḥ prāṇinaṃ laghucetasam ।
na ca vindanti mūḍhā ye mohena parivañcitāḥ ।।

viṣayāścapalāḥ sarve gandharvanagaropamāḥ ।
duḥkhasaṃvartakā hyete narakāḥ pañcahetavaḥ ।।

saṅkalpajo rāgaḥ narakaṃ pātayati
