saṅkalpājjāyate rāgaḥ rāgāt krodhaḥ pravartate ।
krodhābhibhūtaḥ puruṣo narakānupasevate ।।

kāmaparityāgapūrvakaṃ nirvāṇaprāptaye yateta

tasmāt kāmaṃ parityajya krodhaṃ nirvāsya paṇḍitaḥ ।
mohaṃ cāpi parityajya nirvāṇābhimukho bhavet ।।

nirvāṇapathikānāṃ kṛte śatruvadeva kāmaḥ parivarjanīyaḥ

śatruvad viṣayā jñeyā nirvāṇaṃ caiva mitravat ।
pumān viśrāntaviṣayo nirvāṇamadhigacchati ।।

kāmamalairalipta eva vimalaprakāśamāpnoti

alolupaḥ kāmamalairaliptaḥ prahīṇadoṣo hatavāṇatṛṣṇaḥ ।
saṃkṣīṇadoṣo vimalaprakāśaḥ prayāti śāntiṃ svaphalopabhogī ।।

sukhārthī kāmaṃ parityajyaiva śāntimadhigacchati 
yaḥ kāmapaṅkoddhṛtavānadoṣaḥ
sarveṣu sattveṣu sadā sukhārthī ।
sa nirmalo aśāntamanovimuktaḥ
prāpnoti nirvāṇasukhaṃ prasahya ।।

iti kāmajugupsāvargaḥ saptamaḥ ।

tṛṣṇāvargaḥ

tṛṣṇāgnireva narakabhūtaḥ

bhavotārāya tṛṣṇāgnirjvalanaḥ śīta ucyate ।
narake nārake yo agnistṛṣṇāgnistriṣu dhātuṣu ।।

kalpabhūto hyayaṃ vahniḥ yo ayaṃ narakasambhavaḥ ।
bahujvālākulo vahniḥ tṛṣṇāhetusamudbhavaḥ ।।

karmakṣayād vimucyante narakāt pāpakāriṇaḥ ।
triṣu dhātuṣu dahyante narāstṛṣṇāvaśānugāḥ ।।

anādimati saṃsāre tṛṣṇāgniratibandhakaḥ ।
tṛṣṇāgnirnarakaṃ tasmānnāgnirnarakasambhavaḥ ।।

tṛṣṇāgniḥ śarīraṃ manaśca dahati

gātradāhaṃ paraṃ kuryānnārakeyo hutāśanaḥ ।
śārīraṃ mānasaṃ dāhaṃ tṛṣṇāgniḥ kurute nṛṇām ।।

tṛṣṇāgniḥ sāmānyāgninā viśiṣyate

tasmād viśiṣyate vahniḥ tṛṣṇāhetusamudbhavaḥ ।
nārakeyo asamaścaiva tṛṣṇāgnirnitarāṃ smṛtaḥ ।।

ayamagniḥ trikālasambhavaḥ

tristhānagaḥ trihetuśca trikarmaparidīpakaḥ ।
trikālasambhavo jñeyastṛṣṇāgniparakastathā ।।

tṛṣṇāgniḥ sadaiva sarvatra dāhakaḥ

rāgāgnirdahyate svarge dveṣāgnistiryage tathā ।
mohāgnirdahyate pāpe tṛṣṇāgniḥ sarvadā sthitaḥ ।।

tṛṣṇāgneḥ svarūpanirūpaṇam

mānerṣyādhūmaviśikhaḥ saṅkalpe dhanasambhavaḥ ।
lobhāgnirdahate lokaṃ nāgniḥ kāmasamudbhavaḥ ।।

tṛṣṇāgnirviṣayasevanenaiva vardhate
lobhāśīviṣadaṣṭā ye teṣāṃ śarma na vidyate ।
sevito bhāvito lobho bhūya evābhivardhate ।।

lobhasamo ripurbhuvi nāsti

yathā yathendhanaṃ prāpyānalo vardhatyanekaśaḥ ।
śakyaḥ pālayituṃ rlobhavahnirna ।।

cakravad bhramate loko lobhena parivañcitaḥ ।
anādinidhane loke nāsti lobhasamo ripuḥ ।।

viśanti sāgarajale lobhena parivañcitāḥ ।
śastrasaṅghātagahanaṃ yuddhaṃ saṃpraviśanti ca ।।

lobhahetorhi bhūpālā nāśayanti parasparam ।
śastrāsibhairavaprotā yuddhayante dhanatṛṣṇayā ।।

tṛṣṇāviṣavinirmuktā lobhāṅgāravivarjitā ।
samaloṣṭakāñcanā ye nirvāṇasyāntike hi te ।।

lobhāgniḥ sarvāpekṣayā viṣamaḥ

atīvānupapannasya dhanalobhena dahyate ।
na vahnirviṣamastatra lobhāgniryatra vartate ।।

lobhaśāntiṃ vinā nirvāṇakathā vṛthā

lobhādhāraprayatnena hanyāt tān rabhasā budhaḥ ।
anirvāpitalobhasya nirvāṇaṃ dūrataḥ sthitam ।।

bhavasukhaparityāgī bhavajaṃ duḥkhaṃ nāpnoti

bhavābhilāṣiṇīṃ nāndīṃ nābhinandanti ye narāḥ ।
na teṣāṃ bhavajaṃ duḥkhaṃ svapne samupavidyate ।।

tṛṣṇābaddhān janān mṛtyuḥ śambūka iva karṣati
matsyān yathā jālabaddhān śambūkaḥ parikarṣati ।
tṛṣṇābaddhāṃstathā sattvānmṛtyuḥ samupakarṣati ।।

tṛṣṇāviṣaṃ kutrāpi na muñcati

saviṣaiḥ sāyakairviddho mṛgo yatra dhāvati ।
tatra tatra viṣaṃ yāti tathā tṛṣṇāviṣaṃ nṛṇām ।।

pravāhapravahannadyā gatirgatya'nudhāvinī ।
yathā nirdahate bālān śuṣkendhanamivānalaḥ ।।

āpātaramyā vipākajvalanopamāḥ ।
tasmāt tṛṣṇā vimoktavyā yadi saukhyaṃ hi rocate ।।

yathā hi vaḍiśagrastā mīnā mṛtyuvaśānugāḥ ।
tathā prataptā viṣayān paridhāvanti duḥkhitāḥ ।।

tṛṣṇāgniḥ narakādapi mahān

narakaṃ nārakeyaṃ ca tṛṣṇānihitaṃ mahat ।
patanti nidhanā martyāḥ paradāropajīvinaḥ ।।

tṛṣṇāprerito munirapi duḥkhamanubhavati

na ceṣṭitamanopāpatṛṣṇayā prerito muniḥ ।
ṣaḍindriyasamudbhūto viṣayendhanadāhakaḥ ।।

devānapi tṛṣṇāgnirdahatyeva

tṛṣṇāgnirdahate devaṃ kāyāgnirna kathañcana ।
sukhāvṛtāḥ sukharatāḥ sukhe parivañcitāḥ ।।

tṛṣṇāparivañcitaḥ patanamapi nāvagacchati
patanaṃ nāvagacchanti tṛṣṇayā parivañcitāḥ ।
jvālāmālākulaḥ sarvaḥ saṃsārastṛṣṇayāvṛtaḥ ।।

tṛṣṇāgninā vaśībhūtā janā gacchanti durgatim ।
tṛṣṇāgnibhiḥ parivṛtaḥ suralokaḥ samantataḥ ।।

tṛṣṇāgniḥ sadaiva vardhate

dahyate vivaśo raktaḥ kāmabhogavaśīkṛtaḥ ।
yathā yathendhanaṃ prāpya jvalanaṃ saṃpravardhate ।।

tathā tathā sukhaṃ prāpya tṛṣṇāgnirvardhate nṛṇām ।
parivartayate puṃsaḥ kāṣṭhāgnirdāhadīpakaḥ ।।

tṛṣṇāgnirdahate lokaṃ parihātuṃ na śakyate ।
ye viśālāṃ nadīṃ tīrṇā saṅkalpakṛtabhairavīm ।।

tṛṣṇāpāśaśūnyaḥ paramāṃ śāntimāpnoti

te gatāḥ paramāṃ śāntiṃ yān hi tṛṣṇā na bādhate ।
tṛṣṇāpāśavimuktā ye saṅgadoṣavivarjitāḥ ।।

nirmuktapāpakalmāṣā vītaśokā hi te budhāḥ ।
kalpakoṭisahasrāṇi tṛṣṇayā vañcitā narāḥ ।।

tṛṣṇayā vañcito lokastṛṣṇāmevopāste

te tyajanti māyāmohavaśaṃgatāḥ ।
tṛṣṇayā vañcito lokastṛṣṇāmevopasevate ।।

lavaṇodaṃ tṛṣātoyaṃ yathā pibati nārikaḥ ।
na tena janturmuhuśca pariśuṣyati ।।

duḥkhakarīṃ tṛṣṇāṃ na seveta

viṣayeṣveva tṛṣṇārtaśceṣṭate puruṣo adhamaḥ ।
tasmāt tṛṣṇāṃ na seveta sā hi tṛṣṇā durāsadā ।।

tṛṣṇāvaśo naiva pramucyate

tṛṣṇāvaśo hi puruṣaḥ saṃsārānnaiva mucyate ।
anuttamāni saukhyāni bhuktvā deveṣu jantavaḥ ।।

tṛṣṇāpāśavikṛṣṭāḥ narakaṃ patanti

tṛṣṇāpāśavikṛṣṭāste patanti narakaṃ punaḥ ।
asvatantrādikalyāṇaṃ nityaduḥkhamayaṃ kaṭu ।।

tṛṣṇayā kadāpi tuṣṭirna bhavati

tṛṣṇāyāḥ sevanānmuktaḥ sanmārgamadhigacchati ।
satṛṣṇasya kutastuṣṭirviṣayeṣu bhaviṣyati ।।

sā tṛptiryā vitṛṣṇasya vītaśokasya dehinaḥ ।
evaṃ vitarkavihitāḥ pramādena ca vañcitāḥ ।।

tṛṣṇayā devānapi narakaṃ yānti

tṛṣṇayāḥ toṣitā devāḥ patanti narakaṃ punaḥ ।
viḍambaneyaṃ paramā yatsurā narakaṃ gatāḥ ।।

krīḍakāḥ paramā bhūtvā kāmasya vaśamāgatāḥ ।
na codvijanti saṃsārān prāṇinaścittamohitāḥ ।।

tṛṣṇayā duḥkhataraṃ padamāpnoti

duḥkhād duḥkhataraṃ yānti tṛṣṇayā parivañcitāḥ ।
yathā yathā sukhasyāptirvardhate jālinī tathā ।।

jālinīvahnidagdhasya narakānupakarṣati ।
satṛṣṇasya vitarkā ye teṣāṃ saṃkhyā na vidyate ।।

viṣayagāminaḥ tṛṣṇayā mṛtyumukhameva praviśanti

avitarkavitarkantu mṛtyurājo vikarṣati ।
vitarkakāmavaśagāstṛṣṇāviṣayagāminaḥ ।।

kāmāsvādapramattāḥ viṣayiṇo duḥkhinastiṣṭhanti

sukhasya bhoginaṃ dṛṣṭvā na vidvadbhistatheṣyate ।
kāmāsvādapramattānāṃ prāṇināṃ viṣayārthinām ।।

dehinaḥ tṛṣṇayā dahayante

jālinī bādhate nityaṃ yathā badhnanti dehinaḥ ।
pañcālambanametattu tṛṣṇayā naiva dahayate ।।

tṛṣṇāvimuktā vimalā bhavanti

tṛṣṇāvimuktavimalā na pāpapuragāminaḥ ।
saṅkalpadoṣā kuṭilā tridoṣarajasodbhavāḥ ।।

tṛṣṇayā saṃsārasāgare parivarte patanti janāḥ

pramādajalagambhīrāḥ strīrāgakṛtasevanāḥ ।
gītatūryasvarāḥ śīghraṃ surāpānācca cañcalāḥ ।।

sañchannaviṣayā sarve manaḥ kṣiptataraṅgiṇaḥ ।
tṛṣṇānadīṣu viṣame vahanti na ca gocare ।।

gāhante te ca sammūḍhāḥ surā rāgeṇa vañcitāḥ ।
tridoṣakāṣṭhasaṃbhūtāḥ pramādānilavegataḥ ।।

tṛṣṇānalaḥ suragaṇān dahate na ca te viduḥ ।
na kṣaṇo nāpi hi lavo na muhūrta kathañcana ।।

yā na tṛṣṇāvaśagataiḥ suraiḥ samupabhujyate ।
tṛṣṇābhūmiriyaṃ kāṣṭhā vitarkajalasambhṛtā ।।

tṛṣṇāsarpadagdhaḥ kālavaśīkṛto bhavati

yasmin krīḍanti vivaśāḥ devāḥ kāmavaśānugāḥ ।
cittādinā pracaṇḍena tṛṣṇāviṣavisarpiṇā ।।

daṣṭānupañcaśīrṣeṇa kiṃ vṛthā vilapasyatha ।
tṛṣṇānadī viśāleyaṃ pañcatīrthasamudbhavā ।।

tṛṣṇāmohendrajālena viprakīrṇena sarvadā ।
tathā prapañcitā devā yathā na śubhabhāginaḥ ।।

tṛṣṇāviṣayaghṛtasikto vardhata eva

nendriyāṇi sadā kāmaistṛpyanti hi kathañcana ।
saṃvardhate tathā tṛṣṇā ghṛtasikto yathānalaḥ ।।

tṛṣṇayā vividhāsu yoniṣu janāḥ bhramanti

nānāvidhaiḥ sukhaireṣā jālinī lokanāśinī ।
narakapretatiryakṣu bhrāmayantī narān sadā ।।

vītatṛṣṇaḥ nirmuktabandhanaḥ paramāṃ gatimāpnoti

mṛtyūpapattidolāyāṃ śliṣyante bāliśāḥ janāḥ ।
suśīlāvītatṛṣṇāśca gatāste paramāṃ gatim ।।

nirmuktabandhanā dhīrā gataśokā gatavyathāḥ ।
sukhaṃ prāpnuvanti nityaṃ ye na tṛṣṇāvaśānugāḥ ।
janmaduḥkhamayaiḥ pāśairna te vidhyanti sūrayaḥ ।।

tṛṣṇāvisṛṣṭiḥ jñānāya pravartayati

yeṣāṃ sarvāsvavasthāsu jñāneṣu vihitaṃ manaḥ ।
animitte mano yeṣāṃ visṛṣṭā ye ca tṛṣṇayā ।
te vītamalakāntārāḥ pāraṃ prāptāḥ sukhodayam ।।

tṛṣṇāmohapramattāḥ bhave bhave bhramanti

tṛṣṇāmohapramattā ye ratisaukhyāstathaiva ca ।
mohitāste devagaṇā bhramiṣyanti bhave bhave ।।

aharniśaṃ tṛṣṇā tāpayati

kuṭṭanavyavahārā ye paricittāpahāriṇaḥ ।
avidyābahulā ye vā nityaṃ dāhābhikāṅkṣiṇaḥ ।
na rātrau na divā teṣāṃ hṛdayaṃ suprasīdati ।।

lobhābhibhūtāḥ tuṣāgnikalpā bhavanti

lobhābhibhūtamanasāṃ parivittābhikāṅkṣiṇām ।
teṣāṃ tuṣāgnikalpānāṃ viśvasenna svabhāvataḥ ।।

viṣayendhana sarpād bhayamevocitam

bibheti hi naraḥ sarvaḥ sarpādiva viṣendhanāt ।
lobhena viṣayeṇaivābhibhūtāste narā bhṛśam ।।

tṛṣṇāvaśagāḥ vividhāṃ yoniṃ labhante

te mṛtā narakaṃ yānti pretayoniṃ tathaiva ca ।
tasmādapi vinirmuktā narakād vahnisammukhāt ।।

ākāṅkṣiṇaḥ nityaṃ duḥkhabhāgino bhavanti

pañcajanmaśatānyete bhavanti parikāṅkṣiṇaḥ ।
vivarṇā dīnavadanā nityaṃ duḥkhasya bhāginaḥ ।
bhavanti manujāḥ sarve lobhopahatacetasaḥ ।।

vivekasampannāḥ paramāṃ gatiṃ labhante

prahīṇalobhā ye santi nityaṃ jñānābhikāṅkṣiṇaḥ ।
buddhimantaḥ sadā santaḥ te gatāḥ paramāṃ gatim ।
nirvāṇahṛdayā vītalobhamohāḥ sadā narāḥ ।।

lobhākṛṣṭasya vinipātaḥ

lobhāśīviṣadaṣṭasya vinipāto dhruvaṃ sthitaḥ ।
kriyamāṇo dhruvaṃ loko vardhate sa muhurmuhuḥ ।।

śuṣkendhanaṃ samādāya yathā vahniḥ pravardhate ।
dhanatṛṣṇāratāḥ sattvāḥ dhanopārjanatatparāḥ ।।

mṛtyukāle samutpanne tyajanti vivaśā dhanam ।
yacca tatsambhavaṃ yogāt tat sarva na vinaśyati ।।

lobhātmā ghoraṃ narakaṃ yāti

tena vittena lobhātmā nīyate narakaṃ bhṛśam ।
anyaistadbhujyate vittaṃ sa tu pāpena lipyate ।।

prayānti narakaṃ ghoraṃ paścāttāpena dahyate ।
anartho hyartharūpeṇa sukharūpeṇa vā sukham ।।

lobhatyāgaṃ prājñaḥ kuryāt

amitraṃ mitrarūpeṇa lobho ayaṃ hṛdi vartate ।
na lobhaṃ saṃśrayet prājño lobhāgnirdahyate sadā ।।

lobhadagdhāḥ narakagāmino bhavanti

tena dagdhā bhṛśaṃ sattvāḥ paścānnarakagāminaḥ ।
lokasādhāraṇā hyete vibhavāḥ sukhavarjitāḥ ।।

tṛṣṇābhayavimuktireva śreyaskarī

teṣāmarthe kathaṃ pāpa kriyate mandabuddhibhiḥ ।
tṛṣṇābhayavimuktasya nirāśasya hi sarvataḥ ।।

vītakāṅkṣasya dhīrasya nityaṃ padamavasthitam ।
sampattau dhābate loko vipattau nāvabudhyate ।।

sampattiḥ kṣayāntā

vipadantā hi sampattiḥ kṣayāntaṃ divasaṃ yathā ।
yathā tiṣṭhati sampattiḥ vipattiḥ pāpikā tathā ।।

kāmabhogairdevā api narakaṃ yānti

avitṛptasya kāmebhyastṛṣṇayā paridahyate ।
yasyeṣṭāḥ sampado nityaṃ sukhaṃ cābhimataṃ sadā ।।

jani nāśayate tāsāṃ tṛṣṇā naṣṭā sukhāvahā ।
te devā narakaṃ yānti kāmabhogaistathārpitāḥ ।।

analāceṣṭitaṃ sarva tad vadanti tathāgatāḥ ।
manuṣyā yacca narakaṃ prayā śataśastathā ।।

vimugdhāḥ yati jīvanaṃ nāvagacchanti

ceṣṭitaṃ tad viśālāyāḥ yoṣikāyā vidurbudhāḥ ।
vimohitā na vindanti tvaritaṃ svalpajīvitam ।।

tṛṣṇayā sukṛtāni vinaśyanti

sukṛtāni ca naśyanti tṛṣṇā naiva vinaśyati ।
bhave bhave gatā satvāḥ na vindanti śubhāśubham ।।

śubhasya phalameveṣṭaṃ yat surāḥ paribhuñjate ।
aśubhasya tathā dṛṣṭamasukhaṃ vinipātajam ।।

śubhāśubhaprahīṇā eva jarāmaraṇarahitā bhavanti

śubhāśubhaprahīṇā ye saṅgadoṣavivarjitāḥ ।
te gatāḥ paramaṃ sthānaṃ jarāmaraṇavarjitam ।।

tṛṣṇānadīparikṣiptaḥ janaḥ kimapi nāvagacchati

pañcāraṃ bhavacakraṃ tat tṛṣṇānābhipuraḥsaram ।
nadīrāgaparikṣiptaṃ na ca loko avabudhyate ।।

doṣāvartatarā jñeyā saṅkalpamakarākulāḥ ।
tṛṣṇānadī viśāleyaṃ na ca loko avabudhyate ।।

tṛṣṇā triṣu kāleṣu vañcikā

trikāle vañcanī tṛṣṇā nityamajñānakāriṇī ।
na tasyāṃ viśvased dhīmān saṃsārabandhanā hi sā ।।

tṛṣṇā lokabandhanabhūtā

mitravad dṛśyate kāle śatruvacca nikṛntati ।
na tasyāṃ viśvaset prājñaḥ sā hi lokasya bandhanam ।।

śakyaṃ hi bandhanaṃ chettumāyasaṃ dāruvattathā ।
na tṛṣṇābandhanaṃ chettuṃ nityaṃ kāmagaveṣibhiḥ ।।

yasyeṣṭo bandhabhedo ayaṃ yasyeṣṭaṃ sukhamavyayam ।
sa tṛṣṇayā vimuktaḥ prajñāśo bhavet ।।

jñānena tṛṣṇāvṛkṣasya chedanaṃ karttavyam

jñānālokaḥ sukhāloko duḥkhaṃ tṛṣṇātamaḥsmṛtam ।
tasmādālokamāsthāya tamo nudati paṇḍitaḥ ।।

jñānakhaḍgena tīkṣṇena tṛṣṇāvṛkṣaṃ nikṛntati ।
nikṛttavṛkṣaḥ naraḥ sukhaṃ prāpnotyanuttamam ।।

doṣeṇa bahulā hyeṣā nadī prasravaṇākulā ।
doṣā netānahitvā bhavānmuñcati paṇḍitaḥ ।।

prajñānāvamāśritya tṛṣṇānadyāḥ pāraṃ gacchati

tṛṣṇānadīṃ tripathagāṃ pramādāvartadustarām ।
prajñānāvaṃ samāśritya pāraṃ gacchantyanāmayam ।।

mahecchatāmahacchatraṃ yena cāyānti bāliśāḥ ।
tasmānmahecchatā badhyā tvayeyaṃ jñānacakṣuṣā ।।

mahecchaiva hṛdayavraṇabhūtā

mahecchatāvraṇastīvro hṛdaye yasya jāyate ।
na rātrau na divā tasya sukhaṃ bhavati lobhinaḥ ।।

saṅkalpe tu na sambhūtaḥ tṛṣṇāvāyusamīritaḥ ।
mahecchatāmayo vahnirdahate hṛdayaṃ nṛṇām ।।

lobhenātmano ahitaṃ kurvanti janāḥ

lobhenāveṣṭitamanāḥ puruṣo laghucetasā ।
jīvitānyapi sārāṇi jahāti dhanatṛṣṇayā ।।

pāpāni hi ca karmāṇi kurvanti puruṣāḥ kṣitau ।
dhanalābhena tat sarva pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।।

ye sāhasaṃ na kurvanti viśanti jvalanaṃ ca yat ।
tat sarva lobhadoṣeṇa kurvantyahitamātmanaḥ ।।

śastrānilāni duḥkhāni vividhāni ca ।
viśanti narā mūḍhā lobhastatra hi kāraṇam ।।

hṛdayastho manovahnirnityaṃ bahvicchatāṃ nṛṇām ।
alpecchatayā hṛcchāntirbhavatilābhinaḥ ।।

yathāgnirindhanenaiva praśāntimadhigacchati ।
tathā vahvicchatāṃ nṛṇāṃ dhanairvṛddhiḥ prajāyate ।।

alpecchataiva sukham

bhūpālā dhanaistṛptāḥ koṭiśo nidhanaṃ gatāḥ ।
yāsyanti cānye nidhanaṃ tasmādalpecchatā sukham ।।

tṛṣṇāvihīna eva sukhamāpnoti

duḥkhaṃ vahvicchatā nṛṇāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ sukhaduḥkhayoḥ ।
idamuktaṃ parīkṣakaiḥ ।
eṣa panthāḥ śivaḥ śreṣṭho yena tṛṣṇā vaśīkṛtā ।।

।। iti tṛṣṇāvargo aṣṭamaḥ ।।

strījugupsāvargaḥ

striya evānarthamūlam

striyo mūlaṃ pāpasya dhananāśasya sarvathā ।
svahite ye na niratāḥ kutasteṣāṃ bhavet sukham ।।

anarthakarmaratayaḥ śāṭhyerṣyābahulāstriyaḥ ।
lokadvayavināśāya puruṣāṇāmavasthitāḥ ।।

nityaṃ sarāgakuśalā nityaṃ tadvacanāḥ parāḥ ।
anyacca hṛdaye tāsāṃ kathayantyanyadeva vā ।।

āpātamadhurāḥ sūkṣmāḥ vipāke vajracetasaḥ ।
nopakāreṇa satkāraṃ smaranti laghucetasaḥ ।।

striyo vidyutsvabhāvahṛdayā aticañcalāḥ

nāśayitvā priyaśataṃ smarantyekaṃ hi vipriyam ।
vidyutsvabhāvahṛdayāḥ striyaḥ pāpasya bhūmayaḥ ।।

strīṇāṃ nāśasādhakatvapradarśanam

strīhetunāśamicchanti puruṣā vakracetasaḥ ।
strīvināśo vināśo drāgiha loke paratra ca ।।

strīdarśanamevāgnivaddahati

evaṃ tu sarvaviṣayāḥ strīdarśanamihaikajam ।
abhibhūya sarvaviṣayān nāryagnijvalanaṃ mahat ।।

strīdoṣapradarśanapūrvakaṃ nārījugupsāsamīkṣaṇam

saṃśleṣādapi viśleṣaḥ smaraṇāt kathanādapi ।
strīṇāṃ dāhasamuttho ayaṃ vahnirantarjahāsakaḥ ।।

rāgeṇa saha jāyante nityaṃ vai dāruṇāḥ striyaḥ ।
dānena saha jāyante yathā loke hutāśanāḥ ।।

na bhavet tādṛśo dāho yo ayaṃ vahnisamudbhavaḥ ।
yādṛśaḥ strīmado hyasti dehināṃ hṛdayodbhavaḥ ।।

sarvalokavināśāya sarvadharmakṣayāya ca ।
hetavo narakasyaitāḥ striyaḥ proktā maharṣibhiḥ ।।

mukhato madhurāmarṣā hṛdayena viṣopamāḥ ।
anavasthitasauhārdā nāsāṃ kaścit priyo naraḥ ।।

muhūrtena priyastāsāṃ muhūrtena tathāpriyaḥ ।
anavasthitasauhārdāścañcalā kṣaṇikopamāḥ ।।

vañcanāhetukuśalā nityaṃ kāryaparāyaṇāḥ ।
nityaṃ saṃyogamanaso nityaṃ mānaparāyaṇāḥ ।।

devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ piśācoragarākṣasāḥ ।
na bandhabhūtā yādṛśyaḥ striyaḥ kālaviṣopamāḥ ।।

nopakāraṃ smarantyetā na kuśalaṃ nāpi vikramam ।
anavasthitacittāśca vāyuvegasamāḥ striyaḥ ।।

bhavanti sampado yatra rakṣyante yatra yoṣitaḥ ।
vyasaneṣu viraktāstu tyajanti puruṣaṃ dhruvam ।।

yaṃ yaṃ gacchanti puruṣaṃ rakṣyante tatra yoṣitaḥ ।
śīghraṃ śīghraṃ naraṃ hyetāstyajanti puruṣaṃ sthitam ।।

yathā hi bhramarī puṣpaṃ śuṣkaṃ tyajati sarvadā ।
tathā vittena rahitaṃ puruṣaṃ tyajati priyā ।।

nistriṃśahṛdayāḥ krūrāścañcalāstamasāvṛtāḥ ।
striyaḥ puruṣanāśāya jātāḥ kenāpi hetunā ।।

devānāṃ bandhanaṃ nāma yathā strībandhanaṃ matam ।
strībandhananibaddhāstu patanti narakaṃ punaḥ ।।

etadagraṃ hi rāgāṇāṃ yo rāgaḥ strīsamudbhavaḥ ।
strīrāgadagdhamanasaṃ paścād dahati pāvakaḥ ।।

pratyakṣāṇyapi karmāṇi rāgaiścāpahataḥ pumān ।
na vetti mūḍhahṛdayaḥ strīrāgeṇa vimohitaḥ ।।

viśvāsya viṣaye puruṣaṃ bad dhvā priyamanekaśaḥ ।
tyajanti vittanāśena tvacaṃ yadvadbhujaṅgamāḥ ।।

sarvopāyabhṛtā nāryaḥ sarvaśaḥ paripālitāḥ ।
na śakyāḥ svavaśīkarttuṃ striyaḥ paramadāruṇāḥ ।।

āsāṃ sarvasvabhāvānāṃ nārīṇāṃ calacetasām ।
na yāyājjātu viśvāsaṃ pumān dhīreṇa cetasā ।।

strīvidheyāstu ye martyā nityaṃ kāmagaveṣiṇaḥ ।
paścimadarśanaṃ teṣāṃ suraloke bhaviṣyati ।।

pañcāṅgikena tūryeṇa vipralubdhāḥ samantataḥ ।
vindanti vyasane duḥkhaṃ yadavaśyaṃ bhaviṣyati ।।

imāstāścañcalā nāryo yāsāṃ rāgaḥ kṛtastvayā ।
tā bhavantaṃ parityajya punaranyaṃ tato gatāḥ ।।

dvidhā hi prakṛtiryāsāṃ sahacāriṇī ।
bhūyo abhiyanti puruṣaṃ vyasaneṣu tyajanti ca ।।

mṛgavanmohayantyetāḥ puruṣaṃ rāgamohitam ।
paścāt vyasane prāpte tyajanti laghucetasaḥ ।।

nopakāraṃ na satkāraṃ na priyāṇi na santatim ।
smaranti yoṣitastīvrā vyasane samupasthite ।।

mlānaṃ puṣpaṃ yathā tyaktvā bhramaro anyatra dhāvati ।
tathā hi vyasane prāpte tyajanti khalu yoṣitaḥ ।।

anapekṣitasauhārdāścañcalāśca raṇapriyāḥ ।
bhavanti yoṣitaḥ sarvā viṣamiśraṃ yathā madhu ।।

mohayanti narān kāmairvākyaiścāpi viśeṣataḥ ।
na teṣāṃ viśvaseddhīmān puruṣo dhīramānasaḥ ।।

ābhirvimohitāḥ kiṃ vā raṃjitāḥ puruṣāḥ svataḥ ।
na kurvanti hitaṃ vākyaṃ yathā muṣṇikagāmikam ।।

devāsuranarān yakṣān piśācoragarākṣasān ।
indrajālamayā nāryo vañcayanti viśeṣataḥ ।।

etadagrañca pāśānāṃ yadidaṃ strīmayaṃ dṛḍham ।
anena baddhāḥ puruṣā bhramanti bhavacārake ।।

na kaścit pāśapāśo ayaṃ hṛtpāśo yoṣitaḥ param ।
hṛtpāśabandhanairbaddhāḥ puruṣā duḥkhamohitāḥ ।।

dahayate chidyate pāśasstrīmayastu na dahayate ।
narakapretatiryakṣu gacchantamanugacchati ।।

mūrtimān badhyate kāyaḥ pāśena mahatā tathā ।
amūrtigaṃ cittamidaṃ strīpāśena tu badhyate ।।

dṛśyate pāśamanyaṃ yena badhnanti yoṣitaḥ ।
abhijñeyamapramāṇaṃ strīmayaṃ bandhanaṃ mahat ।।

anenāpātaramyeṇa mokṣeṇa sarvadā ।
pāśena baddhāḥ puruṣā na mucyante bhavārṇavāt ।।

ṣaḍindriyāṇi badhnāti pāśo yaḥ strīmayo mahān ।
pāśastu kāyamevaikaṃ kaścit badhnāti vā na vā ।।

bandhanaṃ na dṛḍhaṃ hīdaṃ mokṣavārya ṣaḍāyasam ।
saṃraktacittabhoge hi mandabuddhernarasya ca ।।

snāyuyantreṇa baddhāsu vistṛtakarmabhūmiṣu ।
tīkṣṇaraktāsinā yukto maraṇārthamihāgataḥ ।।

strīṇāṃ daurguṇyam

vañcanācchalakūṭāsu rabhasā nu viśeṣataḥ ।
cañcalo bhrāntacittāsu bhrāntastvaṅgakṣaṇāriṣu ।।

vibhrānto bhrāntakathitairbhūṣaṇānāṃ tathā svanaiḥ ।
haranti puruṣaṃ kṣipraṃ vañcanākuśalāḥ striyaḥ ।।

nānāvidheṣu puṣpeṣu yathā carati ṣaṭ padaḥ ।
nānāvidheṣu martyeṣu tathemāścañcalāḥ striyaḥ ।।

yathā madhurikā pītvā puṣpamanyatra gacchati ।
tathā puruṣamāpīyaḥ prayānti rabhasaṃ striyaḥ ।।

arthādāneṣu kuśalāḥ kruddhā nityaṃ durāsadāḥ ।
vañcayitvā naraṃ śīghramanyatra saṃprayānti tāḥ ।।

sādhyamāyāpraharaṇāḥ kālakūṭaviṣopamāḥ ।
striyaḥ puruṣaghātinyaścāturyeṣu vyavasthitāḥ ।।

vāyvākāśānalā yadvan na śaktā grathituṃ naraiḥ ।
tathopāyaśatairnāryo śaktā rakṣituṃ naraiḥ ।।

anarthavyādhimṛtyūnāṃ duṣkṛtānāñca karmaṇām ।
hetubhūtāḥ paraṃ nāryo mokṣacaryābadhasya ca ।।

yadanekaprakāreṣu śaṭheṣu pāpakarmasu ।
manujā loke tatra hetuḥ parastriyaḥ ।।

na bālayauvanenaiva vārdhakyenaiva śāmyati ।
cāpalyaṃ sahajaṃ strīṇāṃ bhāskarasya yathā prabhā ।।

anityaṃ sauhṛdaṃ tāsāṃ dīptānāmarciṣāṃ kaṇaiḥ ।
vairañca śāśvataṃ tāsāmaśmanāṃ ca yathā vraṇaiḥ ।।

dhanahīne virajyante dhanayuktā bhavanti ca ।
yāvadartha striyastāvadarthahīne kutaḥ striyaḥ? ।।

na sevābhiścadānena nopakāraiḥ pṛthagvidhaiḥ ।
svīkarttuṃ na striyaḥ śakyāḥ jvalanopamacetasaḥ ।।

yathā naro anukūlaśca chandakarttā yathā yathā ।
tathā tathā striyastasya vañcanākuśalāḥ param ।।

puṣpacchatro yathā sarpo bhasmacchatro yathā nalaḥ ।
rūpacchannaṃ tathā cittamāsāṃ bhavati yoṣitām ।।

viṣavṛkṣe yathā puṣpaṃ dṛṣṭiramyaṃ na śāntaye ।
viṣavṛkṣa nāryaḥ parivarjyāḥ samantataḥ ।।

nārīṇāṃ darśanākāṃkṣī viṣayesu ca tatparaḥ ।
naro na sukhabhogāya smilloke na cāpare ।।

nāgninā na ca śastreṇa na balena na jantubhiḥ ।
strīmayaṃ bandhanaṃ hetuḥ śakyate na durāsadam ।।

doṣajālamidaṃ strīmayaṃ carate bhuvi ।
yastrīvivarjito dhīmān asmilloke mahīyate ।।

yathā bhūtairmanuṣyāṇāṃ svakarmotthāpane na ca ।
tathā striyo hi rakṣanti viṣamārtha tyajanti ca ।।

gatārthavibhavaṃ bhūyo varjitaṃ svena karmaṇā ।
devaṃ samīkṣya capalāḥ striyo naiva prabhāvikāḥ ।।

strīsukhaṃ kṣaṇabhaṅguram

kṣaṇabhaṅgamidaṃ saukhyamadhigatamavasthitam ।
catvāryetāni duḥkhāni sevitāni nṛbhiḥ sadā ।।

strī viṣāgnisadṛśā

tasmāt tāni vivarjyāni viṣāgnisadṛśāni hi ।
yaḥ kaściccapalo janturyaśca doṣodbhavaḥ sadā ।।

tasmāt parisamāviṣṭāḥ striyaḥ kāraṇavatsalāḥ ।
na sūryastamaso heturnāgniḥ śītasya kāraṇam ।।

na strīṇāṃ sauhṛdaṃ citte svalpamapyavatiṣṭhate ।
yathā sthirā bhūmiriyaṃ yathā vāyuḥ sadā calaḥ ।।

striyaḥ doṣameva smaranti

tathā strīṇāṃ kṛtaṃ nāsti doṣamayyaḥ sadā smṛtāḥ ।
ciraprayatnāḥ puruṣaiḥ lobhitā bahuśaḥ striyaḥ ।।

tyajanti vyasane prāpte śuṣkaṃ sara ivāśugāḥ ।
nordhvagāḥ sarito dṛṣṭā nāśmano gatiriṣyate ।।

girīṇāṃ gamanaṃ nāsti strīṇāṃ naivāsti sauhṛdam ।
vapukarti sadā nṛṇāṃ dharmārthayaśasāṃ tathā ।।

yoniścānarthajālasya doṣāṇāmudbhavasya ca ।
bhaved vajramayī mṛdvī tyajed ravim ।।

na strī tyajedasādhyāni janmāpekṣā viśeṣataḥ ।
nopacārakriyā dānapriyavākyāpalāpanaiḥ ।।

svīkartuṃ na striyaḥ śakyā jvalanopamacetasaḥ ।
sukheṣu samatāṃ yānti vyasaneṣu tyajanti ca ।।

upakārāṃśca vismṛtya doṣamekaṃ smaranti tāḥ ।
vanopavanaśaileṣu bhuktvā sukhamanekaśaḥ ।।

strī lokasya bandhanam

saṃprāpte vyasane tīvre striya paribhavanti hi ।
lokasya bandhanaṃ nāryo vañcanākṛtivardhikāḥ ।।

adhamāḥ vinipātānāṃ doṣāṇāṃ cāspadaṃ ।
sarvalokavināśāya vaśīkurvanti tṛṣṇayā ।।

yathā strībandhanamidaṃ durviṣahyaṃ kṛtaṃ mahat ।
yadidaṃ bandhanaṃ loke kāmarāgamayaṃ mahat ।।

strīvarjanameva śreyaṣkaram

tathā cānyaprayatnena vicārya upalabhyate ।
vaśīkurvanti tā kāmavāṇairanekaśaḥ ।।

svalpaiḥ parājitaṃ kṛtvā kāmasya vaśagāḥ striyaḥ ।
rāgerṣyāśāṭhyabhūmīnāṃ vidyuccañcalacetasām ।।

lobhāhaṅkārayonīnāṃ na viśvāsyāḥ kathañcana ।
śastrāgnisadṛśāstīkṣṇāḥ kāmapāśaparātmanaḥ ।।

svabhraprapātaviṣamaṃ gaṃbhīrasamacetasām ।
parābhidrohamāyendrajālatadgatamānasān ।।

akālamṛtyuvajrāgnikālakūṭasamātmanām ।
anekadoṣasambhārananditānāmanekaśaḥ ।।

yadi śīlalavaḥ kaścit strīṇāṃ manasi vartate ।
cireṇa dahate vahniḥ sa spṛṣṭāḥ pavaneritaḥ ।।

strīdarśanasamucchreyamātraṃ dahati pāvakaḥ ।
tasmāt striyo vivarjyāḥ syuḥ yadicchet sukhamuttamam ।।

etat sarva paraṃ loke nārīṇāṃ varjanaṃ sadā ।
yadṛcchājālinīhetuṃ yaḥ icched bhūtimātmanaḥ ।।

ya icchati nivṛttiṃ tu sa naraḥ strīṃ vivarjayet ।
sukhāsaktastathārtho kusīdaścañcalaḥ śaṭhaḥ ।।

pāpasevī sumṛṣṭāśī naro bhadraṃ na paśyati ।
udyukto vīryavān dhīro dhārmikaḥ strīṃ vivarjayet ।
dakṣo hetuphalaśraddho naraḥ kalyāṇavān bhavet ।।

।। iti strījugupsāvargo navamaḥ ।।

madyajugupsāvargaḥ

madyapānavarṇanasādhanapradarśanam

madyapānaṃ na seveta madyaṃ hi viṣamuttamam ।
naśyanti kuśalā dharmā madyapānaniṣevaṇāt ।।

yaḥ sevate sadā madyaṃ tasya buddhirasaṃsthitā ।
balabuddhī na dharmo asti tasmānmadyaṃ vivarjayet ।।

nāśānāmuttamaṃ nāśaṃ madyamuktaṃ manīṣibhiḥ ।
tasmānmadyaṃ na seveta nāśayate naram ।।

aniṣṭāḥ pāpakā dharmā madyapānaniṣevaṇāt ।
bhavanti tasmād viṣavanmadyapānaṃ vivarjayet ।।

dhanakṣayaṃ pāpakaraṃ kausīdyakaramuttamam ।
madyapānasthitā doṣāḥ tasmāt tat parivarjayet ।।

rāgasyoddīpanaṃ madyaṃ krodhasyāpi tathaiva ca ।
mohasyoddīpakaṃ bhūyastasmānmadyaṃ vivarjayet ।।

madyamūlamanarthasya hāsasya narakasya ca ।
sarvendriyavināśānāṃ hetubhūtaṃ hyanarthakam ।।

atiharṣābhidhānasya śokasya ca bhayasya ca ।
vāgdoṣasyātidamyasya pāruṣyasyāspadaṃ hi tat ।।

madyenākṣiptamanasaḥ puruṣāḥ paśubhiḥ samāḥ ।
kāryākārya na vindanti tasmānmadyaṃ vivarjayet ।।

madyakṣipto hi puruṣo jīvannapi mṛto mataḥ ।
ya icchejjīvitaṃ saukhyaṃ sa madyaṃ varjayet sadā ।।

madyaṃ sarvadoṣāspadam

sarvadoṣāspadaṃ madyaṃ sarvānarthakaraṃ sadā ।
sarvapāpeṣu sopānaṃ tamasāmālayo mahān ।।

madyena pretaloke narake vā patanam

madyena narakaṃ yānti pretalokaṃ tathaiva ca ।
tiryakṣu yānti puruṣā madyadoṣeṇa vañcitāḥ ।।

viṣādapi viṣaṃ madyaṃ narakānnarakaṃ tathā ।
vyādhīnāṃ ca paraṃ vyādhirmadyamuktaṃ manīṣibhiḥ ।।

madyena hānipradarśanam

buddhīndriyavināśāya dharmaratnaṃ kṣayāya ca ।
yo atirekaparaṃ madyaṃ brahmacaryabadhāya ca ।।

madyena laghutāṃ yānti pārthivā śāstracakṣuṣaḥ ।
kiṃ punaḥ prākṛtā martyā madyapānavilambitāḥ ।।

madyasya vināśakaratvam

kuṭhāraḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ hrīvināśakaraṃ param ।
madyaṃ niṣevitaṃ martyairvināśāyopakalpyate ।।

madyena jñānājñānavivekaśūnyapradarśanam

na jñānaṃ nāpi vijñānaṃ na kāryāṇi na ca kriyām ।
jānīte puruṣaḥ sarva madyena hṛtacetasā ।।

madyasevanasya paritāpasādhanam

akasmāt tapyate janturakasmāt paritapyate ।
bhavatyakasmāt pāpī yo madyamanusevate ।।

madyasya buddhisammohajanakatvam

buddhisammohajanakaṃ lokadvayavināśakam ।
vahniśca mokṣadharmāṇāṃ madyamekaṃ vyavasthitam ।।

madyasya kimpākatvam

abhyāse madhuraṃ madyaṃ vipāke paramaṃ kaṭu ।
kimpākādapi kimpākaṃ madyamuktaṃ parīkṣakaiḥ ।।

narakasya sādhanaṃ madyam

na madye viśvaseddhīmān naraṃ vakṣyati māmiti ।
śītasparśa vipākoṣṇaṃ madyaṃ narakagāmikam ।।

sampattau vyasanaṃ madyaṃ devānāṃ tu viśeṣataḥ ।
yathā yathā sukhā prītistannāśe vyasanaṃ tathā ।।

madyapānamadonmattāḥ sattvā mohavaśānugāḥ ।
sākṣyamohamayaṃ pānaṃ pibanti rasatṛṣṇayā ।।

madyaṃ mohamayaṃ pāna pītvā kālena coditāḥ ।
nākāt pratyakṣanarakaṃ tasmāt madyaṃ na saṃspṛśet ।।

darśanātpānācca madyapānaṃ mohajanakam

darśanāt sparśanāt pānāta madyaṃ mohayate naram ।
tasmāt sa madyapānaṃ ca dūrataḥ parivarjayet ।।

darśanājjāyate lobhaḥ sparśanād gandhasambhavaḥ ।
gandhād rasābhilāṣaśca rasanādadhamā matiḥ ।।

manīṣiṇaḥ madyasevanātpatanti

naikasarvādhamaṃ nyāsaṃ kathayanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।
nāmarūpaniṣedhāya yathā madyaṃ niṣevitam ।।

madyapānaphalasūcanam

vāgbhrāmayati mastiṣkaṃ cakṣuṣīdhvanireva ca ।
sambhrāntivimatirmūḍho na kiñcit pratipadyate ।।

striyo api madyapāyinamupahasanti

striyo apyupahasantīmaṃ puruṣaṃ patitaṃ bhuvi ।
niśceṣṭaṃ kāṣṭhasadṛśaṃ niścalaṃ patitaṃ bhuvi ।।

madyapānaṃ maraṇādapi nikṛṣṭataram

sambhāvitasya maraṇaṃ madyapānaṃ prakīrtyate ।
hālāhalādabhyadhikaṃ kārāvāsādhikaṃ ca tat ।।

madyapānavarjanaṃ śreyaskaram

ādīnavāśca ṣaṭ triṃśanmadyapānādavasthitāḥ ।
tasmādādīnavo jñeyaḥ sa hi tad varjayet sadā ।।

madyapānaṃ viduṣo api jantoḥ malinīkaraṇāya bhavati

atijātasya viduṣo malinīkaraṇaṃ mahat ।
kāśapuṣpasamaṃ jantuṃ kurute laghusattvaram ।।

viṣayānaladagdhaḥ kāryākāryaśūnyo bhavati

pramādauhyati magnānāṃ viṣayairapahṛṣyate ।
madyapānena bhūyaśca manovyāmohakāriṇā ।।

viṣayānaladagdhasya kāryākāryamajānataḥ ।
vanopavanalabdhasya madyapānasya kiṃ punaḥ ।।

madyapānaṃ mohāya pāpāya jāyate

rasena śobhanaṃ madyaṃ pariṇāmena dāruṇam ।
pariṇāmaphalaṃ pāpaṃ narakeṣūpapadyate ।।

pītaṃ janayate mohaṃ mohāt pāpeṣu rakṣyate ।
saṃraktahṛdayo bālo narakānupadhāvati ।।

madyapānamadhamatvasādhanam

prakarṣa janayatyādau vipāke dainyamuttamam ।
tṛṭ chedaṃ kurute cāsau paścāddāhaṃ sudāruṇam ।।

tad buddhiṃ nāśayatyādau paścānnāśayate sukham ।
tasmāt sa puruṣo dhīro yo madyaṃ nānusevate ।।

madyaniṣeviṇo vihagasadṛśā bhavanti

vihagaiḥ sadṛśaṃ yānti puruṣā madyasevinaḥ ।
tulyaṃ vyāmohajanakaṃ madyaṃ mohamahāviṣam ।।

vimohitā durgatimadhigacchanti

yairmadyaṃ viṣavad dṛṣṭaṃ tairdṛṣṭaṃ padamuttamam ।
yaistu tad virasaṃ pītaṃ pītaṃ tāmra lohitam ।।

niṣpratīkārakarmāṇi yaḥ karoti vimohitaḥ ।
madyapānasamāviṣṭaḥ so ante gacchati durgatim ।।

madyapānasevināṃ nāśo bhavati

ekatra sarvapāpāni madyapāna ।
yasmānnāśayate cittamūlaśca saṃvaraḥ ।।

madyapāyī naṣṭadharmo bhavati

naikāṅgitā hi cittasya na dharmāṇāṃ vicāraṇā ।
yaḥ pā nirato bhikṣurbhavenmadyaniṣevaṇāt ।।

madyenākṣiptamanaso kuśalasya ca ghātakaḥ ।
naṣṭadharmasya sattvasya nāyaṃ loko na cāparaḥ ।।

īryyāpathaṃ na jānāti na kālaṃ nāpi deśanām ।
saddharmato viruddhaśca tucchaṃ kimapi bhāṣate ।।

svayaṃ tāvanna jānāti kimidaṃ kathyate mayā ।
vākpāruṣyaṃ kathaṃ cānyaṃ parijñāsyatyaśobhanam ।।

lāghavaṃ yāti lokasya dharmācca parihīyate ।
nidhana puruṣairdṛṣṭaṃ madyajvalanasevanāt ।।

madyapānaṃ kutsāṃ sampādayati

nāśo bhavatyatīte hi vartamāne suhṛjjane ।
anāgate kutsitānāṃ madyaṃ traikālyanāśakam ।।

madyaṃ dharmapradūṣakameva

nāmarūpavināśāya cittanāśāya dehinām ।
utpannadoṣajanakaṃ madyaṃ dharmapradūṣakam ।।

madyavarjanaṃ dharmāya pānañca mṛtyurna bhavati

samāhitā dharmaśīlāḥ puruṣā madyavarjakāḥ ।
te yānti paramaṃ sthānaṃ yatra mṛtyurna vidyate ।।

।। iti madyajugupsāvargo daśamaḥ ।।

atha dvitīyam udānam

(cittañca vāk tathā karma saṃyojanantu pāpakam ।

narakapretatiryakkṣutkausīdyāni vidurdaśa ।। )

cittavargaḥ

cittaṃ rājavat pravartate

agādhaṃ viṣamaṃ tīvraṃ sarvasattvagataṃ mahat ।
cittaṃ sarvasya jagato rājavat sampravartate ।।

cittadhāriṇastajjñāḥ paramāṃ gatiṃ prāpnuvanti

adṛśyaṃ samprati bhayaṃ karma nārakacañcalāḥ ।
ye cittadhāriṇastajjñāste gatāḥ paramāṃ gatim ।।

etannayati vyutthānametannayati durgatim ।
tadevādyantamamalaṃ nirvāṇamadhigacchati ।।

manaḥ pūrvamaṅgamā dharmā manaḥ śreṣṭhā manomayāḥ ।
manasā suprasannena bhāṣate vā karoti vā ।।

cittavaśagasya cittamanudhāvati

yo na cittasya vaśagaścittaṃ tasyāntagaṃ sadā ।
sa nirṇāśayati kleśān tamaḥ sūryodayo yathā ।।

cittadagdhāḥ nāśaṃ yānti

cittaṃ śatruḥ paraṃ śatrurna śatruraparaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
cittadagdhāḥ sadā sattvāḥ kāladagdhā yathā jaḍāḥ ।।

yaścittavaśamāpanno bālo mūḍho ajitendriyaḥ ।
tena duḥkhe samo nāsti nirvāṇaṃ tasya dūrataḥ ।।

cittavaśagaḥ naraḥ narakamadhigacchati

āvarjyaḥ śatruraparo na cittāni ।
eṣa badhnāti puruṣo nṛpateryamaśāsane ।।

viṣayeṣu ratā nityaṃ na sa dharmaḥ kathañcana ।
saddharmapathasammūḍho narakaṃ nayate mahat ।।

durdamānāṃ paraṃ cittamanīnāmagniruttamaḥ ।
durdāntaṃ śīghragantṛ ca narakaṃ nayate dhruvam ।।

ye cittasya vaśaṃ yātā yātāste narakaṃ purā ।
yaistu tad vāryate śīghraṃ na te duḥkhānugāminaḥ ।।

cittānurūpaṃ sukhaṃ duḥkhañca bhavati

yathā yathā cittaṃ pariṇāmastathā tathā ।
kalpānāṃ śubhakarttuśca pāpakarttuśca pāpakam ।।

cittāyattaṃ bhavet karma karmāyattaṃ mano bhavet ।
cittakarma samutthāya saṃsāraḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।।

duṣṭena cetasā karma yaḥ karoti pumāniha ।
pacyate narake tena jālinyā sa viḍambitaḥ ।।

cittakarma evaṃ saṃsāraḥ

cittādhīnaṃ bhavet pāpaṃ saṃsāraḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।
cittapratyayajaṃ hyetat hetupratyayasambhavam ।।

cittena vañcitāḥ sattvā pāpasya vaśamāgatāḥ ।
gacchanti narakaṃ pāpāt kāraṇāgramahābhayā ।।

na bhavet cittavaśago api tu dharmavaśo bhavet
na gacchet cittavaśatāṃ gacched dharmavaśe sadā ।
dharmacārī sukhī nityaṃ pāpacārī na śarmabhāk ।।

cittāyattaṃ sarva phalam

cittāyattā kriyā sarvā cittāyattaṃ phalaṃ smṛtam ।
vicittaṃ hi phalaṃ cittaṃ tathā phalamadhismṛtam ।।

cittena cintitaṃ sarva lokaścittabhavānugaḥ ।
na hi tad vidyate sthānaṃ yanna cittavaśānugam ।।

śubhasya nirvāṇasādhanatvam

mokṣa bandhanayormūlaṃ hetubhūtaṃ paraṃ matam ।
śubhena mucyate janturaśubhenāśu badhyate ।।

cittavaśagāḥ kadāpi nirvāṇaṃ nādhigacchanti
jālinyā mohitāḥ sattvāścittasya vaśamāgatāḥ ।
nirvāṇaṃ nāpi gacchanti jātyandhā iva satpatham ।।

pañcendriyāṇi jitavān pāpaṃ bhuṅkte na karhicit ।
ekacittaṃ tathā karma kurute vividhe bhave ।।

pañcaraṅgojjvalaṃ cittaṃ yathā dṛśyaṃ praśasyate ।
pañcendriyavicitraṃ hi tathā karma bhave bhavet ।।

cittakarttānekadhā bhavati

cittakartā hi puruṣo dṛśyairbhavati naikadhā ।
cittaṃ cittakaraṃ śūnyaṃ sarvathā naiva dṛśyate ।।

cittaṃ śobhanamaśobhanaṃ ca karma karoti

śobhanāśobhanaṃ citraṃ yathā bhittiḥ kṛtistathā ।
śobhanāśobhanaṃ karma tathā cittaṃ karoti hi ।।

cittānugaṃ karma

divārātrau yathā cittaṃ sthitaṃ bhavati citragam ।
divārātrau tathā karma bhave samanuvartate ।।

akṛtvā sukṛtaṃ karma cittavṛttyanugā narāḥ ।
patanti vivaśāḥ pāpe cittāriparivañcitāḥ ।।

karmacittakaro hyeṣa yatra yatra niyujyate ।
caracittena mahatā taccittaṃ ca karotyayam ।।

pariṇāmaviśeṣeṇa yatra yatra niyokṣyate ।
preṣyante tatra cittena tridhā tu gaticāriṇaḥ ।।

cittasya damanaṃ sukhāvaham

cittādhināni vartante sarvakarmāṇi dehinām ।
tasmāccittaṃ sadā dāntaṃ nayate padamacyutam ।।

durviṣahyasya laghunā yatra yatra nipātinaḥ ।
cittasya damanaṃ sādhu cittaṃ dāntaṃ sukhāvaham ।।

yena cittaṃ sadā dāntaṃ tena doṣāḥ sadā jitāḥ ।
jitadoṣasya dhīrasya duḥkhaṃ naiva prapadyate ।।

cittasya laghuceṣṭitameva duḥkham

yacca svakaṃ bhaved duḥkhaṃ yacca duḥkhaṃ paratra ca ।
tat sarvamaviṣahyasya cittasya laghuceṣṭitam ।।

cittameva sarveṣāṃ prabhuḥ

sasurāsuranāgānāṃ piśācoragarakṣasām ।
prabhurekaḥ paraṃ cittaṃ rājā tribhavasya tat ।।

cittabhrāntaduḥkhamaśnute

cittaṃ nayati deveṣu cittañca narabhūmiṣu ।
cittaṃ nayatyapāye cittaṃ bhrāmayati prajāḥ ।।

cittād bhrāntasya naṣṭasya viṣayairmohitasya ca ।
tṛṣṇayā dahyamānasya sthitaṃ duḥkhamanuttamam ।।

cittasya damanāt sukhānubhūtirbhavati

ekacāri sadāmūḍhaṃ durviṣahyaṃ mahābalam ।
sampradāri sadādṛśyaṃ capalaṃ śīghragāminam ।।

evaṃ vidhaṃ hi ye cittaṃ damayanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।
te mārabandhanātītāḥ pāraṃ prāptāḥ sukhodayam ।।

capalaṃ cittaṃ narakāyopakalpyate

saṅkalpakuṭilaṃ tīvramagādhaṃ capalaṃ hi tat ।
cittaṃ tamaḥśritaṃ śubhraṃ narakāyopakalpyate ।।

doṣanirmukto acyutaṃ padaṃ prāpnoti

tadevaṃ doṣanirmuktaṃ nendriyārthavaśānugam ।
aliptaṃ pāpakairdharmairnayate padamacyutam ।।

śuddhaṃ cittaṃ śuddhe karmaṇi pravartate

hetupratyayajaṃ cittaṃ yogavāhi paraṃ ca tat ।
pariṇāmavaśācchīghraṃ tathā tat sampravartate ।।

cittānadhīnatve karma cañcalaṃ bhavati

ekaṃ karoti karmāṇi vividhāni calaṃ ca tat ।
ekānekaṃ caraṃ sūkṣmaṃ kṣaṇādūrdhva na tiṣṭhati ।।

saṃsārasya māyopamatvapratipādanam

durvijñeyaḥ sadā tasya niḥśarīrasya sarvadā ।
ko asau nayati lokāntamatha kena ca gacchati ।।

gataśca tiṣṭhati kutra śarīrakarmakārakam ।
dṛśyāni tasya karmāṇi sañcayo na ca dṛśyate ।।

damanaṃ duṣkaraṃ tasya yasya bhūtirna vidyate ।
sarvasattvagataṃ ghoraṃ laghukāri ca cākṣuṣam ।।

pāpāt pāpataraṃ dṛṣṭaṃ māyopamamidaṃ bhavet ।
puṇyāt puṇyataraṃ dṛṣṭaṃ samyagmārgasamāśritam ।।

māyopamatvasamarthanam

na gatirjñāyate tasya gamanaṃ naiva dṛśyate ।
nīyate ca kṣataṃ sarva jātyuttarasamāni ca ।।

śastreṇa chidyate nedaṃ jvalanena ca dahayate ।
chidyate dahyate caiva janaḥ sarvamacakṣuṣā ।।

dṛḍhaṃ yat karmarajjvādi naraṃ badhnāti duḥkhitam ।
jātyantarasahastrāṇi nayate na ca dṛśyate ।।

dāntameva cittaṃ sukhāvaham

muhūrtena śubhaṃ bhūtaṃ muhūrtenāśubhaṃ ca tat ।
śubhāśubhābhyāṃ racitaṃ dāntaṃ sukhāvaham ।।

ṣaḍ bhirdvāraiḥ prasūteṣu viṣayeṣvatilolupam ।
cittaṃ nayati lokāntaṃ vyasanaṃ na ca budhyate ।।

viprasannacittasya śreyaskaratve anuttamaṃ sukhaṃ bhavati

viprasannaṃ yathā toyaṃ viprasannaṃ yathā nabhaḥ ।
viprasannaṃ tathā cittaṃ nīyate sukhamuttamam ।।

janāḥ sātiśayā vitarkaviṣayodbhavāt ।
pauravāścittarājñaste bhavanti sahacāriṇaḥ ।।

cañcalaṃ manaḥ saṃsāre gatiṃ kārayati

dhāvati yatra ca manastatra dhāvantyajñāninaḥ ।
parasparabalānnī bhramanti tribhavārṇa m ।।

viśeṣacittenottamā gatirbhavati

cittavaiśadya bhāvānāṃ viśeṣaḥ karmaṇāstathā ।
na karmaguṇahīnasya viśeṣa upalabhyate ।।

susamāhitacittasya praśaṃsā

susamāhitacittaḥ sa nityaṃ dharmānudarśakaḥ ।
na doṣavaśamāyāti yathā divyastamonudaḥ ।।

gṛhasthasya samyagdṛṣṭitve nirvāṇaprāptirbhavati

samyagdṛṣṭeścādhimātrā yasya cetasi vartate ।
gṛhastho api sa me jñeyo muktaḥ saṃsārabandhanāt ।।

vijñā devalokaṃ gacchanti

kalyāṇanirmalaṃ yacca tato doṣeṇa bādhyate ।
vijño malamāpnoti devaloke sa jāyate ।।

vinītacittāḥ sukhagāmino bhavanti

viṣayadvāracapalaṃ nadīkuṭilagāminam ।
yairvinītamidaṃ cittaṃ te surāḥ śubhabhāginaḥ ।।

adharmamārgaḥ kalyāṇāya na bhavati

adharmapathamāśritya janāḥ pāpavaśānugāḥ ।
ciraṃ bhramanti saṃsāre cittena parikheditāḥ ।।

cittaṃ kṣaṇe kṣaṇe parivartate

kṣaṇe kṣaṇe cittamidaṃ naikaśaḥ parivartate ।
laghusvabhāvacapalaṃ māyāgandharvasannibham ।।

cañcalacitto baddho bhavati

tasya bandhanameveṣṭaṃ jñānavijñānasammatam ।
dūravṛttirmahāvegaḥ paridhāvatyanekadhā ।।

dhṛtyā cittadhāriṇaḥ sukhamaśnute

hriyamāṇaṃ sadā cittamindriyārthe durāsadam ।
sandhārayati yo dhṛtyā sa dhīraḥ pāragāmikaḥ ।।

dhṛtimajñānamohaṃ ca viṣayottānamānasam ।
sandhārayati yo dhīmān sa loke paṇḍito naraḥ ।।

śubhacittaṃ kāmāvarodhakaṃ bhavati

yo yathā kurute cittaṃ tathā kāmān sa paśyati ।
śubhena kāmaśamanaṃ nāśubhena pravardhanam ।।

apraśāntamatirduḥkhamāpnoti
śāntacittaṃmanāḥ kāmānasyatīha viṣāstravat ।
apraśāntamatiḥ sarpamaṇivat tān sa paśyati ।।

cittavaśago na śubhāṃ gatimāpnoti

indriyāṇīndriyārthāśca cittādhīnā bhavantyamī ।
citta saṃśleṣayogena pariṇāmaḥ pravartate ।।

dhīrapraśaṃsā

tasyaiva vyavadhānena dhīraśca pratibudhyate ।
rūpasāmānyato dṛṣṭaṃ pariṇāmaḥ kathaṃ pṛthak ।।

cittasvarūpanirūpaṇam

yathā rūpaṃ tathā sarva viṣayāścittahetavaḥ ।
cittaṃ dāntaṃ sadā śāntaṃ doṣamiśravigarhitam ।।

ekamekaṃ yathā śāli gandharūpe pṛthagvidhe ।
saṃśleṣo yāti nānātvaṃ tathācittaṃ pravartate ।।

kriyāṃ hi tatra kurute yatra pradhāvati ।
cittasaṃvāhanaṃ tadvākyaṃ loko ayaṃ sampravartate ।।

viṣayād bhrāntamanasaś tivego mahābalaḥ ।
cittaṃ karaṃ dāntaṃ śivaṃ bhavati dehinām ।।

dāntena cetasā tattvadarśanaṃ bhavati

tenādāntena śīghreṇa sarvapāpavihāriṇā ।
bhrāmyate tribhavaḥ sarvaḥ na ca tattvaṃ sa paśyati ।।

samīraṇaraṇodbhrānto lokaḥ saṃsāre bhramati

samīraṇaraṇodbhrānto yathā bhramati sāgaraḥ ।
citteśvarasamāyukto loko ayaṃ bhrāmyate sadā ।।

cittaṃ śubhaṃ sukhamedhīta

śubhopanītaṃ cittaṃ śubheṣvevāpanīyate ।
tathā śubhānucaritamaśnute teṣu dhāvati ।।

yogavāhicittaṃ pratyayaṃ labhate

yogavāhi nṛṇāṃ cittaṃ vāyvambusamameva ca ।
pratyayaśca yathā labhyastathā tat paridhāvati ।।

cittaṃ pradhāvati parivartate ca

śīghraṃ pradhāvate cittaṃ śīghrañca parivartate ।
śīghraṃ nayati deveśa dāyabhūmiṣu ।।

cittasya karttṛtvam

karttṛtvaṃ sarvadharmāṇāṃ bharttṛtvaṃ sarvakarmaṇām ।
netṛtvaṃ sarvakarmāṇāṃ cittatvamiti lakṣyate ।।

cittaṃ na viśvaset

na viśvaseddhi cittasya nityaṃ chidraprahāriṇaḥ ।
durlabhasyāpi vaśyasya capalasya viśeṣataḥ ।।

cittagativarṇanam

muhūrtena śubhaṃ yāti muhūrtena tathāśubham ।
bhavatyavyākṛtaṃ śīghraṃ gatirasya na vidyate ।।

nāyatirjñāyate tasya gamanaṃ naiva vidyate ।
abhūtaḥ sambhavastasya bhūtvā ca pratigacchati ।।

rūparahitaṃ cittam

nākāro vidyate tasya sañcayo api na vidyate ।
grahaṇaṃ tasya naivāsti niḥśarīrasya sarvataḥ ।।

pratyayasādhanavarṇanam

hetupratyayasāmagrayā prāptaḥ sañjāyate punaḥ ।
maṇisomapratyayo pratyayo jñāyate analaḥ ।।

cittamindriyarūpādīn prati dhāvati

tathaivendriyarūpādīn prativijñānasambhavaḥ ।
naikasya jñāyate cittaṃ samavāyyanulakṣyate ।।

cittaṃ durnivāryam

tadevaṃ viṣayaṃ matvā durnivārya ca sarvataḥ ।
saddharmamatirāstheyā na kāmeṣu kathañcana ।।

cittamati capalam

caṇḍāticapalaṃ tīvramaviṣahyaṃ mahāvalam ।
cittaṃ karoti karmāṇi yanna paśyanti bāliśāḥ ।।

duḥkhapravartakaṃ cittam

sarvasya karmaṇaścittaṃ hetubhūtaṃ bhave bhave ।
bhavet pravartakaṃ duḥkhaṃ yena dhāvati bāliśaḥ ।।

cittadoṣo mahādoṣa eva

vātādayo na doṣāḥ syurdoṣā rāgādayo matāḥ ।
vātādibhirapāyeṣu mānavo nopapadyate ।।

cittadoṣo mahādoṣo nityaṃ vidarśakaḥ ।
tasmātteṣāṃ samāśreyo na vātādigamādiha ।।

rāgānugaṃ cittaṃ duṣṭaṃ bhavati

vātādayaḥ praṇaśyanti dehanāśāccharīriṇām ।
na tasya syurjanmāntaraśatairapi ।।

tasmād rāgasya vaśagaṃ na vidheyaṃ kadācana ।
ābhyantikaṃ paraṃ śreyaḥ prāpyate rāgasaṅkramāt ।।

mana eva cikitsako bhavati

yaścittavaidyaḥ sa bhiṣag na śarīrabhiṣag bhṛśam ।
manaścikitsako jñeyo na tathā laukiko mataḥ ।।

svacittakarmaṇā dagdho narake patati

karmacintyaṃ samaṃ cintyaṃ na cittena prapadyate ।
svacittakarmaṇā dagdho narakānupadhāvati ।।

dhyānādeva cittaṃ śuddhaṃ bhavati

yacchreyaḥ samacittasya na tat padyate ।
saṃrakṣyaṃ hṛdayaṃ mūḍhaḥ prayātamanudhāvati ।।

cittavaśago duḥkhamāpnoti

dhyānād dhyeyena kūṭena yaḥ pumān vanamāśritaḥ ।
taṃ muktvā cittakaḥ so ayaṃ saṃprahṛṣyati bāliśaḥ ।।

ye bālāścittapāśena cittakarmavicāriṇaḥ ।
nīyante hyavaśā ghoraṃ narakaṃ karmamohitā ।।

cittavaividhyanirūpaṇam

sucittamapi yaccitaṃ na taccittaṃ satāṃ matam ।
karmacittaṃ mahācittaṃ tridhātugatacitritam ।।

sattvā citrairupāyairhi bhramanti gatipañcake ।
tat sarva karmasācivyaṃ citrakartṛ vicitritam ।।

cittavaśago baddho bhavati

cittacitrakareṇedaṃ karmajātaṃ vicitritam ।
yena sarvamidaṃ baddhaṃ jagad bhramati mohitam ।।

varṣātaparajodhūmaiścittaṃ naśyati bhūbhujaiḥ ।
kalpakoṭisahastreṇa citraṃ cittaṃ vinaśyati ।।

nāśaṃ prayāti basudhā sāgaraścāpi śuṣyati ।
cittenāpi kṛtaṃ citraṃ tasyānubhavane sthite ।।

pramatte citte nānāgatirbhavati

nānāgatisamāvṛttā nānākarmasamānugāḥ ।
nānācittavaśāḥ sattvā bhramanti gatipañcake ।।

bāliśā nṛṇāṃ cittaṃ viṣayaṃ dhāvati ।
na cinotyaśubhaṃ karma yena dhāvati durgatim ।।

cañcalaṃ cittaṃ sadā viṣamaṃ bhavati

tasmāccittaṃ sadā rakṣyaṃ cañcalaṃ viṣamaṃ kharam ।
nityaṃ viṣayasaṃsaktaṃ tṛṣṇāviṣasamāvṛttam ।।

viṣayānuraktaṃ cittaṃ vyasane pātayati

dhāvate viṣayaṃ caitad vyasanaṃ nāvabudhyate ।
paścāttu vyasane prāpte phalaṃ vindati karmaṇaḥ ।।

samāhitacittaḥ sukhamaśnute

apāyabhīrutā tasya tasya cittaṃ samāhitam ।
samāhitena cittena sukhāt sukhamavāpnute ।।

nirjitacittaḥ sukhamāpnoti

viṣamaṃ capalaṃ tīvramaviṣahyaṃ mahābalam ।
yaiścittaṃ nirjitaṃ dhīraiste loke sukhino matāḥ ।।

।। iti cittavarga ekādaśaḥ ।।

vāgvargaḥ

nirvāṇābhilāṣukaḥ pāruṣyaṃ varjayet

pāruṣyaṃ varjayet dhīmān samyagvāg bhīrato bhavet ।
mādhuryābhirato jarntunirvāṇasyāntike sthitaḥ ।।

vācaṃ paśyan sadābhāṣenmalināṃ ca vivarjayet ।
vāṅmanenābhibhūtā ye te yānti narakaṃ narāḥ ।।

ekadharmavyatītasya mṛṣāvādasya dehinaḥ ।
pratīrṇapratilokasya nākārya pāpamastiha ।।

mṛṣāvāg na prayoktavyā

mṛṣāvācaṃ na bhāṣeta sarvā pratyayakārikām ।
yathā badhyati saṃsāre sugatiṃ naiva paśyati ।।

sādhupratyayatenīhā sarvavidveṣakārikā ।
kāntāraḥ sarvādharmāṇāṃ mṛṣāvāca pravartate ।।

jātamātrasya martyasya kaṭhārī jāyate mukhe ।
paścāt chinattyātmānaṃ vācā durbhāṣitaṃ vadan ।।

sarvā kāryapatākā sā sarvapāpaprasūtikā ।
tamasāṃ yonirekā sā yāṃ vācaṃ bhāṣate mṛṣā ।।

satyena hīnāḥ puruṣāḥ sarvasādhuvivarjitāḥ ।
tṛṇavad yānti loke asmin pratyapāyeṣu duḥkhitāḥ ।।

na vadedanṛtaṃ dhīraḥ kaṣṭā hyanṛtavāditā ।
pūtigandhyasukhī cāpi paścāttāpena tapyate ।।

satyamahimā

satyaṃ ca na vivarjeta tasya dharmo na vidyate ।
vinivartitadharmasya sthitaṃ duḥkhamanekajam ।।

satyaṃ sarvadharmāṇāṃ pradīpabhūtam

pradīpaḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ sādhūnāṃ ratnavat priyam ।
svargasya ca paraṃ vartma satyamuktaṃ gatajvaraiḥ ।।

satyaṃ na hi divaṃ yāti mokṣasyāsatyavādinaḥ ।
satyahīnā hi puruṣāḥ paśutulyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।।

jaghanyānāṃ jaghānyāste yeṣāṃ na vidyate ।
satyaṃ dharmasya sopānaṃ jyotiṣāmākaro mahān ।।

panthāśca mokṣadharmāṇāṃ dhanānāṃ dhanamuttamam ।
pāpakaiśca trāṇāṃ satyamuktaṃ manīṣibhiḥ ।।

satyabhūṣitaṃ vāg bhūṣaṇasyāpi bhūṣaṇam

jyotiṣāṃ paramaṃ jyotiścakṣuścakṣuṣmatāmapi ।
draviṇena vinā satyaṃ bhūṣaṇasyāpi bhūṣaṇam ।।

nidhānamatulaṃ satyamahārya ।
gacchanti puruṣāḥ paramāṃ gatim ।।

na tathā bhāsate rājā nānālaṅkārabhūṣitaḥ ।
satyena bhūṣito dhīmān śobhate devavad yathā ।।

na mātā na pitā cātha mitrāṇi na ca bāndhavāḥ ।
trāṇamevaṃ yathā śrutvā tasmāt satyaparo bhavet ।।

anṛtanindā

vahnīnāṃ paramo vahnirviṣāṇāṃ paramaṃ viṣam ।
durgatīnāṃ ca sopānamanṛtaṃ parikīrtitam ।।

viṣāgnitulyasaṃsparśa vartayedanṛtaṃ pumān ।
anṛtena hi yo deva dagdhaityabhidhīyate ।।

satyāsatyayoḥ parasparavirodhitvam

tasmāt sarvābhisāreṇa nṛtaṃ pumān ।
sarva bhayādikaṃ kaṣṭamanṛtaṃ kīrtitaṃ budhaiḥ ।।

vahnīnāṃ paramo vahnirnirdahedapi sāgaram ।
kiṃ punaryo mṛṣāvādī kāṣṭhaloṣṭhasamākṛtiḥ ।।

satyaṃ tyaktvā mṛṣāvādaṃ yo naraḥ pratipadyate ।
ratnaṃ tyaktvā sa pāpātmā pāṣāṇaṃ pratipadyate ।।

yasyātmā na bhavet dviṣṭo yasya vā narakaṃ priyam ।
mṛṣāvādaṃ svadehāgnim abuddhiḥ sa niṣevate ।।

sadedaṃ satyavacanaṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ sarvadehinām ।
satyaṃ tyaktvā mṛṣāvāde kasmād yānti kubuddhayaḥ ।।
satyaṃ guṇānāmagryaṃ vai doṣāṇāmanṛtaṃ smṛtam ।
guṇāṃstyaktvā kathaṃ mūḍho doṣeṣu paridhāvati ।।

bījaṃ sarvasya duḥkhasya mṛṣāvādaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।
tathā satyaṃ sukhasyaiva tasmānnānṛtako bhavet ।।

satyavādī hi puruṣaḥ priyaḥ sarvasya dehinaḥ ।
cakṣurdoṣaimṛṣāvādī tasmānnānṛtako bhavet ।।

devakalpāḥ sadā kṛṣṭāḥ puruṣāḥ satyavādinaḥ ।
nārakeyāstathā mūḍhā janā hyanṛtacetasaḥ ।।

kalyāṇānāṃ paraṃ satyaṃ doṣāṇāmanṛtaṃ tathā ।
doṣavarjī guṇadveṣī puruṣaḥ puruṣottamaḥ ।।

sukhodayaṃ sukhodarkaṃ sukhena paripacyate ।
sukhena labhate satyaṃ nirvāṇagāmikam ।।

duḥkhodayaṃ kaṭuphalaṃ duḥkhena saha pacyate ।
anṛtaṃ sarvaduḥkhāntaṃ kaḥ pumān na vivarjayet ।।

nānyadeśāgataṃ satyaṃ nānyasmāt prārthyate hi tat ।
sarvatīrthottamaṃ satyaṃ na tīrthasalilāvṛtam ।।

dīpānāṃ ca paro dīpaḥ satyaṃ buddhena deśitam ।
auṣadhānāṃ paraṃ tacca sadā duḥkhaniṣūdanam ।।

amṛtañca viṣañcaiva jihvāpāśe sthitaṃ nṛṇām ।
amṛtaṃ satyamityuktaṃ viṣaṃ tūktaṃ mṛṣāvacaḥ ।।

yasyānṛtamabhipretaṃ tasya satyaṃ dhruvaṃ sthitam ।
viṣantu yasyābhimataṃ tasyeṣṭaṃ syānmṛṣāvacaḥ ।।

viṣeṇa niścitaṃ nāśo mṛṣāvādena niścitaḥ ।
mṛtavat sa pumānasti yo mithyātvabhibhāṣate ।।

nātmano hi hitaṃ pathyaṃ sya na kathañcana ।
paścāttu paraduḥkhāya tat kathaṃ sevyate nṛbhiḥ ।।

deśe deśe mayā dṛṣṭaṃ janmamṛtyusahasrakam ।
paraḥ sahastraṃ janayennāśayedanṛtaṃ vacaḥ ।।

abhijātasa niṣkarṣo dvijātīnāṃ ca bhūṣaṇam ।
darśanaṃ mokṣamārgasya satyamityabhidhīyate ।।

tṛṣṇānadī hayamārāṇāṃ satāṃ satyena karmaṇām ।
pūrvavat satyamityuktaṃ paraṃ sugatadeśikam ।।

anādinidhane loke tṛṣṇāpāraṅgatā ।
nāstyatrāṇaṃ yathā satyamiti dharmavido viduḥ ।।

abhidhyāpāśo na sevanīyaḥ

satyavadhyā sadā kleśā vajravadhyā yathā nagāḥ ।
hatā puruṣā bhidhyā parivañcitāḥ ।।

paracittasamenedaṃ rūpādyaiḥ parivañcyate ।
abhidhyāmānasaṃ pāśaṃ sevitaṃ na vicakṣaṇaiḥ ।।

dahyate avikṛta ātmā tailadīptirivānalaḥ ।
abhidhyādagdhamanasaḥ kāraṇaṃ nopalabhyate ।।

vyāpādaḥ sattvān mohayatyeva

yasmāt tat sarvadā varjyaṃ kaṭukāśāviṣodayam ।
vyāpādamohitāḥ sattvā nityaṃ tadgatamānasāḥ ।।
na śāntimadhigacchanti sarpā iva bileśayāḥ ।
atha kūrasvabhāvā ye vyāpādaparamā narāḥ ।।

na teṣāṃ vidyate saukhyamādityena yathā tamaḥ ।
na dharme nārthanikaro na dharmā na ca bāndhavāḥ ।।

rakṣanti puruṣān sarvān vyāpādāhatacetasaḥ ।
tamasāmākaro hyeṣa vyāpāda iha kathyate ।।

vyāpādayati janakaṃ vyāpādaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।
avyāpādaḥ paraṃ śreyo na vyāpādaḥ kathañcana ।।

avyāpādaparā ye tu te yānti padamacyutam ।
niyatātathavādī yo adharmavādī na dhārmikaḥ ।।

sa cauraḥ sarvalokasya na cauraḥ prākṛtaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
dharmavādī naro yastu carate dharmameva yaḥ ।।

sa yāti śāśvataṃ sthānaṃ yatra gatvā na śocyate ।
mithyāvacohata laukikaḥ samprakīrtyate ।।

lokottaraiḥ kalpaśataiḥ kadācit kathyate na vā ।
tasmāt lokottaraṃ vākyaṃ laukikaṃ na kathañcana ।।

saṃsārabandhanaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ laukikaṃ viṣavad vacaḥ ।
tṛṣṇārataḥ sadā puṇyānmucyateti suniścitam ।।

lokottaro dhanyo vidvadbhiḥ samudāhṛtaḥ ।
hitaṃ tattvaṃ ca yo mūḍho na gṛhṇāti gurorvacaḥ ।।

satyavādī sadā devatābhiḥ puraskṛtaḥ

sa paścād vyasane prāpte tapyate svena cetasā ।
satyavādī sadā dānto devatābhiḥ puraskṛtaḥ ।।

priyo bhavati lokasya paścād deveṣu modati ।
priyo bhavati lokasya paścād svāntena ।
darśanīyaṃ mukhaṃ cāsya devalokeṣu jāyate ।।

abhūtavādī puruṣaḥ sarvasattvopapātakaḥ ।
tamonicayasaṅkāśo jīvannapi mṛtaḥ samaḥ ।।

kathaṃ na jihvā patitā vākyasaṃstutikattṛkā ।
mṛṣā vadati yo vācaṃ sadbhūtaguṇanāśikām ।।

mukhe sannihito byālo mukhe sannihito aphalaḥ ।
sañjvalito vahniryo vācā bhāṣate mṛṣā ।।

jihvā saṅgrathitaiḥ pāśaiḥ narakasyāgrahetukaiḥ ।
chettā ca dharmahetūnāṃ mṛṣāvādaḥ pravartate ।।

na tasya mātā na pitā buddho nāpi samvaraḥ ।
yaḥ pāpabuddhiḥ patito mṛṣāvādaṃ prabhāṣateḥ ।।

akasmāllaghutāṃ yāti ṣaḍbhiśca parivartate ।
mucyate devatābhiśca yo vācaṃ bhāṣate mṛṣā ।।

asaṅgṛhītavākyasyāvicārya krodhanasya ca ।
capalasyālpabhāgyasya sthitaṃ duḥkhamanantakam ।।

parasya duḥkhaṃ dṛṣṭvāpi sattvaḥ sattvopapātakaḥ ।
paravyasanavat tajjñaḥ pumān narakagāmikaḥ ।।
ye yathāvādino marttyā na ca tatkāriṇaḥ sadā ।।
satyameva svargasya nirvāṇasya ca sopānam

satyaṃ svargasya sopānaṃ nirvāṇadvārameva tat ।
tasmāt satyaparo nityaṃ nityaṃ dharmagatiḥ smṛtiḥ ।।

anṛtaṃ na vadet

aśokamajaraṃ sthānaṃ prayāti puruṣottamaḥ ।
varjayedanṛtaṃ dhīmān ninditaṃ tattvadarśibhiḥ ।।

।। iti vāgvargo dvādaśaḥ ।।

karmavargaḥ

śubhāśubhakarmaṇāṃ phalabhogaḥ

śubhānāmaśubhānāṃ ca karmaṇāṃ phalaniścayaḥ ।
bhujyate sukṛtaṃ sarva karmabaddhā hi dehinaḥ ।।

kriyate karma tatkṛdbhiranubhūyate ।
cittamānena mūḍhena tṛṣṇānagaravāsinā ।।

svayameva phalaṃ bhuṅkte

sahāyairbahubhiḥ sārdha kurute karma duṣkṛtam ।
ekākī karmaṇastasya phalaṃ bhuṅkte bhave bhave ।।

karmaṇāmavisaṃyogaḥ sarvaiḥ svajanabāndhavaiḥ ।
śubhāśubhaṃ paraṃ loke gacchantamanugacchati ।।

yatra prayānti puṇyāni gandhastatrānudhāvati ।
tathā śubhāśubhaṃ karma gacchantamanugacchati ।
svakarmaphaladāyādā prāṇena karmayojinaḥ ।।

sukṛtaiḥ suralokaṃ gacchanti

sukṛtaiḥ suralokeṣu duṣkṛtaiśca tathāpyadhaḥ ।
yadduḥkhaṃ karmaphalajaṃ jāyate kaṭukodayam ।।

tasyopamānamasuraṃ triṣu dhātuṣu jāyate ।
tridoṣajaṃ tricittotthaṃ triṣu dhātuṣu pacyate ।।

tasya karmavipākasya triṣu dhātuṣu lakṣyate ।
hetupratyayasāmagrīsamutthaṃ ca prameva tat ।।

anyakṛtakarmaṇaḥ phalaṃ nānyo bhuṅkte

na hyanyena kṛtaṃ pāpamanyena paripacyate ।
sukarmaphaladāyādaḥ prāṇināṃ sarva eva hi ।।

pūrvoktānāṃ trividhānāṃ svasya kṛta eva vipāko bhavati

karmaṇastrividhasyāsya na cāpyanyasya pacyate ।
catvāriṃśadvipākasya ghoraṃ bhavati ceṣṭitam ।।

karmaphalavarṇanam

ekaḥ karoti karmāṇi ekaśca phalamaśnute ।
ekastarati durgāṇi sahāyo jāyate aparaḥ ।।

jalāpekṣī jano yastu kurute karma duṣkṛtam ।
na jano janaśatānāṃ bhuṅkte hi vyañjanaṃ ।।

na hyanyena kṛtaṃ karma saṅkrāmatyaparasya tat ।
na manye anādinidhanamasmiṃlloke na cāparaiḥ ।।

duḥkhāsvādaṃ sukhodbhūtaṃ yena duścaritaṃ kṛtam ।
tena carati saṃsāre prerite karmavāyunā ।।

kasya dharmo vardhate?

anapekṣitatattvasya vyākulīkṛtacetasaḥ ।
vardhate sakalo dharmāvṛtamanoharaḥ ।।

ke narakaṃ gacchanti?

manasā vañcitāḥ sattvā manasā vipramohitāḥ ।
gacchanti narakaṃ pāpāstamastamaparāyaṇāḥ ।।

tamovṛte hi saṃsāre durlabhaṃ buddhaśāsanam ।
duḥkhād duḥkhataraṃ yānti yebhyaḥ dharmo na rocate ।।

anādimati saṃsāre karmajālāvṛtā prajā ।
jāyate bhriyate cai svakarmaphalahetunā ।।

jāyante narake devā nārakeyāstathāvidhāḥ ।
manuṣyāḥ pretaviṣaye narakaṃ vā prayānti hi ।।

sukarmaṇaiva sukham

anyonyaprabhavaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ duḥkhaṃ vā yadi vā sukham ।
kleśadharmodbhave janmanyaparādikṛtaṃ ca tat ।।

asaṅkhyeyakṛtaṃ karma saṃsāre prāṇibhiḥ sadā ।
tatra śakyaṃ budhairgantuṃ varjayitvā tathāgataiḥ ।।

nādharmasya phalaṃ sādhu viparītaṃ na pacyate ।
hetoḥ sadṛśatā dṛṣṭā jalasya vividhasya vai ।।

sādṛśyasya hetuphalaṃ viparītaṃ na jātu hi ।
saṃskṛtānāmarūpāṇāṃ hetuḥ pratyayasambhavaḥ ।।

sahetukaṃ sarva karmaphalam

nāhetukaṃ phalaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ narake tu viśeṣataḥ ।
hetusaṅghātasaṃsaktaṃ narakeṣu vipacyate ।।

kṛtoparatagāḍhānāṃ niyataṃ pāpagāminām ।
karmaṇā phalasambandho narakeṣu vipacyate ।।

deśānāṃ prati kālaṃ tu yat karma nivartate ।
tasya neṣṭaṃ phalaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tattvamārgavidarśakaiḥ ।।

udāharaṇapradarśanapūrvakaṃ phalasya karmādhīnatvameveti

dīpādhīnā prabhā yadvat karmādhīnaṃ phalaṃ tathā ।
anyo anyaphalasambhūtaḥ saṃskṛtaḥ sarva eva hi ।।

pratītyasamutpādasamarthanam

anyonyahetukā dṛṣṭā hyanyonyavaśavartinaḥ ।
sādṛśyasyānubandhena dṛśyante tattvadarśakaiḥ ।।

nāhetuphalasandhānamīśvarādibhirāsthitam ।
bhavanti saṃskṛtā dharmā deśitāstattvadarśibhiḥ ।।

anādimatisaṃsāre hetupratyayasambhave ।
sādṛśyaṃ karmaṇā dṛṣṭaṃ viparītaṃ na kalpyate ।।

buddhasya svarūpam

tatstheṣu karmavaśagāḥ prāṇinaḥ karmahetujāḥ ।
sa karmaphalatattvajño ityabhidhīyate ।।

keṣāṃ śāntiḥ na vidyate?

mārgāmārgaviruddhā ye mūḍhā buddhasya śāsane ।
teṣāṃ vidyate śāntirādityasya tamo yathā ।।

karmāyattaṃ sukham

karmāyattaṃ sukhaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ sukhāyattaṃ manastathā ।
mano avaboddhayā dharmā ye vyutpattivicāriṇaḥ ।।

sucaritasya karmaṇaḥ phalam

anityāḥ sarvasaṃskārā jalabud budasannibhāḥ ।
tasmāt sucaritaṃ karma loke martya paratra ca ।।

dṛṣṭaṃ karmaphalaṃ loke dṛṣṭā eva vicitratā ।
yaḥ pramādaparaḥ puṃsāstasyātmā dhruvamapriyaḥ ।।

karmarajjvātidṛḍhayā duṣpramokṣasugāḍhayā ।
baddhā bālā na gacchanti nirvāṇapuramuttamam ।।

।। iti karmavargastrayodaśaḥ ।।

saṃyojanavargaḥ

jñānena nirvāṇādhigamaḥ

jñānaśastre tāṃ chitvā nirmuktā vigatajvarā ।
prayānti nirvṛttiṃ dhanyā yatra jñānyeva vidyate ।।

sadṛśaṃ hi phalaṃ hetoḥ kathayanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।
hetorasadṛśaṃ naiva phalaṃ pacati dehinām ।।

hetupratyayasambaddhajanmapratyayasaṅgatāḥ ।
yathā baddhā hi saṃsāre pramucyante dehinaḥ ।।

paramaśānterūpāyaḥ

tāṃ viśliṣya susambaddhāṃ gāḍhāṃ durviṣehāṃ parām ।
gacchanti paramāṃ śānti yatra duḥkhaṃ na vidyate ।।

karmaṇā niyataṃ jantuḥ karmaṇā paripacyate ।
sūpagaṃ saṃsāre sukhaṃ naivopalabhyate ।।

duḥkhe duḥkhābhiṣaktānāṃ jantūnāṃ mūḍhacetasām ।
sanmārgadeśiko nāsti yo asmād duḥkhāt pramocayet ।।

ye na dharmaparā nityaṃ ye na satyaparāḥ sadā ।
ye ca yoniratā nityaṃ teṣāṃ duḥkhaṃ na hīyate ।।

dharma iha paratra ca sukhāvahaḥ

mātṛvat pitṛvaccaiva bandhuvat sadā ।
dharmo vai deśito buddhairiha loke paratra ca ।।

trigatyavasthitāḥ sattvāstridoṣavaśamāgatāḥ ।
tridhātugatikā nityaṃ trilokyāṃ patitāḥ ।।

trikarmopāntavaśagāḥ strīpānādiparāśca ye ।
na bhavānmuktigatikāḥ syurbhūmau vicaranti te ।।

keṣāṃ duḥkhaṃ na vidyate?

triratne pramādyanti tribodhivaśagāśca ye ।
tridṛṣṭivarjakā ye tu teṣāṃ duḥkhaṃ na vidyate ।।

trikālasthitisaṃlagnā vijvarāstattvadarśinaḥ ।
tribhāgakṛtisantuṣṭā vītaśokā nivṛttigāḥ ।।

trirāśisamavetā ye trikarmapravicāriṇaḥ ।
na te vatsyanti saṃsāre vītadoṣā gatajvarāḥ ।।

mārgāmārgavidhijñā ye bhāvābhāvavicintakāḥ ।
maitrībhāvaviviktā ye te yānti paramāṃ gatim ।।

naraḥ kān bhajet?

anāvilena viprasannena ।
sarvadā dharmavaśagān dhīrān viprān bhajennaraḥ ।।

satyameva prapannā ye smṛtyā manomalam ।
bhāvābhilāṣād viratā muktā niḥsaṃśayaṃ hi te ।।

nityaṃ duḥkhasukhairbaddhā vipralabdhā hyanekaśaḥ ।
narā nidhanatāṃ yānti prāṇino mohavañcitāḥ ।।

kairdurguṇaiḥ svargo na labhyate?

nāhrīkyamanapatrāpyaṃ kausīdyaṃ pāpamitratā ।
naitāni nākabījāni tebhyo rajyenna paṇḍitaḥ ।।

āhrīkyamanapatrāpyaṃ nityaṃ pāpānucāriṇaḥ ।
naraḥ prapātāt patati sa paścāt pratibudhyate ।।

krodherṣyādibhayagrastāḥ svarga na gacchanti

krodherṣyāstyānamiddhaṃ hi tvaśraddhaṃ yanmanastathā ।
mohaśokabhayagrastā na svarga prabhavanti te ।।

amṛtaṃ madyapānaṃ ca mithyādṛṣṭiśca lubdhatā ।
kāraṇāni karaṇasya vyāpādakrūrakarmatā ।।

kudṛṣṭeḥ kuphalam

adarśanaṃ paraṃ śreyo na kudṛṣṭiḥ kathañcana ।
kudarśanena saṃmūḍhāḥ prayānti narakaṃ narāḥ ।।

ahetuṃ hetumāpaśyantya nityavannarāḥ ।
prayānti narakaṃ tīvraṃ mithyāvādena vañcitāḥ ।।

kaṣṭena tejasā teṣāṃ mithyādarśanatatparāḥ ।
prajñābhimānino bhūtā mohayantyaparān janān ।।

mohāndhakāragahane patantyeva mahārṇave ।
loke prakṛtiduḥkhe asmin hetubhūtā hi te janāḥ ।।

śarāṇāṃ tāpanaṃ kṣepaṃ kathayanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।
cittatā yā tudatyante sarvataḥ kleśaparvataḥ ।।

kleśanāgād vimokṣo yo yasya jñānapuraḥ saraḥ ।
prāpyate vītakai rūpaiḥ puruṣaistattvadarśibhiḥ ।।

anyo anyamatibhiḥ sarvā loko ayaṃ vipralobhitaḥ ।
na yāti paramāṃ śāntiṃ yatra mithyā na kathyate ।।

narakahetavaḥ

auddhatyapāpasaṃsargaḥ kausīdyaṃ lubdhatā tathā ।
hetavo narakasyaite śīlasya hi vivarjanam ।।

madyapānaṃ sadā hiṃsā paradārābhidarśanam ।
lobhaḥ kūrā matiścaiva hetavo narakasya te ।।

nāśahetavaḥ

paiśunyaṃ pāpasaṃsargo mithyādṛṣṭirasaṃyamaḥ ।
cāpalyaṃ manasaścaiva nāśayanti naraṃ sadā ।।

avidyayā saha pāruṣyaiḥ mithyāvāgabhimānitā ।
na sukhāya bhavantyete asmiṃlloke na cāpare ।।

ke parivarjanīyāḥ?

yadyasau bhramati prāyo lokesmin kinna cāpare ।
yadyasambhrāmite loke ye ca duḥkhe nimajjati ।।

tacceṣṭitamavidyāyāḥ kathayanti tathāgatāḥ ।
mithyāmāno atimānī ca sarvathā ।
parivarjyāḥ sadā hyete duḥkhavṛkṣasya hetavaḥ ।।

jñāninaḥ paramodārā nityaṃ kleśavadhe ratāḥ ।
chitvā bandhanaṃ sarva gacchanti padamacyutam ।
ādimadhyāntakalyāṇamasmiṃlloke na cāpare ।।

doṣasevanaiḥ nāśo bhavati

doṣāṇāṃ sevanaṃ dṛṣṭamavidyāsampravartakam ।
varjanīyāḥ sadā kleśāḥ sevyaṃ jñānamanuttamam ।।

jñānena muktirbhavati

jñānena muktirbhavati na ca kleśairihocyate ।
jñānāgninā hi dahayante kleśakāṣṭhā na śeṣataḥ ।।

kāmamayajñānaṃ kleśajanakam

kleśaiḥ kimartha saṃruddhā jālinī viṣa ratā ।
punaḥ kāmamayaṃ jñānaṃ cakṣuḥpaṭalabādhakam ।।

rāganindā

nirvāṇayati sambuddhavākyabhaiṣajyabhojanaiḥ ।
saddharmasenāpatinā rāgasenā vigarhitāḥ ।।

śubhā vāṇī prayoktavyā

udīritā śubhā vāṇī niścetavyā prayatnataḥ ।
catvāro hi viparyāsā budbudavaccakāsate ।
lokadharmāstathā cāṣṭau nāśayantyakhilaṃ jagat ।।

jñānaplavaḥ santaraṇasamarthaḥ

jālinīprabhavā nadyo vitarkaśatadustarāḥ ।
jñānaplavaṃ samāruhya taranti munayaḥ śivāḥ ।।

keṣāṃ muktirna vidyate?

mūḍhā ye bhūtamanaso narāḥ kāmasya sevinaḥ ।
sadā ca pañcabhiḥ sthānairmuktisteṣāṃ na vidyate ।।

ayoniśomanaskārairyo vahniḥ samudīryate ।
sa yoniśomanaskāravarṣaṇaiḥ pratikalpate ।।

avidyāsaṃbhavam andhatvaṃ kathaṃ dūrībhavet?

andhatvaṃ cirakālotthamavidyāsambhavaṃ nṛṇām ।
tadalpakāle jātena pradīpena na paśyati ।।

jñānalokena trayo doṣāḥ vinaśyanti

rāgamūḍhā vipacyante narake mandamedhasaḥ ।
jñāninastu na naśyanti nirvāṇagamanā yathā ।
trayo do vinaśyanti jñānalokena dehinām ।।

tasmādaśeṣavijñānaśīlakṣāntirato bhavet ।
amūḍhānāṃ praṇaśyanti trayo doṣāḥ śarīriṇām ।।

jñānānalena mandaśca kleśendhana mahāttviṣaḥ ।
vyādhinirmagnatanavaḥ śayyāveṣṭanagocarāḥ ।।

yatra yāti paraṃ vedaṃ manomohamayaṃ phalam ।
yāni duḥkhānyanekānyanekā bhujyate gatiḥ ।।

pañcakaiḥ prāṇibhinityametanmohasya ceṣṭitam ।
trayo vā nirjitā doṣā yairidaṃ dahyate jagat ।।

jñānayogena sukhaṃ bhavati

tamagniṃ jñānayogena nirvāpya sukhito bhavet ।
tasmājjñānāgninā nityaṃ nirdahet kleśaparvatam ।
kleśaparvatadagdhasya sukhaṃ padamavasthitam ।।

।। iti saṃyojanavargaścaturdaśaḥ ।।

pāpavargaḥ

pāpaphalasya ajñātā paritāpaṃ labhate

kriyamāṇasya pāpasya vijñeyaṃ kaṭukaṃ phalam ।
yo na jānāti mūḍhātmā paścāt sa paritapyate ।।

labhate puruṣaḥ sarvapāpasya karmaṇaḥ ।
tasmāt pāpaṃ na seveta yadīcchet sukhamātmanaḥ ।।

alpādapi mahāghorāt narakāt pāpacetasaḥ ।
muktyartha pāpāni bhūyo mohavaśaṃ gatāḥ ।।

na viśvaseddhi pāpasyā narakagāmikām ।
alpena vahninā śaile dahayante sarvato drumāḥ ।।

nāsti pāpasamo śatruḥ

pāpena narakaṃ yāti pāpena paridahyate ।
pāpena naiti nirvāṇaṃ nāsti pāpasamo ripuḥ ।।

pāpācāro hi puruṣo na kvacit sukhamedhate ।
tasmānna seveta yadīcchet sukhamātmanaḥ ।।

sādhukāraṃ ca sādhūnāṃ pāpamārgasya duṣkaram ।
kurvantaḥ pāpakān sattvā modante ।।

vipākakaṭukaḥ paścāt paritāpo alpacetasaḥ ।
kuto apacitagātrasya karmaṇo dṛśyate phalam ।।

tasmāt pāpaṃ na kurvīta kaṣṭā pāpasya vedanā ।
pāpaṃ pāpavipākaṃ ca pāpināṃ pacyate dhruvam ।।

na hi pāpaṃ na pāpasya tasmāt pāpaṃ vivarjayet ।
parivarjitapāpasya na pāpād bhayamasti hi ।।

svakṛtaṃ bādhate pāpaṃ parīkṣyaṃ naiva bhujyate ।
kalyāṇasya phalaṃ sādhu kaṣṭaṃ pāpasya pacyate ।।

kṛtvā tu puruṣaḥ pāpaṃ kalyāṇaṃ nānusevate ।
na śastrāgniprapātebhyo duḥkhaṃ syāt tādṛśaṃ nṛṇām ।।

yathā niṣevitaṃ mithyāpāpaṃ pāpeṣu kalpyate ।
vinivarjitapāpasya nityaṃ ca śubhacetasaḥ ।।

śāntasya bhikṣornirvāṇaṃ nātidūram

śāntavaktrasya nirvāṇaṃ nātidūrataḥ ।
tīvrāt tīvrataraṃ yānti narāḥ kukṛtakāriṇaḥ ।।

sukhāt sukhataraṃ yānti narāḥ sukṛtakāriṇaḥ ।
na hi tīvrasya pāpasya sukhaṃ phalamavāpyate ।।

sukhasya vā phala tīvraṃ viparītaṃ na pacyate ।
anādimati saṃsāre sukṛtānāṃ phalaṃ sukham ।।

karmaṇāṃ sukṛtānāṃ ca tathā duḥkhaphalaṃ smṛtam ।
pāpaṃ pāpānugaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ śubhasya ca śubhaṃ tathā ।।

pāpī narakeṣupapadyate

pāpācāraḥ śubhadveṣī narakeṣūpapadyate ।
parivarjitapāpasya nityaṃ ca śubhacetasaḥ ।।

hastāvalambi nirvāṇamadṛṣṭaṃ tadanāvilam ।
ādimadhyāntakalyāṇā dharmā nityaṃ sukhodayāḥ ।।

tasmāt pāpaṃ vivarjayet

ādimadhyāntakaṭukaṃ phalaṃ pāpasya karmaṇaḥ ।
tasmāt pāpaṃ sadā varjyamālambyañca śubhaṃ sadā ।।

parivarjitapāpasya nityaṃ sukhamavasthitam ।

anādimati saṃsāre dagdhāḥ pāpaiḥ punarnarāḥ ।
khedaṃ kasmānna gacchanti bālā mohavaśānugāḥ ।।

āpātamadhuraṃ pāpaṃ pariṇāme agnisannibham ।
pāpakārī tu puruṣaḥ sarvaloke vigarhitaḥ ।
śubhakārī sadā śāntastasmāt pāpaṃ vivarjayet ।।

dhīraistattvanidarśakaiḥ pāpavivarjanam
aniṣṭamahitaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ vipāke kaṭuvedanam ।
pāpaṃ pāpavipākaṃ ca tasmād dhīmān vivarjayet ।।

asti pāpaṃ dhruvaṃ pāpe pāpamasti na pātakam ।
pāpāceṣṭā kṣayāpekṣā kṛpā cittasugāmitā ।।

pāpaṃ pāpāśritaṃ nityaṃ dharmo dharmāśritastathā ।
unnayatyuktametaddhi dhīraistattvanidarśakaiḥ ।।

pāpavirahitāḥ paramaṃ sukhaṃ prāpnuvanti

acetanā dhruvaṃ bālā yeṣāṃ duścaritaṃ priyam ।
vinivarjitapāpāstu gacchanti paramāṃ gatim ।।

atīva vañcanāghorā niyatā pāpagāminī ।
mānuṣyaṃ durlabhaṃ prāpya yasya pāpaṃ priyaṃ bahu ।।

śubhāśubhaphalayoḥ pariṇāmabhedaḥ

pāpād virajyate yastu śubhe vātīva rajyate ।
sa sukhāt sukhamāpnoti nivṛttiṃ vā prayāti hi ।।

naro bhavati dhanyo ayaṃ yaḥ śubhānyupasevate ।
sa tvadhanyatamo loke yaḥ pāpamupasevate ।।

ādimadhyāntanidhanaṃ sadbhireva vigarhitam ।
pāpaṃ pāpānugaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ narakāyopakalpyate ।।

śubhakarmā sukhamāpnoti devalokaṃ ca gacchati
atīva śobhate loke śubhakarmā jitendriyaḥ ।
kāyasya bhedāt satataṃ devaloke sa jāyate ।।

pāpasya pariṇāmaḥ sudāruṇaḥ

duṣkṛtasyānubaddhaṃ hi duṣkṛtaṃ phalamucyate
sukṛtasya tathā dṛṣṭaṃ phalaṃ sukhavipākajam ।
bījasyāśuvibhītasya pariṇāmaḥ sudāruṇaḥ ।।

nimittaṃ sadṛśaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ phalaṃ pāpasya karmaṇaḥ ।
pāpenākṛṣyate jantuḥ durgatau baḍiśairiva ।।

baḍiśairmucyate mīnaḥ pāpaṃ pāpānna mucyate ।
dina pīḍāpi pāpasya sarvathā duḥkhakārikā ।।

amedhyasya yathā gandhaḥ pratikūlo hi dehinām ।
śubhasya vāsanā ramyā vipraṇaṣṭasya durgatau ।।

vileṣu vāsanaṃ yadvat puṣpe naṣṭe pradṛśyate ।
calatyayaṃ pāpakārī nityaṃ kāmavaśānugaḥ ।।

ke śubhacāriṇaḥ?

ālasyānṛtiko nityaṃ nāsau kalyāṇamarhati ।
anantā rajanī teṣāṃ pāpe sthitaṃ manaḥ ।।

prabhātaṃ rajanī teṣāṃ yeṣāṃ pāpe sthirā matiḥ ।
anīrṣyakāḥ sakalyāṇāḥ puruṣāḥ śubhacāriṇaḥ ।।

alpapāpī sukhamāpnute

ye na pāpātmano bhūtāste nityaṃ koṭacāriṇaḥ ।
alpabhārā yathā nāvā plavate na nimajjati ।।

pāpīmitreṇa duḥkhaṃ bhavati

tathālpapāpapuruṣaḥ plavate na nimajjati ।
na pāpamitrasaṃsargāt puruṣaḥ sukhavān bhavet ।।

pāpamitraṃ samāsādya sarvānalaparo bhavet ।
karmārambha vidhijño yo nityaṃ sūkṣmārtha ।।

nāsau limpati pāpena paṅkena gaganaṃ yathā ।
aśrutaṃ puruṣaḥ śṛṇvan śrutañcāpi bhaved dṛḍham ।।

paṇḍitalakṣaṇam

pāpaṃ ca varjayed dhīmān pretya deveṣu jāyate ।
guṇadoṣaparijñānammetat paṇḍitalakṣaṇam ।।

mūḍhalakṣaṇam

guṇadoṣāparijñānametanmūḍhasya lakṣaṇam ।
guṇeṣu guṇasañcāro doṣeṣu ca tathaiva ca ।।

mūḍhāmūḍhayorlakṣaṇam

sadoṣaguṇatattvajño nityaṃ bhavati śokabhāk ।
pāpakarttā puruṣaḥ śatruvaccātmanaḥ sthitaḥ ।।

śubhakarttā tathā puṃso mitravat pratipadyate ।
tamonirayabhūmiṣvamṛto ayaṃ pratipadyate ।।

yasya pāparatā buddhirnityaṃ viṣayatatparā ।
viṣayārāmacapalā nityaṃ rāgānucāriṇī ।।

yasya buddhirna dharmeṣu narasya duḥkhabhāginaḥ ।
hetutaśca mahāduḥkhāntahetorvahnisaṃyutāt ।।

kṣīṇapāpā vayaṃ sarve bhūyo lokamihāgatāḥ ।
sukṛtasya phalaṃ sādhu hyanekaguṇamaṇḍitam ।।

duṣkṛtasya phalaṃ duḥkhaṃ visaṃvādakamiṣyate ।
te vayaṃ sukhaduḥkhābhyāṃ bhūyāma bhavasaṅkaṭe ।।

karmavāyusamudbhrāntāḥ samudrasya yathormayaḥ ।
kṛtaṃ pāpeṣvamanasaḥ pāpaiḥ rakṣanti ye janāḥ ।।

te tasya hetornarakaṃ prayāntyaśubhacāriṇaḥ ।
tasmāttu narakānmuktāḥ te gacchanti triviṣṭapam ।।

te hi duḥkhaṃ saṃsmṛtya punaḥ kāmavaśānugāḥ ।
kharībhūtamidaṃ cittaṃ dolādolaiḥ sukhāsukhaiḥ ।।

viyogo ayaṃ parīghāto na ca duḥkhairna vidyate ।
apāradārasaṃyukta indriyaiḥ parivañcitaḥ ।।

tṛṣṇāpāśavaśagaḥ saṃsāre bhramati

jano bhramati saṃsāre tṛṣṇāpāśavaśānugaḥ ।
narakāt pretabhuvanaṃ tiryagyoniṣu pretataḥ ।।

tiryagbhyo nākabhuvanaṃ nākād bhūyo nṛjātiṣu ।
ekakarmaparibhrānto jagad bhramati cakravat ।।

sarva duḥkham

na ca khedavaśaṃ yānti vaśamāgatāḥ ।
rakṣanti nākabhuvanaṃ virajyante tathā sukhaiḥ ।।

sukhāt sukhaparibhrāntā bhramanti bhramacāriṇaḥ ।
duḥkhaṃ padmasahasrāṇi padmakoṭiśatāni ca ।।

duḥkhāni bhuṅktāni na ca kliśyanti bāliśāḥ ।
na sukhaṃ vidyate loke sarvaduḥkhaiḥ pariplutam ।।

duḥkhasya hetuḥ bhavati

udvegaṃ naiva gacchanti prāṇino mohapīḍitāḥ ।
duḥkhena khidyate bālo duḥkhahetau ca vartate ।।

hetau śataphalaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ bījaṃ prati yathā phalaiḥ ।
sukhaduḥkhakaśābaddhāḥ prāṇinastribhavānugāḥ ।।

na yānti paramaṃ kṣemaṃ sarvaduḥkhavivarjitam ।
smaryate yadā duḥkhaṃ tadā vidhyati dehinam ।।

vismṛte ca punarduḥkhe caranti vigatajvarāḥ ।
nārakaṃ tu sadā duḥkhaṃ smṛtaṃ bhavati dehibhiḥ ।।

tadā kṛṣṇamidaṃ saukhyamanumānena tiṣṭhati ।
tadeva viditaṃ matvā jagat sarva samanvitam ।।

śreyasi kriyatāṃ buddhirdoṣebhyo vinivāryate ।
kṣaṇādhikāracapalaṃ jīvitaṃ veti vartate ।।

kṣīyante cāpi karmāṇi tasmācchreyaḥparo bhavet ।
cittavegaṃ manaḥ sarva jīvitaṃ veti vartate ।।

anāgatād duḥkhāt jñānī na bibheti

tasmānna jīvikāhetau pāpaṃ kuryādvicakṣaṇaḥ ।
anāgatasya duḥkhasya na vibheti mahājanaḥ ।।

yenā pacyate pāpaṃ mohapāpavaśaṅgatam ।
mohitaḥ pāpakairdhamairaśubhaiḥ śuklavarjitaiḥ ।।

mūḍhaḥ pāpavaśād narakaṃ gacchati

nīyate narakaṃ mūḍho yatra pāpaṃ vipacyate ।
yasya pāpād bhayaṃ nāsti sa pāpaṃ kurute bahu ।।

sa pāpānantasandagdhaḥ paścānnarakamāpnute ।
sūkṣmāgnikaṇikā yathā dāhāya kalpate ।।

pāpavirahitāḥ sukhamicchanti

anyairapi tathā pāpairnarakaṃ yāntyabuddhayaḥ ।
apāpabhīrutā tasmāt kartavyā sukhamicchatā ।।

hiṃsā mithyāvaco abrahmacarya bhūyaḥ sukhodayam ।
āhrīkyamanapatrāpyamauddhatyaṃ pāpamitratā ।।

viṣāgnisadṛśaṃ pāpam

viṣāgnisadṛśā hayete tebhyo rakṣet prayatnataḥ ।
duḥkhaṃ hi māradharmo ayaṃ sukhaṃ dharmasamantataḥ ।।

sukhaduḥkhayorlakṣaṇam

lakṣaṇaṃ duḥkhānāṃ vidustattvavido janāḥ ।
satyaṃ dānaṃ tathā kṣāntiḥ sadā cāpāpamitratā ।
maitrī sadābhibhūteṣu prasthānaṃ tridivasya ।।

।। iti pāpavargaḥ pañcadaśaḥ ।।

narakavargaḥ

aṣṭau narakāgnayaḥ

kṛtvā duṣkṛtakarmāṇi sattvā viṣamajīvinaḥ ।
yā gatiḥ pretya gacchantī tānapāyān śṛṇu ।।

sañjīvaṃ kāmasūtraṃ ca sampātaṃ dvau ca rauravau ।
tamoparaṃ mahācitrapatanaṃ ca pratāpanam ।।

ityete narakā aṣṭāvākhyātā duratikramāḥ ।
raudrakarmābhisaṅkīrṇāḥ pratyekaṃ kṣobhadā ।।

narakāgnīnāṃ bhayānakatvam

catuḥskandhāścaturdvārā vibhaktā bhāgaśo mitāḥ ।
ayaḥ prākāraparyantā ayasā pratiduḥkhitāḥ ।।

taptāyomayasaṃ bhūmirjvalantī tejasodgatā ।
anekayojanaśataṃ dahati svaciṃṣā ।।

kandarpadamanā ghorā arciṣmanto durāsadāḥ ।
romaharṣaṇarūpāste apyāhurduḥkhā bhayānakāḥ ।।

narake patitā bhṛśaṃ tapyante

ete patanti narake ūrdhvapādā avāṅmukhāḥ ।
ṛṣīṇāmativaktāraḥ saṃyatānāṃ tapasvinām ।।

te punastatra pacyante taptāmbhasi kṛtā iva ।
krandamānā divārātrau, nagā vāteritā iva ।।

praṇadanti mahānādaṃ tīvraduḥkhaiḥ pratāpitāḥ ।
sarvā diśaśca dhāvanti nārakaiḥ puruṣairdrutāḥ ।।

kudṛṣṭyā mohayitvārthe mohapāśāvṛto janaḥ ।
prāpnoti narakaṃ ghoraṃ kāraṇodadhisaṃvṛtaḥ ।।

kudṛṣṭyā dagdhasarvasvo manuṣyaḥ puruṣādhamaḥ ।
tathā baddho asti narake mānināṃ ghorakāraṇam ।।

ye mithyāvaśamāpannāḥ puruṣā mandamedhasaḥ ।
te sarve narakaṃ yānti cittairhi parivañcitāḥ ।।

kukṛtaphalam

yastvayā duṣkṛtaṃ pūrva kṛtaṃ cittānuvartinā ।
tasya bhuṅktaphalaṃ mūḍha vipākottama ।।

hāryāṇi paricittāni, saṃsevyāḥ parayoṣitaḥ ।
hrasvā jantavo nityaṃ svacittaparivañcitāḥ ।।

tasya karmavipākasya vaśa eva tvamāgataḥ ।
kiṃ krandasi svayaṃ kṛtvā kukarma puruṣādhama! ।।

ye narāḥ kukṛtaṃ kṛtvā pañcatvaṃ yāntyamedhasaḥ ।
yeṣāṃ tu niṣphalaṃ janma bījamuptaṃ yathoṣare ।।

alpamādhuryasaṃyuktān kāmān kaṭuvipākinaḥ ।
sevate yastvasau mūḍhaḥ sa yāti tamaso tamaḥ ।।

kiṃ kṛtaṃ mūḍha bhavatā putradārasukhārthinā ।
dahasye narake caikaḥ svakarmaphalavañcitaḥ ।।

keṣāṃ duṣkaraṃ jīvanam?

yaḥ putradāravaśagaḥ sevate duṣkaraṃ naraḥ ।
sa yāti narakatvaṃ pāpaṃ tadanubhūyate ।।

na dārā na sutā nārtha na mitrāṇi kathañcana ।
mṛtyukāle samutpanne rakṣanti samupasthitāḥ ।।

yeṣāṃ sāṃkleśikaṃ cittaṃ tṛṣṇayā parivañcitam ।
sahāyatā kutasteṣāṃ kasmāt paritapyase? ।।

hṛto asi pūrvaviṣayaistṛṣṇayā parivañcitaḥ ।
kiṃ krandasi svayaṃ kṛtvā kukṛtaṃ mūḍhacetanaḥ ।।

na tathāgnirna śastrāṇi na viṣaṃ nārayaḥ sthitāḥ ।
bādhate puruṣaṃ loke yathā duṣkṛtyamātmajam ।।

pakṣiṇāṃ nīḍavāsavat bhavacakram

digbhāge hi yathā gatvā saṃśrayante vanaspatīn ।
vihagāḥ kālamutthāya tathā prāṇisamāgamaḥ ।।

nāśayitvā paraṃ dravyaṃ kṛtvā lokavyatikramaṃ ।
kiṃ karotyaśubhaṃ karma mohena parivañcitaḥ ।।

yena yāti parāṃ śāntiṃ yena yātyasurālayam ।
tatra hetuḥ paraṃ mohastamasāmapi yat tamaḥ ।।

kuṭumbāya kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ narake pātayati

putradāramayaiḥ pāśaiścānītā narakālayam ।
yadartha kriyate pāpaṃ yuṣmābhiścittavañcitaiḥ ।।

mitrāṇi putrāḥ bandhujanabāndhavāḥ ।
yeṣāmarthe kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ bhavadbhirmandabuddhibhiḥ ।।

nūnamātmā na te kānto babhūva narabhūmiṣu ।
yena tvayā kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ putrārthena narādhamaḥ ।।

yena pūrvakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ paścānna paritapyate ।
sa yāti narakaṃ ghoraṃ putrakāraṇavañcitaḥ ।।

pāpakarmaphalam

kiṃ kariṣyanti putrāste kiṃ dārāḥ kiṃ ca bāndhavāḥ ।
dahasyanādinarake vahniḥ karma dunotyasau ।।

svayaṃ kṛtvāśubhaṃ karmāsukhodayamaninditaḥ ।
tapyase api vṛthādhānaḥ paścānmohena vañcikaḥ ।।

rāgadveṣānugāḥ pāpaṃ mohena parivañcitāḥ ।
aghaṃ prayānti te sarve putradārasukhārthinaḥ ।।

antargatena ca punarbahiḥsthena ca vahninā ।
dahyamāno duḥkhena narake pāpakarmaṇā ।।

vaśaṃ prāptāḥ svacittasya sarva eva viḍambitāḥ ।
kiṃ krandasi vṛthā nāde vahninā paritāpitaḥ ।।

pāpānugaphalaṃ dṛṣṭam

atha pāpāni karmāṇi kṛtavānasi manyase ।
durmate tatra mā kranda kiṃ vṛthā paridevase ।।

pāpeṣu rakṣyate mūḍhaḥ kāraṇāśuci rakṣyate ।
pāpānugaphalaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ hetupratyayasambhavam ।।

kasmānna sevito dharmaḥ pāpañca nahi varjitam ।
pāpād bahiśca puruṣo narakaṃ naiva paśyati ।।

yo na vindanti mūḍhātmā phalaṃ pāpasya karttṛkam ।
so avaśyaṃ labhate doṣān kathaṃ bhokṣyasi durmate ।।

pāpena vañcita pūrvaṃ pāpena paridahyate ।
na kariṣyasi pāpāni tvaduḥkhenaiva yāsyasi ।।

kṛtavānasi pāpāni śubhāni na kathañcana ।
pāpena dahyate tasmādaśubhe na manaḥ kṛthāḥ ।।

kiṃ duḥkhādapi duḥkham?

nāsti duḥkhādato duḥkhaṃ yaḥ pāpamanusevate ।
tasmāt pāpaṃ na seveta yadi duḥkhaṃ na vāñchasi ।।

kuṭumbijanānāṃ spaṣṭoktiḥ

tasyāntarhṛdaye bimbaṃ kintu śāntirna vidyate ।
kāruṇyāspadabhūtāḥ smo nāsmākaṃ karuṇāhṛdi ।।

yathā kṛtaṃ bhavadbhiśca pāpaṃ mohāvṛtairbahu ।
tad vaḥ pradhāvate gāḍhaṃ na ca ye tatra hetavaḥ ।।

śīlaṃ na rakṣitaṃ mūḍha pāpaṃ ca bahu sañcitam ।
sambhūtasya ca pāpasya phalametadupasthitam ।।

na vayaṃ kāraṇaṃ tatra yūyameva hi kāraṇam ।
yaḥ pāpaṃ kurute karma sa hetustasya karmaṇaḥ ।।

bhavadbhiryat kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tṛṣṇāśāpaviḍambitaiḥ ।
tad vo prapadyate ghoraṃ kimasmān paribhāṣata ।।

nākṛtaṃ pacyate pāpaṃ na pāpaṃ syādahetukam ।
yena yaddhi kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tasya tat paripacyate ।।

pāpī narakaṃ yāti

tad bhavantaḥ kriyāhīnā madyapānena vañcitāḥ ।
patitā narake tīvre kiṃ vṛthā paritapyatha ।।

te yūyaṃ kāmaparamāḥ ghoraṃ narakamāgatāḥ ।
kāraṇeṣvapi tīvreṣu kiṃ tathā paritapyatha ।।

yadā kṛtāni pāpāni bhavadbhiḥ kāmamohitaiḥ ।
tadā kasmānna nikṛṣṭaṃ kimadya paritapyatha ।।

hetubhūto hi narako mṛṣāvādasya deśitaḥ ।
heturvai sevitaṃ pūrva niṣphalaṃ paridevatha ।।

nārthena labhate satyaṃ na kṛcchreṇopapadyate ।
tasmāt satyaṃ parityajya mṛṣāvādeṣu rajyase ।।

pūrveṣu pāpamahitaṃ bhavatā mūḍhacetasā ।
kṛtaṃ bhavadbhiḥ kukṛtaṃ paripacyate ।।

pāpakṣayād vinirmukto narakaṃ nopalabhyate ।
nākrandamānāḥ puruṣāḥ vimucyante kathañcana ।।

pāpakartṛ phalaṃ svayameva bhuṅkte

kiṃ krandatha vṛthā mūḍhā vañcitāḥ svena karmaṇā ।
muñcitā vañcitā bālā vṛthā krandantyabuddhayaḥ ।।

ahitairhitarūpaistvaṃ mitrarūpaiśca śatrubhiḥ ।
vipralabdho asi bho martya! gacchannasi mahat tamaḥ ।।

nānyaḥ śatruryathā karma duṣkṛtaṃ tava pāpakam ।
karmaṇā trividhenātha nīyase yamasādhanam ।।

kasmādasi tato mūḍha, vañcitaḥ putrasaṃjñakaiḥ ।
na dānādiṣu buddhistaiḥ kṛtā mohavañcitā ।।

asmāṃllokātparaṃ lokaṃ śatrupṛṣṭhorago yathā ।
śatrūṇāṃ prathamaḥ śatruḥ sarvapāpanidarśakaḥ ।।

viṣāgniśastrapratima! svayaṃ hi duṣkṛtaṃ kṛtam ।
tvayā kṛtāni karmāṇi tvamevamanubhokṣyase ।।

yasya śāntaṃ sadā cittaṃ viṣayairyo na hanyate ।
na hyavasthāmimāṃ yānti tathātvamanupaśyasi ।।

narakasya dhvaniṃ śrutvā kathaṃ krandasi durmate! ।
kiṃ punaryatra vahnistvāṃ dhakṣyati śuṣkakāṣṭhavat ।।

na dagdhā vahninā ye ca dagdhāste kukṛtaiḥ svakaiḥ ।
vahnistu śāmyate kvāpi duṣkṛtāgnirna śāmyati ।।

nāgnirniryāti lokāntaṃ nāgnispṛṣṭo naro ।
kukṛtāgnimayaṃ pāpaṃ yad dhakṣyati hi tattvataḥ ।।

kukṛtāgnividagdhā ye te dagdhā narake narāḥ ।
pāpāgnivarjitā ye tu na teṣāṃ narakodayaḥ ।
yadyātmanaḥ priyo nityaṃ vibheṣi narakād yadi ।।

vivarjaya svapāpāni tato duḥkhaṃ na yāsyasi ।
yānti pāpamaye nityaṃ mohavaśānugāḥ ।।

prāpnoṣi narakaṃ ghoraṃ kimaśrūṇi vimuñcasi? ।
duḥkhaṃ duḥkhavipākaṃ ca duḥkhāntagamanaṃ tathā ।।

sukṛtaṃ nādimadhyāntaśobhanaṃ paripacyate ।
nātra loke tvayāpāpaṃ yatkṛtaṃ sukṛtaṃ ।।

tasya tīvravipākasya phalamadyopabhokṣyase ।
hetupratyayasādṛśyaṃ viparītaṃ na kalpyate ।।

hetuḥ kṛto yathā pūrva tathā phalamavāpsyasi ।
yathā tava tathānyeṣāṃ prāṇarakṣā prayatnataḥ ।।

kasmāt prāṇātipātāste kṛtāḥ pāpānuvartinā ।
prāṇatyāgena puruṣairyad dhanaṃ samupārjitam ।।

karmodayakṛtaṃ tatte yattvayā samupārjitam ।
sarveṣāṃ dayitā dārāḥ prāṇebhyo api garīyasaḥ ।।

tattvayā rāgaraktena kasmādapakṛtāvanāt ।
buddhervyāmohajanakaṃ dharmāṇāṃ dūṣaṇaṃ param ।।

dharmapānaṃ tvayā kārya karmānuparivarjitam ।
jihvāviṣasamutthaṃ yat sarvāpratyayakārakam ।।

mṛṣāvādaṃ tvayā pāpaṃ karmānuparivarjitam ।
evaṃ pañcavidheyeṣu yasmāt tvamanuraktavān ।।

tasmāt saṃmukṣya mā rodi kiṃ vṛthā paridevase ।
viṣayaṃ pāpakā dharmā yasmānnu parivañcitaḥ ।।

tasmāt prāpnoṣi narakaṃ jvālāmālākulaṃ mahat ।
etat tṛṣṇāgninā sarva pradīptaṃ bhuvanatrayam ।।

dharmācaraṇe sāvahitena bhavitavyam

dṛṣṭvā nācarito dharmaḥ kimadya paritapyase ।
te madhuraṃ cittaṃ kāmamandirakaṃ vacaḥ ।।

udīrite mahāpāpe tasmai tatphalamāgatam ।
sa kṛtvā pāpakaṃ karma niyatā pāpavedanā ।।

karuṇaṃ vikalaṃ dīnaṃ kimadya paritapyase ।
karmakṣayeṇa narakāt mucyante pāpakāriṇaḥ ।।

vikrośamagnā bahuśo na mucyante kathañcana ।
aniṣṭaṃ pāpakaṃ karma kṛtvā rogavaśe sthitāḥ ।।

ajñānino aśubhamācaranti

paridevati yo mūḍho vṛthā sa paridevati ।
anāgataphalajño yaḥ pratyutpannaśubhe rataḥ ।।

krośate narake nāsau yathā tvamanutapyase ।
mayā kṛtāni karmāṇi phaladāni mamaiva hi ।।

rogeṇa śatruṇā dagdhaḥ paścānnarakamāgataḥ ।
pramādabhūmiraśubhā rāgadagdhasya dehinaḥ ।।

tena pāśena baddho ahaṃ gato avasthāmimāṃ bhṛśam ।
durācāraratānāṃ tu nṛṇāmasya phalaṃ kaṭu ।।

ajñānabādhito asmīti svakṛtaṃ bhujyate mayā ।
nirdayānāṃ sughorāṇāṃ pāpānāṃ vaśamāgataḥ ।।

muktiḥ kathaṃ syāt?

muktirasmāt kathaṃ syādvai duḥkhasaṃsārasāgarāt ।
duḥkhād duḥkhataraṃ karma mayedaṃ paripacyate ।।

sukhāvāptiṃ na paśyāmi kṣemaṃ vā narakasya me ।
jīvalokādahaṃ bhraṣṭo abuddha iva mārgataḥ ।।

jīvo ayaṃ vivaśo bhūtvā vikṛtaiḥ parivāritaḥ ।
jvālāmālākulaṃ sarvamantarikṣaṃ nirantaram ।।

diśaśca tridiśaścaiva pṛthi ca nirantarā ।
kṛpaṇo ajñānago duḥkhī nivāsaṃ nopalakṣaye ।।

kṣuradhārāvitaptasya nṛpasyāsyātibhīṣaṇam ।
kāntāre bāhyamānasya niḥ sahāyasya sarvataḥ ।
trātāraṃ nāvagacchāmi yo asmād duḥkhāt pramocayet ।।

niḥśaktiravaśo duḥkhī vahninā paritāpitaḥ ।
nīye ahaṃ vivaśaḥ kvāpi bāhubandhanayantritaḥ ।।

na vārthā nāpi mitrāṇi na putrā na ca yoṣitaḥ ।
trāyante vyasanādasmāt kṛtaghnā bata te mama ।।

adharmacāriṇo na kvāpi śaraṇam

nirānandasya na sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ ।
mṛtyupāśena baddhasya śaraṇaṃ nopalakṣyate ।।

saṃkruddhā iva te, krūrā bhaviṣyanti samantataḥ ।
nirānandā diśaḥ sarvā vyālaiśca parivāritā ।।

narakaṃ pātakasyaiva pateyaṃ dhṛtibhāvataḥ ।
yacca yaccehaṃ paśyāmi jaṅgamaṃ sthāvaraṃ tathā ।
tat sarva vyākulaṃ caiva vahninā paridīpitam ।।

nādhigacchāmi śaraṇaṃ niḥsahāyo asmi sarvataḥ ।
ghore tamasi majjāsi sāgare ca hṛtaplavaḥ ।।

gaganaṃ naiva paśyāmi nakṣatragrahatārakam ।
viparītamidaṃ sarva tamasā parivāritam ।।

pañcendriyāṇi sarvāṇi viratāni hi sarvataḥ ।
krakacaistu tadā sarva śarīraṃ paripāṭayate ।।

nādhigacchāmi śaraṇaṃ kāmaṃ bandho bhaviṣyati ।
vardhante duḥkhanikarā sarvataḥ parivārataḥ ।।

muhurmuhuśca vardhante vedanāñcitadehajāḥ ।
duḥkhaiśca nissahāyaṃ ca sarvataḥ ।।

samīkṣya karmajaṃ nityaṃ dhyeyo hetuḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।
kathayanti sukhaṃ vṛddhāḥ svakarmaphalajairdṛḍham ।।

yat pūrva karaṇīyaṃ te tatpaścāt paricintyase ।
mohena vañcitaḥ pūrvaṃ kimadya paritapyase ।
kiṃ punaḥ pāpakartturyaḥ kaṭukaṃ paripacyate ।।

anekaduḥkhahetūtthaṃ tava duḥkhaṃ bhaviṣyati ।
trāṇaṃ naiva yatrāsti vinā karmaparikṣayāt ।।

evaṃ satyasya nāśena yamadūtairanekaśaḥ ।
nīyate narakaṃ ghoraṃ karmapāśavaśaṅgataḥ ।।

catuṣkoṇaścaturdvāro vibhakto bhāgaśo mitaḥ ।
pacyate yatra vivaśā nārakeyā hyanekaśaḥ ।।

bhedaprāyeṇa bahuśo yattvayā kathitaṃ bahu ।
kalmaṣaṃ bhūtadharmāṇāṃ tasyaitat phalamāgatam ।।

paiśunyasevino narakaṃ yānti

bhasmībhavanti te nityaṃ mitrasvajanabāndhavaiḥ ।
eṣāmabhimataṃ duṣṭaṃ paiśunyaṃ sadvigarhitam ।।

tasmānna carito dharmaḥ paiśunyaṃ ca na varjitam ।
paiśunyaṃ saphalaṃ bhuktvā kimadya paritapyase ।।

jihvādhanavinirmuktaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ viṣamamucchritam ।
pāruṣyamiti sandṛṣṭamaho! tatphalamīdṛśam ।।

sattvaṃ pāruṣyaparamaṃ ghoraṃ narakamāgatam ।
jihvāyātaṃ tavākṛtyai kimadya paridevase ।।

sahastraguṇaparyantaḥ svato hṛdayasambhavaḥ ।
kṣutpipāsāmayo vahniḥ samādahati mārutam ।।

paruṣavāco narakasya cāntaram

yadantaraṃ himāgnyorhi merusarṣapayośca yat ।
tadantaraṃ jihvayoktyā narake jvalanasya ca ।।

narakaprabhavo vahnirna kvāpyanyatra prāpyate ।
kṣutpipāsāmayo vahnirdeveṣvapyupalabhyate ।।

yo hyataḥ kāraṇāttīkṣṇo vahnirbhavati nārakaḥ ।
na tathā sa prabhavati yathā vahnistadudbhavaḥ ।।

pūrvottarā baddhapadaṃ nirarthakamasaṅgatam ।
vistrabdha yattvayā proktaṃ tasyaitatphalamāgatam ।।

pareṣāṃ sampadaṃ dṛṣṭvā mama syāditi cintitam ।
tamo abhikhyāsamutthasya viṣasya phalamāgatam ।।

vyāpārānaladagdho asi mānuṣyaṃ puruṣādhama! ।
dahanād dahanaṃ prāpto tapyase ca vikatthyase ।।

vyāpāraparamohe tu narakāyopapattaye ।
rajjvaitayaiva baddho asi puruṣaḥ parikrandase ।।

vyāpādenākṛṣṭo asi ghoraṃ narakamāgataḥ ।
karmakṣayād bhavenmokṣo narakācca vimokṣyase ।।

adharmakathanaṃ dahatyeva

adharmo dharmarūpeṇa sādhurūpeṇa pāpakam ।
yat tvayā kathitaṃ pūrva tat tvāṃ dahati nānalaḥ ।।

kathaṃ tattvavinaṣṭānāṃ dharmādharmanicchatām ।
deśitaṃ vivaraṃ pāpaṃ niyataṃ pāpagāmikam ।।

tvayā varjito dharmaḥ sādhavaścāpi ninditāḥ ।
yattvayopārjitaṃ kṛṣṭaṃ tattvayādya vipacyate ।।

tṛṣṇāviṣayayuktena mohavegena sarvadā ।
yataḥ sadharmavinayaiḥ kiṃ tathā paridevase ।।

sa bhavet pāpakṛnnityaṃ mohapāśavaśaṅgataḥ ।
ki tapyase rodiṣi ca karma kṛtvā sudāruṇam ।।

hetupratyayamūḍhasya dharmādharmeṣu sarvadā ।
prāpto asi narakaṃ ghoraṃ nārakāgraṃ sudāruṇam ।।

kāmavaśānugā narakaṃ yānti

kāmaiḥ kramati saṃyuktairyanna bhavati ceṣṭitam ।
sukṛtaṃ karmavirasaṃ phalametadupasthitam ।।

kṣapayitvā pramādena sukhāsaktena cetasā ।
sukṛta narakaṃ yānti devāḥ kāmavaśānugāḥ ।।

āryāpavādakā narakaṃ yānti

āryāpavādakā ye ca ye ca karmaphaladviṣaḥ ।
te mṛtvā narakaṃ yānti ye ca mithyāvinītakāḥ ।।

dharmavañcakā eva narakagāminaḥ

jananīgṛhapāpīyā ye cānye dharmavañcakāḥ ।
teṣāmiṣṭakarā loke narakasya ca gāminaḥ ।।

pāparatā duḥkhamanubhavanti

ye cānye sukhasaṃsaktā nityaṃ pāparatā narāḥ ।
duḥkhād duḥkhaṃ tu te yānti cittena parivañcitāḥ ।।

avadyakāryāṇi narake pātayanti

tasmādavadyakārye na matiṃ ।
hīnānyavadyakāryāṇi narake pātayanti ca ।।

ataḥ kuśalakarmāṇi karttavyāni

kuryāt kuśalāni nityaṃ parārthabaddhena manorathena ।

। sevyo apavargo daśadharma eṣaḥ ।।

।। iti narakavargaḥ ṣoḍaśaḥ ।।

pretavargaḥ

adānasya kutaḥ sukham?

adāntasya kutaḥ śāntiranuptasya kutaḥ phalam? ।
adīpikā prabhā nāsti adānasya kutaḥ sukham ।।
hṛcchāntirhi tathā nāsti nayanārthasya dehinaḥ ।
dānena virahāt tadvat sukhaṃ pretairna labhyate ।।

kukarmī pretalokaṃ gacchati

yaṃ pretya pretalokasya triloke ca yathādhamāḥ ।
bhrameṇa paramodvignāstanmātsaryakṛtaṃ phalam ।।

na dātrā labhyate kiñcit kṛtanāśo na vidyate ।
svakarmaphalabhoktāraḥ prāṇinaḥ karmabhoginaḥ ।।

tava yatkukṛtaṃ dagdhāḥ pretyalokeṣvavasthitāḥ ।
kṣutpipāsāmayeneha vahninā paridīpitāḥ ।।

kadā tu viṣayo asmākaṃ bhaviṣyati sukhodayaḥ ।
paridāhāt kadā cāsmāt parimokṣo bhaviṣyati ।।

mārgāmārgavihīno duḥkhita eva jīvati

mārgāmārgavivikto ahaṃ na jñātaṃ karmaṇaḥ phalam ।
kṣutpipāsāmayo vahnirajñātaḥ prakaṭodayaḥ ।।

kleśāndhakāravadanā nirāśāstyaktajīvikāḥ ।
tvaksnāyujālabaddhāḥ sma jīvāmo bata duḥkhitāḥ ।।

na trātā sarvato asmākaṃ hanta kṛcchragatā vayam ।
utpanneṣu manuṣyeṣu khaṇḍitāḥ svena karmaṇā ।।

kasmānna carito dharmo ratnadīpeṣu sañcitaḥ ।
yaḥ karoti śubhaṃ nityamaśubhaṃ na ca sarvadā ।।

samadṛṣṭipathenaiti svargasopānamāśritaḥ ।
yeṣāmarthe kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ kleśayan mānasaṃ bahu ।।

anena te gatāḥ sarve bhavānāṃ trāsane sthitaḥ ।
baddho asi bandhanaistīvrairyamadattairadhiṣṭhitaḥ ।।

pāparajjvākṛṣyamāṇaḥ svakṛtaṃ bhunakti

prāpto asi tamaso ghoraṃ yamalokaṃ durāsadam ।
ihopabhokṣyase karma yattvayā kukṛtaṃ kṛtam ।।

svakṛtaṃ bhujyate bāla! pareṣāṃ naiva bhujyate ।
ākṛṣyamāṇa eṣo atra pāparajjvā sughorayā ।।

analaḥ pretalokasya kṣutpipāsāmayo mahān nāgniśastraviṣāṇāṃ hi nipātastādṛśaḥ kaṭuḥ ।।

kṣutpipāsāmayāgneśca nipāto yādṛśaḥ ।
na kṣaṇo nāpi hi lavo na muhūrto na śarvarī ।।

duḥkhānvitā vayam

yatra saukhyaṃ bhavenmṛtyurnityaṃ duḥkhāvṛtā vayam ।
duḥkhād duḥkhataraṃ prāpto duḥkhaheturniṣevitaḥ ।।

duḥkhāt kadācinmokṣaḥ syād bhaviṣyati sukhodayaḥ ।
notsave dṛśyate toyaṃ taḍāgeṣu ca śuṣyati ।।

karmaphalasvarūpanirūpaṇam

sarito nāśamāyāsuḥ kathaṃ dhāvāmahe cayam ।
te vayaṃ śuṣkasalilāḥ saśailavanakānanāḥ ।।
