paridhāvāmahe bhūmau nityaṃ salilakāṃkṣiṇaḥ ।
te vayaṃ dagdhatanavaḥ kṣutpipāsāhatā narāḥ ।।

śaraṇaṃ nādhigacchāmaḥ kaṣṭaṃ vyasanamāgatāḥ ।
vajradaṃṣṭrairmahātīkṣṇaiḥ kākolūkaiśca sammataḥ ।।

abhidruto na paśyāmi śaraṇaṃ saukhyadāyakam ।
pratibimbamidaṃ tasya karmaṇaḥ samupasthitam ।।

kṛtaṃ karma yathāsmābhistathedaṃ phalamāgatam ।
karmavāyuragā baddhāḥ karmasūtreṇa pācitāḥ ।।

karmakṣayādṛte na muktiḥ

palāyanaṃ na paśyāma ṛte karmakṣayāditi ।
yasya pāpānyaniṣṭāni vahnivat tāni paśyati ।।

kīdṛśaṃ pretabhavanam?

sa naiti pretabhavanaṃ kṣutpipāsānalāvṛtam ।
muhurmuhuḥ pravardhante vedanā narakodbhavāḥ ।।

jvālāmālākulasyaiva śailasya sadṛśā vayam ।
jvalitaḥ śāmyate śailaḥ salilenaiva sarvathā ।।

sa samudropamo vahnirammākaṃ naiva śāmyati ।
kasmin kṣaṇe samudbhūtastṛṣṇāvāyusahāyavān ।।

karmāgnirnirdahatyasmān parivāryasamantataḥ ।
te vayaṃ pāpakarmāṇaḥ śukladharmavivarjitāḥ ।।

pretalokamimaṃ prāptāḥ svargasya phalamohitāḥ ।
kṣutpipāsāmayo vahnirdvitīyaścāgnisambhavaḥ ।।

kukarmaṇaiva mudgarāśimayā janāḥ pretabhavanaṃ gacchanti

mudgarāśimayā na putrāḥ na ca bāndhavāḥ ।
vañcito asmi svacittena karmaṇā parivañcitā ।।

prāpto asmi pretabhavanaṃ mitrajñātinirākṛtaḥ ।
na dārāḥ nāpi mitrāṇi na putrāḥ nāpi bāndhavāḥ ।।

kukṛtaphalanirūpaṇam

trāyate karmapāśena nīyamānaṃ balīyasā ।
nānyastrātā yathā karma trividhaṃ bhujyate mayā ।।

dānaṃ śīlaṃ śrutaṃ cāpi trividhaṃ parikīrtitam ।
mohajālavṛteneha yanmayā kukṛtaṃ kṛtam ।।

śubhakarmaṇaiva pretalokāt muktirbhavati

karmaṇo hetubhūtasya yatkṛtaṃ phalamāgatam ।
yadi mucyāmahe pāpāt pretalokād durāsadāt ।।

aśubhāni kukarmāṇi vivarjayet

na bhūyaḥ pāpakaṃ karma kariṣyāmi kathañcana ।
uṣṇānyuṣṇavipākāni mahāpīḍākarāṇi ca ।
kukarmāṇyaśubhānīha tasmāttāni vivarjayet ।।

।। iti pretavargaḥ saptadaśaḥ ।।

tiryagvargaḥ

paradrohaṃ kadāpi na kuryāt

bhakṣaṇaṃ bhavadanyonyavadhabandhāvarodhanam ।
tiryagyoniṃ samāsādya tasmād drohaṃ vivarjayet ।।

mohopahatacittāśca śīladānavivarjitāḥ ।
tiryagyonau va jāyante bālāstṛṣṇāviḍambitāḥ ।।

gamyāgamyaṃ na vindanti bhakṣyābhakṣyaṃ tathaiva ca ।
kāryākāryabahirbhūtā dharmādharmatiraskṛtāḥ ।।

pañcendriyajarāmūḍhāstṛṣṇāpāśavaśānugāḥ ।
krodherṣyāmatisaṃgrastāstiryagyonyupagā narāḥ ।।

paryeṣṭyupahatā martyāḥ pramādopahatāḥ surāḥ ।
kṣuttarṣavyasanāḥ pretāḥ kāraṇātte ca nārakāḥ ।।

ke tiryagyoniparāyaṇāḥ?

parasparabadhātyuktāstiryagyoniparāyaṇāḥ evaṃ bahuvidhaistaistairvyasanairākulaṃ jagat ।।

mātsaryopahato duṣkṛta na kuryāt

na kuryāda duṣkṛtaṃ karma mātsaryopahataḥ param ।
mātsaryopahatā yānti pretāstiryakṣu jantavaḥ ।।

keṣāṃ saphalaṃ janma?

teṣāṃ hi saphalaṃ janma teṣāṃ buddhiravañcitā ।
te ca pūjyāḥ sadā sadbhiryeṣāṃ dharme sadā matiḥ ।।

jñānarathāvarūḍhairmuktirbhavati

evaṃ tridoṣākṛtakarmasāraṃ jagad bhramatyeva durāvagādham ।
karoti yastasya ca śuddhasattvo avamānanāṃ jñānarathāvarūḍhaḥ ।।

।। iti tiryagvargo aṣṭādaśaḥ ।।

kṣadhāvargaḥ

kṣudhāpīḍitā narā aśubhaṃ kurvanti

saṃsāre prāyaśo duḥkhaṃ traidhātukakṣudhāmayam ।
yeneme pīḍitāḥ sattvāḥ kurvantyaśubhamātmanaḥ ।।

svadehe yuktito vahnirbubhukṣetyadhīyate ।
śeṣo dahati lokān vai kalpānala iva drumān ।।

lokottaramimaṃ vahniṃ gacchantamanugacchati ।
nātmanirvāṇasandṛṣṭaṃ kalpāntaraśatairapi ।।

nānalasya hi tadvīrya kṣudhāyā yādṛśaṃ balam ।
traidhātukamidaṃ kṛtsnamāhāraṃ prati vartate ।।

mohayed vividhā cintā loke manujasambhavāḥ ।
tāḥ sarvā bhojanārthāya bhavanti tribhavārṇave ।।

duḥkhamanirvacanīyam

antarābhavasaṃsthasya kṛṣyamāṇasya karmabhiḥ ।
dīrghāgamasya yad duḥkhaṃ na tad varṇayituṃ kṣamam ।।

avidyendhanamagnasya dahyamānasya coṣmaṇā ।
garbhasthasya hi yad duḥkha na tad varṇayituṃ kṣamam ।।

āhārarasagṛddhasya nityaṃ tadgatacetasaḥ ।
yad duḥkhaṃ paragṛddhasya na ca varṇayituṃ kṣamam ।।

dṛḍhā vidagdhamanasaḥ kāme vā taptacetasaḥ ।
yad bhavatyadhikaṃ duḥkhaṃ na tad varṇayituṃ kṣamam ।।

apriyaiḥ saha saṃsargo viṣayāstasya nityaśaḥ ।
praṇaṣṭe hṛdi yad duḥkhaṃ na tad varṇayituṃ kṣamam ।।

tṛṣṇāviṣavidagdhasya nityaṃ paryeṣaṇātmakam ।
āmṛtyu yad bhave duḥkhaṃ na tad varṇayituṃ kṣamam ।।

avyucchinnaṃ bahuvidhaṃ yad duḥkhaṃ pāpamitrajam ।
apāyajanakaṃ yasya na tad varṇayituṃ kṣamam ।।

vyasanaṃ putradārāṇāṃ yad dṛṣṭ hṛdi jāyate ।
narakāṇāṃ mahāmārgo na tad varṇayituṃ kṣamam ।।

kṣutpipāsāvidagdhasya dīpyamānasya vahninā ।
yad duḥkhaṃ naṣṭamanaso na tad varṇayituṃ kṣamam ।।

ajastraṃ paribhūtasya mitrajñātisuhṛjjanaiḥ ।
yad bhavecchokajaṃ duḥkhaṃ na tad varṇayituṃ kṣamam ।।

dārapralambanagataṃ duścalaṃ priyacetasaḥ ।
yad duḥkhaṃ jīrṇakāyasya na tad varṇayituṃ kṣamam ।।

mṛtyunā hriyamāṇasya tasmāṃllokātmano rasāt ।
yad duḥkhaṃ jāyate vṛttau na tad varṇayituṃ kṣamam ।।

dānairaśubhanāśaḥ

yat kurvantyaśubhaṃ bālā yacca gacchati durgatim ।
tadāharati dānena kathayanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।।

ataḥ sukṛteṣu manaḥ kāryam

pratiduṣkṛtakarmāṇi varjanīyāni sarvadā ।
sukṛteṣu manaḥ kārya dānaśīlavibhūṣitam ।।

।। iti kṣudhāvarga ekonaviṃśaḥ ।।

kausīdyavargaḥ

kausīdyena jñānahāniḥ

kausīdyamatimāyā ca dambhaḥ pāruṣyameva ca ।
niyātabhūmayo dṛṣṭā jñānasya ca vivarjanam ।।

saṃśleṣaścāpyasādhūnāṃ sādhūnāṃ varjanaṃ tathā ।
nāśasya hetavaḥ śaktā mithyādarśanameva ca ।।

adeśakālasaṃraṃbho vācyāvācyamajānataḥ ।
anarthabhūmayo hyetā visrambhaścāpi tanmayaḥ ।।

anarthabhūmayaḥ

yena tena ca samprītiḥ yatra tatra ca bhojanam ।
lāghavaṃ janayatyante apraśaṃsā cātmanastathā ।।

dhairyanāśaḥ smṛtibhraṃśo virodhaḥ pārthivena ca ।
akrāntamṛtyavo hyete krūratā manasi sthitā ।।

akarmāphalatattvajño dharmādharmavahiṣkṛtaḥ ।
puruṣaḥ sādhunirmuktaḥ prapātagamanāśayaḥ ।।

kausīdyamatinidrā ca rasanā gṛhyate tathā ।
puṃdveṣayonayaḥ proktāḥ pāruṣyavacanaṃ tathā ।।

lobho apamānasya kāraṇam

atilobho apamānaśca atimānaśca cāpalam ।
dharmavarjyā kāmasevā mohasya paridīpikāḥ ।।

doṣāṇāṃ mūlaṃ kausīdyam

trayāṇāmiha doṣāṇāṃ kausīdyaṃ mūlamucyate ।
vīryārambheṇa duṣyante doṣā manasi sambhavāḥ ।।

vīryārambheṇa hi phalaṃ hyavaśyamupabhujyate ।
nyāyenārabdhatattvasya karmaṇo dṛśyate phalam ।।

karmaṇastrividhasyāsya phalaṃ trividhamucyate ।
trirāśiniyataṃ tacca triśūlaṃ tribhavānugam ।।

kausīdyasevino durgatiḥ

pāpasevī pracaṇḍo yaḥ kausīdyamapi sevate ।
dharmavidveṣakaḥ krūro anutpathānupadhāvati ।।

yasya tasya ca santuṣṭo yasya tasya prakupyati ।
yatra tatra ca saṃsakto sa mūḍha iti kathyate ।।

kausīdyaṃ svamanasaḥ pramādaviṣamūrcchitam ।
prapātaṃ taṃ ca saṃrabdhamavisaṃvādakaṃ param ।।

vīryārambhe mahāpāpakausīdyamalavarjitāḥ ।
vimukterupabhoktāraste janāḥ sukhabhāginaḥ ।।

kausīdyaṃ sarvadharmāṇāmajarāmarakārakam ।
tena doṣeṇa mahatā narā duḥkhasya bhāginaḥ ।।

sahāyaśca sukhāveśī tasmāt tat parivarjayet ।
tena viddho hi puruṣaḥ svadhistutyaḥ samantataḥ ।।

kusīdasyālpabhāgasya mohāpahṛtacetasaḥ ।
kutsitaḥ svajanaiḥ sarvairna gatirvidyate śivā ।।

kausīdyarataḥ pāpībhavati

kausīdyapāpasaṃsargīstyānamiddhaṃ tathaiva ca ।
mokṣadvāravighātāya bhavantyete mahābhayāḥ ।।

duḥkhasyaitāni harmyāṇi

āhrīkyamanapatrāpyamauddhatyaṃ pāpamitratā ।
duḥkhasyaitāni harmyāṇi tebhyo rakṣennu paṇḍitaḥ ।।
kausīdyenābhibhūtā ye nirārambhā gatitviṣaḥ ।
socchvāsamaraṇaṃ teṣāṃ jīvitaṃ cāpi niṣphalam ।।

jīvamānā na jīvanti kausīdyopahatā narāḥ ।
mṛtyoratyadhikaṃ hyetat kausīdyamiti manyate ।।

ārabdhavīryā eva bhavasāgaraṃ taranti

kausīdyapaṅkamagnā ye magnāste duḥkhasaṃstare ।
ārabdhavīryā ye puṃsaste tīrṇā bhavasāgarāt ।।

kausīdyānmandavīryo yaḥ sadā pāparataśca yaḥ ।
sa jīvamāno api mṛto mṛtastu narakāya saḥ ।।

mānavānāṃ nirdhanatve kausīdyaṃ kāraṇam

nirdhanāḥ paśubhistulyāste narā duḥkhabhāginaḥ ।
parapiṇḍāśino dīnāḥ kausīdyaṃ tatra kāraṇam ।।

prāyaśastu kusīdānāṃ paradāropajīvinām ।
ratābhilāṣo atyadhiko maithune ca sadā ratiḥ ।।

te tattvakārikā riktāḥ kevalāhāratatparāḥ ।
mṛtyukāle samutpanne dahyante svena cetasā ।।

śītoṣṇaṃ ca sahantyete kṣutpipāse tathaiva ca ।
gātrāntā ca kriyā kāryā yātrā dharmāya sarvadā ।।

ataḥ kausīdye na matiḥ kāryā

na kausīdye matiṃ kuryāt kuśīle śīlakāmukaḥ ।
saṃsāre sīdati nityaṃ na ca duḥkhāt pramucyate ।।

kudīdānvitaḥ lokavañcito bhavati

paribhūya satāṃ madhye kusīdāllokavañcitaḥ ।
vañcitaśca bhavatyante śarmaṇo vā vimucyate ।।

dharmeṇa vimuktirbhavati

vīryavān smṛtisaṃlabdha ekāntanirataḥ sadā ।
vimuktapāpakaidharmairmokṣaṃ prāpnoti yatnataḥ ।।

kukarmeṣu matiḥ na kāryā

evaṃvidhā duḥkhaparamparā hi, sattvaḥ kukarmeṣu na kuryāt ।
loke tridoṣānalasampradīpte, kuryāt parāṃ śāntikṛpā mṛte na ।।

।। iti kausīdyavargo viṃśaḥ ।।

cittañca vāk tathā karma saṃyojanantu pāpakam ।
narakapretatiryakkṣutkausīdyāni vidurdaśa ।।

।। iti dvitīyam udānam ।।

atha tṛtīyam udānam

(karuṇādānaśīlāni kṣāntirvīryamathāpi ca ।
dhyānaṃ prajñātha nirvāṇo mano bhikṣuśca te daśa ।। )

karuṇāvargaḥ

karuṇā māteva hitakāriṇī bhavati

kṛpā sarveṣu bhūteṣu māteva hitakāriṇī ।
yāṃ samāśritya puruṣāḥ prayānti sukhamuttamam ।।

dayānveṣīha puruṣaḥ sarvasattvahite rataḥ ।
pūjanīyaḥ satāṃ yāti pretya svarge ca modate ।।

dayāvantaḥ sadāvarta sarvabhūtahite ratam ।
tamevaṃ puruṣaṃ nityaṃ praṇamanti divaukasaḥ ।।

karuṇānvito devalokaṃ gacchati

prayāti devalokaṃ ca śīlavān karuṇānvitaḥ ।
kṛpānvitaḥ sa puruṣo candramā iva śobhate ।।

sukhārthinā karuṇā sevitavyā

āśrayanti ca bhūtāni gataśokā gatavyathā ।
tasmād dayāprayatnena sevitavyā sukhārthinā ।।

kāruṇyena yaśavṛddhirbhavati

yasya vāk kāyacitte kāruṇyena vibhūṣite ।
tasya mitramayā lokā bhavanti yaśasā vṛtāḥ ।।

kāruṇyārdrasya viduṣo nirvāṇaṃ yāti

kāruṇyārdrasya viduṣo nityaṃ mṛdvindriyasya ca ।
samyagdṛṣṭiprayatnasya nirvāṇaṃ nāti dūrataḥ ।।

kāruṇyavibhūṣitā manuṣyalokaṃ devavad bhūṣayanti

manuṣyaloke te devā ye kāruṇyena vibhūṣitāḥ ।
kāruṇyena daridrā ye te daridrāḥ satāṃ matāḥ ।।

mṛdvāśayā martyāḥ sādhavaḥ

mṛdvāśayā hi ye martyāḥ sādhuvat kāñcanopamāḥ ।
kāruṇyamakṣayaṃ yeṣāṃ sadā manasi vartate ।।

ke dharmaparāyaṇā bhavanti?

te ca sattvāḥ sadodyuktā nityaṃ dharmaparāyaṇāḥ ।
yeṣāṃ kāruṇyadīpena hṛdayaṃ samprakāśitam ।।

na rātrau na divā teṣāṃ dharmo hi vinivartate ।
yeṣāṃ sarvāsvavasthāsu karuṇābhirataṃ matam ।।

kāruṇyaṃ śītalaṃ cittam

kāruṇyaśītalaṃ cittaṃ sarvasattvahite ratam ।
bhuktvā saukhyaṃ nirupamaṃ paścād gacchati nirvṛtim ।।

kāruṇyamavināśi dhanam

kāruṇyaṃ munibhiḥ śastaṃ kāruṇyaṃ nirmalaṃ saraḥ ।
kāruṇyaṃ doṣanirghāti kāruṇyaṃ dhanamavyayam ।।

guṇānāṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ cāgraṃ sarvadoṣavighātakam ।
kāruṇyārdrā hi paramaṃ prayānti dhanamacyutam ।।

kāruṇyaṃ dhanaṃ yasmānmādhuryapayasā yutam ।
na dāhaḥ krodhajastasya hṛdaye sampravartate ।।

kāruṇyanāvamāruhya janā bhavasāgaraṃ taranti

kāruṇyanāvamāruhya prītirdhairyaparāyaṇaḥ ।
tridoṣormimahāvege bhrāmyate bhavasāgare ।।

karuṇāyāḥ paribhāṣā

guṇānāmadvayaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ vinā cittena bhūṣaṇam ।
sādhūnāṃ dayitaṃ nityaṃ kāruṇyamiti kathyate ।।

mārdavaṃ yasya hṛdaye vilīnamiva kāñcanam ।
sa jano hi tu kalpānte duḥkhādāśu vimucyate ।।

dayāloḥ śreyāṃsi rohanti

yasya pātrīkṛtaṃ cittaṃ mārdaveṇa samantataḥ ।
śreyāṃsi tasya rohanti kedāra iva śālayaḥ ।।

cetogṛhe nidhānaṃ tadavyayaṃ dehinaḥ ।
nirvāsayati dāridrayaṃ nṛṇāmadhyāśayaṃ mahat ।।

tīkṣṇendriyasyāśāntasya nidhyānasya vicāriṇaḥ ।
viṣayeṣu pramattasya duḥkhaṃ naiva pradhāvati ।।

maitreṇa cetasā nityamanukampādayā parāḥ ।
te hetuphalatattvajñā duḥkhapāśād vinirgatāḥ ।।

na saṅkalpe mano yeṣāṃ ramate doṣavarjitam ।
te doṣabhayanirmuktāḥ padaṃ gacchantyanuttaram ।।

kṣāntikriyāsamāyukte mitravānakutobhayaḥ ।
priyo bhavati loke asmin paścād deveṣu modate ।।

dayāratnaṃ sadā sevyam

mātṛvat pitṛvaccaiva sarvalokasya te janāḥ ।
dayāratnaṃ sadā yeṣāṃ manasi sthitamuttamam ।।

kṛpaiva sukhasya mūlamasti

sukhasya ca paraṃ mūlaṃ kṛpaiva parikīrtitā ।
yasya kṛpā nāsti sa duḥkhī parikīrtyate ।।

maitrī eva sukhāvahā

ekasatyottaraṃ brahma ekasyānuttaraṃ śivam ।
ekavidyā paraṃ mātā maitrī caikā sukhāvahā ।।

ahiṃsakā eva dhanyāḥ

ahiṃsakāḥ sadā dhanyāḥ saddṛṣṭiḥ paramā śubhā ।
etad ṛju sadā satyaṃ pāpānāṃ cāpi varjanam ।।

karuṇāyā māhātmyam

karttavyaḥ puruṣaistasmāt kṛpāsaṃvegamānasaiḥ ।
dānaśīlakṣamāmaitrījñānābhyāsaśca nirmalaḥ ।।

।। iti karuṇāvarga ekaviṃśaḥ ।।

dānavargaḥ

śuddhāśuddhadānaparibhāṣā

guṇadvādaśasaṃyuktaṃ malairdvādaśabhirvinā ।
dānaṃ bhavati śuddhaṃ tad viparītaṃ sakalmaṣam ।।

dānarahitā eva puruṣādhamāḥ

devānāmatha nṛṇāṃ dhanasya balamuttamam ।
dānena rahitā pāde patanti puruṣādhamāḥ ।।

lobhamātsaryamalināḥ putradāravaśānugāḥ ।
manujā nidhanaṃ yānti kevalāhārakāṃkṣiṇaḥ ।।

lobhagranthivimokṣāya yāñcāvṛkṣakṣayāya ca ।
tamonicayanāśāya pradānamiha dīyate ।।

dātā paralokaṃ gacchati

aghatāṃ carate dānaṃ dātāpi tadanantaram ।
mārgasandarśavad dānaṃ paralokaṃ samṛcchati ।।

dānāmbhasi narāḥ snātvā śīlormiparibhāvite ।
jñānavistīrṇa pāraṃ duḥkhasya yānti vai ।।

doṣanāśakāḥ trayo dīpāḥ

puruṣeṇa trayo dīpāḥ prajvālyā hitamicchatā ।
dānaṃ śīlaṃ tathā jñānamete doṣavināśakāḥ ।।

tṛṣṇāvivarṇā durgandhivitarkormijhaṣākule ।
duḥkhārṇave plutā hyete jñānaśīleṣu rakṣitāḥ ।।

kleśasya bheṣajaṃ dānaṃ, śīlaṃ, jñānam

kleśavyādhinihantārastrayo vai bheṣajāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
dānaṃ śīlaṃ tathā jñānamete nityaṃ sukhāvahāḥ ।।

pramādaviṣamaṃ saṃkalpakuṭilaṃ laghu ।
vadhyate bandhanairetaistribhirjñānādibhirnṛṇām ।।

doṣāgnibhiḥ pluṣṭo yairidaṃ dahyate tadā ।
dānādijñānayogena hatvā gacchati nirvṛtim ।।

na dānajñāna śīleṣu yeṣāṃ sammiśritā matiḥ ।
te nityaduḥkhitāḥ sattvāḥ sukhaṃ teṣāṃ na vidyate ।।

dātāro mātsaryamalavarjitā bhavanti

adānavrīḍitasukhāścittadoṣeṇa vañcitāḥ ।
bhavanti vibudhāḥ hitvā tasmād dānaparo bhavet ।।

dānotkarṣakramairyuktāḥ mātsaryamalavarjitāḥ ।
bhavanti hṛṣṭamanaso devāḥ krīḍāparāyaṇāḥ ।।

kṣutpipāsāmayo vahnirya pradhānaṃ pradhāvati ।
mātsarya vai phalaṃ sarva taduktaṃ tattvabuddhibhiḥ ।।

dānapraśaṃsā

yo dadāti sukhaṃ tasya nīyate jāyate sukham ।
sukhaṃ bhavati dānāddhi tasmād dānaṃ praśasyate ।।

lokālokakaraṃ dānaṃ gacchantamanugacchati ।
gataṃ ca mantradānena yujyate bhadravatsalaiḥ ।।

avisaṃvādakaṃ sthānametaduktaṃ tathāgataiḥ ।
avisaṃvādakatvācca nityaṃ dānaparo bhavet ।।

dānī bhavārṇavaṃ tarati

mātsaryāriṃ vinirjitya kṛtvā cittaṃ śubhānvitam ।
ye prayacchanti dānāni te taranti bhavārṇavam ।।

kṣayaistu trividhairdānaṃ triṣukāraṃ tridhārjitam ।
tasya kṣatānvitasyaivaṃ phalaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tricakṣuṣā ।।

kaḥ mārgaḥ sukhāvahaḥ?

dānamādau sadā deyaṃ śīlaṃ labhyaṃ prayatnataḥ ।
tṛṣṇā jñānena hantavyā mārga eṣa sukhāvahaḥ ।।

anityā pāpikā tṛṣṇā lokasyāhitakārikā ।
na śakyaṃ tadvinā śreyaḥ prāptuṃ padamanuttamam ।।

adānasya pariṇāmaḥ

adāne na manaḥ kārya nityaṃ dānarato bhavet ।
adānāt kṣutpipāsābhyāṃ dahyate pretabhūmiṣu ।।

dānena śīlarakṣā sadā kāryā

rājā bhavati dānena cakravartī sudhārmikaḥ ।
dānabhūmiṃ samāśritya śīlaṃ rakṣanti paṇḍitāḥ ।।

śīlavānapi kālajño ajñānād parimucyate ।
duḥkhanairyāṇiko mārgaḥ śasto ayaṃ munipuṃgavaiḥ ।।

taṃ viditvā mahāvīro nityaṃ dānarato bhavet ।
adā dapi deveṣu devā hi na sukhā matāḥ ।।

dānī yatra kutrāpi vasan sukhī bhavati

ājanmavipine martyā bhavanti sukhabhāginaḥ ।
dānasya tatphalaṃ sarvacetanābhāvitasya hi ।।

tiryakṣvapi samutpannā bhavanti sukhabhāginaḥ ।
tatsarva dānajaṃ saukhyaṃ kathayanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।।

yat pretāḥ pretabhavane bhavatyākārabhojinaḥ ।
svayaṃ kṛtasya dānasya phalaṃ bhavati tādṛśam ।।

dānavirahitasya durdaśā bhavati

dadyāt kṣutpipāse ca dahyante yena dehinaḥ ।
sarvadā na tapastābhyāṃ phalaṃ bhavati śītalam ।।

pramādī mṛtyusamaye dāhaṃ prāpnoti

pūrva pramādacārī yo na dānādiṣu vartate ।
sa paścānmṛtyusamaye dahyate svena cetasā ।।

dānasya phalam

priyo bhavati dānena cetasāmapi tuṣyati ।
paścād bhavati sa śrīmān dānasya phalamīdṛśam ।।

yatra dānādi cittasyāstyupabhogāya sarvadā ।
tatra nirdhanataiṣā vā dayayā parirakṣitam ।।

yad bhujyate sadā cittaṃ gurubhyaścāpi dīyate ।
yad vanaṃ śobhanaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ viparītaṃ yathā tṛṇam ।।

durbalānāṃ sadārtānāṃ sattvānāṃ cakṣuranvitam ।
dānaṃ niḥkalpasaṃyantramasmiṃlloke paratra ca ।।

manuṣyabhūmau dānasya phalam

manuṣyabhūmau dānāni dattvā yānti śubhāṃ gatim ।
na devā dānapatayaḥ phalabhūmirasau matā ।।

karmamāhātmyam

karmabhūmirmanuṣyāṇāṃ phalabhūmiḥ surālayaḥ ।
karmāyattaṃ phalaṃ sarva na phalaṃ syādahetukam ।।

ko mṛtaiḥ samaḥ?

dhyānādhyayananirmukto dānaśīlavivarjitaḥ ।
suvarṇakaṃkaṇairyukto jīvannapi mṛtaiḥ samaḥ ।।

sa jīvati hi loke asmin yo dharmamanuvartate ।
dharmamūḍhaḥ sadā mūḍho jīvannapi mṛtaiḥ samaḥ ।।

ajñānī tu bāliśa eva

manuṣyacarmaṇā channastiryag bhavati bāliśaḥ ।
yasya jñānapradīpena hṛdayaṃ nāvabhāsitam ।।

bhavatyetāvatā puruṣaḥ yaḥ śīlamanuvartate ।
śīlabhraṣṭaḥ pumān sarvaścābhistutyo aparākramaḥ ।।

dānahīnaḥ pretavigrahavān

dānahīnaḥ pramādī pāpacārī calendriyaḥ ।
nāsau martya iti jñeyaḥ preto vigrahavānayam ।।

jñānena hīno mṛta eva

jñānaśīlavinirmukto dānaratnavivarjitaḥ ।
jīvamāno api puruṣo mṛta ityabhidhīyate ।।

ko devaḥ?

dānaśīlatapodhyānād vīryasmṛtisamādhimān ।
puruṣaḥ puruṣaireje devairapi sa vandyate ।।

guṇavāṃstu naro vandyaḥ nirguṇaḥ paśubhiḥ samaḥ ।
guṇāguṇavidhijño yaḥ sa deva iti kathyate ।।

keṣāṃ saphalaṃ jīvanam?

sujīvitaṃ bhavettasya yasya tyāge sthitaṃ manaḥ ।
nahi tyāgavinirmuktaṃ jīvitaṃ jīvanaṃ matam ।।

dānaṃ nityaṃ sukhāvaham

pañcagatyupapannānāṃ sattvānāṃ svena karmaṇā ।
mātṛvat pitṛvad dṛṣṭaṃ dānaṃ nityaṃ sukhāvaham ।।

dānaratā bhavasaṅkaṭānmucyante

etāṃ bhūmimavasthāpya sattvo dānarato bhavet ।
dānaśīlaratā nityaṃ mucyante bhavasaṅkaṭāt ।।

।। iti dānavargo dvāviṃśaḥ ।।

śīlavargaḥ

śīlaṃ sūrya iva śobhate

dhanānāmuttamaṃ śīlaṃ sūryo jyotiṣmatāmiva ।
vihāya gacchati dhanaṃ śīlaṃ sthitamivāgrataḥ ।।

śīlena tridaśān yāti dhyānagocarameva vā ।
nāsti śīlasamaṃ jyotirasmiṃlloke paratra ca ।।

alpena hetunā svarga prāpnoti svargakāmikaḥ ।
tasmād duścaritaṃ hitvā nityaṃ sucarito bhavet ।।

cetanābhāvitaṃ dānaṃ śīlaṃ ca parirakṣitam ।
nīyate devasandattaṃ pañcakāmaguṇānvitam ।।

surakṣitena śīlenaiva sukhaṃ prāptuṃ śakyate

na mātā na pitā nārthā dayitā nāpi bāndhavāḥ ।
na sukhā tathā dṛṣṭā yathā śīlaṃ surakṣitam ।।

śīlavān puruṣo sukhamavāpnute

śīlaṃ trāṇamihāmutra śīlaṃ gatirihottamam ।
śīlavān puruṣo nityaṃ sukhāt sukhamavāpnute ।।

dānaśīlasamācārā ye narā śubhacāriṇaḥ ।
te yānti devasadanaṃ racitāḥ svena karmaṇā ।।

nidhānamavyayaṃ śīlaṃ śīlasaukhyamatarkitam ।
śīlādhikā hi puruṣā nityaṃ sukhavihāriṇaḥ ।।

śīlaṃ rakṣatu medhāvī yathā yānaṃ sukhatrayam ।
praśaṃsāvṛttalābhaṃ ca pretya svarge ca modate ।।

śīlavān nirvāṇaṃ prāpnoti

śīlavān yo hi puruṣaḥ śīlamevāti sevate ।
sasukho nirvṛttiṃ yāti yatra mṛtyurna vidyate ।।

anādimati saṃsāre tṛṣṇāmohādibhirvṛte ।
jyotirbhūta sadāśīlaṃ tasmācchīlamanāvilam ।।

śīlaṃ dhanamasaṃhārya rājacaurodakādibhiḥ ।
tasmācchīlaṃ sadā sevyaṃ dauḥśīlyaṃ ca vigarhitam ।।

śīlābhiratapuruṣaḥ nirvāṇaṃ hyantike sthitam ।
śīlavān puruṣo dhanyaḥ śīlavāṃścāpi sevyate ।।

ravivad bhrājate śīlaṃ dauḥśīlyaṃ caiva garhitam ।
nirmalaṃ vītakāntāraṃ nirjvaraṃ vītakāṅkṣi ca ।।

śīlapraśastasambuddhairnirvāṇapuragāmikam ।
āyuryāti dhruvaṃ dhīmān nityaṃ śīlenaṃ vṛṃhitam ।।

śīlarahitāḥ paśubhiḥ samāḥ

na bibhenmṛtyukāle ca śīlena parirakṣitaḥ ।
śīlamādyantakalyāṇaṃ sarvasaukhyapravartakam ।
śīlavān puruṣo dhanyo dauḥśīlyābhirataḥ paśuḥ ।।

tīraṃ naiva samāyānti puruṣāḥ śīlavarjitāḥ ।
kāryākārya na vindanti tasmācchīlaṃ samācaret ।।

śīlavastreṇa ye channāste channāḥ puruṣā matāḥ ।
śīlena varjitā ye tu nagnāste paśubhiḥ samāḥ ।।

śīlavān puruṣaḥ svarga gacchati

śīlavān puruṣaḥ svagamudyānamiva gacchati ।
bandhuvanmanyate tatra śīlavān pramāgataḥ ।।

śuciśīlasamācārāḥ śubhadharmasamanvitāḥ ।
devalokopagāsteṣu janāḥ sukṛtakāriṇaḥ ।।

śīlena paribṛṃhitā guṇā vardhante

yo na prārthayate kāmān śīlavān puruṣaḥ sadā ।
guṇāstasya pravardhante śīlena paribṛṃhitāḥ ।।

śīlaṃ svargasya sopānam

mahārghamuttamaṃ śīlamasmiṃlloke paratra ca ।
tasmāt prahāya traiguṇyaṃ śīlameva sadā caret ।।

devebhyo rocate taddhi trāṇaṃ śīlaṃ śubhānvitam ।
bhāvitaṃ paramaṃ dhanyaṃ paralokopagāmikam ।।
śīlavān yadi jānīyāt phalaṃ śīlasya yādṛśam ।।
śastraṃ sutīkṣṇamādāya vāṇaṃ chindyādihātmanaḥ ।
astropamasya nindyasya abhisaukhyasamanvitam ।।

śīlasya phalaṃ sugatena pradarśitam

phalaṃ śīlasya vimalaṃ sugatena pradarśitam ।
ādau śastaṃ tathā madhye nidhane śastameva tat ।।

phalaṃ śīlasya vipulaṃ sukhāt sukhamuttamam ।
śīlacaryā paraṃ saukhyaṃ dhanacaryā na tādṛśī ।।

narā dhanena hīyante śīlena na kathañcana ।
śocate puruṣastena pṛthak vā tadvirājate ।।

śubhaṃ tasmānmunivaraiḥ praśastaṃ sārvagāmikam ।
udyānamiva gacchanti puruṣāḥ śubhacāriṇaḥ ।
devalokasamaṃ teṣāṃ saukhyānāmākaraṃ ।।

svargagamanārtha śīlaṃ samācaret

suśīlitasya śīlasya bhakṣitasyāpyanekaśaḥ ।
phalaṃ vipacyate svargastasmācchīlaṃ samācaret ।।

śīlaṃ svargasya sopānamākaraṃ sukhanirvṛte ।
śīlavarjī hi puruṣo na kvacit sukhamedhate ।।

śīlavān asaṃkhyāni saukhyāni labhate

śīlāmbhasā prasannena viprakīrṇena sarvadā ।
snātvā gacchanti puruṣā devaloke ca nirvṛte ।
yaddivyamālyābharaṇairdivyaiḥ saukhyaiḥ samanvitāḥ ।।

ramate devabhavane tat sarva śubhahetukam ।
asaṃkhyāni ca saukhyāni vardhamānāni sarvadā ।।

labhate puruṣaḥ sarva yaḥ śīlamanuvartate ।
śubhacārī sadā satyaḥ pūjyate so aparājitaḥ ।।

anekasaukhyadāyakaṃ śīlamācaraṇīyam

śubhena śobhate martyaḥ pūjyate rājabhiḥ sadā ।
śubhena śobhate martyastasmācchīlaṃ samācaret ।।

anekasaukhyajanakaṃ sarvamāśvāsakārakam ।
śīlaṃ sucaritaṃ kārya duṣkṛtaṃ ca vivarjayet ।।

ye dānaśīlakarttāraḥ svargatadgatamānasāḥ ।
teṣāṃ sakalmaṣaṃ śīlaṃ viṣamiśraṃ yathaudanam ।।

nānāvidhasya śīlasya rakṣitasyāpyanekaśaḥ ।
śubhakāryavipākāya deveṣu paripacyate ।।

śīlāmbhasā prasanneṣu saṅkīrṇeṣu ca sarvadā ।
snātvā gacchanti manujā devāṃścātyantikaṃ sukham ।।

dānaśīlāḥ sadā dāntāḥ sarvabhūtahite ratāḥ ।
jñānayuktā maitracitā gatāste devasammitim ।।

hatadoṣāḥ kriyāvantaḥ śīlaratnena bhūṣitāḥ ।
sarvasattvadayāvantaḥ suralokeṣu te budhāḥ ।।

viśuddhakāñcanaprakhyā nirdhmātamalakalmaṣāḥ ।
samyak karma susaṃlagnā devalokeṣu te budhāḥ ।।

sarvasattvadayāvantaḥ sarvasattvahitaiṣiṇaḥ ।
sarvapāpaviraktā ye teṣāṃ vāsaḥ surālaye ।।

ahanyahani ye śīlaṃ rakṣanti suparīkṣakāḥ ।
ahanyahani teṣāṃ hi sukhaṃ bhavati naikaśaḥ ।।

śīlavājinamārūḍhā devabhavanaṃ prayānti

śīlavājinamārūḍhāḥ puruṣāstattvacintakāḥ ।
prayānti devabhavanaṃ krīḍāyuktamanekaśaḥ ।।

yā krīḍā devabhavane yacca saukhyamanuttamam ।
tat samagrasya śīlasya phalamuktaṃ tathāgataiḥ ।।

devasukhaṃ śīlajameva

yaddivyamālyābharaṇā divyāmbaravibhūṣitāḥ ।
krīḍanti vibudhāḥ sarve tatsarva śubhahetukam ।।

padmotpalavane ramye vanopavanabhūṣite ।
svarge ramanti ye devāstat sarva śubhajaṃ phalam ।।

yadākāśa ivātasthurdivyaratnavibhūṣitāḥ ।
virājante amalā devāstacchīlasya mahat phalam ।।

yatkānaneṣu ramyeṣu citreṣu puṣpiteṣu ca ।
ramanti giripṛṣṭheṣu surāstacchīlajaṃ phalam ।।

svagṛhaṃ hi yathā martyāḥ praviśanti gatavyathāḥ ।
tathā śīlasamācārāḥ prayānti tridivaṃ narāḥ ।।

etat sujīvitaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ yacchīlaparirakṣaṇam ।
maraṇānāṃ paraṃ mṛtyuḥ yacchīlaparivarjanam ।।

śīlamanupamaṃ kāryam

etān guṇān sadā matvā priyatvamapi cātmanaḥ ।
śīlaṃ surakṣitaṃ kārya dauḥśīlyaṃ ca vivarjayet ।।

śīlacārī sadā dāntaḥ kṣamāvāṃśca sudarśanaḥ ।
sopānamiva cārūḍhaṃ prayātyānandasannidhim ।।

śīlena plavabhūtena saṃsārottaraṇam

phalaṃ śīlasya tu sukhaṃ devalokeṣu pacyate ।
śīlena plavabhūtena saṃsārāduttaranti ca ।।

śīlāmbhasā viśuddhā ye svāyattā dhīracetasaḥ ।
jāmbūnadamayaiḥ puṣpaiste atrārcanti divaukasaḥ ।।

ye navādātamanaso nityaṃ śīlena bhūṣitāḥ ।
te yānti devasadanaṃ yatra saukhyamanantakam ।।

saukhyāt saukhyataraṃ yānti narāḥ sukṛtakāriṇaḥ ।
krīḍanti devasadane śīlena paribṛṃhitāḥ ।।

śīlasopānamārūḍhāḥ sugatiṃ prayānti

śīlasopānamāruhya jñānena paribṛṃhitāḥ ।
narāḥ prayānti sugatiṃ jñānena ca parāyaṇā ।।

suprasannena manasāśīlaṃ yadabhirakṣitam ।
tasya śīlasya śītasva sukhametadupasthitam ।।

śīlasya pariṇāmo sukhadāyakaḥ

surakṣitasya śīlasya bhāvitasyāpyanekaśaḥ ।
pariṇāme sukhībhūtvā nirvāṇaṃ cādhigacchati ।।

śīlaṃ rakṣatyupāyena śīlaṃ nayati saṅgatim ।
tasmācchīlaṃ sadā rakṣyaṃ pariṇāmo asya śītalaḥ ।।
mṛtyukāle samutpanne śīlavānakutobhayaḥ ।
na me durgatinā trāṇaṃ śīlaṃ hi trāṇamuttamam ।।

kutsitaśīlasya kutsitaḥ pariṇāmaḥ

kācābhrapaṭalaṃ yasya śīlaṃ bhavati kutsitam ।
sa kutsitena śīlena kutsito jāyate naraḥ ।।

śīlavirahitaḥ mūḍho bhavati svargamapi na yāti

śīlamūlena labdhvedaṃ sukhaṃ svargeṣu dehibhiḥ ।
tṛṣṇākṣayo na bhavati sa paścāt paritapyate ।।

tasmācchīlavatā nityaṃ śīlameva viśiṣyate ।
niḥśīlaḥ puruṣo mūḍho na svargamadhirohati ।।

pañcakāmopamaṃ divyaṃ yadidaṃ bhujyate sukham ।
tacchīlasya viśuddhasya prāpyate hi phalaṃ mahat ।।

yattejaḥ kāñcanasyāsya meruparvataśālinaḥ ।
tacchīlatejasastejaḥ kalāṃ nārhati ṣoḍaśīm ।।

dīpyamānaiḥ sadā śīlaiḥ nirdhātukanakatviṣā ।
saṃyuktāstridivaṃ yānti paṇḍitā svena karmaṇā ।।

trividhaśīlasya trividhaṃ phalam

hīnamadhyaviśiṣṭasya śīlasya trividhasya vai ।
phalaṃ hi trividhaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ hīnamadhyottamaṃ tathā ।।

pramādarahitaṃ śīlamapramādopabṛṃhitam ।
nityaṃ tat sukhadaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ dharmateyaṃ vyavasthitā ।।

śīlaprabhayā sūryasahastrasyādi parābhavaḥ

śīlodbhavā yā vimalā prabhā bhavati dehinām ।
na sā sūryasahastrasya saṃyuktasya bhaviṣyati ।।

śīlaṃ saptavidhaṃ ramyaṃ yo rakṣati narottamaḥ ।
sa kāmaṃ bhuñjati phalaṃ sugatena ca deśitam ।।

śīlacaryā vinā svarga na yānti

śīlacaryā samāśritya samyagdarśanatatparaḥ ।
martyalokād divaṃ yānti na kaṣṭaṃ tapacāriṇaḥ ।।

yacchīlaṃ śīlasaṃsparśa pariṇāme api śītalam ।
niṣevate sadāmūḍhaḥ sa paścāt paritapyate ।।

saptavidhena śīlena devasānnidhyaṃ prāpyate

śīlaṃ saptavidhaṃ dhanyamavisaṃvādakaṃ padam ।
śīlena rakṣitaḥ puruṣo devānāmantikaṃ gataḥ ।।

śīlena śobhanaṃ phalaṃ milati

yathā pakṣairdṛḍhaiḥ pakṣī svedacchatraṃ nihanti ।
tathā naro dṛḍhaḥ śīlairdevalokāya kalpyate ।।

śrutimātraṃ ca ramyād ramyataraṃ ca tat ।
labhate puruṣaḥ kartā phalaṃ śīlasya śobhanam ।।

dānaśīlataporatnaṃ hṛdayaiśca samāśritam ।
devatā vā manuṣyo vā labhate paramaṃ padam ।।

antarbahiśca niḥsārāḥ puruṣā dharmavarjitāḥ ।
saṃsārāt phalakāṅkṣibhyaḥ saddharmo na rocate ।।

antarbahiśca ye sārāste narā vastuto dṛḍhāḥ ।
ye dharmacāriṇaḥ śāntāḥ parasattvahitaiṣiṇaḥ ।।

anuttaraḥ śīlavatāṃ sugandhaḥ

na ketakī campakapuṣpagandhā, tamālake nāgarucaśca gandhaḥ ।
prayānti gandhā hiṃ yathā sureṇa, anuttaraḥ śīlavatāṃ sugandhaḥ ।।

dauḥśīlyaṃ sadā varjyam

tasmācchīlaṃ sadā kārya dānajñānatapodhanaiḥ ।
dauḥśīlyaṃ ca sadā varjyaviṣaśastrānalopanam ।।

śīlena eva sukhamavāpnute

evaṃ surakṣitaṃ śīlaṃ narān nayati saṅgatim ।
na hi śīlādṛte kaścit padaṃ sukhamavāpnute ।।

devaguṇasadṛśaṃ śīlaṃ sadācaret

tasmād devaguṇaṃ matvā śīlameva sadācaret ।
na śīlasadṛśaṃ kiñcidanyat trāṇamihāsti vai ।।

।। iti śīlavargastrayoviṃśaḥ ।।

kṣāntivargaḥ

kṣamābhūṣaṇenaiva bhūṣito bhavati pumān

kṣāntyā vibhūṣitaḥ jīva bhūṣito netarairdhanaiḥ ।
dhanaṃ vinā samāyāti kṣāntiṃ naiva kathañcana ।।

kṣamāvān puruṣaḥ sarvapriyo bhavati dehinām ।
pūjyate daivatairnityaṃ tasmāt kṣāntiḥ parantapa ! ।।

kṣamāvān puruṣaḥ sarvatra pūjyate

kṣamāvān puruṣaḥ sarvaiḥ krodhadoṣairvivarjitaḥ ।
yaśasā pūjyate nityamiha loke paratra ca ।।

kṣāntidhanaṃ sarvottamam

kṣāntirdhanaṃ dhanaṃ śīlaprajñāvardhanameva ca ।
dhanānyanyāni śastāni na hitasya kathañcana ।।

sadbhiḥ kṣamāvāneva pūjyate

pūjyate satataṃ sadbhiryaśasā caiva pūjyate ।
kṣamāvān puruṣaḥ sarvastamāt kṣāntiparo bhavet ।।

krodhaviṣasya kṣamaiva bheṣajam

kṣāntiḥ krodhaviṣasyāsya bheṣajaṃ paramaṃ matam ।
kṣāntyāvināśitaḥ krodho anarthāyopajāyate ।।

jñānaśīlābhibhūtānāṃ bāliśānāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
pratīpakārya kurute kṣāntirmārganidarśikā ।।

kṣamāvanta eva loke dhaninaḥ

sa dharmadhanahīnānāṃ bhramatāṃ gatipañcake ।
yeṣāṃ kṣāntimayaṃ dravyaṃ te loke dhaninaḥ smṛtāḥ ।।

tamonicayakāntāre dṛḍhakrodhena dustare ।
kṣāntyā yathā smṛtāḥ sadbhistaranti khula mānavāḥ ।।

saddharmapāṭhanaṣṭānāṃ deśikā kṣāntiruttamā ।
apāyabhayabhītānāṃ na bhayaṃ kṣāntirucyate ।।

nṛṇāṃ kṣāntiḥ sukhāvahā

sukhāvahā sadā nṛṇāṃ duḥkhasya ca vighātikā ।
kṣemasamprāpikā nityaṃ viśvāsaguṇakārikā ।।

śubhāsti nāyikā dhanyā hyaśubhebhyo vivarjitā ।
mokṣasaṃdeśikā puṃsāṃ saṃsārabhayanāśikā ।।

kṣāntiḥ narakāgnivināśikā svargasopānabhūtā ca

svargasopānabhūtā sā narakāgnivināśikā ।
trāyate pretalokātsā tiryagyonau tathaiva ca ।।

kṣāntiḥ sanmārgāmṛtadīpikā

sā guṇaudhaiḥ sadā pūrṇā śivā bhavati dehinām ।
sā praśaste sukhe prāpte kṣāntiḥ kāryā prayatnataḥ ।
sarvalokasya māteva sanmārgāmṛtadīpikā ।।

।। iti kṣāntivargaścaturviṃśaḥ ।।

vīryavargaḥ

deśakriyāyuktāni kāryāṇi siddhayanti

deśakālopapannasya kriyātithyocitasya ca ।
nyāyenārabhyamāṇasya vīryasya sakalaṃ phalam ।।

nyāyadeśakriyāhīnā adharmeṇa vivarjitāḥ ।
sīdanti kāryanikarā vīryeṇa parivarjitāḥ ।।

ārabdhavīryā mokṣaṃ prāpnuvanti

dhyānenārabdhavīryeṇa mokṣaṃ gacchanti paṇḍitāḥ ।
bhavakṣipta ivākāro devaloke prayānti ca ।।

yānyārabdhāni kāryāṇi vīryavad balinā nṛṇā ।
tāni tāni prasiddhāni vipulāni bhavanti ca ।।

ye arthā lokottare siddhā ye ca lokeṣu sammatāḥ ।
te vīryeṇa prasādhyante vīryahīnā na jātu vai ।।

mandavīrya cirotsāhaṃ saddharmeṇa vivarjitam ।
naro viśati lokaṃ śaśāṅkamiva kalmaṣam ।।

vīryavattā paramāṃ gatiṃ pradadāti

āryāṣṭāṅgena mārgeṇa na jñānaparipālitaḥ ।
vīryavattāmahotsāho prayāti paramāṃ gatim ।।

bodhiḥ vīryeṇāvāpyate

vīryaṇāvāpyate bodhiḥ svavīryeṇa tathā mahī ।
arhattvaṃ vīryavadbhiśca tasmānnāgnisamā gatiḥ ।।

uttamasthānaprāptyartha vīryārambhe matiḥ kāryā

tasmād devān guṇān matvā vīryavān niyatendriyaḥ ।
vīryārambhe matiṃ kuryārnnāsti vīryasamarthanam ।।

vīryārthī smṛtimān yaśca naro jñānaparāyaṇaḥ ।
prayātyanuttamaṃ sthānaṃ jarāmaraṇavarjitam ।।

।। iti vīryavargaḥ pañcaviṃśaḥ ।।

dhyānavargaḥ

svasthaḥ kaḥ?

asaṃsaktamaternityaṃ nityaṃ dhyānavihāriṇaḥ ।
viśuddhamanaso nityamekāgrabhiratasya ca ।।

yasyaikāgrakaraṃ cittaṃ tasya doṣā na bādhakāḥ ।
sa doṣabhayanirmuktaḥ svastha ityabhidhīyate ।।

ekāgrābhiratañceto vivekamanudhāvati ।
sarvatarkavinirmuktaḥ svastha ityabhidhīyate ।।

cittasyaikāgratāṃ varṇayati

yasya cittaṃ dhruvaṃ śāntaṃ nirvāṇābhirataṃ sadā ।
na tasyendriyajā doṣā bhavasya śubhahetavaḥ ।।

yacca dhyānakṛtaṃ saukhyaṃ yacca samādhijam ।
cittaṃ tatsarvamekāgramate bhavati dehinaḥ ।।

yatiḥ alaukikaṃ sukhaṃ bhuṅkte

ekārāmasya yatino yat sukhaṃ jāyate hṛdi ।
yat saukhyamativijñeyaṃ na saukhyaṃ laukikaṃ matam ।।

kīdṛśaṃ cittaṃ śāntiṃ samadhigacchati?

ekāgrābhirataṃ cittaṃ viśuddhākṛtameva ca ।
doṣajālavinirmuktaṃ śāntiṃ samadhigacchati ।।

jñānāmbhasā tṛṣṇāgniṃ hanti

ekāntamanasā nityaṃ saṃkṣiptendriyapañcakaiḥ ।
tṛṣṇāgninātivṛddhaṃ ca hanti jñānāmbhasā budhaḥ ।।

tasya tṛṣṇāvimuktasya viśuddhasya sukhaiṣiṇaḥ ।
akṣayaṃ cāvyayaṃ caiva padaṃ hi sthitamagrataḥ ।।

nirvāṇapuragāmi vartma

vitarkakuṭilaṃ ceto yatra yatropapadyate ।
ekālambanayuktena dhārya tena samādhinā ।
tasmādetat paraṃ vartma nirvāṇapuragāmikam ।।

manonigrahaphalam

etadagraṃ manaḥ kṣutvā hanyādarisamūhakam ।
mano hīdaṃ vinirgṛhya vetti dhyānajairdṛḍhaiḥ ।।

nirupamaṃ dhyānajaṃ sukham

।
prayānti paramaṃ sthānamaśokaṃ hatakilviṣam ।।

nirviṣaskasya tuṣṭasya nirāgasyāpi dhīmataḥ yat sukhaṃ dhyānajaṃ bhāti kutastasyopamā parā ।।

dhyānaiḥ paramaṃ padaṃ prāpyate

etatsāraṃ sudhīrāṇāṃ yogināṃ pāragāminām ।
yadevedaṃ manaḥ śrutvā prayānti padamacyutam ।।

।। iti dhyānavargaḥ ṣaḍviṃśaḥ ।।

prajñāvargaḥ

prajñā māteva hitakāriṇī

dharmānusāriṇī prajñā vīryeṇa parivṛṃhitā ।
samādhibalasaṃyuktā māteva hitakāriṇī ।।

prajñā gatipañcakāt trāyate

sā hi santrāyate sarvān puruṣān gatipañcakāt ।
na mātā na pitā tatra gacchantamanugacchati ।।

prajñāśikharamāruhya śīlakandaraśobhanam ।
bhavadoṣamidaṃ sarva paśyati bhūṣaṇaḥ ।।

samādhinā bhavārṇavaṃ tarati

indriyāṇīndriyārthebhyo yadā vindanti tatpadam ।
tadā samādhinā jñāna bhavasāgaramuttaret ।।

dānaśīlatapodhyānairjñānamevāgramucyate ।
apavargād yadā jñānaṃ jñānaśīle sukhāvahe ।।

prajñā aṣṭamo mārgastathāgatenopadiṣṭaḥ
cakṣuṣāṃ ca parā dṛṣṭā prajñoktā sunirmalā ।
mārgāṇāṃ cāṣṭamo mārgaḥ śivaḥ proktastathāgataiḥ ।।

prajñābalaṃ sarvottamam

caturṇā caiva satyānāmagre dve tu prakīrtite ।
bālānāṃ ca sadā dṛṣṭaṃ prajñābalamihottamam ।।

janmapadvatirjñānaśastreṇa chettavyā

jñānaśastreṇa tikṣṇena latā chedyā durāsadā ।
hantavyā doṣanivahāśchettavyā janmapaddhatiḥ ।।

na jñānātparo bandhuḥ

amṛtānāṃ paraṃ jñānaṃ śreyasāṃ nidhiruttamam ।
na jñānācca paraṃ bandhurna jñānāddhanamuttamam ।।

jñānaśīlayutā prajñā sevitavyā

jñānaśīlayutāvṛddhā vītarāgā gataspṛhāḥ ।
sevitavyāḥ sadā santastattvamārganidarśakāḥ ।।

kleśādīn prajñāśastreṇa vidārayet

prajñāvajreṇa tīkṣṇena mahodayavasena ca ।
mahāyogarathārūḍhaḥ kleśādīn pravidārayet ।।

।। iti prajñāvargaḥ saptaviṃśaḥ ।।

nirvāṇavargaḥ

kleśakṣaya eva nirvāṇamārgaḥ

kleśakṣayāt paraṃ saukhyaṃ kathayanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।
eṣa nirvāṇago mārgaḥ kathitastattvadarśakaiḥ ।।

tatpadaṃ śāśvataṃ juṣṭaṃ kathayanti tathāgatāḥ ।
yatra janma na mṛtyurna vidyate duḥkhasambhavaḥ ।।

vibhūtasyāpramattasya śāntasya vanacāriṇaḥ ।
alolupasya vīrasya nirvāṇasya vibhūtayaḥ ।।

viṣayeṣvapramatto nirvāṇaṃ nāticiraṃ prāpnoti

mitrāmitraprahīṇasya bhavarāgavivarjinaḥ ।
viṣayeṣvapramattasya nirvāṇaṃ nātidūrataḥ ।।

śubhakarttṛ nirvāṇaṃ prāpnoti

śubhakāryeṣu saktasya maitrīkāruṇyabhāvinaḥ ।
saṃsārabhayabhītasya nirvāṇaṃ nātidūrataḥ ।।

kausīdyavirahitaḥ tvaritaṃ nirvāṇaṃ yāti

kleśakṣayavidhijñasya nairātmyasyāpi tasya ca ।
kausīdyāccaiva muktasya nirvāṇaṃ nātidūrataḥ ।।

vaśyendriyasya śāntasya nirvāṇaṃ samīpataram

catuḥsatyavidhijñasya tridoṣavadhasevinaḥ ।
vaśyendriyasya śāntasya nirvāṇaṃ nātidūrataḥ ।।

sukhaduḥkhapāśairmukto muniḥ pāraga ucyate
sukhaduḥkhamayaiḥ pāśairyasya ceto na hanyate ।
sa doṣabhayanirmuktaḥ pārago munirucyate ।।

śubhānveṣī nirvāṇamadhigacchati

puruṣo apāyabhīruśca pramādabalavarjakaḥ ।
śubhakārī śubhānveṣī nirvāṇamadhigacchati ।।

।। iti nirvāṇavargo aṣṭāviṃśaḥ ।।

mārgavargaḥ

āryacatuṣṭayopāsakaḥ pāraṃ gacchati

satyāni catvāri śivāni tāni, subhāvitānyeva samīkṣya vidvān ।
sucintako jātijarābhayebhyaḥ, pramucyaye pāramupaiti śāntaḥ ।।

kāmeṣu saktaḥ bhavabhogabaddhaḥ bhavati

acintako yastu vibhūtabuddhiḥ kāmeṣu sakto bhavabhogabaddhaḥ ।
sa bandhanaiḥ kāmamayairnibaddho, na mucyate jātijarābhayebhyaḥ ।।

bhavārṇave sukhadraṣṭā ante narakaṃ yāti

vicintya yo duḥkhamidaṃ viśālaṃ, na khedamāyāti bhavārṇavebhyaḥ ।
sa kāmavāṇairnihato hi mūḍhaḥ, kaṣṭāmavasthāṃ narake api yāti ।।

ābhyantaraṃ kṣemasukhaṃ ca hitvā, kiṃ kāmabhogābhiratā hi bālāḥ ।
naite bijānanti bhayaṃ ca tīvramabhyeti mṛtyurjvalanaprakāśaḥ ।।

tattvamārgapradarśakaiḥ kimuktam?

anityaduḥkhaśūnyo ayamātmā kārakavarjitaḥ ।
saṃsāraḥ kathito buddhaiḥ tattvamārgapradarśakaiḥ ।।

tena sarvamidaṃ tattvajñānaṃ jñeyaṃ samāsataḥ ।
jñānajñeyavinirmuktaṃ tṛtīyaṃ nopalabhyate ।।

kaḥ tattvavidhijñaḥ?

antapāravidhijño yaḥ ṣoḍaśākāratattvavit ।
ūrdhvagatividhijño hi kṣāntitattvavicakṣaṇaḥ ।।

tattvavideva dharmatāmanuviśati

agralokaikadharmajñaḥ samanantaratattvavit ।
sa dharmatāmanuviśed yathā na vikampate ।।

dvayopāyavinirmukto naṣṭān nāśayate muhuḥ ।
naṣṭapāpagatirvīraḥ strotāpanno nirucyate ।।

srotāṃsya kuśalā dharmā jīryante pāpagāminaḥ ।
mokṣāgninā pratapyante srotāpanno bhavatyataḥ ।।

prasrabdhijaṃ mahodarkamuktaṃ saṃsāramokṣakam ।
tṛṣṇākṣayasukhaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ satyataḥ sukhakārakam ।।

kaḥ sadaiva sukhī bhavati?

nāvabadhnāti yaṃ tṛṣṇā na vitarkairvihasyate ।
samprāptabhavapārastu sukhī bhavati sarvadā ।।

ārya mārgacatuṣṭayam anyonyaphalasambhūtam

anyonyaphalasambhūta sarvataḥ sampravartate ।
tadeva kāraṇaṃ jñeyamāryamārgacatuṣṭayam ।।

āryasatyeṣu viditaḥ puruṣo vidyate dhruvam ।
viṣayeṣu hi saṃghuṣṭaṃ jagad bhramati cakravat ।।

kaḥ śreṣṭho mārgaḥ?

sa mārgo deśakaḥ śreṣṭho yo mārgo bhāṣitaḥ śivaḥ ।
yena mārgeṇa prācīnā yātā manīṣiṇaḥ ।।

triśaraṇagata eva sukhaṃ jīvati

sujīvitaṃ bhavet tasya yasya buddhau sthitaṃ manaḥ ।
nahi buddhivinirmuktaṃ jīvitaṃ jīvitaṃ bhavet ।।

sujīvitaṃ bhavet tasya yasya dharme sthitaṃ manaḥ ।
nahi dharmavinirmuktaṃ jīvitaṃ jīvitaṃ bhavet ।।

sujīvitaṃ bhavet tasya yasya saṅghe sthitaṃ manaḥ ।
nahi saṅghavinirmuktaṃ jīvitaṃ jīvitaṃ bhavet ।।

keṣāṃ sujīvitaṃ jīvanam?

sujīvitaṃ bhavet tasya yasya satye sthitaṃ manaḥ ।
nahi satyavinirmuktaṃ jīvitaṃ jīvitaṃ bhavet ।।

sujīvitaṃ bhavet tasya yasya mārge sthitaṃ manaḥ ।
nahi mārgavinirmuktaṃ jīvitaṃ jīvitaṃ bhavet ।।

nirvāṇagamane yasya nityaṃ buddhiravasthitā ।
sa doṣādeva nirmukto na devaḥ krīḍati svayam ।।

kīdṛśī krīḍā sukhodbhāvikā?

yā bhavavyāpinī krīḍā nityamekāgracetasaḥ ।
sā sukhodbhāvikā krīḍā na krīḍā rāgakārikā ।।

kena mārgeṇa śivaṃ sthānaṃ milati?

sukhādīniha satyāni yathā dāntena vindati ।
tadā kṣemaṃ śivaṃ sthānaṃ prāpnoti puruṣottamaḥ ।।

।। iti mārgavarga ekonatriṃśaḥ ।।

bhikṣuvargaḥ

ādarśo bhikṣuḥ lokamārgadarśakaḥ

yo hinasti na bhūtāni mitravettā sadākṣayaḥ ।
pitṛvat sarvabhūtāni lokastamanupaśyati ।।

adattādānavirato nityaṃ jñānī jitendriyaḥ ।
praśāntadehakarmā tīrṇasambhavasaṅkramaḥ ।।

nāpyālekhyagatā nāpi cakṣuṣā sā nirīkṣyate ।
hatakāmo dṛṣṭasatyo muktastādṛśa ucyate ।।

samaloṣṭāśmakanakaḥ vītaśokaḥ samāhitaḥ ।
na kleśoragasampṛktaḥ sa saukhyaṃ dhruvamāpnuyāt ।।

kaḥ bhikṣurvidyate?

arthānarthasamo yasya lābhālābhau tathaiva ca ।
sukhaduḥkhasamāyuktaḥ bhikṣuḥ sa khalu kathyate ।।

mitrāmitraprahīṇo yaḥ samacetā jitendriyaḥ ।
vibheti yo na viṣayaiḥ vijñeyastādṛśo yatiḥ ।।

viṣayadveṣī nirvāṇamadhigacchati

viṣamatvāddhi viṣayān dveṣṭi dhīro gatavyathaḥ ।
na tasya dūre nirvāṇaṃ samyaksambuddhadeśitam ।।

udayavyayatattvajñaḥ samyagdṛṣṭiralolupaḥ ।
himavāniva niṣkramya saṃsārānmuktahetukaḥ ।।

tṛṇacandanatulyo hi samatṛṣṇāmbarāśinaḥ ।
sa kauśeyasaṅghaṭitatṛṣṇayā naiva bādhate ।।

lābhasatkārasantuṣṭaḥ santuṣṭastṛṇasaṃstaraiḥ ।
vahnivallābhasatkāraṃ yaḥ paśyati sa paśyati ।।

buddhadeśitāḥ bhikṣudharmāḥ

vāhyate yo na viṣayaistṛṇanadyā na vāhayate ।
svakarmaphalatattvajñaḥ sa bhikṣurbuddhadeśitaḥ ।।

nātītaṃ śocate yo hi buddhayā gataspṛhaḥ ।
pratyutpannakriyāyogī na buddhistasya lipyate ।।

nirvāṇe matiryasya dharme nityaṃ sthitā bhavet ।
na vartate sa saṃsāre śukladharmasamāvṛtaḥ ।।

nāvilaṃ kriyate yasya cittaṃ vidyāgnikalpayā ।
dāruvadviṣayā yasya tasya duḥkhaṃ na vidyate ।।

indriyāṇi vaśe yasya cendriyeṣu vaśānugaḥ ।
hriyate yaḥ pumarthaino nikaṣastādṛśo muniḥ ।।

sādhuvaddhimano yasya kṣamāvān priyadarśanaḥ ।
prahlādayati cetāṃsi sa nṛṇāṃ śaśivanmuniḥ ।।

aruṇābhirato yastu harmyāgreṣu na rajyati ।
santuṣṭaḥ pāṃśukūlena bhikṣurbhikṣārato bhavet ।।

śānto dāntaḥ sudhīrarthāt tattvavit sukhaduḥkhayoḥ ।
sa yātyuttamamadhvānaṃ yatra gatvā na śocati ।।

ṛjumatpātakānyasya nityaṃ dhyānaparāyaṇaḥ ।
prākṛtaiśca malai sa yogī satyavartmani ।।

sarvendriyavighātī yaḥ sarvabhūtahite rataḥ ।
śānto dāntendriyaḥ svastho bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

ṣaḍindriyarathārūḍho rāgaśatrunivārakaḥ ।
prajñādhīraḥ kriyāvān yaḥ sa śāntipadamaśnute ।।

araṇyavāsī santuṣṭo bhūmivāsī samāhitaḥ ।
dhunāti pāpako dharmaścāyurmeghānivāmbaraḥ ।।

śubhaṃ vā dehakarmāntaḥ śubhacaryāsu saṃrataḥ ।
tattvadṛṣṭiḥ kriyādakṣo nāśayanmārasādhanam ।।

dayālurbhikṣurnirvāṇamārge sthito bhavati

rāgātyaye na bādheta śubhacittaṃ gatālayam ।
maitryā kāruṇyabahulo bhikṣurnairyyāṇike sthitaḥ ।।

yasya rūpādayo neṣṭā viṣayā bandhahetave ।
sa yāti paramāṃ śāntiṃ yatra gatvā na śocyate ।।

hetupratyayatattvajñaḥ sūkṣmārthe kṛtaniścayaḥ ।
mokṣasrotasyabhiratastṛṣṇayā naiva rajyate ।।

yo nādatte aśubhaṃ karma śubhakarmarataḥ sadā ।
candrāṃśunirmalagatiryogī bhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

pradahan pāpakān dharmān śuṣkendhanamivānalaḥ ।
vibhrājate tribhuvane muktapāyo gatavyathaḥ ।।

mokṣe asti yasya tu mano na saṃsāre kathañcana ।
nāsau badhnāti saṃsāre muktaḥ pakṣī yathāmbare ।।

vedanodayatattvajño vedanāphalaniścayaḥ ।
sa mukta iti vijñeyastattvavid ṛtavāṃśca saḥ ।।

tathāpyete sukhaduḥkhe mṛṣṭāmṛṣṭairna lipyate ।
dīptaṃ paśyati saṃsāraṃ yaḥ sa yogī satāṃ mataḥ ।।

bhikṣurbhavati kīdṛśaḥ?

athāmūḍhamatirnityaṃ nityaṃ dharmaparāyaṇaḥ ।
bhikṣuvṛttāvabhirato bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

na tṛptirdarśanārāmaiḥ sādhūnāṃ darśane ratiḥ ।
niṣkrāntagṛhakalmāṣo bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

na nṛtyagītasandarśī ca punarīkṣate ।
saṃrakṣito śmaśāneṣu bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

ekāhaṃ paramaṃ piṇḍamādatte anyatra kāṅkṣati ।
tribhāgakukṣisantuṣṭo bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

vastrottamavivarjī yaḥ pāṃsukūleṣu rajyate ।
muktāhāravihāro yo bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

karmāṇyārabhate yo na nirāśaḥ sa ca karmasu ।
niruddhako noparato bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

kāyakoṭivinirmukto mohadhvāntavivarjitaḥ ।
aliptaḥ pāpakairdharmaibhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

sarvāśayajanānītaḥ sarvāśayavivarjitaḥ ।
sarvāśayavinirmukto bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

āryāṣṭāṅgena mārgeṇa nirvāṇapurataḥ sthitaḥ ।
sarvārthadharmatā hyeṣā bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

śāntendriyo dṛḍhamatiḥ kāmapākavivarjitaḥ ।
ekāgrasaṃsthitamanā bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

bhūmisaṅkramaṇajño yo bhūmitattvanidarśakaḥ ।
bhūmeḥ parāparajño yo bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

sambhavāsambhavān dharmān hetupratyayasambhavān ।
jānīte vidhivat sarvān bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

brahmacārī ṛtujñānī styānamiddhavivarjitaḥ ।
kalpodagro avanau dakṣo bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

śamasthovipaśyanāśca caturdhyānarataśca yaḥ ।
ālaye muditārāmo bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

pakṣiṇo gaganasthasya chāyevānugataḥ sadā ।
saddharmasyānujīvī sa bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

kleśopakleśabadhakaḥ samadarśī śubhānvitaḥ ।
anāpānavidhijño yo bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

anukramavidhijño yo yogavit tattvadarśakaḥ ।
pārāpāravidhijño yo bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

yo na hṛṣyati harṣeṣu bhayeṣu na bibheti ca ।
mukto harṣabhayodvegairbhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

janmamaraṇatattvajñaḥ surāsuranamaskṛtaḥ ।
parāvarajñaḥ sattvānāṃ bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

saṅghāṭimātrasaṃhṛṣṭaḥ sañcayeṣu na rajyate ।
alpeccho brahmacārī yo bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

ekāśī vṛkṣamūle yaḥ sadā dhyānaṃ samīhate ।
lābhasatkāravirato bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

upekṣākaruṇārāgo mokṣadoṣavivarjitaḥ ।
nirdagdhadoṣasarvasvo bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

mandavīryakusīdānāṃ bhikṣūṇāṃ darśanāya ca ।
nānyayogābhirakto yo bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

kausīdyābhirato bhikṣuḥ nahi kalyāṇamarhati
na śayyāsanasambhogī bhikṣurbuddhena bhāṣitaḥ ।
kausīdyabhirato yastu nāsau kalyāṇamarhati ।।

kleśānāṃ mūlapākaṃ hi kausīdyaṃ yasya vidyate ।
tasya duḥkhaṃ mahāghoraṃ saṃsāre sampravartate ।।

kausīdyameva yasyāsti tasya dharmo na vidyate ।
kevalaṃ vastramātreṇa abhikṣuḥ' sa iti kathyate ।।

bhikṣurbhavati na tādṛśaḥ

nādhyāpane ratiryasya na dhyānenāśu rakṣati ।
kevalaṃ vastumātreṇa bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

vihārābhirato yastu na rato dharmagocare ।
strīmadyalolupamatibhikṣurasti na tādṛśaḥ ।।

pāpakarmaṇi ।
sa bhikṣurdeśito buddhaiḥ na bhoktā svakagocare ।।

varamāśīviṣaviṣaṃ kathitaṃ tāmrameva ca ।
bhuktasyātyantaduḥśīlairadhikaṃ pāpabhojanam ।।

yo hi nārhati piṇḍāya nāsau piṇḍāya kalpate ।
yasya piṇḍikṛtāḥ kleśāḥ sarpā iva vileśayāḥ ।।

sa bhikṣuḥ piṇḍabhojī syānna strīdarśanatatparaḥ ।
bandhakaṃ yadi cātmānaṃ kṛtvā paraśubhakṣatim ।।

bhikṣurdurguṇānāṃ svarūpam

kathaṃ sa bhikṣurvijñeyaḥ saṅgharatnapradūṣakaḥ ।
yasyeṣṭā lābhasatkārā viṣayā yasya sammatāḥ ।।

nāridarśanasākāṅkṣī na bhikṣurna gṛhīva saḥ ।
rājaseviṣu sṛṣṭāśo madyapaḥ krodhanastathā ।।

sadā bhikṣurbañcayate dāyakānnanu cetasā ।
upāyanānyupādāya rājadvārāśritā hi ye ।
saṃrabdhā gṛhibhiḥ sārdha yathā nāgā vanāśritāḥ ।।

tasmāt tāneva puṣṇanti vāterṣyāste samāgatāḥ ।
putradārān parityajya ye śāntā ratnamāśritāḥ ।।

bhikṣorguṇānāṃ māhātmyam

prahāya doṣān yo bhikṣurasti darśanatattvavit ।
rūpādiskandhatattvajño mokṣāya yatate sadā ।।

dharmāvabodhābhirato dhyānārāmavihāravān tattvalakṣaṇasambodhāt prāpnuyāt padamavyayam ।।

maitryārāmo hi satatamudyukto dharmagocare ।
tattvalakṣaṇatattvajño bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

yoniśastu matiryasya kāmakrodhairna hanyate ।
sa bhikṣuriti vijñeyo viparītastato anyathā ।।

sarvabhūtadṛḍhaḥ śāntaḥ sarvasaṅgativarjitaḥ ।
sarvabandhananirmukto bhikṣurbhavati tattvavit ।।

karmaṇi yasya vijñānaviṣayairyo na hanyate ।
nirmalaḥ syāt kanakavat santuṣṭo bhikṣurucyate ।।

priyāpriye mano yasya na lepamanugacchati ।
saṅkalpānāṃ vidhijño yaḥ sarvapāpavivarjitaḥ ।।

anyasaṃduṣṭacarito dharmaśīlo jitendriyaḥ ।
ahīnasatvo matimān bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

śāstre śāstrārthavijñāne matiryasya sadā ratā ।
na pānabhojanarataḥ sa bhikṣuḥ śāntamānasaḥ ।।

bhikṣoḥ svarūpanirūpaṇam

vanāraṇyavihāreṣu śmaśāne tṛṇasaṃstare ।
ramate yasya tu mano bhikṣurbhavati tādṛśaḥ ।।

doṣāṇāṃ karmatattvajñaḥ phalavit pariśeṣataḥ ।
hetupratyayatattvajño bhikṣuḥ syād vītakalmaṣaḥ ।।

kilviṣakāntāro hatadoṣo jitendriyaḥ ।
punarbhavavidhijño yo bhikṣuḥ śāntamanāḥ ।।

notkarṣo hṛṣṭahṛdaye nindayā naiva rūṣyati ।
samudratulyagāmbhīryo yogavān bhikṣurucyate ।।

āveṇiko dṛḍhamatiḥ sūkṣmavādī na lolupaḥ ।
kāmavādī samo dakṣaḥ sa bhikṣuḥ śānta ucyate ।।

kāmadhātūpagān hetūn rūpadhātau tathaiva ca ।
āruṣyeṣu ca tattvajñaḥ śāstrā bhikṣuḥ sa ucyate ।।

na laukikakathāsaktaḥ śatrudoṣabadhe sadā ।
viṣavad yasya viṣayāḥ sa bhikṣurdeśito budhaiḥ ।।

śuddhā yasya kāmeṣu matirbhavati nityaśaḥ ।
sa nirmuktamatirbhikṣurmuktaḥ saṃsārabandhanāt ।।

dhyānādhyayanakarmaṇyaḥ kausīdyaṃ yasya dūrataḥ ।
hitakārī ca sattvānām āraṇyo bhikṣurucyate ।।

praśnottaramatiryasya pratibhāvan jitendriyaḥ ।
sa dharmaḥ kathito jñeyo viparītastṛṇaiḥ samaḥ ।।

buddhaśāsane kīdṛg bhikṣuḥ śastaḥ?

kāyamānasabhīryasya sarvadā naiva khidyate ।
sarvakṛtyakaro jñeyo yaḥ saṅghāya ca tatparaḥ ।।

na parārtha na lobhārtha yaśo artha kurute na tu ।
saṅghakārye matiryasya sa muktaḥ sarvabandhanaiḥ ।।

na svargārtha matiryasya lābhārtha yaśase na vā ।
nirvāṇārtha kriyā sarvā sa bhikṣuḥ srota ucyate ।।

pāpebhyo nityavirataḥ satkṛtyeṣu rataḥ sadā ।
na pāpamitrasaṃsargī bhikṣuḥ syād buddhaśāsane ।।

maitryā bhāvitacittasya dakṣasya ṛjucetasaḥ ।
śikṣāpadeṣu raktasya nirvāṇaṃ nātidūrataḥ ।।

jarāmaraṇaśīlasya saṃsāravimukhasya ca ।
dhyāne api na pramattasya nirvāṇaṃ nātidūrataḥ ।।

anityatāvidhijñasya śūnyatāvatkriyāvataḥ ।
dhyānotkarṣavidhijñasya nirvāṇaṃ nātidūrataḥ ।।

dhīro ayamagracoro ayaṃ yo ayaṃ bhikṣurasaṃvṛtaḥ ।
antaḥpurīvarasrāvī bahiścīvarasaṃvṛtaḥ ।।

dharmavinayād rikto bhikṣurduḥkhabhāgī bhavedeva

yathā yatnamayo rāśiḥ sarvo asāraśca durbalaḥ ।
evaṃ sañcarati rikto vitatho bhikṣuvādikaḥ ।।

sa nārakeyo duḥśīlaḥ saṅgharatnabahiṣkṛtaḥ ।
kāyasya bhedānnarakaṃ nīyate cittavañcitaḥ ।।

vañcito dharmavinayād yāti tat svena karmaṇā ।
malinastamasā baddho duḥkhabhāgī bhaviṣyati ।।

aprāvṛtaḥ śubhadhaman nagnaḥ sādhujugupsitaḥ ।
nayate narakaṃ ghoraṃ yathā dharmabahiṣkṛtaḥ ।।

aśobhanasya nicayo duḥkhadvāramanāvṛtam ।
saṃsārabandhanaṃ tīvraṃ dauḥśīlyamiti kathyate ।।

asaṃvareṇa yo dagdhaḥ sa dagdho vahninā bhṛśam ।
tasya saṃvarakṣīṇasya vinipāto dhruvaṃ sthitaḥ ।।

kukartṛbhikṣurapi narakaṃ yāti

manasā saṃvarasthena svācāraiḥ saṃvarāyate ।
samūḍhacaryāmāruhya narakāyopakalpate ।।

aśubhaṃ vardhate tasya divārātrau ca sarvataḥ ।
yasya śīlamayaṃ ratnaṃ dauḥśīlyena nivāritam ।।

dharmaśūnyasya riktasya tamasā saṃvṛtasya ca ।
vidyate asaṃvarastasya yo na śaucāya kalpate ।।

asaṃvaramayaḥ pāśo malinaḥ sādhuvarjitaḥ ।
ākarṣati sa duḥśīlān pāpiṣṭhān śīlavarjitān ।।

asaṃvaraiśca dauḥśīlyaiḥ pāpaiśca saha saṅgatiḥ ।
dūtakā narakasyaite kāmānāmapi sevakāḥ ।।

asaṃvṛtaprasūtasya capalasya viśeṣataḥ ।
pāpakarmābhiyuktasya narakaṃ nātidūrataḥ ।।

kimete nāvagacchanti karmaṇāṃ sadṛśaṃ phalam ।
akṣipātāya mūḍhāya durmatau vimohitāḥ ।।

ahanyahani vardhante pāpanadyo durāsadāḥ ।
duḥkhormimālāścapalāḥ pāpiṣṭhajanahāriṇaḥ ।।

na teṣāṃ sukaraṃ janma na teṣāṃ sukaraṃ manaḥ ।
aśīlāḥ puruṣā ye vā śukladharmavivarjitāḥ ।।

dharmo atyuccaḥ śubho mārgaḥ

atyuccaśca śubho mārgaḥ sa adharma' iti kathyate ।
taṃ prāpyamanujaḥ śīghraṃ prayāti padamacyutam ।।

tato apavādāḥ sādhyante śaktimantaḥ sukhāstu ye ।
saṃvarasya sadā dāsāsteṣāṃ duḥkhaṃ na vidyate ।
dauḥśīlyaparamo hyeṣa malinīkurute nṛṇām ।।

ye śaikṣyapadavibhraṣṭā bhāgino narakasya te ।
evaṃ jñātvā naraḥ sarva saṃvaraṃ pratipadyate ।।

śubhadharmī bhikṣurnirvāṇaṃ nāticiraṃ prāpnoti

bhavārṇasya sarvasya setubhūto hi saṃvaraḥ ।
śuddhājīvaviśuddhasya śāntavaktrasya karmaṇaḥ ।।

dhyāyino vipramuktasya nirvāṇaṃ nātidūrataḥ ।
dhūrdharasyāpramattasya śmaśānavanasevinaḥ ।।

śāyino bhūtale nityaṃ nirvāṇaṃ nātidūrataḥ ।
pāṃśuśayyāvalambāṃsapātamekaṃ sajarjaram ।।

santoṣaḥ phalamūlaiśca sa sukhī buddhasambhavaḥ ।
vipramuktasya kāmebhyaḥ santoṣo hītarasya ca ।।

savimuktakacittasya nirvāṇaṃ nātidūrataḥ ।
kuhakāmalamuktasya rajo vā tasya tāyinaḥ ।।

ākāśasamacittasya nirvāṇaṃ nātidūrataḥ ।
bahubaddhapadairyuktā vijñeyā cārikā ।।

nāśikā brahmacaryasya nirvāṇagatiduḥkhikā ।
sevyate yā janairnityaṃ prākṛtaiḥ śīlavarjitaiḥ ।।

ajastraṃ parivarjyā sā dhyāyibhistattvadarśibhiḥ ।
daurbalyamūlamekā sā manaskārapraṇāśikā ।।

nāśinī brahmacaryasya narakasya pradarśikā ।
bhraṃśikā svargamārgasya duḥkhasāgaraśoṣikā ।।

dūtikā pretalokasya tiryagyoninipātikā ।
nāmnā saṅgaṇikā sevā saṃsāre bandhamātṛkā ।।

dhyānādhyayanaśaktaiva varjyā nityaṃ hi bhikṣubhiḥ ।
dhyānādhyayananirmukto nimittābhirataḥ sadā ।।

paradharmo bhayāvahaḥ

vivarjitaḥ śubhairdharmairapāpagamanāya saḥ ।
svadharma yaḥ parityajya paradharmeṣu rajyate ।।

dharmadvayaparibhraṣṭo vinipātāya kalpate ।
svagṛhaṃ yaḥ parityajya paraveśyāni tiṣṭhati ।।

sadāyaṃ lāghavaṃ yāti nidhanaṃ cāśu gacchati ।
tathā yo vimatirbhūto vidvanmānī janecchayā ।।

svadharmaviratiṃ kṛtvā paradharmeṣu vartate ।
adharme cāśayastasya paraliṅgopajīvinaḥ ।।

tṛṇavidyābhilipto ayaṃ pretaḥ pāpeṣu pacyate ।
yaśo antaṃ padamāsthāya pāpakarmaṇi vartate ।।

nāsau bhikṣurihocyate

śaśvat sa patito dṛṣṭaḥ śāsanāntāt pravartate ।
nispṛhaḥ kāmacaryāsu nirāmodaḥ pravarjitaḥ ।।
ārabdhavīryaḥ santuṣṭo dhyāyī bhikṣurihocyate ।।
na ca kāmeṣu saṃsakto nityāhāravihāravān ।
kāṣāyasaṃvṛtaḥ kṣauro nāsau bhikṣurihocyate ।।

nimittabodhako nakṣatragaticintakaḥ ।
rājasevāpramattaśca na sa bhikṣurihocyate ।।

vaidyakarmāṇi kurvaśca śruti saṅgrathanaṃ tathā ।
saṅkīrṇā dinacaryā ca kurvan bhikṣuḥ praṇaśyati ।।

dhyānādhyayanavidveṣī rataḥ saṅgaṇikāsu ca ।
lobhasatkāralābhaṃ ca kurvan bhikṣuḥ praṇaśyati ।।

suvarṇadhātusaṃsakto bahumitraratiśca yaḥ ।
anyalābhābhilāṣito bhikṣuḥ patati śāsanāt ।।

tapasaḥ saṅganirmukto na pāpagaṇasevakaḥ ।
saktūdakena santuṣṭaḥ sa bhikṣurniṣṭhuraḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

kaḥ śuddho bhikṣuḥ?

āgatān viṣayān sarvān tyajati jvalanopamān ।
viśuddhadoṣo maṇivacchuddho bhikṣurihocyate ।।

antarbahirviśuddhātmā jñānādibhiralaṅkṛtaḥ ।
śraddhayā śīlavastreṇa kriyāvān bhikṣurucyate ।।

lobhadharmavyatīto yaḥ sthito merurivācalaḥ ।
sarvalokapriyaḥ śāntaḥ pārago bhikṣurucyate ।।

trirātrivāsī kutrāpi kuśāsanavidhārakaḥ ।
girigahvarasevī ca vimukto bhikṣurucyate ।।

pāpabhīrurasaṃsparśī saṃvṛtaḥ ca susaṃvṛtaḥ ।
jñānasevī sthiraḥ śānta ekākī bhikṣurucyate ।।

acalaḥ priyavādī ca pāpamitravivarjitaḥ ।
aśaktaḥ sarvakṛtyeṣu mukto bhikṣurihocyate ।।

rājasevā kukaṣāyoktisevā

rājasevā vigarhyāsti bhikṣoścāraṇyavāsinaḥ ।
kukaṣāyoktisevāsau mṛtyutaskarajīvikā ।।

na hi rājasevako bhikṣuryaḥ sevyo devatairapi ।
na hiṃsāsavasaṃsṛṣṭo mahate aśucisevakaḥ ।।

bhikṣoḥ rājasevā na śobhate

nirmalasya nirāmasya nispṛhasya ca dehinaḥ ।
saṃsārabhayabhītasya rājasevā na śobhate ।।

vanāraṇyaśmaśāneṣu palvalo giribhūmiṣu ।
prāntabhūmiṣu grāmasya sthitaḥ bhikṣuḥ praśobhate ।।

vanāraṇyaśmaśāneṣu bhikṣurna rājasevayā ।
dhyānādhyayananirmuktaḥ kavalāhārabhojitā ।
na bhikṣuriti vijñeyaḥ piśācasamamānasaḥ ।।

dhyānāddhi vimalaṃ saukhyaṃ pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।
na tatsukhātsukhaṃ cānyadasti loke kathañcana ।।

taduttamadhyānasukhaṃ muktvā yaḥ puruṣādhamaḥ ।
raseṣu ramate bālastena mūḍho vihanyate ।।

viṣayairbhrāmitasyāsya nityaṃ tadgatacetasaḥ ।
vardhante akuśalā dharmāḥ paralokāpakarṣakāḥ ।।

ātmajño bhikṣurnirvāṇamadhigacchati

ātmano yānahīnaśca gurupṛcchanakastathā ।
bhikṣurudyuktavīryaśca nirvāṇamadhigacchati ।।

śrutaṃ yāvad bhavatyeva tāvadeva prabhāṣate ।
ātmajño mānahīnaśca bhikṣurbhavati tattvavid ।।

mānāpamānahīno yo mārgāmārgavicakṣaṇaḥ ।
svaparārthavidhijño yaḥ sa tuṣṭo bhikṣurucyate ।।

māninaḥ kutaḥ śāntiḥ?

māninaḥ krūramanasaścapalasyālpamedhasaḥ ।
lābhasatkārayātasya kutaḥ śāntirbhaviṣyati? ।।

prasannācārayuktasya jñānagocarasevinaḥ ।
saṃsāradoṣabhītasya pravrajyā saphalā matā ।।

svabhāvaparabhāveṣu yasya buddhirnamuñcati ।
na karmaṇyavipāke ca mārgāmārge tathaiva ca ।।

nivāsopahato bhikṣuḥ sukhaṃ na vindati
sadācāraviyuktasya sukhaduḥkhābhayasya ca ।
nivāsopahato bhikṣurbālavad dṛśyate paraiḥ ।।

tṛṇavallaghutāṃ yāti svārthācca parihīyate ।
nivāsopahato bhikṣuḥ parihīṇavane sthitaḥ ।।

dhyānādhyayanakṛtyeṣu mano naiva pravartate ।
nivāsopahato bhikṣurjanasañcayatatparaḥ ।।

sañcayavyagramanasā jīvitaṃ parihīyate ।
kṣiṇoti retasaṃ svasya jīvitaṃ naiva gacchati ।।

kaḥ durgatiṃ yāti?

na ca vindati yat kṛtvā sukhamanyatra bhujyate ।
nivāsopahato bhikṣurjanasañcayatatparaḥ ।
pāpāni yāti nityaṃ sa tena gacchati durgatim ।।

śrāmaṇyadharmasya mahattvam

anabhipretamanaso nirāśasya ca dehinaḥ ।
sarvasaṅgavimuktasya śrāmaṇyaṃ saphalaṃ matam ।।

girigahvaravṛkṣeṣu nityaṃ dhyānavihāriṇaḥ ।
prasīdati śubhaṃ jñānaṃ dauḥśīlyaparivarjitam ।।

keṣāṃ saphalaṃ jīvanam?

sarvasaṅgavinirmukto viṣayairna ca vañcitaḥ ।
bhikṣu niṣphalo jñeyaḥ śuṣkendhanamivānalaḥ ।।

nirvāṇābhiratasya bhikṣoḥ praśaṃsā

nirvāṇābhirato yo hi bhītasya vibhavārṇavāt ।
bhikṣurbhavati śuddhātmā na nivāsena karhicit ।।

tṛṣṇā eva anarthakarī

lobhamoheṣu ye śaktāste śaktā tṛṣṇayā sadā ।
tṛṣṇābandhanabaddhānāṃ nāyaṃ loko na cāparaḥ ।।

dharmajño durgati na labhate

asaṃśaktā matiryasya mithyākarmasu sarvadā ।
apakṣapātī dharmajño na sa gacchati durgatim ।।

kaḥ munirucyate?

doṣapaṅkemano yasya na limpati kathañcana ।
ekārāmavihārīyo nirāśo munirucyate ।।

nirmukto vimalācāro nivṛttamalakalmaṣaḥ ।
mukto yo viṣayaiḥ sarvairāraṇyo munirucyate ।।

lokadharmairna nirvedaṃ samāyāti kathañcana ।
sukhaduḥkhasamaprajño nirmalo munirucyate ।।

santoṣaḥ paramo nityaṃ kāmavivarjitaḥ ।
nirāmayaḥ kṛcchrajīvī śucirmunirihocyate ।।

nayenna tena saṃśleṣaṃ yatra yatrānugacchati ।
ekacārī dṛḍhamatiḥ kriyāvān munirucyate ।।

śubhāśubhānāṃ sarveṣāṃ karmaṇāṃ phalatattvavit ।
śubhāśubhaparityāgī loke asau munirucyate ।।

udyukto doṣanāśāya nityakāmagatiḥ smṛtaḥ ।
udayavyayatattvajño buddhimān munirucyate ।।

deśakālavidāṃ śreṣṭho advayavādī jitendriyaḥ ।
saṃsārabhayabhīto ayaṃ praśānto munirucyate ।।

kaḥ bhikṣuḥ nirvāṇamadhigacchati?

ekārāmagato bhikṣuḥ saṃkṣiptendriyapañcakaḥ ।
dehalakṣaṇatattvajño nirvāṇamadhigacchati ।।

vīryavān bhikṣurnityaṃ doṣavivarjitaḥ ।
udyānamiva krīḍāyā nirvāṇamadhigacchati ।।

kalyāṇadharmī bhava

dagdhe kleśe vayaṃ dagdhā vanaṃ dagdhaṃ yathāgninā ।
kalyāṇadharme saṃraktā na raktā kāmabhojane ।।

māyayā janāḥ vañcakāḥ bhavanti

nityaṃ prāptyutsukā ye nityaṃ svajanasaṃratāḥ ।
māyayā vañcakā mūḍhāste dharmavartmani ।।

śubhakarmaṇi manaḥ kāryaḥ

ramaṇīyānyaraṇyāni tatraiva ramate manaḥ ।
ramante vītarāgāste na tu kāmagaveṣiṇaḥ ।।

sa kathābhirato yastu rato viṣayatṛṣṇayoḥ ।
na yāsyati puraṃ śāntaṃ yo ca mṛtyuṃ na vindati ।।

advayavādī bhava

yo atyantaśāntamanasā nityaṃ dhyānaparāyaṇaḥ ।
ādimadhyāntakalyāṇo nityamadvayagocaraḥ ।।

।। iti bhikṣuvargastriṃśaḥ ।।

karuṇādānaśīlānikṣāntirvīryamathāpi ca ।
dhyānaṃ prajñātha nirvāṇo mano bhikṣuśca te daśa ।।

।। iti tṛtīyam udānam ।।

atha caturtham udānam

(puṇyadevasukhairmitrarājastutibhiranvitāḥ ।
saddharmasmṛtivaipulyai gṛhīto ayaṃ samuccayaḥ ।।

puṇyavargaḥ

puṇyapraśaṃsā

ramaṇīyāni puṇyāni phalaṃ teṣāṃ paraṃ śubham ।
tasmāt kuruta puṇyāni nāsti puṇyasamaṃ dhanam ।।

puṇyaṃ nidhānamakṣayyaṃ puṇyaṃ ratnamanuttamam ।
pradīpasadṛśaṃ puṇyaṃ mātṛvat pitṛvat sadā ।।

puṇyaṃ kṛtvā gatā devāḥ puṇyaṃ nayati sadgatim ।
puṇyaṃ kṛtvā narā loke modante tridive hi ।।

puṇyaṃ paraṃ sukham

puṇyādhikā hi puruṣā bhavanti sukhinaḥ sadā ।
tasmāt kuruta puṇyāni nāsti puṇyasamaṃ sukham ।।

puṇyaṃ kṛtvā gatā devāḥ puṇyapriyadhanasya ca ।
hetubhūtaṃ sadā dṛṣṭaṃ tasmāt puṇyaṃ paraṃ sukham ।।

puṇyādṛte sukhamasaṃbhavam

puṇyaṃ nityottamaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ chāyāvadanugāmikam ।
tasmāt sukhaṃ paraṃ puṇyaṃ nāsti puṇyādṛte sukham ।।

puṇyāpuṇyaphalayorantaram

puṇyottīrṇāḥ punardevā patanti sukṛtānugāḥ ।
puṇyāpuṇyaphalo lokastasmāt puṇyaṃ samācaret ।।

apuṇyanindā

ye puṇyahīnā durdāntā nityaṃ kugatigāminaḥ ।
kutasteṣāṃ sukhaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ sikatāsu yathā ghṛtam ।।

vittena vañcitā mūḍhāḥ puṇyena parivañcitāḥ ।
na teṣāṃ vidyate śarma duḥkhaṃ teṣāmanuttaram ।।

puṇyavaśād devalokaṃ gacchati

mānuṣyaṃ sukṛtaṃ hyetat kṛte bhavati dehinaḥ ।
tena karmavipākena svargalokeṣu jāyate ।।

priyo bhavati yasyātmā yasya saukhye sthitā matiḥ ।
sa karotu mahatpuṇyaṃ devalokopapattaye ।।

dharmacārī puruṣa eva sukhamavāpnute

dharmacārī hi puruṣaḥ sukhāt sukhamavāpnute ।
nirmalaśca parāṃ śāntiṃ kṣipramevādhigacchati ।
tasmāt kuruta puṇyāni sāṃpracāyikam ।।

puṇyakarttṛ avyayaṃ sukhamaśnute

puṇyakārī sadā dānto padaṃ gacchati cāvyayam ।
ramaṇīyāni puṇyāni karaṇīyānyanekaśaḥ ।।

puṇyasya vaicitryaṃ dharmasya upādeyatā ca

vicitraṃ hi kṛtaṃ puṇyaṃ vicitraṃ paripacyate ।
dharmādharmapradhānasya jīvalokasya sarvataḥ ।
śamatrāṇo yathā dharmastasmād dharmarato bhavet ।।

adharmī duḥkhaṃ prāpnoti

yo dharma parityajya ramate kukṛte naraḥ ।
tasya duṣkṛtadagdhasya duḥkhaṃ bhavati nityaśaḥ ।।

dharme eva manaḥ kāryam

yāvannābhyeti maraṇaṃ yāvat sakalacintanam ।
tāvad dharme manaḥ kāryamupaśāntirbhaviṣyati ।।

paropakartṛ nirvāṇapuraṃ yāti

yo hi deśayate dharma pareṣāṃ hitakāṅkṣayā ।
sa mātā sa pitā caiva nirvāṇapuradeśakaḥ ।।

śāstuḥ subhāṣitamamūlyam

śubhādhikaparaścaikaḥ yo deśayati deśikaḥ ।
sa gatyantaramārgajño nātho bhavati dehinām ।
na mūlyaṃ vidyate śāstuḥ subhāṣitapadasya vai ।।

sādhāraṇadravyād dharmadravyasya vailakṣaṇyam

na padaṃ labhate śāntaṃ yad dhanairupalabhyate ।
dravyaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ na dharmo buddhibandhanam ।।

dharmadravyamakṣuṇṇamasti

dravyaṃ vinaśyati nṛṇāṃ dharmadravyaṃ na jātu vai ।
ābhyantarasahastrāṇi dharma eko anugacchati ।।

na dhanaṃ padamapyekaṃ gacchantamanugacchati ।

hīyate draviṇaṃ teṣāṃ rājacaurokāgnibhiḥ ।
dharmavittaṃ na tacchakyamapahartu kathañcana ।।

ato dharmaparo bhavet

acireṇāpi kālena bhuktvā saukhyamanekaśaḥ ।
bhavatyavaśyaṃ patanaṃ tasmād dharmaparo bhavet ।।

dharma ekaḥ paraṃ trāṇaṃ dharma ekaḥ parā gatiḥ ।
dharmeṇa pūrvavartyeṣa maraṇaṃ cāpyadharmataḥ ।।

dharmacāriṇaḥ praśaṃsā

varaṃ dharmo dharmacārī dharmameva niṣevate ।
sa sukhāt sukhamāpnoti na duḥkhamanupaśyati ।।

adharmacāriṇo nindā

adharmacārī puruṣo yadādharma niṣevate ।
sa tadā duḥkhamāpnoti narakeṣu punaḥ punaḥ ।।

nirvāṇamahattvam

ratnatrayaprasādasya bhāvitasyāpyanekaśaḥ ।
phalaṃ bhavati nirvāṇaṃ pūrvasvargopajīvinaḥ ।।

ātmanaiva puṇyamācaraṇīyam

ātmanā kriyate puṇyamātmanā pratipadyate ।
sukhaṃ vā yadi vā duḥkhamātmanaivopabhujyate ।।

śīlavataḥ puṇyaprabhāvo vipulaḥ

nadīstrota ivājastraṃ puruṣasya pravartate ।
puṇyaprabhāvo vipulo yasya śīle rataṃ manaḥ ।।

bhavajanyaṃ phalaṃ yasya dharmo na rocate ।
dharmo hi nayati svarga dharmacārī sukhānvitaḥ ।।

dharmādṛte puruṣaḥ narakaṃ yāti

etadeva hi paryāptaṃ yad dharmaparipālanam ।
dharmādṛte hi puruṣo narakānupadhāvati ।।

dharmavigarhaṇānmaraṇaṃ śreyaḥ

śreyo bhaveddhi maraṇaṃ na tu dharmavigarhaṇam ।
dharmeṇa varjito lokaḥ saṃsāre sarvadā bhramet ।।

dharmavirahitasya duḥkhamayaṃ jīvanam

dharmacakṣurvimuktasya mohenākrāntacetasaḥ ।
vṛthā saukhyamidaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ dṛṣṭvā yāto yathāparaḥ ।।

dharmāṅkuro manaḥ kṣetre naiva rohatyacetasaḥ ।
yasya śīlapradā buddhiḥ dharmācaraṇatatparā ।।

śubhena saviśuddhena bhāvitena prayatnataḥ ।
prayānti tat padaṃ śāntaṃ yatra duḥkhaṃ na vidyate ।।

indriyavaśī māraṃ nātivartate

indriyāṇāṃ vaśe yastu viṣayeṣu tathaiva ca ।
sa sarvabandhanairbaddhaḥ sa māraṃ nātivartate ।।

pāpakairdharmairalipta eva svasthaḥ

aliptapāpakairdharmaiḥ nirdhanāt kanakadyutiḥ ।
sa muktabhavakāntāraḥ svastho bhavati sarvataḥ ।।

buddhādīnāṃ pūjayā nirvāṇalābhaḥ

buddho yeṣāṃ bahumato nityaṃ dharmaśca gocaraḥ ।
śuśrūṣācāryapādānāṃ śraddadhānaśca karmaṇām ।।

triratnapūjayā nityaṃ sadbuddhiśca nirmalā ।
mātāpitṛṇāṃ pūjātaḥ nirvāṇapuragāminām ।।

pravrajyābhāvadharmāśca sameṣāṃ samprakīrtitāḥ ।
brahmacaryāttacaryāṇāṃ sarvasaukhyāgrakārakāḥ ।।

dharmadānaṃ sarvottamam

dānānāmuttamaṃ dānaṃ dharmadānaṃ prakathyate ।
udyogānāṃ sadā dhyānaṃ yena gacchati nirvṛtim ।।

agrayastathāgataḥ proktaḥ

ūrdhvādhastiryaguktasya lokasyānekakarmaṇaḥ ।
agrayastathāgataḥ prokto dharmāṇāṃ tattvadarśakaḥ ।।

vargāṇāṃ cārthasaṅghore pravaraḥ śānta ucyate ।
kṣetrāṇāṃ trividhaṃ puṇyaṃ guṇaduḥkhobhayaṃ tataḥ ।।

mātā pitṛsamaḥ pūjya upādhyāyaḥ sadā bhavet ।
sa unmīlayate cakṣurvaśagocaratāṃ prati ।।

niḥsukhā viṣayā matāḥ

agrāhyā vā sadā dṛṣṭā muninā tattvadarśinā ।
sukhasya bhūmayo hyetā niḥsukhā viṣayā matāḥ ।।

yadyevaṃ kurute dharma nirmalaṃ mārgadarśinam ।
saukhyaṃ tasya bhavennityaṃ na saukhyaṃ devabhūmiṣu ।।

bhavāntareṣu sukṛtaṃ pṛṣṭhato dehināṃ sthitam ।
sa āhūya prayatnena sevitavyaḥ sadā naraiḥ ।।

anāgate bhayaṃ yo hi paśyati buddhacakṣuṣā ।
sa paṇḍitaḥ sadā dhīro mūrkhatvādatibhīrukaḥ ।।

vipattijaṃ bhayaṃ dṛṣṭvā paśyati buddhimān ।
sa hi vighne tu samprāpte na viṣādena bādhyate ।।

atha mūḍhamatirnityaṃ viṣayāneva sevate ।
vimohitaḥ sa viṣayaiḥ paścāttāpena dahyate ।।

samagraṃ janma puṇyāni karaṇīyāni

yāvat samagraṃ janmedaṃ jñānaṃ yāti vināvilam ।
tāvat kuruta puṇyāni duḥkhaṃ hayakṛtapuṇyatā ।।

kṣayaṃ prayānti puṇyāni tvaritaṃ yāti jīvitam ।
dharmasaṅgrahaṇe yatnaḥ karttavyastuṣite suraiḥ ।।

yo hi dharma parityajya pramādopahato naraḥ ।
na sañcinoti puṇyāni sa paścādapi tapyate ।।

na yāvadāyāti jarā na vyādhiḥ saha mṛtyunā ।
tāvat kāryāṇi puṇyāni mā paścāt paritapyatha ।।

asaṅgṛhītapuṇyasya pramādopahatasya ca ।
narake kāraṇaṃ duḥkhaṃ pramādastvāṃ haniṣyati ।।

kiṃ tasya jīvitenārthaḥ kiṃ bhāgyaiḥ kiṃ ca bāndhavaiḥ ।
sabalendriyatāṃ prāpya yo na dharmarataḥ sadā ।।

ahanyahani karttavyaṃ dharmasaṅgrahaṇe manaḥ ।
viratiścāpi pāpebhyaḥ sādhūnāṃ darśane na ca ।।

śīlena yaḥ suro janma labdhvedaṃ kāmamohitaḥ ।
na sañcinoti puṇyāni sa bhavaṃ nātivartate ।।

dharmaratāḥ sadā vandyāḥ

jñānārambhābhiratayaḥ śīlaratnavibhūṣitāḥ ।
kāmarāgāddhi ye bhītā devānāṃ devasammatāḥ ।।

devāste hi sadā vandyā ye dharme niratāḥ sadā ।
ye tu nityaṃ bhavāsaktāste sarve nidhanaṃ gatāḥ ।।

dharmasetumimaṃ prāpya pārāvāragataṃ mahat ।
na sañcarati yastūrṇa bhavānnaiva pramucyate ।।

śubhaṃ naiva praṇaśyati

śubhānucāridharmaiśca śubhaṃ bhavati sarvadā ।
kalpakoṭisahastreṇa śubhaṃ naiva praṇaśyati ।।

puṇyaprāptyarthe karaṇīyāni karttavyāni

saṅgṛhītaṃ sadā śīlaṃ jñānaṃ ca parivartitam ।
dānaṃ cābhikṣayā dattaṃ bhavati svarasātmakam ।।

sadaiva guṇāḥ sevyāḥ

doṣāstrayaḥ praṇaśyanti tribhirdānādibhirnṛṇām ।
tasmād doṣān parityajya guṇāḥ sevyāḥ prayatnataḥ ।।

jñānena laukikaṃ duḥkhaṃ naśyati

saṃsargo dharmaśīlānāṃ jñānārambhaḥ prayatnataḥ ।
naśyati bhavajaṃ duḥkhamarkapādairyathā tamaḥ ।।

abhyupeyo devarato devatābhiśca vandyate ।
prāpya janmāntara cāpi nirvṛtiṃ cāśu gacchati ।।

।। iti puṇyavarga ekatriṃśaḥ ।।

devavargaḥ

saugatamārge carantaḥ puruṣā devatulyāḥ

panthāno muninā śāstre uktā ye tattvadarśinā ।
taistu samprasthitāste puruṣā devasammatāḥ ।।

sugatokto mārgaḥ

satyaṃ hi dānaṃ ca tathaiva maitrī sattveṣu rakṣā priyavāditā ca ।
samyaktvadṛṣṭirvimalaṃ manaśca panthānamāhustridivasya buddhāḥ ।।

śukladharmasamāyuktaḥ śuklacittasamanvitaḥ ।
sukhāt sukhataraṃ yāti jyotirjyotiḥparāyaṇaḥ ।।

jyoti rjyotiṣā pūrṇa dīpo dīpāntarād yathā ।
tasmāddhi paramāṃllokān prayātā samprapadyate ।।

ācāravān devānāmantikaṃ vrajet

yasya śuddhaṃ sadā cittaṃ nirmalaṃ maṇivat sadā ।
sa śānto nirmamo dhīmān devānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।

dhyānaśīlasamādhibhyo yasya cittaṃ śubhānvitam ।
sa dhīmān kāñcanaprakhyo devānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।

prāṇātipātād virataḥ sarvasattvadayāparaḥ ।
ṛtusroto anukampāśca devānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।

śrutavān sarvalokasya krūrakarmavivarjitaḥ ।
aliptaḥ pāpakairdharmairdevānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।

tṛṇavat kāñcanaṃ yasya kāmā yasya viṣopamāḥ ।
sa kāmavarjako dhīmān devānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।

nākṛṣyate manaḥ kāmairviṣayai rāgahetubhiḥ ।
samantātbhavakāntārairdevānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।

bhinnāḥ paramparā ādau mitravān dhanabāndhavaḥ ।
yaḥ karoti susaṃśliṣṭā devānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।

yasya buddhisthitaṃ veśma na buddhiḥ kvāpi rāgiṇī ।
sa jitārirviśuddhātmā devānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।

praśastakāyakarmānto yaḥ pāpavirataḥ sukhī ।
sa kāmavirato dhyāyī devānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।

pāpamitravinirmuktastṛṣṇāviṣavivarjitaḥ ।
na baddhaḥ strībhayaiḥ pāśairdevānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।

prayatnavādī yo dharme dānaśīlasamādhimān ।
nityodyukto dṛḍhamatirdevānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।

samyagbandhano yena pāśaśchinno yathāsinā ।
sacchinnapāśaḥ svavaśī devānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।

śubhakarmavipākena devaloke udbhavaḥ

manuṣyabhūtā ye sattvāścaranti sukṛtāvahāḥ ।
tena karmavipākena suraloke prasūyate ।।

dharmapathāśritā eva balinaḥ

manuṣyāṇāṃ balād devā devānāṃ balino narāḥ ।
anyonyabalino te ye saddharmapathamāsthitāḥ ।।

tistro apāyabhūmayaḥ

devānāṃ sugatirmartyāḥ martyānāṃ sugatiḥ surāḥ ।
apāyabhūmayastisraḥ śubhakarmavivarjitāḥ ।।

sarva sukhaṃ dharmādhīnam

dharmādhīnaṃ sukhaṃ sarva dharmādhīnā hi nirvṛtiḥ ।
dharmaḥ supteṣu jāgarti dharmo hi paramā gatiḥ ।।

devairasurā jitāḥ

dharmeṇa nirjito adharmaḥ satyenānṛtiko jitaḥ ।
jñānena varjito moho devaistu hyasurā jitāḥ ।।

devalokaṃ sukhodayam

sopānabhūtā ye tāni karmāṇi tridivasya hi ।
yoniṃ tyaktvā narā yānti devalokaṃ sukhodayam ।।

vāksaṃyamena budhāstridivaṃ sukhaṃ bhuñjanti

caturvidho vāṅniyamaḥ ko api trividhapañcadhā ।
saptasopānamārūpyaṃ gacchanti tridivaṃ budhāḥ ।।

prabhayā te ca divyantaḥ svaśarīreṇa jātayā ।
ramante svargabhuvane rañjitāḥ svena karmaṇā ।।

śīlameva śubhasya kāraṇam

nityāmodavihārā nityaṃ saukhyavihāriṇaḥ ।
yad devā devabhavane śīlaṃ tatra hi kāraṇam ।।

yadapsaraḥ parivṛtā yat sūryaśaśisannibhāḥ ।
devāḥ samantād deveṣu tatsarvaśubhahetukam ।।

yadīpsitaṃ sambhavati sambhūtaṃ ca na hīyate ।
vartate ca śubhaṃ nityaṃ tat sarva śubhahetukam ।।

śubhacārī devānāṃ samatāṃ vrajet

śubhacārī sadā dānī sarvabhūtadayārataḥ ।
dānamaitryā sadā yukto devānāṃ samatāṃ vrajet ।।

prāṇātipātād virataḥ sarvasattvadayāparaḥ ।
samyagājīvakarmānto devānāṃ saṅgatiṃ vrajet ।।

adatte na ratiḥ kiñcid dāne cāsya sadāmatiḥ ।
śāntendriyamatirdhīmān devasaṅgatimaśnute ।।

mithyākāmairvimukto yaḥ satpathābhirataḥ sadā ।
nirvāṇakāṃkṣī vimalo devānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।

vimanaskaṃ hi yat prīte puruṣe kurute laghu ।
madyavarjī paraṃ dhīro devānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।

pramādavirahitaḥ sukhamāpnoti

sukha hi yo devaḥ pramādaṃ nānusevate ।
sukhāt sukhamavāpnoti nirvṛttiṃ cādhigacchati ।।

kṣayāvasānaṃ tat saukhyaṃ nirvāṇamiti śāśvatam ।
tat saprāpyavimāneṣu rājante puruṣottamāḥ ।।

uccāduccaro merustasmāduccaṃ sadā sukham ।
śubhena niyato janturakaniṣṭhān surān ।।

niravadye kutastṛptirdevaloke viśeṣataḥ ।
atīva saukhyaṃ labhate kasmād deveṣu sarvadā ।।

kaḥ saukhyamupalabhyate?

tṛṣṇāgniparidagdhena na saukhyamupalabhyate ।
evaṃ sukṛtadagdhena na saukhyamupalabhyate ।।

trividhaṃ sukṛtaṃ kṛtvā triprakāraṃ trihetukam ।
etadagryaṃ tribhūmiṣṭhaṃ phalaṃ mahat ।।

ahiṃsādānaparamā ye saddharmaparāyaṇāḥ ।
satyakṣāntidamairyuktāḥ tridivaṃ samāgatāḥ ।।

divyābharaṇasampannā divyamālyavibhūṣitāḥ ।
yad devā divyamatayaḥ śubhameva tat ।।

devānāṃ yanmahatsaukhyaṃ nyūnādhikyamāsthitam ।
nyūnamadhyaṃ tu yasyaitat phalaṃ puṇyasya dṛśyate ।।

puṇyakartā devalokaṃ gacchati

yena yāvaddhi yat puṇyaṃ kṛtaṃ bhavati dehinā ।
tasya tāvaddhi tat saukhyaṃ devalokeṣu pacyate ।।

śīlasaṃrakṣaṇamāvaśyakam

svāgataṃ tava bho bhadra! sukṛtaṃ kṛtavānasi ।
saptadhā rakṣitaṃ śīlaṃ tasyaitat phalamāgatam ।।

ramasva saha daivataiḥ

vanopavanaśaileṣu padmākaravaneṣu ca ।
harmyāgreṣu ramasva sadaivataḥ ।।

vanopavanaśaileṣu vaidūryaśikhareṣu ca ।
vanādriṣu ca naikeṣu ramasva saha daivataiḥ ।।

kalpavṛkṣeṣu ramyeṣu nadīprastravaṇeṣu ca ।
saritsu ca viśālāsu saha daivataiḥ ।।

strotasvinyādiyukteṣu parvateṣu nadīṣu ca ।
nagareṣu mahārtheṣu ramasva saha daivataiḥ ।।

madagandhipraroheṣu nīlotpalavaneṣu ca ।
yakṣasadmasu ramyeṣu ramasva saha daivataiḥ ।।

bhūmibhāgeṣu cānteṣu ratnākaravaneṣu ca ।
vimāneṣu ca ramyeṣu ramasva saha daivataiḥ ।।

pañcāṅgikena tūryeṇa manaḥprahlādakāriṇā ।
nṛtyamānaḥ sukhī nityaṃ ramasva saha daivataiḥ ।।

śīlabījaṃ śodhayitvā śīleṣu vividheṣu ca ।
krīḍa tvaṃ vividhairdivyairyathārthamanusevase ।।

yatprabhāmālino devā ramante vividhaiḥ sukhaiḥ ।
tacchubhasya phalaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ nirmalasya viśeṣataḥ ।।

yadetairvividhaiḥ saukhyairdevāḥ krīḍantyanekaśaḥ ।
na vayaṃ hetavastatra purākṛtam ।।

kūṭāgārāṇi sarvāṇi karmacitrāṇi sarvadā ।
bhunakti devo deveṣu satkṛtenopabṛṃhitaḥ ।।

pāśatrayavimuktasya pañcabhiḥ pālitasya vai ।
ekadharmavyatītasya devaloko mahīyate ।।

pramudyaccetasāṃ puṃsāṃ spaṣṭaceṣṭā samāhitā ।
āgatā devasadanaṃ svakarmaphalasākṣiṇī ।।

sukṛtaphalam

uparyupari saukhyāni sukṛtasya vai ।
bhuñjanti vibudhāḥ svarga yaddhi pūrvakṛtānugam ।।

sākṣibhūtā ime sarvakarmaṇāṃ vividhā drumāḥ ।
nirantaraṃ susadṛśaṃ kathayanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।।

bhāgyaṃ phalati sarvatra

yena yena vipākena yatra yatropapadyate ।
puruṣo labhate svasya prārabdhasya śubhāśubham ।।

śubhakarmaṇā prāṇī nityaṃ deveṣu jāyate

śubhena karmaṇā janturnityaṃ deveṣu jāyate ।
tathāśubhena narake patanti puruṣādhamāḥ ।।

kāmino maraṇaṃ nāvagacchanti

śubhāśubhābhyāṃ saṃraktāḥ kāminaḥ kāmamohitāḥ ।
nāvagacchanti maraṇaṃ yadavaśyaṃ bhaviṣyati ।।

śubhāśubhavipāko ayaṃ yo vṛkṣeṣūpalabhyate ।
na saukhyād viramantyete manaḥ saukhyena mohitāḥ ।।

sukṛtaṃ kṛtvā mānavāḥ deveṣu yānti

trividhaṃ sukṛtaṃ kṛtvā bhāvayitvā ca saptadhā ।
trisaṃkhyākān ripūn hatvā yānti deveṣu mānavāḥ ।।

kaḥ devānāmantikaṃ vrajet?

nāsūyati kriyākleśān na ca nandīmasūyati ।
sa nandyasūyakaḥ śuddho devānāmantikaṃ gataḥ ।।

vinindya mātsaryamidaṃ duḥkhasyāyatanaṃ mahat ।
samaṃ ca trividhaṃ dattvā devānāmantikaṃ gataḥ ।।

prāṇināṃ praṇayaṃ nityaṃ rakṣayitvānukampayā ।
maitracittaḥ sadā dānto devānāmantikaṃ gataḥ ।।

adattaṃ ca dhanaṃ dattvā dattvānandaṃ ca sarvataḥ ।
cetanābhāvitamatirdevānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।

mātṛvat paradārāṃśca dṛṣṭvā tattvārthacintakaḥ ।
alipto pāpakairdharmairdevānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।

svacittaprītyartha jihvāraṇisamudbhavaḥ ।
kathyate sa mṛṣāvādastaṃ hitvā sugatiṃ vrajet ।।

paiśūnyaṃ ca sadā hitvā maitryanarthakaraṃ padam ।
ślakṣṇaprabhaḥ ślakṣṇamatiḥ devānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।

pāruṣyaṃ śatruvaddhīro varjayatyeva sarvadā ।
ślakṣṇaprabhāmatirnityaṃ sarveṣu gatigāmikaḥ ।।

adharmo yasya jihvāgre na bhūto na bhaviṣyati ।
sadā duṣkālatattvajño devānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।

yenedaṃ rakṣitaṃ śīlaṃ saptadhā buddhadeśitam ।
sa dhīraḥ śīlatattvajño devānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।

kaḥ saphalaḥ dharmajñaḥ?

vividhakarmavaśagaṃ janmedaṃ labhate suraiḥ ।
tatprāpya yo na dharmajñaḥ sa paścāt paritapyate ।।

sukarmaṇā śubhajaṃ phalam

vanopavanaramyo ayaṃ latāvedikamaṇḍapaḥ ।
yadvicitramayo lokastat sarva śubhajaṃ phalam ।।

yena yena yathā karma kṛtaṃ bhavati śobhanam ।
tasya tasya tathā dṛṣṭaṃ phalaṃ tadanugāmikam ।।

pratyakṣaṃ dṛśyate devairhīnamadhyottamaṃ sukham ।
yena yena yathā cīrṇaṃ tasya tasya tathā phalam ।।

kukarmaṇā duḥkhajaṃ phalam

vicitraveṣāḥ saṃmūḍhā devā mohavaśānugāḥ ।
tannāśānmanasā mūḍhā na paśyanti mahadbhayam ।।

vicitrakāmaratayo vicitraphalakāṅkṣiṇaḥ ।
na vā kurvanti karmāṇi te asurā mūḍhacetasaḥ ।।

ke premaparāyaṇāḥ?

phalaṃ yeṣāṃ priyaṃ cittaṃ na ca śīle ratā matiḥ ।
te pradīpaṃ parityajya premālokaparāyaṇāḥ ।।

hetuphalatattvajñāḥ sukhino bhavanti

ye hetuphalasādṛśyenecchanti surasattamān ।
te hetuphalatattvajñā bhavanti sukhabhāginaḥ ।।

jñānādeva muktiḥ

vinābījaṃ phalaṃ nāsti vinā dīpaṃ kutaḥ prabhā? ।
vinā śīlaiḥ kutaḥ svargo muktirjñānaṃ vinā kutaḥ? ।।

kaḥ dhīmataḥ?

tatsukhaṃ tadvimuktasya gatakāṅkṣasya tāyinaḥ ।
vimuktakāmatṛṣṇasya nirmamasya ca dhīmataḥ ।।

sukarmaiḥ sukhaṃ bhavatyeva

yadidaṃ karmajaṃ saukhyaṃ sarva kalmaṣam ।
yaṃ neṣṭakaṃ bhavatyeva tat sarvamamalaṃ smṛtam ।।

devalokasya varṇanam

yo manorathakṛtsnasya bahirantaśca ।
sarvālokaḥ sadāloko devatāgaṇasevitaḥ ।।

virājate girivaro ratnamāṇikyasannibhaḥ ।
prabhūtasalilo yaśca padminībhiḥ samāvṛtaḥ ।।

vanopavanaramyo ayaṃ mṛgapakṣiniṣevitaḥ ।
kandarodarasaṃrambho bhitvā gaganamutthitaḥ ।।

kutra devataiḥ sevyate?

sevyate devatairnityaṃ divyamālyavibhūṣitaiḥ ।
nṛtyagītaprakṛṣṭābhirdevatābhiśca sarvataḥ ।।

pañcāṅgikena tūryeṇa prerita iva lakṣyate ।
śirobhūto mahāramyaḥ prabhāmālī samantataḥ ।।

sukṛtena śubhenāyaṃ karmaṇādhiguṇena vai ।
yaṃ samāśritya krīḍanti devavṛndāni sarvataḥ ।।

ke svarga gacchanti?

dānaśīlayutā vṛddhā nityaṃ tadgatamānasāḥ ।
ye bhavanti sadā dāntāste janāḥsvargagāminaḥ ।।

saṃkṣiptamanasaḥ śāntāste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।
vairiṇāṃ viṣayo nityaṃ praśāntamanasastu ye ।।

svargagāminaḥ ।
bhavābhavena tīvreṇa bādhate sādhanam ।
sudāntamānasāṃ dhīrāste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

satyamārgavilambena hayatīva sukhabhāginaḥ ।
sārāsāravidhijñāśca te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

saṃsāre ye na rakṣanti svamano dehinaḥ ।
nirvāṇābhiratā nityaṃ te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

vṛkṣamūle śmaśāne vā tathā ca girikandare ।
dhyāyinaḥ sattvamanasaste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

mātrajñā deśakālajñāḥ pāpamitra varjitāḥ ।
maitreṇa cetasā ye tu te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

na snānadarśanaratā narāḥ manmathavāriṇā ।
ekāntagāminaḥ śāntāste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

kṣaṇe kṣaṇe sadā kāyaṃ paśyantyaśucisambhavam ।
kāryākāryavidhijñā ye te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

dharmāṇāṃ dharmatāṃ ye ca paśyanti vividhā samāḥ ।
na ca rakṣanti saṃsāre te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

vedanā madhyatattvāntamanekavidhasambhavam ।
paśyanti ca na rakṣanti te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

māyopamaṃ ca kṣaṇikaṃ gandharvanagaropamam ।
ye jānanti cittāḥ te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

ekalakṣaṇatattvajñā vilakṣaṇavidaḥ svayam ।
nirvāṇarāgamanasaste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

mātṛvat paradārān ye pitṛvat sarvadehinaḥ ।
paśyanti ye bhayaṃ loke te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

śūnyavargagato nityaṃ sattvānāṃ priyavādinaḥ ।
akrūrā ṛddhimanasaste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

kāṣṭhavalloṣṭhavat sarva paravittasamīkṣakāḥ ।
saṃtuṣṭāḥ svena cittena te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

na rātrau na divā yeṣāṃ kausīdyadyutiriṣyate ।
nityodyuktavihārā ye te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

kaukṛtyaṃ styānamiddhaṃ ca kausīdyaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।
varjayanti sadā dhanyāste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

dauḥśīlyaṃ pañcarandhrebhyaḥ pariśuddhamanekadhā ।
saṃkṣipanti sadā duḥkhaṃ te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

upādānacatuṣṭvajñāḥ satyāni ca tathaiva ca ।
ye paśyanti budhāḥ prajñāṃ te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

duḥkhaṃ duḥkhavipākaśca duḥkheṣu ca manaśca yat ।
paśyanti ye sadā tattvaṃ te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

tīvravyasanamāpannā ye dharmāvimuñcakāḥ ।
śāntāśca dharmamatayaste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

śuklāvadātaṃ ye vastraṃ pāṃsukūlaṃ tathaiva ca ।
piṇḍapātaratā nityaṃ te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

adaṇḍāḥ śāntamanaso nityaṃ dhyānavihāriṇaḥ ।
naiṣkarmyaniratāḥ sarve te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

mṛṣṭaṃ ca yadi vāṅmṛṣṭaṃ yathecchāvidhimāgatam ।
santuṣyanti na kupyanti te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

śuklāvadātaṃ ye vastraṃ pāṃsukūlaṃ tathaiva ca ।
saṃvṛtau caiva saṃtuṣṭāste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

śayyātale yathā bhūmau harmyāgre vā tathāpare ।
na duṣyanti te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

cakṣurviṣayamāpannaṃ yatkarma sāmparāyikam ।
tattvato ye prapaśyanti te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

apriyaṃ vā priyaṃ vāpi ye śrutvā tīvrasambhramāt ।
akṣubdhamatayo muktāste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

ṣaḍindriyāṇi sarvāṇi viṣayāṃstu tathaiva ca ।
saṃkṣipanti na rakṣanti te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

yathā karma kṛtaṃ sarvamaviśeṣeṇa tattvataḥ ।
paśyantyamanaso dhanyāste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

karmaṇāṃ ca vipākaṃ ca kṛtaṃ ।
bibhyatīha sadā duḥkhete janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

ityetāni mahārthāni nityaṃ duḥkhakarāṇi ca ।
kurvanti vidhivat sarva te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

।। iti devavargo dvātriṃśaḥ ।।

sukhavargaḥ

sukhasvarūpanirūpaṇam

anuttareṣu saukhyeṣu dhyānopātteṣu ye ratāḥ ।
teṣāṃ sukhaṃ yathāvat syāt nirvāṇapuradarśakam ।।

navena sukhaduḥkhena purāṇamabhihanyate ।
devasyaitannavenaiva purāṇamabhihanyate ।।

dhū miśraṃ yathā kāṣṭhaṃ vi miśraṃ yathodanam ।
tathā sukhamidaṃ sarvamasvatvaṃ nāvagamyate ।।

nirvāṇapuragāmināṃ sukham

tat sukhaṃ yad vitṛṣṇānāmekāntasukhacāriṇām ।
nirmohiṇāmarāgāṇāṃ nirvāṇapuragāminām ।।

teṣāṃ vimalamādyantaṃ saukhyānāmapi tat sukham ।
yeṣāṃ tṛṣṇānugā cāśā sarvathā naiva cetasi ।।

saṅgṛhītasya cittasya nirātmasya ca sarvataḥ ।
kāryākāryeṣu mūḍhasya sukhaṃ nityamupasthitam ।।

kaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ sukhī?

sā bahirnihatā yena nandisaṃsārahetukī ।
sa dhīraḥ pāragaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ sukhī nirvāṇamāśritaḥ ।।

naitat sukhena tṛṣṇānāṃ yad rāgadveṣasaṃyutam ।
yatra rāgādinirmuktaṃ tat sukhaṃ nirmalaṃ matam ।।

kutra tṛṣṇā na bādhate?

devaloke samāsādya yaḥ suro nāvamanyate ।
sa sukhāt sukhatāṃ yāti yatra tṛṣṇā na bādhate ।।

tadantyasukhi śreyo yatra mṛtyurna vidyate ।

mṛtyupāśairna baddhasya na sukhaṃ vidyate kvacit ।
yat sukhaṃ kāmajanakaṃ na tat saukhyaṃ satāṃ matam ।।

yatra kāmavinirmuktastatsukhāt sukhamuttamam ।
yat sukhaṃ janayet śreyaḥ yathodanam ।।

yatra tṛṣṇāvinirmuktiḥ payomiśraṃ yathodanam ।
yathā padmavane gṛddhā yānti kravyabhakṣiṇaḥ ।।

evaṃ śānteṣvaraṇyeṣu na bhāntyaśubhacāriṇaḥ ।
kvacicchāntaṃ vanaṃ ramyaṃ kvacid devāḥ pramādinaḥ ।।

kaḥ paramaṃ sukhaṃ prāpnoti?

viparītaṃ na sadṛśaṃ bhānoḥ śītā yathā prabhā ।
gatatṛṣṇasya yat saukhyaṃ muktaduḥkhasya tāyinaḥ ।।

tasyāntareṇa saukhyasya sukhametanna gaṇyate ।
dhyāyinastvapramattasya muktapāpasya sarvadā ।।

tat sukhaṃ tat paraṃ saukhyaṃ nedaṃ tṛṣṇāvidāṃ matam ।
munisevyaṃ vanamidaṃ sevitaṃ ca subhāṣitaiḥ ।।

nārhā rāgagaṇaṃ sevituṃ bho surottamāḥ ।
yadetad bhavatāṃ saukhyametanna khalu śāśvatam ।।

tat sukhaṃ paramaṃ śāntaṃ vītatṛṣṇai niṣevyate ।
niḥsevitaṃ vanamidaṃ ye gatāḥ paramaṃ padam ।।

yat prāpya sarvaduḥkhasyacchedo bhavati sarvathā ।
brahmacaryādanirmuṣṭāḥ śīlālāpena vañcitāḥ ।।

bhikṣūṇāṃ vane vāsa eva sukhāvahaḥ

nārhanti sevituṃ ramyaṃ vanaṃ śāntaṃ subhāṣitam ।
śāntaṃ ca bhāvitaṃ ramate śubhagocare ।।

na rāgacāriṇāṃ cittaṃ ramate vanagocare ।
na rāgavyākulaṃ cittaṃ vaneṣu labhate dhṛtim ।।

kaḥ puruṣottamaḥ?

śravyāmūḍhā matiryasya nityaṃ tribhuvanaṃ kare ।
sa ratiṃ labhate śāntiṃ vane puruṣasattamaḥ ।।

sukhāya vanaṃ sevyam

sa kalparāgakuṭilo nityaṃ rāgādibhirvṛtaḥ ।
sa śāntiṃ naiva labhate vane śānte sukhāvahe ।।

yeṣāṃ tu manasā nityaṃ vane dhyānaniyoginām ।
vanaṃ teṣāṃ sadāramyaṃ na tu rāgagaveṣiṇām ।।

vaneṣu bhāvitaṃ cittaṃ nagareṣu na kupyate ।
tasmād vanaṃ sadā sevyaṃ nagaraṃ naiva śasyate ।।

vikṣipyate hi nagare nṛṇāṃ rāgādibhirvṛtaḥ ।
vikṣipta mohakuṭilaṃ vanaṃ bhūyaḥ prasīdati ।।

tasmād vanaṃ paraṃ śāntaṃ yogināmālayaṃ mahat ।
saṃsevyaṃ vītamanasā yasya tad vītakalmaṣam ।।

ratiṃ mā kṛthā

praśāntendriyacittasya yā ratiryogino hṛdi ।
nāsau śaktiḥ sahasrasya bhaviṣyati ।।

yā dhyāyino ratirdṛṣṭā vyavadānāya sarvadā ।
na yāmeṣvapi sā dṛṣṭā nityaṃ rāgānurāgiṇī ।।

ratiryā kāmavaśagā sā nityaṃ duḥkhasambhavā ।
yā tu kleśavaśāt prītiḥ śāśvatā nahi ।।

kaḥ śreyaspadaṃ prāpnoti?

śreyo vaneṣu caritaṃ tattaduccaritaṃ nṛbhiḥ ।
yasmāt tat pratibaddhaṃ hi śreyasāṃ padamucyate ।।

susambhṛtena dharmeṇa rakṣiteneva cetasā ।
sudṛṣṭaṃ labhate sthānaṃ yatra doṣo na vidyate ।।

yaḥ kṣiptamanasā nityaṃ na ca dharmaparāyaṇaḥ ।
teṣāṃ vṛthā sukhamidaṃ gacchati na nivartate ।।

tattvajñā duḥkhaṃ na paśyanti

ye tu tattvavido dhīrāḥ paśyanti jagataḥ sthitim ।
anityaduḥkhaśūnyānāṃ teṣāṃ duḥkhaṃ na vidyate ।।

sukhadharmasya caraṇaṃ jñānasya ca niṣevaṇam ।
ahiṃsā satyavacanaṃ tadapyekāntataḥ sthitam ।।

kaḥ svarga yāti?

ekadharmavyatītā ye ye adharmaparivañcakāḥ ।
tristhānalakṣaṇāviṣṭāste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।

sukhasya svarūpam

udayavyayadharmāṇāmanityaṃ karmajaṃ hi tat ।
tat sukhaṃ sāstravaṃ nityaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati ।।

tat sukhaṃ tadvitṛṣṇasya nīrāgasya hi dehinaḥ ।
muktirbhavati doṣasya pārasthasya hi tāpinaḥ ।।

tat kiñcit sāsravaṃ saukhyaṃ tat sarva kṣaṇikaṃ matam ।
rāgabandhād vinirmuktaṃ tat sarva niścalaṃ sukham ।।

ye na kṣipanti duḥkhena sukhe yeṣāṃ na saṅgatiḥ ।
te duḥkhasukhanirmuktā nirvāṇasukhagāminaḥ ।।

anupāyena ye mūḍhāḥ prārthayanti sukhaṃ sadā ।
bālukābhiryathā tailaṃ yallabhyaṃ nityameva tat ।।

na cetasā naraḥ prājño manorathaśatairapi ।
śakro api tat sukhaṃ kartu yathā karma kṛtaṃ mahat ।।

sukhāya dharmamācaret

sasukhaṃ yasya tu manaḥ saddharmānucaro bhavet ।
duḥkhairmuktyabhilāṣo ayaṃ sa dharme kurute matim ।।

nāhetukaṃ sukhaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ duḥkhaṃ vā trividhātmakam ।
sukhe duḥkhe pṛthagbhāve tasmānnu sukṛta caret ।।

nedaṃ saukhyaṃ sadā śastamadhruvaṃ vipralopi ca ।
tṛṣṇāviṣeṇa sammiśraṃ viṣamiśraṃ yathodanam ।।

tat saukhyaṃ satāṃ śastaṃ yatra mṛtyurna vidyate ।
na ca priyeṇa viśleṣo nāpriyeṇa samāgamaḥ ।।

kīdṛśaṃ sukhaṃ duḥkhajanakam?

yadetat strīmayaṃ saukhyametad duḥkhāya kalpyate ।
tadbījavartakā dṛṣṭā narakeṣūpapattaye ।।

yat sukhaṃ duḥkhajanakaṃ kathaṃ tat sukhamiṣyate? duḥkhād duḥkhataraṃ jñeyaṃ pariṇāmavaśena tat ।।

yadetad bhujyate saukhyametat kālena naśyati ।
sūryastāstaṅgatasyaivaṃ raśmayaḥ saha cāriṇaḥ ।।

vikṛtiṃ yasya manaḥ sukhaduḥkhairna gacchati ।
sa dhīmān suraloke ca gatvānyallabhate sukham ।।

bhuktaṃ sukhaṃ purāṇaṃ tu hīnakarma karoti ca ।
purāṇaṃ sukṛtaṃ śīrṇa mṛtyukāle na budhyate ।।

sarva sukhamanityaṃ bhavati

yadidaṃ dṛśyate saukhyaṃ manovākkāmajaṃbhṛśam ।
