anityaṃ tad vināśatvamacireṇa bhaviṣyati ।।

phenabudbudasaṅkāśaṃ marīcyudakasannibham ।
cañcalormi sukhaṃ sarva vinipāto bhavārṇave ।।

niṣpratīkāraviṣamaḥ sarvabhūtabhayāvahaḥ ।
cakravātapravego mṛtyurājaiṣa dhāvati ।।

nāśayitvā sukhaṃ sarva nāśayitvā ca jīvitam ।
karmasaṅkalpavāhyeṣu lokamanyatra neṣyati ।।

yadatīva sukhaṃ nṛṇāṃ taddhi saukhyāya kalpyate ।
yannaiṣyati sukhaṃ kiñcit taddhi naiva vigaṇyate ।।

vartamānaṃ tu yat saukhyaṃ tṛṣṇāviṣavivarjitam ।
sarva hyanātmajaṃ duḥkhamanityaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ balam ।।

laukikaṃ sukhaṃ na sukham

yad sukhaṃ triṣu lokeṣu na śastaṃ tattvadarśibhiḥ ।
tena matvā kathaṃ devā bhavanti vigatajvarāḥ? ।।

aviṣṭovatakālo ayaṃ bhairavo yāti sattvaram ।
yo bhokṣyate surān sarvān śuṣkendhanamivānalaḥ ।।

atiyāti sukhaṃ sarva kriyatāṃ śraiyasaṃ manaḥ ।
mā paścāt saṃbhavo yoge mṛtyukālo bhaviṣyati ।।

sukhamasthiraṃ bhavati

janmāntarasahasreṣu yad muktaṃ karmajaṃ sukham ।
taraṅgasannibhaḥ kvāyaṃ bāliśo asthiram ।।

kaḥ sukhena prasīdati?

na sukhaistṛpyate bālastathā kāṣṭhairyathānalaḥ ।
tasmānna saktasya sukhaṃ bhavati naiṣṭhikam ।।

viṣasya doṣamuktasya kāmadoṣānudarśinaḥ ।
dhyāyinaścāpramatasya tat sukhaṃ yadanāvilam ।।

sukhī bhavati tat prāpya na sukhaṃ bhavajanmanaḥ ।
bandhamiśraṃ viṣaṃ yadvad dharmasaukhyodayastathā ।।

kāmavirahitaḥ sukhamaśnuvate

tasmāt tatsukhasaktānāṃ nityaṃ kāmagaveṣiṇām ।
bhavantyanekasaukhyā tasmāt kāmo na jāyate ।।

jñānenaivendriyāṇi svagocare nivartante

nendriyāṇāṃ jayaḥ śakyaḥ karttu viṣayagocare ।
jñānena hi nivartante indriyāṇi svagocare ।।

bālā eva gatipañcake bhramanti

duḥkhe sukhābhisaṃsaktā nityaṃ bālā medhasaḥ ।
viparyayā paribhrāntā bhramanti gatipañcake ।।

kutra sukhaṃ duḥkhasadṛśaṃ bhavati?

yadatyantasukhaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tat sukhaṃ satyamucyate ।
yatra duḥkhaṃ vipākaṃ syāt tat sukhaṃ duḥkhameva tat ।।

pāpasyākaraṇameva sukham

anyāgatasya duḥkhasya pratighātayate budhaḥ ।
pāpasya hetujaṃ duḥkhaṃ pāpasyākaraṇaṃ sukham ।।

।। iti sukhavargo trayastriṃśaḥ ।।

mitravargaḥ

kaḥ pāpānnivārayati?

tanmitraṃ mitramityuktaṃ yanmitraṃ sāmparāyikam ।
nivartayati yaḥ pāpād vyasanāccāpi rakṣati ।।

praveśayati yannityaṃ taddhitaṃ sāmparāyikam ।
mitraṃ bhavati tannṛṇāṃ na mitraṃ pāpakārakam ।।

saṃsargajā doṣaguṇā bhavanti

apūtiḥ pūtisaṃśleṣāt pūtirevopajāyate ।
na pūtiḥ pūtasaṃśleṣamapūtiṃ karttumarhati ।।

yādṛśena saṃśleṣaṃ kurute puruṣaḥ sadā ।
taddoṣāt sadṛśo dṛṣṭaḥ śubho vā yadi vāśubhaḥ ।।

na śubhaṃ duḥkhakārakam

śubhārthī puruṣaḥ sarvānaśubhānnaiva sevate ।
tenāsau duḥkhamāpnoti na śubhaṃ duḥkhakāraṇam ।।

guṇadoṣayorlakṣaṇam

saṃśleṣajā guṇāḥ dṛṣṭā doṣāḥ saṃśleṣajātayaḥ ।
lakṣaṇaṃ guṇadoṣāṇāmidamuktaṃ svabhāvajam ।।

yaśasā yujyate yo hi nityaṃ sādhusamāgamāt ।
asādhu'saṅgamācchrīghraṃ prayāti puruṣādhamaḥ ।।

satsaṅgatiphalam

etat sāraṃ sadā kārya yadasādhuvivarjanam ।
sādhubhiśca sadā vāso duṣṭāṇāṃ ca vivarjanam ।।

doṣān samuddhareddhīmān guṇavṛddhiṃ samācaret ।
mitraṃ prakurvīta kausīdyavimukho bhavet ।।

na māninaṃ kusīdaṃ vā nityaṃ sarvānuśaṅkinam ।
liptapāpamatikrūraṃ mitraṃ kuryānna paṇḍitaḥ ।।

udyuktaṃ mṛdujātīyaṃ dharmiṣṭhaṃ doṣavarjitam ।
samyagdṛṣṭiracapalaṃ mitraṃ seveta paṇḍitaḥ ।।

na pāpakaṃ bhavenmitraṃ bhaveduttamapauruṣaḥ ।
uttamaṃ bhajamānasya na doṣebhyo bhayaṃ bhavet ।।

kaḥ laghutāṃ yāti?

rūpaiśvaryakulādīni bhidyante dehinaḥ ।
bhayapradaṃ taṃ mātaṅgaḥ prayāntaṃ naiva paśyati ।।

udvṛttaḥ puruṣo nityaṃ pramādākulitendriyaḥ ।
laghutāṃ yāti loke asmin pretyapāpeṣu pacyate ।।

rūpaiśvaryamadārthā ye te narāḥ pāpakāriṇaḥ ।
teṣāṃ na suśamaṃ pretyapāpeṣu pacyate ।।

rūpaiśvaryakulārthā ye na te tattvasya bhāginaḥ ।
atattvabuddhayo bālā na taranti bhavārṇavam ।।

jñānaśīlādiyutaṃ kulaṃ śreṣṭham

etatkulaṃ ye vibhavā yaccānyat sukhamiṣyate ।
sarvāṇyetānyanityāni tasmātteṣu na viśramet ।।

na jñānaśīlanirmuktaṃ kuśalaṃ yānti paṇḍitāḥ ।
yeṣāṃ jñānaṃ ca śīlaṃ ca te kule mahati sthitāḥ ।।

carituṃ cāmalaṃ śīlaṃ śīlameva mahādbhutam ।
mahākulaprasūtāste vaśamāninaḥ ।।

dānaśīlatapodhyānasatyaiśvaryaparākramaiḥ ।
saṃyuktā ye kulīnāste ye na dharmavivarjitāḥ ।।

naiśvaryajñānahīnasya na kulaṃ nāpi saṅgatiḥ ।
tasmātkulaṃ jñānamayaṃ jñānahīnaṃ na tat kulam ।।

।। iti mitravargaścatustriṃśaḥ ।।

rājāvavādavargaḥ

dhārmiko rājā svarga yāti

bhuvaṃ parijano paśyan dharmacārī jitendriyaḥ ।
sa rājā dhārmiko dhīmān svargalokopapattaye ।।

kaḥ lobhanirmukto rājā?

niyataṃ yaḥ karaṃ kāle dharmeṇa paribhujyate ।
sa rājā lobhanirmukto yāmānāmadhipo bhavet ।।

rājñaḥ svarūpam

kṣamāvān priyavākyo yaḥ krodhaharṣādidhārakaḥ ।
sa mahīṃ pālayettvenāṃ loke hi śreṣṭhatāṃ gataḥ ।।

apakṣapātinaḥ śraddhā mitreṇa ca hanyate ।
sa rājanyasabhājetā devalokāya kalpyate ।।

baddhadarśī mahātmā yo gurupūjaka eva ca ।
alolo yo dṛḍhamatirdevānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।

pūrve yat pitṛbhirdattaṃ devānupadiśanti ca ।
na ca hiṃsati bhūtāni sa deveṣūpapadyate ।।

dānaśīle sadā dakṣo dharmavādī jitendriyaḥ ।
sa matvāryāṃ mahīṃ kṛtsnāṃ devalokaṃ mahīyate ।।

nādhārmikaṃ dhārayati dhārmikeṣu ca rakṣati ।
sa dharmaśīlasaṃśuddho devānāmantikaṃ vrajet ।।

na strīṇāṃ vaśago rājā sādhūnāṃ ca vaset sadā ।
sa nirmalamatirdhīraḥ suralokopapattaye ।।

na sarvasya vacogrāhī priyaḥ sādhujanasya tu ।
so amṛtastattvadarśīvā nākṛṣṭa iva rohati ।।

ko yāmānāmadhipo?

yo dharmalobhamāyāti draviṇaṃ naiva lapsyate ।
sa lobhamalanirmukto yāmānāmadhipo bhavet ।।

na mithyādarśanenāpi strītvadarśanatatparaḥ ।
sa śuddha eva vimalo yāmānāmadhipo bhavet ।।

kaḥ rājā devapriyo bhavati?

prājñaḥ śīle sadāyukto dānenābhīkṣṇatāṃ gataḥ ।
pravijitya mahīṃ kṛtsnāṃ pretya devapriyo bhavet ।।

priyasya tu bhaved vākyaṃ stotrotsavakaraṃ param ।
āhlādayitvā vasudhāmante devopapattaye ।।

avisaṃvādakaṃ vākyaṃ yasya merurivācalam ।
satyasopānamāruhya devānāmantike gataḥ ।।

hrāsavṛddhī ca bhūtānāmakasmāt kurute hi yaḥ ।
sa rājā vai paro devairdevaloke ca tiṣṭhati ।।

manuṣyāntaratattvajño yo vetti hi balābalam ।
sa dhībalābhyāṃ saṃyukto yāmānāmadhipo bhavet ।।

traidhātukapadaṃ yacca ratnatrayamihocyate ।
yastat pūjayate rājā sa deveṣūpajāyate ।।

kālaṃ niyatadarśī yaḥ prajānāṃ ca hite rataḥ ।
sarvato bhadrakāntāro devānāmadhipaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

nindāmalavinirmuktaḥ saṅgadoṣavivarjitaḥ ।
jñānagocarasampūjyo niyataṃ deva eva saḥ ।।

kaḥ svarga yāti?

kausīdyadoṣarahito nityaṃ dṛḍhaparākramaḥ ।
nāśayitvā sa doṣaughān pretya svargeṣu jāyate ।।

sanmitraiḥ parivārito rājā devādhipo bhavati

hitāni yasya mitrāṇi karmakartṛṇi nityaśaḥ ।
sa mitraiḥ samparivṛto nṛpo devādhipo bhavet ।।

nānuseveta durvṛttān vākkṣepeṇa ca varjitaḥ ।
sa sadyo viṣanirmuktaḥ surāṇāmadhipo bhavet ।।

krodhaharṣavighātāya na ca pāpeṣu rakṣyate ।
sa pāpapaṅkanidhautaḥ suralokādhipaḥ sadā ।।

na śaktaḥ pānabhojyeṣu saṃsaktastu śubhe sadā ।
sa śuddhadharmasandarśī vibudho adhikatāṃ vrajet ।।

kaḥ padamuttamaṃ prāpnoti?

sucintitaṃ cintayati dharmeṣu ca vartate ।
dharmodayena dṛṣṭena yathā yāti triviṣṭapam ।।

saṃsārād dīrghasūtrād yastvaritaṃ dharmamācaret ।
sa dīrghasūtranirmuktaḥ prayāti padamuttamam ।।

dharmeṇa prajāpālakaḥ svargasukhaṃ yāti

dharmeṇaiva prajā nityaṃ prapālayati nṛpaḥ ।
sa dhārmikaḥ praśastātmā suraloke mahīyate ।।

daśeme kuśalā dharmā ihoktāstattvadarśinā ।
yaste prakurute dharmān sa surādhipatāṃ vrajet ।।

hetupratyayasandarśī mārgāmārgau tathaiva ca ।
sa dṛṣṭimalanirmukto vibudho adhikatāṃ gataḥ ।।

kīdṛśairguṇayutaiḥ rājā devānāmadhipo bhavati

yo devatāṃ pūjayati yathā cāhni mahīpatiḥ ।
sa devapūjito bhūyo devānāmadhipo bhavet ।।

anāvilena manasā prasannaścādhidārakaḥ ।
svasvadāraiśca santuṣṭo devānāmadhipo bhavet ।।

kaḥ śīlavān?

hīyate yo na viṣayaiḥ sarvabālāpahāribhiḥ ।
sa śīlavān divaṃ yāti nityaṃ śīlena rakṣitaḥ ।।

avidyāvarjakān nityaṃ sevate yaḥ sudhārmikān ।
saddharmacintakaḥ saukhyaṃ kalpate sura sadi ।।

pārṣadālāpahāribhiḥ ।
sa śīlavān divaṃ yāti nityaṃ śīlena rakṣitaḥ ।।

saddharmī rājā eva vasudhādhipatiḥ

sadvyāpārāddharmamimaṃ pālayan vasudhādhipaḥ ।
praśāsti ca mahīṃ kṛtsnāṃ yāmānāmadhipo bhavet ।।

satkarmaniratasya rājño bhṛtyo api śobhate

satkarmanirato bhṛtyo nṛpe sadguṇaśālini ।
jano nirmalatāṃ yāti śaraccandra ivāmbare ।।

kaḥ rājā devatulyo bhavati?

hetulakṣyavidhijñā ye aviruddhāḥ parasparam ।
samyaksvāmyarthakarttāraḥ devānāṃ vaśamāgatāḥ ।।

।। iti rājāvavādavargaḥ pañcatriṃśaḥ ।।

stutivargaḥ

buddhastutiḥ

samasattvāgravedāya sarvasattveṣu bandhave ।
sanmārgasārthavāhāya bhavabandhanabhedine ।।

nādṛṣṭivibhedāya sarvasaṃśayamocine ।
samyagdṛṣṭiniveśāya namaḥ sañjñānacakṣuṣe ।।

sarvasaṅkaṭabhedāya tridoṣamalaśodhine ।
namo nakṣatrabhūtāya sarvabījaphaloruhe ।।

sarvaprajñākarāgrāya sarvadhyānāgravedine ।
sarvaratnottamāryāya namo alānāgradarśine ।।

iyaṃ sā lokanāśasya viprayuktasya tāpinaḥ ।
pratimā dṛśyate śāntā mokṣamudghāṭyakārikā ।।

samarcatīmāṃ nityaṃ puruṣaḥ śāntamānasaḥ ।
sa mucyate bhavabhayānnivṛttiṃ cādhigacchati ।।

etacchāntapadaṃ ramyametannaiṣṭhikamucyate ।
yadayaṃ bhāṣate dharma nirvāṇapuradeśikaḥ ।।

asya vākyaṃ samālambya puruṣādhīnavikramāḥ ।
ākarṣanti padaṃ nityaṃ yadanantasukhāvaham ।।

etat pūrva samāruhaya puruṣāstattvacintakāḥ ।
trilokaughārṇavaṃ ghoraṃ taranti bhavasāgaram ।।

ayaṃ sa cakṣurlokasya samantāddhi vicakṣuṣaḥ ।
ayaṃ jyotiḥ paraṃ jyotiryajjyotiḥkāṣṭhasambhavam ।।

kalpāntaṃ prāṇināṃ citte nṛṇāṃ rāgādibhirmalaiḥ ।
jñānatoyena mahatā śodhayatyeva vāṅnṛpaḥ ।।

yanna dṛṣṭaṃ padaṃ sarvaistīrthikairjñānapāṇibhiḥ ।
tatpadaṃ vimalairvākyaistvayā nṛṇāṃ pradarśitam ।।

pramādaparamo anātho jano ayaṃ tāritastvayā ।
tīrṇaḥ pāragato nāthastārayatyaghanāśanāt ।।

hitārtha sarvajagatastvamevaiko vyavasthitaḥ ।
ahitānāṃ hitāyaiva tvameva puruṣottamaḥ ।।

anādimati saṃsāre nṛṇāṃ kleśāpahārakaiḥ ।
tvayā viśodhito vākyaistamaḥ sūryodaye yathā ।।

akṣayaḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ jñānalokakaro mahān ।
tvamevaiko jagannātha lokottaraguṇārṇavaḥ ।।

।। iti stutivargaḥ ṣaṭtriṃśaḥ ।।

puṇyadevasukhairmitrarājastutibhiranvitāḥ ।
saddharmasmṛtivaipulyai gṛhīto ayaṃ samuccayaḥ ।।

।। iti caturtham udānam ।।

ye ca dharmā hetubhavā teṣāṃ tathāgato avadat ।
teṣāṃ ca yo nirodhaścaivaṃvādīmahāśramaṇaḥ ।।

puṇyamavāptamantrakleśaṃ vibhidyājanavalāśrīkam ।
yāvajjagadvyākulaṃ tarkaniṣṭhaiḥ samākulaṃ vetti satyavacanaiḥ ।।

vaipulyamahāgambhīrodadhisūtravarād bhikṣu avalokitasiṃhenoddhṛtamiti ।

mohāśivādirahitasya vākyavidyasya vipulārjanasya adharmasamuccayo' nāma dharmaparyāyaḥ samāptaḥ ।

।।
